Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka ákɛ́ kɛmɛ kɛ́mbé. Dɔ̌ ká Mandɛm antɛmsi mmu anɛ ákʉ́ ntɨ bɛbʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, “Mɛ kɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kɛ́mɛ kɛ́mbé. Mɛ kɛ nchí kap mmu ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́.”
Mbɔŋ bɛ́rɛm ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ chi ɛnyɨŋɨ́ ntíánwɔ́p.
Ghatí mmu anɛ átwɔ̀ nɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ ándɔ́ barak ákɔ́rɛ́., Mbák ɔ́ngátí yí ndɔŋ amɔt, ndɔŋ ɛ́pay, abhɨkɨ ghók, fɛrɛ́ nti nɛ yi.
Yesu asɔt akɛ́m awɔ, abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ntí ághá nɛ́ arɛ? Nɛ nnyɛ́n chi ɛnɛn ághá?”
Sakio asɛp amɨk áyák, anak Yesu ɛkɛt yi nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák.
kʉ bɛ́ mandɔ wɔ ɔmbak Mfɔ wap; nɛ bɛ mánkʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́yaŋ bo mankʉ fá amɨk, mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛchi awu amfay.
Nɛ be babhɔŋ bǎkʉ̀ batɨ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́, mǎnyiɛ nɔkɔ batɨ̌ bǒ nkwɔ́ nsɛm amɔt.
Barɔk ntá bǒbatí bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk baghati bhɔ bɛ, “Sɛ́nyǔ nku, sɛ́yɨ́kɨ́ mmʉɛt bɛ́ sɛ́pú nyiɛ́ nɛ sɛ́pú nyú yɛ̌nyɨŋ tɛ sɛ́ngway Pɔ̌l.
Mɛ kɛ nchí mbǐnywɔp. Mmu anɛ áfʉɛ̀t ntá ya kɛ anchwe, ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́pú tɔk yi. Ǎchwè, amfú mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ákɔ́ŋɔ́, ambɔ́ŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ.
Bápɛ́rɛ ghoko mmɨk, mmu anɛ achi Ɛyɔŋ anáŋ achi nyaka. Abhak nɛ Mandɛm, nɛ abhak Mandɛm.
Mpok Yesu achi ɛtɔkɔ́fu, mmu ɛbhaŋákwa amɔt arɔk akwɛ́n yí bɛkak abho mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá yi bɛ́, “Acha, mbák ɔkɔŋ, ɔ̌kway bɛkʉ mɛ ntaŋ.”
Bǒbhó bare bɨk bɛ, “Chi ɛyɔŋ mandɛm. Puyɛ chi ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ nkwǎŋwaŋ!”
Kɛ mmʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ achák wu are sayti yi bɛ, “Yɛ̌ndu ɔ́gù ndǔ ɛkotákátí mbɔ Yesu, ɔpú cháy Mandɛm-ɛ́?
Yɛ̌ chí nɛ́nɛ, sɛtɨ sɛ́chí bhʉɛrɛ́, nɛ bákway bɛkpɔt yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɛpu nyu bɛrɨ́tɨ́ kɛpɛm tɛ ndǔ bakaŋ, mangʉɛp angó.”
Kɛ ɛwak Hɛ́rɔd ánáká ɛpǎ nɛbhe ɛyi, mmɔ̌ Hɛródias anɛ mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ abhɛ́n nɛbhɛ́n sayri bɛsí bo abhɛn bachi ndǔ ɛpǎ yɔ. Nɛbhɛ́n ɛni nɛkʉ Hɛ́rɔd abhɔŋ bɛyǎ maŋák,
Dɔ̌ yɛ́ ka ɛpɨŋ ɛyɛka ɛ́ngɔ́ mbɔ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́. Ɛpɨŋ ɛyɛka ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛbhak mbɔ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́ bo mángɔ́, mámbɨti Ɛtayɛka mmu achi amfay.”
Abhak nɛ Mandɛm tɛ ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt.
Ghɔ́ ká amɔ ya nɛ bɛkak ɛbha, mǎndɨŋɨ bɛ chi mɛ tɛtɛp. Mɔ́ ká mmʉɛ́t ya mǎngɔ bɛ chi mɛ. Ɛfóŋó ɛ́pú bhɔŋ mmʉɛt nɛ bɛghɛp mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎghɔ́ bɛ mbɔŋ.”
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áchyɛ́ be nkɔ́p manyiɛp mǎnyú mbɔnyunɛ bǎchí bakoŋo abhɛn Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, apu nɔ́k bɛbhɔŋ akap.” 
Mandɛm Acha akʉ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi bɛ́jwi nɛ mɛ tontó mbɔ nnyɛ́n ɛnɛ́n nɛ́jwí, nɛ́gbóko, nɛtaka ɛbhɨ. Akʉ mɛ mbɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu, achyɛ́ mɛ ɛkɔŋ nkwɔ́. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ bo abhɛn bábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Mmǔ ntí bǒnkwɔ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ nɛ abhɔŋ bɛ́bhɔŋ chí ngɔrɛ́ amɔt. Abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mɛ́ŋwaka ndu yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Abhɔŋ bɛbhak mmu anɛ ákɛ̀m mmʉɛt, nɛ abhɔŋ bɛ́bhʉɛrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bo báchyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó, nɛ abhɔŋ bɛbhak mmu anɛ ásɔ̀t mankɔ sayri, nɛ abhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛrɨ́tí ntɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ mmu ánchyɛ chyɛ́ ɛrɨ́tí bakak ntá Mandɛm, nɛnɨkímʉɛt ɛnɔ nɛ́pú chyɛ mmu achak bɛtaŋ.
Bɔ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛghok máyi nɛ ɛtayi, mbɔnyunɛ bǎchi bakoŋo Acha nɛ ɛchi chak bɛkʉ nɔ.
Bápɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́yɔ́kɔ yi, báfɛ́rɛ nkú chu yi amʉɛt, básɔ́t ɛyi yímbɔŋ bákɛ́mɛ yi amʉɛt. Básɔ́t yɛ yi bárɔ́k bɛgo ndǔ ɛkotákátí. 
Tɛ́mté wu, batɨ̌ bǒ nkwɔ́ Yesu bátɨ́k Pɔ̌l bɛ andɔk tɛ angɔkɔnyɛ́n, kɛ Sáilas nɛ Tímɔti bárɔ́p Bɛ́roa.
Kɛ Kristo achyɛ mmʉɛt yi mbɔ akap ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bho ndɔŋ amɔt nɛ akap wu ákwáy ndǔ mpoknkɛm. Akó yɛ amfay achɔkɔ amɛm mɔ́kɛt anɛ achi Nyáŋá, ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm Mandɛm.
Bakoŋo bhi bárɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re tat ɛnɛ bǒ batí Israɛl báyàŋ bɛ́tɛmti wɔ nɛ batay mángwáy, ɔbhɛ́ ɔ̌pɛtnsɛm arɛ́?”
Nɛ́nɛ, nchí rɛm ntá yɛka bo bǎpú bo Israɛl, tɛ̌ndu nchí mǔnto ntá yɛka, bɛ́ mpú sɔt bɛtɨk ɛbha mbɔ ndaká ntok,
Kɛ abhɛ́nɛ́fú bɛ, “Chí Ɛláija.” Báchák bárɛ́m bɛ, “Ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ amɔt anɛ tɛ nyaka”
Kɛ mbák bǎchyɛ̀ kɛnókó ntá mbɔk bho, mǎmbyaka nɔkɔ abhɛ́nɛ́fú, nɔ́ bǎkʉ bɛbʉ́ ndǔ bǎkwɛ̀n ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ bǎchí bo abhɛn bǎpú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm.
Jɔ̌n achi nyaka mbɔ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnɛ ɛ́dù ɛ́ngɔ nɔkɔ ŋwaaŋ, ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok, bǎka ɛyɔŋ ɛyi nɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋ maŋák ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmú anɛ ákwàk bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Mandɛm, abhɔŋ bɛbhay chi ngɔrɛ́ amɔt. Yí nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi bábhɔŋ bɛ́kɛm bɔ̌bhap nɛ ɛfo yap ɛnkɛm sayri.
Nɛ chɔŋ nkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay mɛ́mfakari amfay, nɛ ntɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay fá amɨk. Chɔŋ manoŋ ambak, ngó ambak, mɔ́ngo ambak.
Ɛ́fákári bɛ bachwi achak anɛ áfú Tibérias átwɔ́ kɛkwɔt ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bɔ mányíɛ́ nyaka brɛt mpok Acha ánaŋ áchyɛ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ mbɔk batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm abhɛn báfú Yerúsalɛm, bátwɔ́ nyaka bákáp Yesu.
Bo báfú Judɛ́ya bátwɔ́ Antiɔk bábhó bɛtɔŋ bǒnkwɔ Yesu mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mandɛm apú kway bɛ́pɛ́mɛ mmu mbák babhɨkɨ syɛp yí bɛkoŋo ɛbhé Moses.”
Kɛ wɔ Tímɔti, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌tɔ̀ŋ wɔ, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛna, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌kay ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ ndu mbɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Yesu, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ ndǔ mɛ̌kɛ̀pntɨ, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ ndu mbɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkɔŋ nɛ bho, nɛ ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ ndǔ mɛ̌tè kákáti mpok ɛsɔŋɔri.
Kɛ Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re pay amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mfɔ Debhít ákʉ́ nyaka nɛ bǒ abhɛn báchí nɛ yi mpok nsay ákɛ́mɛ́ bhɔ́?
Asɛmti bhɔ́ bákɛ́ pɔkɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ nɛkɔ ɛnap, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́fʉɛt chí ntɛ́m. Yí bákɛ́ pɔkɔ nɛnyíɛ́, nɛ yɛ̌ bɛbhǎ-nɛkɔ, nɛ yɛ̌ chi nkáp.
Bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn Antiɔk baghoko nɔkɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ágábɔs árɛ́mɛ́, báká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛ mánchwɔp nkáp manto ndu bɛkwak batɨ̌ bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn báchi atú Judɛ́ya. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛ́chyɛ mbɔ ɛnyu amɔ yi atɔŋɔ.
Bǒ bakáp, bǎchyɛ́ bɛsɔŋ ntá bataŋá manyé nɛ bákʉ́ bachɛ́bhɛ́bho mǎnkwɛn manyé, nɔ chi bo abhɛn bábhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ mɛnu nɛ bhe mánchɛ́t bhe mbi. 
Bakwǎŋwaŋ abhɛn bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ way, kɛtɨ́knsɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bághókó nɛ amɔ. Bɔ́ kɛrɔ bɛchyɛ kɛnókó ntá bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ, nɛ ntá bɔmandɛm nsé abhɛn bɔ babhɔŋ bághókó nɛ pú, nɛ abhɛn bághókó nɛ silbha, nɛ abhɛn bághókó nɛ brɔ́ns, nɛ abhɛn bághókó nɛ batay, nɛ abhɛn bághókó nɛ mɛnɔk, nɛ bɔmandɛm nsé bhɔ bápú ghɔ mbaŋ, bápú ghok mbaŋ, nɛ bapu kɔ!
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí nyaka nɛ ngɔrɛ́ Lɔt.
Mpok yɔ, ɛpǎ bo Israɛl ɛnɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Ɛpa Bɛ́tɛm   ɛ́rɔp kɛkwɔt.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́, ɛ́táká nɛntɨ bǒnkwɔ bɛ nkoŋo Yesu wu abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛ́gu. Kɛ, sayri sayri, Yesu abhɨ́kɨ́ ghati nyaka Píta bɛ Jɔ̌n apu gú. Arɛm chi bɛ, “Mbák mɛ̌yáŋ bɛ yi ákɛ́ gú tɛ́ mpɛtnsɛm, ɛyɔ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ́ ná?”
Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bhɛsɛ nɛ Pɔ̌l, abho bɛkoŋo bhɛsɛ ambɨkɨ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Bǒbhɛn chí bǒ bɛtok Mandɛm mfay! Bághàti bhe ɛnyu Mandɛm ápɛmɛ bho.”
Nchí ghati bhe tɛtɛp bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛfakari, kɛ mkpáká bho abhɛn ɛchɔŋ amfʉɛ́t.
Apɛtnsɛm ɛbhě manyu Jɔ́dan, ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Jɔ̌n ájwìti nyaka bho, abhak arɛ́.
Mmu ywɛka anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ngɔrɛ́, ákɛ́ rɔ yí. Anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ ngɔrɛ́, ákɛ́ nu bɛ́bháy ngɔrɛ́.
barɛm bɛ, “Ghatí bhɛsɛ, ntɨkɨ bɛtaŋ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ́ ɔ́kʉ̀? Agha áchyɛ́ wɔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɔ?”
“Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ ɛbhé Moses ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Mbák mmu achɔ́ŋtí nyɛ́sɛ́ ntɨ mánchɔ́ŋtí ɛni nkwɔ. Nɛ mbák mmu áfɛ́rɛ́ nɛ́nyɛ́n ntɨ, bábhɔŋ bɛfɛrɛ ɛni nkwɔ.’
Ndu ɛchi yɛ nɔ, yɛ̌ sɛ́bhʉɛ́t chi fá amɨk, yɛ̌ sɛ́chí chí awu nɛ yí, nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ chi bɛ́ sɛ́nkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛkʉ yi ámbɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ bhɛsɛ mpoknkɛm.
Baghɔk Yesu bágháti bhɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ mpok yi átó bhɔ. Bárɔ́ yɛ bɔ mándɔk nɛ mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu.
Báfa bárɔk, bághɔ mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu wu sɛsɛ́t nɛfí ɛkɛt, nɛ́kú mbi. Bábho bɛ́kaŋarí yɔ.
Ángɛl anɛ ájwí batay apɨkɨri ɛyi ɛkwɔp ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛnɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ. Ɛjuri ɛ́kwɛ́n amʉɛt bo abhɛn yi achi Mfɔ wap. Bǒ bábho mɛŋa barɨ yap ndǔ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ bɔ bachi arɛ,
Nɛwú, bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ amfay nɛpɛ́m bɛchi fá? Bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́sɔ̀t bɛsak bho bɛ́chí fá?
Mandɛm aywǐntí kɛ̌ ákʉ́ bɛ́ mǎnkwáy bɛ́bhát mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo. Yí kɛ̌ apɛt ákʉ́ bɛ Yesu ánchyɛ́ bhe nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛ́n tɛtɛp, nɛ ɛ̌ti Yesu kɛ̌ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ be mbɔ bǒ abhɛn báchí chák bɛsí bhi. Akʉ bɛsɛ́ sɛ́mbák pɛ́pɛ́p, bakwap tí. Yesu rɛ́ kɛ̌ ákʉ́ bɛ́ sɛ́ndɔ́p chí bo Mandɛm nɛ achyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni bɛ́kú bɛsɛ́ sɛ́kɛ́ pɛrɛ bhák ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́.
Arɔk yɛ nɛ Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas. Ndu bárɔ̀ŋ, mángati nɔkɔ bo ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bachwɔbhɛ arɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒnto nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk abhɛn bachi Yerúsalɛm bárɛ́mɛ́, nɛ mánsɛmti nɔkɔ bhɔ́ bɛ mámbʉrɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɔ sayri.
Achwe nyáká amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm anyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn báchyɛ́ mbɔ akap ntá Mandɛm. Achyɛ ntá bǒbhi nkwɔ, mányíɛ́, ɛnɛ́ ɛbhé ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka nyaka bɛ mmu achak anyiɛ, ɛbhɨkɨfʉɛt nkʉbɛtɨk amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Ɛ́fákári nɔ ndǔ mpok anɛ Abíata achi mǔngo ndǔ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm.”
Tɛ̌ndu Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ kɛ áchyɛ́ bɛsɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ́nɛ, sɛbhɔŋ bɛrɔ yi ámbɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ.
Ɛ́rɔp manywɔp apay ndu mɛ́nyiɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ ndu bɛ́tɨk nɛfɛrɛ Mandɛm áfɛ́rɛ́ bo Israɛl ndǔ kɛsɛm amɛm ɛtɔk Íjip, nɛ Ɛpǎ Brɛt anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yís. Bo bati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses báre yaŋ mbi bɛkɛm Yesu bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ mangway.
Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Twɔ́ nyiɛ́ ká nɛnyíɛ́.” Kɛ yɛ̌ nkoŋo amɔt kɛmɔ bɛbhɛp yi bɛ, “Ɔchí agha?” Bárɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ chí Yesu Acha.
Básɨ́ŋ amɔ achí nyaka ndǔ bɛyɔŋ ɛtɔk bɛrat, ndǔ ɛyɔŋ bo Israɛl, nɛ ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ Latin, nɛ ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́ Grik. Nɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bágó Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí abhak kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ ɛtɔk ɛgho. Ɛ́kʉ́, bɛyǎ bo Israɛl bápáy basɨ̌ŋɨ́ mɔ.
Bákʉ Jáson nɛ bǒnkwɔ bhɔ bághɔ́kɔ nkáp ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ bápú pɛrɛ chyɛ ɛsɔŋɔri. Bárɔ́ yɛ bɔ́ mandɔk. 
Abhɛ́p yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛbhé yɛsɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ sɛ́nkʉ yi ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt? Bɛ́ sɛ́nkʉ bɛrɨ kɛ chi bɛbʉ́? Chi bɛ́pɛ́mɛ kɛ chí bɛchɔŋti nɛpɛ́m?” Bárɔp kpákpák.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ syɛp bhɔ ndǔ nkwɔmʉɛt kɛ bábhʉ̀ɛrɛ ɛbhé mándɛm chɔŋ bɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛchi nɛ be bo Israɛl mbɔnyunɛ bǎpu bhʉɛrɛ ɛbhé yɛ̌ndu Mandɛm achyɛ nyaka bhe bɛbhé ɛbhɛn básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɨk, apɛt achyɛ bhe ɛpɨŋ bɛsyɛp bho.
Kɛ mbák Acha ǎtàŋ bhɛsɛ́, ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ́ ntɛ́msí ndu mɛ́nyúrɛ bhɛsɛ́ bɛ́ ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mmɨk, ákɛ́ tɛmsi bhɛsɛ́ nkwɔ́.
Nɛ nɛfyɛ́ báfyɛ́ mɛ fá mbɔ mǔkɛnɔŋ ákʉ́ bɛyǎ bǒnkwɔ básɨkɨntɨ nɛ Yesu Acha sayri, kpatɛ bághàti bho báchák Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛcháy.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu arɨŋɨ bɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhi mɛmay. Ndu bɛkʉ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp, arɛm bɛ, “Manyiɛp ǎkwak mɛ.”
Kɛ Mandɛm akʉ yí ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, afɛrɛ yí ndǔ bɛbě nɛwú mbɔnyunɛ nɛwú nɛpu kway nyaka bɛbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy yi.’”
Ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm ɛ́móko tɛ́mté ɛrɔk ɛ́tɛ́mɛri Yesu. Mánɨk yi mmʉɛt bɛ ándɔ́ atú ɛtɔk ɛyap.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu afa nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́ wu arɔk aghɔ́ mbɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛ́nti anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Lɛ́vi chɔkɔ amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́bɛtɨk yi. Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Twɔ́, bhák nkoŋo wa.”
Kɛ anɛ áfʉɛ̀t ndǔ nyǔbhá, chí mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n.
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ ndǔ nkubhɛ bɛti ɛbhɛn Mandɛm anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́, Mandɛm anɛ mɛ̌chyɛ kɛnókó, ató ángɛl aywi átwɔ́ áté mɛ nɛpak mmʉɛt,
Tɛ̌ndu manoŋ Kristo árɔ́ŋɔ́ amɨk ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ, Mandɛm ásɔ̀t bɛ sɛ́chí chak bɛsí bhi nɛ́nɛ. Ɛchi mbɔ̌ŋ tɛtɛp ɛcha bɛ Kristo ǎpɛmɛ chɔŋ bhɛsɛ bɛ bɛběntɨ Mandɛm bɛ́kɛ́ bhak nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Bápú tɛmsi mmu anɛ ánókó yi, kɛ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ ka mɛnoko, bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛchi nɛ yi mbɔnyunɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ ka mɛnoko Njaŋa-Mɔ Mandɛm.
“Bǎrɨŋɨ ndǔ ɛbhé Moses ɛ́pɛ́t ɛ́ghàti nyaka bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bɛ, ‘Kɛ́ fyɛ́ bariɛp bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ntɨ bɛkʉ yɔ. Mmu abhɔŋ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyɨ́kɨ́ bɛkʉ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Mandɛm.’
Mbɔk ɛyap bábho bɛ́páti Yesu batiɛ́ amʉɛt. Básɔt ndɛn bágwɔt yi amɨ́k. Báre dɛpti yi mándɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ghatí bhɛsɛ! Agha ádɛ́bhɛ́ nɔ́ wɔ?” Babhabhɛri básɔt yi. Ndu bárɔ̀ŋ, mándɛpti nɔkɔ yi. 
Yesu áchwé nɔ́kɔ́ ɛtɔk, arɔk amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Abók bakɔ̌siɛ nɛ bo abhɛn bákù mɛnyɨŋ. Atakati bɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ ɛsiɛ bakap bɛwupsi. Atakati nkwɔ́ mɛnɔk bo abhɛn bátì bɛbhóŋó.
Babhɔ̌ŋ bǒbatí bárɔ́k yɛ mánɨkmʉɛt ntá Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas bɛ mǎmfóŋórí bhɔ́. Báfɛ́rɛ yɛ bɔPɔ̌l ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, mánɨ́kmʉɛt ntá yap bɛ mándɔ́ ɛtɔk ɛyap.
Ndǔ ngwɛnti, ngɔrɛ́ wu nkwɔ agú.
Akabhɛ́ nya bɛsɔŋ bɛchyɛ wɔ ápú chyɛ wɔ maŋák. Yɛ̌ chí akap anɛ bo báchyɛ bɛ ampɔkɔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap apu chyɛ wɔ maŋák.”
“Mandɛm akɔŋ nyaka bǒ mmɨk tontó, kpát achyɛ Njaŋá Mɔ́ywi bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ánókó yi, ákɛ́ gu ánɛ́m, kɛ ámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛ́nti.
Mandɛm afʉɛ́t ntá yi kɛ ǎghoko mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm. Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ ghoko yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi apu nɛ yi.
Bǎrɔŋ nyaka amɛm baso bɛghɔ yi? Mmu anɛ afyɛ́ bɛrɨ́tí ndɛn amʉɛt kɛ? Bǒ abhɛn báfyɛ̀ mɛnyǔ ndɛn ɛbhɔ báchɔ̀kɔ chi amɛm bɛkírí-bafɔ!
Ndǔ ɛkáti ɛnɛ njámbɨ ntǒ bhe, ngátí bhé bɛ bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ barak ɛpúsí.
Mbɔk bho bárɛ́ rɛm bɛ, “Chí yi.” Báchák bɛ, “Ǎe, kɛ achí mbɔ yi,” kɛ yímbɔŋ arɛm bɛ, “Chí mɛ.”
Ángɛl anɛ ngɔ́ ndu atee nɛ ɛkak ɛ́mɔt ndǔ manyu, ɛkak ɛchak ɛbhɨ, asá awɔ́nɛm ywi amfay.
Ɛnyǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɔ nɛ́pú fú ntá Mandɛm, nɛ́fù chí ntá bǒ- mmɨk. Ɛnyǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɔ nɛ́fù chí ntá bo abhɛn Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ɛ́pú nɛ bhɔ́ nɛ nɛ́fù chí ntá mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ.
Wáwák! Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌yàŋ bɛkʉ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ chí bɛ akap anɛ́ bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm báchyɛ̀, báchyɛ̀ chí ntá bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ, puyɛ̌ chí ntá Mandɛm. Nɛ mpú yáŋ mǎnchɛ́m mmʉɛt nɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ.
Bábhe Mpɛmɛ ywɛka ɛchɔŋ ɛtɔk Debhít. Yí kɛ achi mmu anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò. Yi chi Acha.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághók bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ághátí bǒnkwɔ Sádusi ɛ́kʉ́ manyu áchók bhɔ. Báté ɛyu, báyáŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ɛnɛ bábhɛp Yesu.
Kɛ mpok mmu átɨ́kɨ́nsɛm ndǔ ɛsɨ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni, ǎtwɔ̀ ntá Acha bɛ amfɛrɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kútí ntɨ ɛni.
Ngók ndǔ ángɛl anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfǎy manyɛ́n árɛ̀m ntá Mandɛm bɛ, “Wɔ ɔ́chí Nyáŋá. Wɔ ɔ́chí nɛ́nɛ nɛ ɔchí nyaka! Ɔchí chak ndǔ ntɛmsi anɛ ɔ́chyɛ̀.
Ángɛl anɛ ájwí manwi apɨkɨri ɛyǐ ɛkwɔp ndǔ mmok. Báchyɛ mmok bɛtaŋ bɛsɔŋ bǒ mbɔ ngó.
Mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛfakari, abɨti Mandɛm, andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛp, mmǔ-nɛ achí mbʉ chak bɛsí Mandɛm!”
Ngɔ bɛ́ ɔbhɔŋ ɛpɔ̌ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ ɔ́kwɛ̌n nsɛm antɛn bɛbʉ́.”
Mbák kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ abhɔ̌ŋ bɔ nɛ yɛ̌chi bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ, bɔ́ bábhɔŋ bɛ́kwak nnɛrɛ́kɛt wap mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm áyàŋ. Bábhɔŋ bɛ́kap bachi nɛ manɔ bhap ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bákʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ́ ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ Mandɛm maŋák.
Yesu afa, arɔk Násárɛt, ɛtɔk ɛnɛ máné yi arɛ́. Mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛpɨŋ ɛyi ɛchi nyaka, arɔk amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, afate bɛpay Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Aghati yɛ bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ bɛ manchɔkɔ amɨk ndǔ tákɔ. Asɔt yɛ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt bhɔ bɛ́táy nɛ nsi ɛpay. Ayoŋ amɨk mfay. Achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm, abho bɛ́bɔ́kɔ́ti brɛt wu anchyɛ nɔkɔ ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ mánkɔ́rɛ́ nɛ nsi ntá bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ.
Nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhákántɨ bɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari ɛnyu ɛyɔ, ǎbhʉ̀rɛ ntɨ ɛni pɛ́pɛ́p mbɔ Kristo.
Kɛ be bǎpú koŋo nɛpɛ́m bakwǎŋwaŋ. Bǎkòŋo chi Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm tɛ̌ndu yi achi nɛ bhe. Mmu anɛ Ɛfóŋó Kristo apu nɛ yi apú mmu Kristo.
Mbák ɔ́ntɛ́p mánɛ́n amɨk, ɔ́nchyɛ mɛ kɛnókó, mbɔ Mandɛm ywɛ, chɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm mɛ́nndɔp ɛbhɛ.”
Kɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chí ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti ya ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chá ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Jɔ̌n árɛ̀m. Nkúbhɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́kʉ̀, bɛ́tè mɛ ntísiɛ bɛ Ɛta kɛ átó mɛ.
Bárɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛta, chyɛ̌ bhɛsɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɔ mpoknkɛm.”
Bǒbatí bhɔ ɛsǎ nsɛm manwi nɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnwi ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí nɛpɛ́m bákwɛ́n bɛsí Mandɛm mmu achi chɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyi mánchyɛ nɔkɔ yi kɛnókó bɛ, “Amen. Haleluya.” 
Sɛ́nsɔ́t bɛ́ mmu ywɛká amɔt, yɛ̌ ngɔrɛ́, yɛ̌ mbakanɛm, anɛ áchí ntɨ mmu Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ndɛn ɛnɛ yí afyɛ́ amʉɛt nɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn yi ányìɛ.
Kɛ ayibhiri mmʉɛ́t, anɔnɛ, afʉɛ́t nɛntɨ nap arɔk ɛbhakayi. 
Mpú pɛrɛ ghati bhe bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔnyunɛ mfɔ mmɨk ǎtwɔ̀. Abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay ya.
Chɔŋ bɛcháy mɛ́nkɛ́m bakɔ̌siɛ abhɛn bákwɛ́nɛ́ nyaka bǒ bakáp ndu bátì mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhap ntá bo Bábilɔn. Chɔŋ bɛcháy mɛ́nkɛm bɔ ɛ̌ti ɛrɛm ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ bǒ Bábilɔn bachi arɛ́, mánte nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ mándi, nɛ basɛ́mɛ́ antɨ mandɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ,
Kɛ mbák mmu ǎbhɔ̀ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti yi achi mmu Kristo, ntíánwɔ́p ákɛ́ kɛm yi. Ánkáká nɔ́kɔ́ kaka Mandɛm bɛ yi aká nnyɛ́n bɛ mmǔ Kristo.
Batɨ̌ bǒ bɛtɨk bághɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́, batɨ ábé bhɔ tontó. Bárɔ́k bágháti mfɔ wu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, ɛnɛ ɛfakari.
Ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bo báchyɛ̀ be ɛsɔŋɔri, fá ká arɛ́ áyák mǎndɔk ɛtɔk ɛ́chák. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ bǎpú kway bɛkɔ ndǔ bɛtɔk Israɛl mɛnkɛm bɛkʉ bɛtɨk ɛbha ɛnɛ́ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɨ́kɨ́ re pɛtnsɛm.
Ǎghɔ̀ ntínso nɛ bǒ abhɛn báchyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó, ndǔ mkpáká bho ɛnkɛm.
Yesu ató yɛ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n nɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká toŋtí mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́ sɛ́nyíɛ́ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ.”
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnap nɛ́fù chí arɛ́? Nɛ bǒ abhɛn báwày nnya ɛnɛ́ bo bátwɔ̀ nɛ yɔ́ mbɔ akap, bábhɔ̀ŋ nɛnyíɛ́ ndu nnya ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ báwày?
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ rɔ bɛkoŋo bɛkaká nɛkɔ ɛbhɛsɛ mbɔnyunɛ bɛyǎ bho bachi abhɛn bɛpɨŋ ɛbhap bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ bɔ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ árɛ̀m bɛ́ Kristo agu ndǔ ɛkotákátí ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ. Nnáŋ nchí ghati nɔkɔ bhe ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mpok nɛ mpok, nɛ nɛ́nɛ, mpɛt nchí ghati bhe nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́rɛ́ nɛ babhɛsɛ amɨ́k.
Mmu ákɛ́ pɔkɔ́ ɛbhǎ nɛkɔ, nɛ yɛ̌ chí nkú áchák, nɛ yɛ̌ chí nkwɔbhánya ɛ́chák, nɛ yɛ̌ chí ntɛ́m. Bo bábhɔŋ bɛ́chíɛ nkʉbɛtɨk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ.
Mmu ǎkwáy bɛ́rɛ́m bɛ, “Mbɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ nkɔ́ŋɔ́.” Ɛ́chí tɛtɛp, kɛ ɛ́chí nkwɔ́ tɛtɛp bɛ́ puyɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ kɛ̌ ɛ́kwày bɛ́kwák bhe. Mbɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌bhák nsɛm antɛn ɛyi ɛ́pú.
Ntɨkɨ mpok ɔ́twɔ́ mbɔ kɛnkɔ, kɛ sɛ́sɔ́t wɔ chí mbɔ mɔ́mayɛsɛ? Ntɨkɨ mpok ɔ́chɛ́bhɛ́ ndɛn, kɛ sɛ́chíɛ wɔ ndɛn?
Mǔngo bachiǎkap afate arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkɛmɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒbhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ ɔkʉ?”
Ɛ́rɨ ntá yɛka ɛcha mbák bǒ básɔ̀kɔti bhe ɛ̌ti bǎchi bakoŋo Kristo mbɔnyunɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ Ɛfóŋó bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm, nɔ chi Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm, achi nɛ bhe.
Kɛmmʉɛrɛ Hɛ́rɔd nɛ Páílet kɛ́bho ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ nywɔp ɛnɔ. Ndǔ mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm bachi nyaka chi ndǔ mpap. 
Tɨk ka nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bǎté arɛ ndu bɛrɔŋ kɛkwɔt nɛ Mandɛm. Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ te chi ndu nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mmu ákway bɛtɔk nɛ awɔ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo Israɛl báté nyaka anɛrɛ́-njiɛ Sináy, mángɔ́ nɔkɔ ndǔ ngó ádù amfǎy njiɛ gum gum gum, bághɔ́ ɛjuri ɛnɛ ɛ́giri pyɔɔ ndu ɛ́chwé, mbaŋ kɛpɛrɛ ghɔ, nɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ ánu nɔkɔ.
Chɔŋ nchyɛ́ bɛtaŋ ntá batísiɛ bha bapay, mámbak nɛ ndɛn ákpá amʉɛt, nto bhɔ bɛ mandɔk mangati bo ntó ɛna, ndǔ manywɔp (,) nka amɔt nɛ bɛsay byo nɛ arat.”
Nɛka ɛnɛn chi nɛ nnɔ Moses kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ bábhɛ́sɛ́ yi anywɔ́p ndǔ bataŋ arat mpok bábhé yi, bɛ́ bákɛ́ way yi. Bákʉ nɔ ndǔ bághɔ́ bɛ Moses arɨ acha, bɔ kɛchay bɛkwɛn ɛbhé Mfɔ Íjip.
Ǎtwɔ̀ bɛkpɔt manyé bo mmɨk nkɛm, antɛmsi abhɛ́n bápú kʉ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bo Mandɛm ɛ̌ti bɛpɛpti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bárɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti yi.”
Báchɛ́m arɛ́ baka ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛ mánkɛ́m Yesu bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ mángwáy.
Mbɔk bho báchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ kɛnókó kɛ bachak bábyak bhɛsɛ byak. Mbɔk bho bárɛ̀m ɛrɨ́rɨ́ ɛ̌ti ɛyɛsɛ, kɛ báchák bárɛ̀m chi ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti ɛyɛsɛ. Bo básɔ̀t bhɛsɛ mbɔ bǒ bapu, ɛnɛ́ sɛ́rɛ̀m chi tɛtɛp.
Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ̀ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ nɛ afyɛ́ bho ntɨ, ánkwák be mǎmbak ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ batɨ bɛkoŋo ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Yesu Kristo árɔ́,
Mánáŋ mánáŋá bɛ́gháti bǒ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ bɔ mangati bho, nnya mbʉ́mbʉ anɛ áfu ndǔ nɛpi ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti ǎnù nɛ bhɔ ansɔt awɔ́nɛm, angway bhɔ.
Yesu abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɔ̌yáŋ mɛ nkʉ́ wɔ yi?” Nnɛ́mámɨk wu akɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Acha, nchí yaŋ bɛ mpɛt ngɔ́ mbaŋ.”
Ndu ɛchi yɛ̌ nɔ, sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛsɔt mpok sɛ́mbʉrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́náŋ sɛ́ghɔ́kɔ́ bɛ sɛ́kɛ́ rɔ bhɔ sɛnɛm ɛbhɨ.
Bɔ mankɛm babhak mbɔ batí byo nɛ apay.
Nkúbhɛ́ mmu anɛ ásɛ́bhɛ́ amɨk kɛ ákó kpát afʉɛ́t nɛbu, bɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm mɛ́mbak mbɔ ɛnyu bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛbhak.
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, chɔŋ mǎndi babhɛsɛ ansɛp nɔkɔ amɨ́k nɛ mámbɔŋ basɛ́mɛ́, kɛ bǒ mmɨk mámbɔŋ maŋák. Chɔŋ mǎmbɔ́ŋ basɛ́mɛ́ kɛ basɛ́mɛ́ amɛka anjibhiri andɔp chí maŋák.
Ángɛl anɛ ájwí bátándát afe ayi mmbá. Ngók ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú ndǔ bati ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap pú bɛsí Mandɛm.
Apɛt árɛ̀m nɛbhʉɛt achak bɛ, “Chɔŋ ɔ́mbak nchiakap mpoknkɛm mbɔ ɛnyu bárɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ɛ̌ti Mɛlkísɛdɛk.”
Ngók yɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛchak ɛnɛ ɛ́fú amfay ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Bǒbha, fú ká, mǎndɔ ɛtɔk Bábilɔn kɛka mǎmfyɛ mmʉɛt ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ. Fú ká, bɛ ntɛmsi Mandɛm anɛ átwɔ̀ ntá yi akɛ bhak nɛ bhe.
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bárɔk ntá Yesu bábho bɛkɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ yi. Báré yaŋ mbi mɛmɔ yi. Bábhɛ́p yi ankʉ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔŋ bɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛ́fú chi ntá Mandɛm.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, aghɔ́ ndu kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́-ngɔrɛ anɛ ɛyi ɛ́pú átwɔ́, afyɛ́ bɔ̌bɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nkáp bapay abhɛn bapu yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Nchí yaŋ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ nchí nu tontó ɛ̌ti nkwɔ Kristo anɛ Laodísia nɛ ɛ̌ti bakwɔ́ bho bachak ankɛm, abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́re ghɔ mɛ.
Tɛ̌ mmɨk ábhó, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re ghók bɛ mmu akʉ amɨ́k ánɛ́nɛ́ mmu anɛ bábhé yi amɨ́k nɛ́mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́.
Bɔ̌ma, mbák mmu árɛm bɛ́ yí abhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm kɛ yí kɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ yi ánkʉ, ɛyɔ ɛ́kwàk yi ná? Bɛ́rɛ́m chi nɛ nyu bɛ yi abhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm, apú kwáy bɛ́pɛ́mɛ yi wáwák ndǔ ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bo.
Mandɛm aywǐntí kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ́fyɛ bɛbhé, nɛ ndiɛrɛ yí aywǐntí, kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛ́táŋ bo. Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́pɛ́mɛ mmu, nɛ yí kɛ árɛ̀m bɛ́ mmu ángú, angú. Kɛ mbák chí wɔ́, ɔkáysí bɛ́ ɔchí agha bɛkʉ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ ntaŋá manyé, ɔ́ndɛm bɛ́ ntɨ mmu Mandɛm abɛp. 
Mámɔ́ mɛ amɛm baso ɛnyu ɛyɔ, nɛ bághɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nkʉ́ nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnap ndǔ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛpay.
Bákway mɛnoko mpok bághɔ̀ kɛnókó ɛkɛn báchyɛ̀ Mandɛm nɛ ndǔ bǎchí chak bɛsí bhi.
Bě babhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ́ nkʉ bɛtɨk nɛ amɔ́ya ndu bɛbhɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ nɛ bo abhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀ bɛtɨk Mandɛm nɛ bhɔ sɛ́chɛbhɛ.
Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Twɔ́ ká mǎmbák bakoŋo bha nɛ chɔŋ ntɔŋ bé ɛnyǔ bǎkʉ bɛ́ bo báchák mambak bakoŋo bha.”
mángati nɔkɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu. 
nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka anɛ áyàŋ bɛbhak mmǔ mbɨ abhɔŋ bɛbhak nsɛm aywɛka,
Mfɔ akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, ‘Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bǎkʉ nyaka bɛrɨ ntá bo abhɛn báchí mbɔ bɔ̌maya, yɛ̌ chí ntá mmu wap amɔt anɛ ápú yɛ̌nyɨŋ, ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔt mbɔ bɛ bákʉ̀ nyaka bɛrɨ ɛbhɔ chi ntá ya.’
Nɛsɔt Júdas ásɔ́rɛ́ brɛt wu, Satan akó yi anti. Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ chɔŋti mpok bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́yàŋ bɛkʉ.”
Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu anɛ átó mɛ áyàŋ nkʉ chi bɛ nkɛ́rɔ yɛ̌ mmu amɔt anɛ yi áchyɛ́ mɛ ánɛ́m, kɛ bɛ́ nkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn ngwɛnti.
Sɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ Milɛ́tɔs, Pɔ̌l ató ɛyɔŋ bɛ bǒbatí nkwɔ Yesu abhɛn Ɛ́fɛsɔs mántɛ́mɛ́rí yi arɛ.
“Bǎkɛ́ kɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ nɛ awɔ. Yɛ̌ chi bɛghokoti, bǎkɛ́ ghokoti ɛnyǔ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɔ. Yɛ̌ bɛtɔk, bǎkɛ́ tɔk ɛnyǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ.”
Kʉ yɛka batɨ̌ yɛka bɛ bǎpú sɛmɛ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔŋɔ bɛrɛm ndu bɛtaŋa mmʉɛt,
Báchyɛ́ yi ɛkáti ɛnɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya. Anɛnɛ yɔ́, ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́:
Yí bɛ́ bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛghɔk nnyɛ́n mánkɛ́m bɛbhɔ́k ɛnɔk nɛ bɛbhɔ́k áchwí anɛ ádákáti mánkwák mmʉɛt mǎnkó ɛbhɨ. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛ́fákárí kɛ bhɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́kó ɛbhɨ nyɔ́rɛ́ɛ́.
Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, mbabhɛri ɛkɛrákap amɔt anɛ áchí arɛ́ téé, adɛp Yesu nɛ awɔ́ arɛm bɛ, “Kwáé, ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɔ́rɛ̀m kɛpɨ ntá mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm-ɛ?”
Yí amʉ́ɛ́t kɛ̌ kɛnɛ́m Mandɛm kɛ́tɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ nɛ ɛnyǔ mmu Mandɛm achi, nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu mmu wu kɛ yi achi. Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ nɛ yɔ kɛ yi ásɔ̀t bɛkɛm mmɨk nkɛm. Mpok yi ánáŋá bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ Mandɛm amfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bho bɛ mámbák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí bhi, akó amfay achɔkɔ ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm Mandɛm mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm.
Bɔangɛl abhɛn tándrámɔt bátóŋti yɛ mmʉɛt bɛfe mmbá ɛyap tándrámɔt.
Wáwák! Yɛ̌ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achi nsěnse, Mandɛm ákʉ̀ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́. Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, “Ɔ̌tɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́rɛ̀m bɛ ɔchí chak, nɛ mpok bákpɔt manyé yɛ, bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛpu bhak nɛ wɔ.”
Páílet apɛt arɛm kɛpɨ ntá yap nɛ nkaysi bɛ́fɛ́rɛ Yesu amɔ.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, chɔŋ Mandɛm amkpɔ́t manyé áyák anchyɛ bǒbhi. Kɛ mpok Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm, chɔŋ angɔ́ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm fá amɨkɨ́?” 
Mpok yɔ ǎyibhiri mmʉɛt andɛm yɛ ntá bo abhɛn bachi ɛbhe awɔghɔ ywi bɛ, ‘Fǎ ká mɛ bɛsí, bě bho ntɛmsi Mandɛm achi nɛ bhe! Fǎ ká, dɔ́k amɛm ngo anɛ apu nɛmɛ yɛ̌ ɛwak, ngó anɛ́ Mandɛm aghókó ábhʉ́rɛ́ ntá Satan nɛ bɔángɛl abhi.
Kɛ mpok anɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm mɛ́mbak antɛn Kristo kɛ̌ mbɔŋ Mɔ́ywi afyɛ́ mmʉɛt antɛn Mandɛm, mmu afyɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ antɛn yi, bɛ Mandɛm aywǐntí ambak Mfɔ, nɛ yɛ̌ mmu achak ákɛ́ bhak mbɔ Mandɛm.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛnɛ ɛchi nɛpɛ́m ndǔ ɛbhɛn mɛnwi ɛ́chyɛ bɔángɛl bhɔ tándrámɔt bɛkwɔp ɛbhɛn pú tándrámɔt. Bɛjwi nɛ bɛběntɨ Mandɛm anɛ achi nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ánjɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀, nɛ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ sayri áŋák nɛ mmʉɛt ɛyi, kɛbhak bɛ ǎyɛ̀nti mmʉɛt nɛ mmǔ achak.
Bakoŋo Yesu bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Acha, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́fàkari chɔŋ fá?” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɛgú-nnya ɛchi, arɛ́ kɛ̌ kɛnɛn ɛkɛn kɛ́nyìɛ̀ bɛgú nnya kɛ́chɛmɛ.”
chi-bɛtɨk ywi ǎkway bɛ́twɔ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn yi abhɨkɨ kaysi bɛ yi ǎkway bɛpɛtnsɛm.
Mfɔ, ndu nchí rɔ́ŋ, bɛ́gháka nɛ́ntɨ́ ngósí, bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chá ɛbhɛn nnyɔ́mok bɛ́fú amfay bɛ́kwɛ́n bɛkap mɛ nɛ bo abhɛn mɛ́kɔ̀ nɛ bhɔ.
Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ mmu Íjip ádɛ̀n mmu Israɛl amɔt, arɔk bɛkwak yi. Akɛmɛ kɛ́mbé, kpát awáy mmu Ijip wu.
Mǔngo bachiǎkap nɛ bǒ ɛchɛmɛ́ bǒ batí ɛtɔk bákwày bɛ́te mɛ ntísiɛ bɛ́ nchí kʉ nyaka ɛnyu yɔ. Ntá yap kɛ nchi nsɔt nyaka bɛkáti ndu bɛrɔŋ ntá batɨ̌ bo Israɛl abhɛn Damáskɔs. Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́kɛ́mti bakoŋo Yesu arɛ́ bɛ mpɛ́tnsɛm Yerúsalɛm nɛ bhɔ́ mánchyɛ́ bɔ́ ntɛ́msí. 
Mbák mmu ǎtɔ̀ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pu ndɔ́ŋ ámɔ́t nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ngáti wɔ, ansɔt bɛyɔŋ Yesu Kristo Acha mbɔ ndaká-nsé nɛ yí kɛka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́tɔ̀ŋ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛ́m bǒ nkwɔ́ Yesu,
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mbák mǎnchɔ́ŋtí ɛkɛrákap ɛnɛ, chɔŋ mpɛt nte yɔ́ ndǔ manywɔp arat.”
Kɛ mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ báfɛrɛ mbǎyngɔrɛ́ ntá yap. Chɔŋ mántarɛ nɔkɔ nsay mpok yɔ.”
Mǔngo wu akaa. Pɔ̌l ate yɛ ndǔ nkɔ́k anɛ bɛchwe anywɔ́p asá awɔ amfay bɛ bo mánkwɛn kpák. Bákwɛ́n nɔ́kɔ́ kpák, abho yɛ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ bhɔ ndǔ Híbru, ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛyap.
Arístakɔs mmu achi fá ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ nɛ mɛ ǎtò be bakak. Mbák Mák manɔ Banábas mmu ngátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi ántwɔ́ awu, sɔt ka yí nɛ amɔ́ apay.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ɛnɛ mɛ̌yaŋ mǎndɨŋɨ chi bɛ mbák bo bati apay mánká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt fá amɨk ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ́ báyàŋ nɛ mánɨ́kmʉɛt, Ɛtaya mmu achi amfay, ǎghók nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnap.
Bɔ̌ma, fyɛ́ ká bhɛsɛ ndǔ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt.
Nsyɛ́p anɛ bǎsiɛ̀p bo bɛtɔŋ bɛ bachí bo Mandɛm chi ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ mbák bǎbhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé, kɛ mbák bǎpú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm nsyɛ́p anɛ bǎsiɛ̀p bo achi chi ndɛ́ndɛm.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm kɛ̌ nchí mmu anɛ ápɨ́ nchwi amɛm nkɨ.
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɔnókó mbɔnyunɛ ɔ́ghɔ́ mɛ nɛ amɨ́k? Ɛrɨ ɛcha ntá bo abhɛn mánòko yɛ̌ndu bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k.” 
Ɛkɛt Ɛtaya ɛbhɔŋ bɛyǎ bɔ̌bɛkɛt. Mbɔ ɛ́pú nɔ, mbʉ mbɨ́kɨ́ ghati bhe bɛ nchí rɔ́ŋ arɛ́ bɛ́tóŋti ɛbhak ntá yɛka.
Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ nyaka Yesu ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m achɔkɔ ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm ywi awu amfay ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Kristo achi arɛ mbɔ Mfɔ.
Bábho bɛbɨk mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ́, “Yesu, Ɛta, ghɔ́ bhɛsɛ ntínso.”
Aghɔ̌ nyaka bɛ ɛ́rɨ mámbyak yi ɛ̌ti Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò ɛcha yi bɛbhɔŋ kɛnɛ́m ɛtɔk Íjip. Ɛ́bhak ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ yi ǎnòŋ nyaka chi akap anɛ átwɔ̀ ambɨ.
Bǎchǐ mbɨ bhɛsɛ́ mányìɛ nyaka mana mpok bákɔ̀ amɛm baso. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, ‘Achyɛ nyaka bhɔ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́fù amfay!’”
Kɛ mbák mǎmàkati bɛ bawú bapu kway bɛpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɔ bǎrɛm bɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re pay ndǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ágháti bhe? Ɛ́chí amɛm ɛkáti bɛ́ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ,
Píta nɛ mamʉɛrɛ bhi bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛyɔ, bɛcháy bɛkɛm bhɔ tontó, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ákwɛ́n, atɛp bɛsí amɨk.
Yesu afa yɛ nɛbhʉɛ́t wu are rɔ́ŋ atú ɛtɔk anɛ achi kɛkwɔt Táya nɛ Sídɔn. Arɔk achwe ɛkɛt ɛ́mɔt abhak arɛ́. Akɛ yáŋ mándɨŋɨ bɛ́ yi achi arɛ́. Yɛ̌ nɔ, akɛ rɔp bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́.
Bákɔŋ kɛnókó ɛkɛn bǒ mmɨk báchyɛ̀ bhɔ, ɛcha kɛnókó ɛkɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ.
Ndak anɛ apu anɛ́ maknkay. Yɛ̌ chí mbɔŋ Satan ǎyibhiri mkpá ankʉ mbɔ bɛ achi ángɛl anɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm bɛ́ghɔ̀ yi amʉɛt.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, ndǔ mpok yɔ anɛ mɛ̌pɛtnsɛm, bǒ bati apay bákway bɛbhʉrɛ ndǔ bɛkɔ́k mɛ́mɔt, mánsɔt amɔt mandɔk nɛ yí, mándɔ anɛfu.
Bǒ bhɔ báyàŋ nyaka Yesu, nɛ ndu báchɛ́mɛ́ amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm báré bhɛ́p batɨ bɛ, “Bǎkáysí bɛ́ yí? Bǎkáysí bɛ́ apu twɔ ndǔ ɛpǎ?”
Mbák ɔ̌chyɛ̀ mmu ɛnyɨŋ mbɔnyunɛ ɛyi ɛ́pú, kʉ nɔ́ ɛnyunɛ yɛ̌ mmu apu rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́kʉ̀.
Yɨŋɨ́ ká kɛnɛn. Kɛ́pú kwaŋ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ kɛ́pú fɛrɛ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ kɛmbay ndǔ bɛtɛm. Yɛ̌ nɔ, Ɛtayɛka mmu achi amfay ǎchyɛ kɔ nɛnyíɛ́. Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ bǎchá kɛnɛn-ɛ?
Barɛm bɛ, “Bě bo Galili, ndáká yi bachi afɔ téé mánjɨŋɨ nɔkɔ awu amfay? Chɔŋ Yesu mmu árɔ́ be arɔŋɔ amfay, ampɛtnsɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎghɔ́ yi árɔ̀ŋ amfay.” 
Arɛm nɔ, bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ, “Ndu bo abhɛn ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ nɛm yɛ amɔt,” ɛmfu tɛtɛp.
nɛ mbák mbɛ́p bé ɛnyɨŋ, bapú kɛmɛ mɛ.
Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ bábhɨkɨ ghɔ́ Píta, achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mánjáŋ yi. Báyáŋ yí kɛ bákɛ ghɔ yi. Hɛ́rɔd abhɨŋɨ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bhɔ, ábhɛ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ, achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mángwáy bhɔ́. Hɛ́rɔd afa atú Judɛ́ya anɛ́ yí áchí arɛ arɔk atú Seséria áchák achɔkɔ arɛ́. 
Mmɛ, Tɛ́tiɔs mmu Pɔ̌l ághátí mɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nsɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ nchí to nkwɔ be bakak mbɔ ntɨ nkoŋo Acha.
Tɛ̌ndu bachí mbɔ manyiɛp amɛn ásɔ́tí, kwɛn bě kɛkwɛn, sɔ́ŋ bě kɛsɔŋ, chɔŋ mpá be mfɛ́rɛ́ anyu wa.
Ángɛl anɛ ajwi barat árɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́, achak abhesi andɛmɛ nɔkɔ nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ agha anɛ áchyɛ̀ kɛnókó ntá nnya mbʉ́mbʉ anɛ áfú amɛm manyu nɛ ntíako yi, nɛ anka bɛ mámfyɛ́ ɛrɨŋ ɛyi ndǔ yɛ̌ chí nɛfó ɛni nɛ yɛ̌ chí ndǔ awɔ aywi,
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ yi, mbɔnyunɛ mfú chí ntá yi, nɛ yi kɛ átó mɛ.”
Mpok mmǔ ntantaŋ ábhabhɛri ɛkɛt ɛyi nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛnu bhi, yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛghɛp mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Mbák ɛnɔk ɛ́rɨ, kɛpɛm ɛki nkwɔ kɛ́rɨ́. Mbák ɛnɔk ɛbhɔ̌ŋ nɛme, kɛpɛm ɛki nkwɔ́ kɛ́bhɔ́ŋ nɛme. Mmu ǎrɨŋɨ ɛnɔk chí ndǔ kɛpɛm ɛki.
Ɛbhak mbɔ ɛnyǔ Aisáya ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm asɨŋɨ nyaka amɛm ɛkáti yi bɛ: “Mmǔ achi amɛm baso ǎbɨ̀k nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Toŋtí ká mbi anɛ Acha áfʉɛ̀t arɛ́. 
Bárɛ̀m bɛ́ bárɨŋɨ Mandɛm, kɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɔ́ bákʉ̀ bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ́ bábhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ yi. Bábɛp báchá, bátàŋ ntí nɛ Mandɛm, nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bákwày bɛ́kʉ ɛ́pú.
Nɛ bo abhɛn mánóko mankɛm babhák ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔ́t, mánkɔrɛ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhap ndǔ nsoŋ amɔt.
Mmu amɔt ndǔ bǒbhɔ bati apay abhɛn bághoko nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Jɔ̌n árɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu, nɛ abho bɛkoŋo yi aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Andru. Abhak manɔ Símun Píta.
Mǔfu aghati yi bɛ, “Máyɛ nɛ bɔ̌mayɛ báchí nɛfí téé báyàŋ bɛghɔ wɔ.”
Nchí rɛm nɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ básyɛ́p mmu yɛ̌ bábhɨ́kɨ́ syɛp, ɛyɔ ɛ́pú kwak ndǔ yɛ̌ mbi. Nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ chí bɛ́bhʉrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm.
Ngufú mmu ǎkwáy bɛ́kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí bɛ, “Akap Mandɛm áchyɛ́ mbɔk bho chi nɛka ɛnɛ́n bɔ́ bábhɔ́ŋ nɛ yí, ɛnɛ́ akap anɛ bo báchák chi bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mánkʉ”. Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́rɛ́m ntá ɛnyǔ mmǔ wu chí bɛ, “Ghatí mɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ ɔbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm mbák ɔpú kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mánkʉ́?” Mbák chí mɛ́, mɛ̌kwáy bɛ́sɔ́t mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀ ntɔ́ŋ wɔ́ bɛ́ nká nɛ Mandɛm tɛtɛp.
Pú bɔ́ mankɛm bachi chi bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhi nɛ Mandɛm átò bhɔ bɛ mankwak bǒ abhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛpɛmɛ?
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛghati bhɔ bɛ, “Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ Yesu, ndɨŋɨ Pɔ̌l, kɛ báchí ntɨkɨ bho?”
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, Yesu abho bɛghati bakoŋo bhi nɛ bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi ɛbhak ɛ́mɔt nɛ yi bɛ,
Bo abhɛn bábhàbhɛri bakók bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bábʉɛ́ ntiɛ́t ntiɛt bárɔ́k ɛtɔk ɛ́gho nɛ amɛm bakɨ mángati nɔkɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákári. Bo báfú báre rɔŋ bɛghɔ nɛ amɨ́k ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákárí.
Batísyɛ abhɛn bapay kɛ báchi téé bɛsí Mandɛm mmǔ mmɨk nkɛm achi yi awɔ. Bɔ́ báchi mɛnɔk ólif bɛpay nɛ mɛnɔk ɛbhɛn bɛ́pɔ̀kɔ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛpay.
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ngu mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi árɛ́mɛ́. Kɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ɛncha ntá mmu wu nɔ átì mɛ ntá bǒmpap abha!”
Kɛ mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu ǎyáŋ nyaka bɛ́pɛ́mɛ Pɔ̌l. Ɛ́kʉ́ akɛ chyɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu mbi bɛ́wáy bǒkɛnɔŋ. Achyɛ ɛyɔŋ chí bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛghɔk nnyɛ́n ánjámbɨ ángɔ́k ánkó ɛbhɨ.
Mbák abhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛghok bhɔ nkwɔ, kʉ nkwɔ Mandɛm mándɨ́ŋɨ́. Nɛ mbák bo Mandɛm bárɛm kɛ yí ǎchòk chi batú, dɔ̌ yi ambak yɛ̌ mbɔ mmǔ anɛ ápú chyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó, nɛ mbɔ mbɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛ́nti.
Jɔ̌n akɛmɛ bɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ sɔt nkábhɛ́nti ɛ́ncha anɛ́ bǎbhɔŋɔ bɛsɔt.”
Nɛ bápú kwáy bɛtɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ́ nkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bábhàt nɛ́ mɛ amʉɛt.
Sɔt nɔ́kɔ́ nkaysi ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ngátí-nɛ́ wɔ, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ mbɔŋ Mandɛm Acha ankwak wɔ ɔ́mbɔ́ŋ nɛjwǐmɛm ndu bɔ́ mɛnkɛm.
Báchák bábhák Fílip nɛ Batolómyo, nɛ Tɔmás, nɛ Mátio mbɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛ́nti, nɛ Jems mmɔ̌ Alfeyɔs, nɛ Tadiɔs.
Kɛ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka ákɛ́ bhɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti yi achi ngwayti bho, yɛ̌ chi ɛ̌ti yi achi ngɛp, yɛ̌ chi ɛ̌ti yi achi nkʉ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ, nɛ ɛ́kɛ́ bhak chi ɛ̌ti yi ákɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchwe ndǔ baraka bo bachak.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ɛbhě manyu ɛnɛ Yesu árɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ bakoŋo bhi, bághɔ́ yi arɛ, babhɛp yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, ɔpě ɔtwɔ wɛn ntɨkɨ mpok?”
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ mbák mǎnchyɛ́ mmʉɛt ntá mmu bɛkʉ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áyàŋ mǎnkʉ, nɔ bǎchi basɛm ntá mmu wu? Mmu ǎkway bɛkoŋo bɛbʉ́, nɛ bɛbʉ́ mɛntwɔ yi nɛ nɛwú. Mbák ɛpu nɔ, mmu ǎkway bɛkoŋo Mandɛm, nɛ Mandɛm ankʉ yí ambak chak bɛsí bhi.
Kɛ kɛ́ka nɛ bhɔ́. Bǒ bhap bábhɛ́sɛ́ ambi mánòŋ bɛ mankɛm yí mangway. Bácha batí bɛsa bɛpay. Nɛ mányǔ nku bɛ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bápú nyiɛ nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bápú nyú kpátɛ mángwáy yí. Mánaŋ batoŋti mmʉɛt, barɔbhɛ noŋ chí bɛ́ ɔ́ntó Pɔ̌l antwɔ.”
bɛ́fyɛ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bo bachak, nɛ ɛbɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ, nɛ bɛrwɔ bho, nɛ ɛpɔ̌ ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu apu kɛm mmʉɛt, nɛ mpap amɨ́k, nɛ bɛchɔŋti nnyɛ́n mmu, nɛ nɛyoŋómʉɛt nɛ ɛchɨŋti.
Bápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ bhɔ, bakʉ bɔ baté bɛsí ɛchɛmɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk. Mǔngo bachiǎkap abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ
Bǒ abhɛn nkɔ́ nɛ bhɔ́ bághɔ́ nkwɔ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɔ kɛ bákɛ ghók ɛyɔŋɔ́ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m kɛpɨ nɛ mɛ.
Kɛ Mandɛm ábhɨ́kɨ́ tó nyaka Ɛláija ntá yɛ̌ kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ amɔt, ɛbhɨ́kɨ́fʉɛt chi anɛ achi ɛtɔk Sárɛfat, atú Sídɔn, ɛtɔk bo bachak.
Bɔ̌ma, ɛ̌ti sɛ́chi bo Yesu Kristo Acha nɛ ndǔ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ákʉ́ sɛ́nkɔŋ batɨ, nchí nɨk be mmʉɛt bɛ mǎnu mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm ɛ̌ti ya nɛ ntɨ nɛnkɛm mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɛmbɔŋ nchí kʉ.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, mɛ Pɔ̌l mǔkɛnɔŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu Acha, nchí sɛmti bhe bɛ ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛyɛka ɛ́mbák ɛnɛ ɛ́kwáy nɛ bo abhɛn Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mambak abhi.
bɔ́ batí apay mándɔp chi mmǔ amɔt.’ Bɔ́ kɛpɛrɛ bhak yɛ bati apay, kɛ mmǔ amɔt. Mmu ákɛ fyɛ yɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ nɛ́ntɨ bo abhɛn Mandɛm áchɛ́mɛ́.”
Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ kɛ ákʉ̀ chɔŋ bo mándɨŋɨ tɛtɛp nkɛm anɛ áyɨ́ŋɨ́ Mandɛm. Anaŋ ántwɔ́ chɔŋ ankʉ mǎndɨŋɨ tɛtɛp nkɛm, mbɔnyunɛ ápú rɛm chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú yi antɨ. Ɛnɛ́ yi aghoko kɛ árɛ̀m, nɛ chɔŋ angati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ ambɨ.
Nɛ mbák awɔ́nɛm ywɛ átò wɔ ndǔ bɛbʉ́, kpɔ́t wú gʉɛ́p. Ɛ́rɨ bɛ ɔ́nɛ́m ɛpókómʉɛt ɛyɛ ɛ́mɔt ɛcha wɔ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́, mánsɔt mmʉɛt ɛyɛ nkɛm mámɛsɛ amɛm nɛpǐngo.” 
Bárɨ́ŋɨ bɛ yi kɛ áchɔ̀kɔ nɔ́kɔ́ nyaka ndǔ Ɛrɨ́tí Nyǔbha anɛ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm anɨŋɨ nɔkɔ nkáp. Ɛkʉ bábhák maknkay, nɛ manyu arɔp bhɔ fúfú bɛghɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari. 
ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ mpɛtnsɛm ɛbhak ɛnɛ mfú.’ Nɛ ɛ́náŋ ɛ́mpɛ́tnsɛm, ɛngɔ bɛ mányɔ ɛsɨ ɛkɛt ɛyi, bághókó sayri,
Nɨk ka mmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ámfɛ́rɛ́ bhɛsɛ amɔ bɛbɛ́ptí bho. Puyɛ̌ bo mankɛm abhɛn bághòk Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ kɛ mánóko.
Jɔ̌n apu nyaka ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ yɔ. Atwɔ́ chí bɛ́gháti bho ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi arɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ yɔ.
Mbɔk bho bákaysi bɛ Mandɛm ǎchɔ̀ŋti mpok tontó ndu bɛ́bhʉɛ́rɛ bariɛp ami. Ápú chɔŋti mpok mbɔ ɛnyu bɔ́ bákáysí. Ǎkɛp chi ntɨ nɛ bhe, ndu ápú yaŋ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu angu anɛm. Ǎyàŋ chi bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi.
Mpok anɛ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí twɔ, mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɛ́chí nyaka mpok Nóa.
Nɛ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghɔ̀ fá amɨk bɛ́chi mandú tontó, nɛ bɛ́pu tat. Bɛ́kwàk bhɛsɛ kwak bɛ sɛ́nkwáy bo abhɛn sɛ́chwè ndǔ bɛyǎ maŋák Mandɛm ɛwak ɛ́mɔt. Maŋák amɔ acha yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, Yesu aghati baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ mándɔ́k mǎnchwe amɛm áchwí, mámpe nnyɛ́n manjambɨ ndǔ ɛbhě manyu ɛchak. Arɔp ansɛm bɛkʉ bɛyǎ bo bhɔ abhɛn bachi arɛ mangurɛ.
Sɛ́ghɔ bɛ sɛbhɔŋ mǔngo bachiǎkap anɛ ákó áchí amfay nɛ Mandɛm. Yí chí Yesu, Mmɔ Mandɛm. Sɛ́ndɔ́k yɛ ambɨ bɛkɛm sayri mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́nókó ɛ̌ti yi.
Báchyɛ̀ chɔŋ be bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn, mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Ɛtaya nɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛ.
Yesu ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ntó ɛnɛn arɛm bɛ, “Nɛme ɛnɛ́n nɛ́pú nɛmě nɛwú, nɛ́chí chí bɛ́kʉ bo mángɔ́ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm. Nɛ́twɔ chí bɛ nɛ́mbák ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kʉ̀ bo mángɔ́ bɛ Mmɔ Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ.”
Kɛ Yesu aghɔ nɔkɔ nɔ, ntɨ nɛ́bé yi amɛm, arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ká mǎmbɔ mántwɔ ntá ya, bǎkɛ́ chyɛt bhɔ mbi mbɔnyunɛ bo abhɛn bachi mbɔ bhɔ kɛ̌ Mandɛm abhak Mfɔ wap.”
Mpok bɔ́ bárɔ̀ Yesu, Píta arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛta, ɛ́rɨ tontó bɛ sɛchi fá! Dɔ̌ sɛ́nté bɛtɛm bɛrat, Ɛmɔt ntá yɛ, ɛchak ntá Moses, nɛ ɛnɛ́fú ntá Ɛláija.” Píta kɛrɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi arɛmɛ.
Ɛ̌tíyɔ kɛ mbɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe bɛ mǎntwɔ́ ndɛ́m kɛpɨ nɛ bhe tɛ̌ndu nchí fá mbɔ mǔkɛnɔŋ ɛ̌ti mmu anɛ bo Israɛl mankɛm babhaka ntɨ bɛ́ ǎtwɔ̀ bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bhɛsɛ.
Ɛ̌ti nɛka ɛnap, Mandɛm arɛm bɛ bǒbhɔ mankɛm bákʉ́ sayri. Yɛ̌ nɔ, yɛ̌ mmu wap amɔt akɛ bhɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɔ.
Mbɔk bho bárɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bágúrɛ ɛbhɨ ndu kɛ́mbwɔ́bhɛ́ ntí ti.
Bǎkɛ́ kaysi bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́chí ndɛ́ndɛm, nɔ́ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ básɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ, “Ɛfóŋó ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ nkwǎ, ɛ́fyɛ̀ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bo báchák ɛ́chá.”
Bětí běti, bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses báte ɛyu nɛ nkwɔ́ ɛchɛmɛ́ bǒbati ɛtɔk báchák mankɛm. Báfyɛ́ yi ngɛm amɔ́, básɔt barɔk ntá Páílet, mmu Rom anɛ achi nyaka gɔ́bhanɔ atú Judɛ́ya mpok yɔ.
Bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛ bɛbhɔŋ bɛbhák ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ manyu ánchók bo nɛ ntíánwɔ́p ámbák nɛ bo abhɛ́n bápú ka nɛ wɔ ndu bábhɨkɨ bhɔŋ mbi bɛrɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ.
Kɛ puyɛ̌ bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bághókó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ kɛ báká yɔ́. Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ Aisáya arɛmɛ bɛ, “Acha, agha ánókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́ghátí bhɔ?”
“Agha ánáŋ áchyɛ́ Mandɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi áyàŋ Mandɛm ankɛmɛ yi yɔ?”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛ nkwɔ́ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛbhɛp be. Mbák mǎnkɛ́mɛ́ mɛ yɔ, chɔŋ mɛ nkwɔ ngati bhe mmu anɛ áchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀.”
Acha akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mbɔ bǎbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm ɛnɛ́n nɛ́chí yɛ̌ chi nɨ́ŋɨ́nɨ́ŋɨ́ mbɔ mɔ́sɛpɛm anɛ ɛnɔk ɛ́nɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ *mɔ́stat, mbʉ bǎkway bɛ́ghati ɛnɔk ɛnɛ bɛ, ‘Fǎ fá nɛ bakaŋ dɔ́k tě awu amɛm manyu’, nɛ yɔ́ ɛ́ngok be.” 
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́bɨ̀ti nɛ bɛ́chyɛ kɛnókó nɛ bakak ntá yi mmu achi chɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ, yi mmu achi nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm,
Kɛ mbák mpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nnáŋ ndɔ́, nɔ nchí mbɔ̌ŋ mmu bɛbʉ́.
Ghɔ́ ká ntínso nɛ bo abhɛn bachi ɛkak ɛ́mɔt nɛfí, ɛkak ɛ́mɔt anywɔ́p.
Bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyu Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bo mámbák chak bɛsí bhi. Mánù chi bɛkʉ wap mbi anɛ bɔ babhak chak bɛsí bhi. Ɛ́kʉ bábhɨ́kɨ́ ka mbi anɛ yi ákʉ̀ bo mambak chak bɛsí bhi.
Kɛ chɔŋ nkʉ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛ, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ fá amɨk bɛfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bho.” Arɛm ntá mbɛ́ntí wu bɛ, “Faté, pɔkɔ́ bɛkpaka bhɛ gurɛ!”
Josɛ́f aŋɛmɛ, asɔt mmɔ́ nɛ máyi, afa, arɔk ɛtɔk Íjip nɛ bhɔ nkúbhɛ́ bɛti ɛbhɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ángɛl Mandɛm aghati yi.
Ndu sɛ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ, sɛ́bháká ntɨ ndu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛrɨ ɛcha. Sɛ́bhaka ntɨ bɛ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛn kɛbhesi chɔŋ nɛ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm ywɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Mmu ápɛ̀mɛ bhɛsɛ.
Mbák mǎnkʉ ɛnyu yɔ, Acha ǎkʉ mǎmbɔŋ mpok nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ndǔ bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛka,
Kɛ mmǔ wap amɔt anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Káyfas anɛ achí nyaka mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm ndǔ mmíɛ́ ɛnɔ, arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yɛ̌nyɨŋ!
Kristo afɛ́rɛ́ bɛsɛ ndǔ kɛsɛm bɛ sɛ́kɛ́pɛrɛ bhak basɛm. Tě yɛ ka kpirí nɛ bǎkɛrɔ yɛ̌ mmu ankʉ mǎmpɛtnsɛm ndǔ kɛsɛm.
Júdas anáŋ ayámbɨ achyɛ́ nyaka bhɔ ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kwák bɔ́ mándɨŋɨ Yesu. Akʉ nɔ́, ndǔ ághátí bhɔ́ bɛ, “Mmu anɛ mɛ̌bhɛnɛ chɔŋ, chí yi. Kɛ́m ká yi!”
Ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt achák amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm, básɨŋ bɛ, “Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǒ mmɨk bákáysí bɛ́ chí nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak, ɛ́pú yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛsí Mandɛm.”
Arɔk anyiɛ́ bɛti nɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bábhàbhɛri ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, ɛnyu yi ákway bɛti Yesu ntá yap.
Yírɛ kɛ achi mǔnti anɛ bǒnkwɔ, nɛ bǒnkwɔ chi mmʉɛt yi. Yí kɛ ágháy nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́mɨk ntá bǒnkwɔ.
Yesu ágháká kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ Yerúsalɛm, aghɔ́ ɛtɔk, adi kɛbhɔ ndǔ ntínso nɛ́kɛm yi nɛ Yerúsalɛm,
Yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka apú kwáy yɛ bɛrɛm bɛ́ mɛnjwítí bhé ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna bɛ́ mǎmbák bakoŋo bha.
Ngɔ́ nkwɔ ɛkáti nɛ́nɛ́p ndǔ awɔ́nɛm mmu anɛ achɔkɔ ndu ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ. Basɨ́ŋ abhak yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak amɛm nɛ ansɛm ɛkáti. Báfyɛ́ bɛ́bhánɛ́ anyǔ ɛkáti ndǔ bɛpók tándrámɔt, baghaŋa.
Bǎkɛ́ ghok bhɔ chi ndiɛrɛ bɛsí bhap nɛ ndǔ bɛkʉ bɔ mambɔŋ maŋák. Kɛ kʉ ka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ mǎnkʉ nɛ ntɨ nɛnkɛm mbɔ basɛm Kristo.
Bɛti mɛ́naŋ bɛ́fʉɛ̀t, nɛ nywɔp nɛbho bɛyi. Sɛ́ndɔ́ yɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ̀ amɛm ɛjuri, sɛ́nsɔt mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛnu ɛbhɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnu nɛ bhɔ nɛ nywɔp ámfay mbɔ bo abhɛn mánaŋ báfú ndǔ ɛjuri.
Ngɔrɛ́ amɔt anɛ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri mɔ́ywi anɛ ngɔsɔ́ŋ aghok ɛ̌ti Yesu. Arɔk ntá yi kɛchɔŋti mpok, akwɛ́n bɛkak ɛbhi.
Baghokotǐ kɛpɨ bhɔ bárɔ́ŋɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ntá Yesu, babhɛp yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́rɛ̀m nɛ ɔ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛchi chak. Sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɔpú yɨŋɨ mmu ndǔ bɛsí ɔ́ncháy yi, kɛ ɔ̌tɔ̀ŋ tɛtɛp ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mánkʉ.
Are tɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛcháy. Mpók nɛ mpok ándɛm nɔkɔ ɛ̌ti Yesu ntá bo Israɛl abhɛn bárɛ̀m ɛyɔŋɔ Grik, ankɛm nɔkɔ ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bhɔ́. Ɛkʉ bare yáŋ chí bɛ́wáy yí.
Anɛnɛ yɛ nkaysi yap bɛ mánjwimɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm akɔŋ bhɛsɛ tontó ɛnyu ɛnɛ́, sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ batɨ nkwɔ.
Bák ká mbɔ mɔ̌nkɔ mmu áŋwaka mɛnyu amɨ mpoknkɛm. Bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkwak nɛbhɨ ɛnɛn mbɔŋ, nɔ chi, Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Yɔ́ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ mǎngo Mandɛm ápɛmɛ bhe.
“Dɔ̌ ka ngati bhe ɛ̌ti Kɛfɔ Mandɛm. Kɛ́chí mbɔ Mfɔ anɛ ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ bǒ bɛtɨk abhi bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ wap ánkɛ́mɛ́ nkáp anɛ yi ákɛ̀m yi.
Ndǔ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antifu, ngɔ́ mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk nɛ bǒ abhɛn bákɔ̀ yɔ. Báfyɛ́ ndɛ́-nɛnu ɛnɛ́ bághókó nɛ ɛsé ndu bɛkuti mbeápak ɛyap. Ndɛ́ nɛnu ɛyɔ ɛbhak chuu mbɔ ngó, ɛ́bhák mbɔ nkwɔbhɛ́ nɛbu, ɛ́bhák nkwɔ mmʉɛt sɛkɔk sɛkɔk. Batí mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk abhak mbɔ bati nkʉ. Ngó nɛ mɔ́ngo nɛ *ɛriɛbhɛ́ sɔ́lfɔ,   ɛ́ré fu mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk ɛyɔ anyu.
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ chɔŋ Mandɛm mmu ábhó ɛrɨ́tí bɛtɨk amɛm batɨ yɛka andɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ bhɔ kpátɛ mpok anɛ yi ánaŋa bhɔ ndu nywɔp ɛnɛn Yesu Kristo ápɛtnsɛm.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛ kɛ nchí nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m. Mmu anɛ átwɔ́ ntá ya apu pɛrɛ ghok nsay nɛ mmu anɛ ásɨ̀kɨ ntɨ nɛ mɛ, apú bhɔ́ŋ ɛkwaká manyiɛp wáwák.
Kɛ abhɛ́n ɛkɔŋ, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛghɔkɔntɨk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́mɔt! Nɛ Ɛta Mandɛm, nywɔp nɛmɔt nɛchi mbɔ nká mamiɛ́, nɛ nká mamiɛ́ achi mbɔ nywɔp nɛmɔt.
Mbɔ ɛrɨ́tí ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu Yesu Kristo, ɔbhɔŋ bɛ́te kákáti ndu ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ bakoŋo Yesu báchák bábhɔ̀ŋ.
Kɛ Mandɛm ǎtɔŋ bɛsɛ bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu, nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ bɛsɛ́ bɛtaŋ amfǎy nkaysi bɛ́fyɛ ámɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bo báchák. Ɛ́chí mbɔnyǔ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm apú ka nɛ mmu anɛ áyòŋ mmʉɛt, kɛ ǎyɛt mmu anɛ ásɛ̀pti mmʉɛt mbɔ bɛ yí ápú yɛ̌nyɨŋ.”
Nɛ mpok ághɔ́ yɔ ǎbhɨŋɨ mamʉɛrɛ nɛ bakokosi bhi, angati bhɔ bɛ ‘Ŋák ká nɛ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ ngɔ̌ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nkap ɛnɛ ɛnɛmɛ.’
Mbák bádɛ̀p awɔ antɨ bɛ́ báchi bo Hibru, mɛ nkwɔ nchí mmu Hibru. Mbák báchí bo Israɛl, mɛ nkwɔ nchí mmu Israɛl. Mbák báchi bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham, mɛ nkwɔ nchí ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Ábraham.
“Mmɔ̌káti apu kway bɛrɨ̀ŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ancha ntɔ̌ŋ ywi. Nɛ mǔbɛtok apú cha chi-bɛtok ywi.
Bě nkwɔ bǎchi nyaka nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ nɛ Mandɛm, bǎbhak bǒmpap abhi ndu nkaysi yɛka ɛ̌ti bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀ nyaka.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ sɛ́fyɛ̀ bɛtaŋ bɛ́kʉ bɛtɨk nɛ sɛ́nù bɛ bo mándɨŋɨ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛ́n tɛtɛp mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́bhaka ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm anɛ ápɛ̀mɛ bǒ mankɛm, sayri sayri, abhɛn mánókó.
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mmu anɛ áyàŋ bɛbhɔŋ ɛrɨ́tí nɛpɛ́m, nɛ áyàŋ bɛbhak maŋák, ánkɛ́m nɛ́rɨ ɛni bɛ ákɛ́ rɛm ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ, bɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́kɛ́ fu yi anyu.
Báfyɛ́ yi nkú chu amʉɛt anɛ ágháká yi tɛ bɛkak. Básɔt bɔ̌batábhɛ́nɔk abhɛ́n báchí nsěnse mánɨ́ ntá báfyɛ yi anti bɛ chi ayǐ nta kɛfɔ.
Dɨŋɨ́ yɛ́ ka bɛ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm kɛ̌ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm ɛnyǔ mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ nɛ ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.” 
Bápáy nɔkɔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm mbɔ ɛnyu Moses asɨ́ŋɨ́ nɛ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú ndǔ basɨŋɨ́ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ, bǒ batí ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛyɔ bátó mmu bɛ ángátí bɔPɔ̌l bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, mbák bǎbhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛkway bɛfyɛ bhɛsɛ ntɨ, ghatí ká bhɛsɛ.”
Dɔ́k yɛ ká mǎnkɛm mɔ́sɛnɛ́ mpɔŋ mǎngwáy mǎnkʉ nɛnyíɛ́ bɛ sɛ́nyíɛ́ sɛnkʉ maŋák,
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu arɔk ɛyi ɛtɔk ndu bɛsɨŋ nnyɛ́n.
Ɛ́kʉ́ mbo bɛ́gháti Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛtɔk Damáskɔs, nɛ nkɔ ndɔk nɔkɔ Yerúsalɛm, nɛ atú Judɛ́ya ankɛm, kɛ nde rɔ́ŋ ntá abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nkwɔ, bɛ́ bɔ́ mántɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap mámpɛtnsɛm ntá Mandɛm nɛ mámbo bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ bɔ́ bátɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap.
Ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap ɛnɛ bághákó nɛ pú ɛbhak amɛm mɔ́kɛt wu. Amfay ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ ɛyɔ kɛ básɔ̀ŋ nyaka ɛnyɨŋɨ́ ɛriɛp ɛnɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ ínsɛns. Ɛkʉbhɛ́ Nku ɛ́bhak nkwɔ amɛm. Bákúti yɔ ɛnkɛm nɛ pú. Mɔ́te anɛ mána achi amɛm abhak amɛm ɛkʉbhɛ́ yɔ. Ntɛ́m Arɔn ɛnɛn nɛ́tɛ́mɛ́ bɛyé nɛ́bhák nkwɔ amɛm. Bɛ́gbáká batay apay anɛ Mandɛm ásɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛbhé arɛ kɛ áchyɛ ntá Moses bɛbhak nkwɔ amɛm ɛkʉɛp ɛyɔ.
Kɛ yi kɛbhɔ́ŋ bakaŋ amɨk. Ante kákáti ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok. Kɛ mpok ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́twɔ́ nɛ bo mámbo mɛnyok yi ɛ̌ti Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ yi anoko, amfɛrɛ amɔ tɛ́mté.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ áyàŋ bɛpɛmɛ mmʉɛt yi ǎnɛm nɛpɛ́m ɛni. Kɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áká mɛnɛm nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛ̌ti ya nɛ ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, ǎbhɔŋ chɔŋ nɔ.
Bɔ̌ma, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔkɔntɨk ndu sɛ́re kʉ bɛtɨk, sɛ́mkpɔt nɔkɔ nsɔ́ŋti bɛti nɛ ngósí mpok sɛ́chí awu nɛ bhe. Sɛ́kʉ̀ nyaka bɛtɨk ɛnyu yɔ bɛ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chɛ́bhɛ́ bhɛsɛ. Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ nyaka bɛbhak ntu ntá yɛka mpok sɛ́ghàti bhe Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm.
Akparɛnja anɛ áfù anyǔ mmu anɛ achi ndǔ mpɔŋɔndɨ́k anɛ pɛ́pɛ́p awáy bafɔ bhɔ nɛ bakwɔ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bhap. Nɛ kɛnɛn ɛkɔ kɛnkɛm kɛ́nyíɛ́ bɛrɛnɛ́ bawú, kɛjwi.
Yesu atɛ́m nɛkay ɛnɛ́n bɛ, “Mǔnkáp amɔt achi nyaka anɛ afyɛ́ ndɛn bɛyǎ nkáp, anyiɛ nɔkɔ ɛpa yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp.
Ɛchi nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bɛbʉ́ bɛpú pɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay mmu anɛ ánáŋ ágú.
Mmǔ wap amɔt anɛ áchí ɛsáyrí ntɔŋ ɛbhé Moses arɔk mɛmɔ Yesu. Abhɛ́p yi bɛ,
Mandɛm mmu ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ be bɛ mǎmbák bǒbhi, ǎbhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp ami, nɛ chɔŋ ankʉ nɔ.
“Bě bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, chɔŋ ɛmbɛp ntá yɛka ɛncha, mbɔnyunɛ bapú kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak ntá bho nɛ bǎbhɨkɨ kɔŋ Mandɛm. Bǎsɔt ndu bɛrɨ amɔt ndǔ baru byo mǎnchyɛ ntá Mandɛm, mǎnkʉ ɛnyumɔt nɛ mbwɔt achak. Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ mǎmbak sayri nɛ bho kɛ bǎbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛghɔkɔntɨk bɛbhé bɛ́chák.
Bǒ bɛtok, bɔ́ŋ ká nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt bɛsí bachi abhɛka nɛ kɛnókó kɛnkɛm. Bǎkɛ́ bhak ɛnyu ɛyɔ ndiɛrɛ nɛ abhɛn bɛrɨ̌ntɨ nɛ abhɛn bákɛ̀m be sayri. Bák ká ɛnyu yɔ yɛ̌ chi nɛ abhɛn báchí bɛběbɛbe.
“Batɔŋ-ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi kɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛghati bho mbɔ̌ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí amɛm bɛkáti ɛbhɛn Moses asɨ́ŋɨ́.
Yesu Acha árɛ̀m bɛ, “Ghɔ́ ká, mɛ́twɔ̀ mbɔ ngɛ́p. Chɔŋ ɛ́ndɨ ɛncha ntá mmǔ anɛ achi pě nɛ ǎkɛ̀m ndɛn ɛyi sayri bɛ ákɛ́ kɔ ɛbhowɔ, ntíánwɔ́p ankɛm yi bɛsí bho.”
Mandɛm achyɛ nnya anɛ ájwí ɛpay mbi, yɔ́ akʉ ɛ̌yu ɛnɛ ɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m ɛ́chwe amʉɛt ntíako anɛ́ nnya anɛ mbɨ. Ntí-ako wu abho bɛrɛm kɛpɨ. Akʉ bɛ mángwáy bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ yɔ kɛnókó.
Yɛ̌ ɛ́mbak chí bɛ́ bo báchák bábhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ́ nchí mǔnto Yesu Kristo, be bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ nchí mǔnto Yesu. Nɛbhat anɛ bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Acha, ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ nchí mǔnto ywi tɛtɛp.
Yesu Acha akɛmɛ yɛ yi bɛ, “Bě bǒ bɛtabha! Ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka ápú kaŋari yɛ chí mpɔŋ yi, yɛ̌ chi mpɔŋɔ batu yi ándɔ́k anchyɛ yɔ́ manyiɛp ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt?
Chɔŋ bo abhɛn mánókó mámbɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́kʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay. Chɔŋ mámbok bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna, chɔŋ mándɛm bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn bábhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna.
Ɛsakámu yɔ arɛm bɛ, “Nnáŋ nchí bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ɛ́bhʉɛ́t kɛ́?”
Kɛ mpok anɛ mmok áfú, ásɔ́ŋ yɔ́ ndǔ bakaŋ ayi ábhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛchwe amɨk sayri. Anɨŋti, awɔsi.
Bǒ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nnyɔ́ yɔ áchí yi awɔ jɨ́ŋjɨŋjɨ́ŋ, bábho bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Tɛtɛp, mmǔ-nɛ chí ngwayti bho! Yɛ̌ndu ábʉɛ́ nɛwú anyɛ́n, Mandɛm mmu ákɛmɛ kɛ́mbé abhɨ́kɨ́ rɔ yi ambak nɛpɛ́m.”
Kɛ bǒ bɛtɨk bhɔ bághɔ nɔkɔ yi, bábho bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, ‘Yɨŋɨ́ mbɔ̌ŋ mɔ́ywi nɛ́, nɛ yí kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnyiɛ nɛwú ɛtayi. Twɔ́ ká sɛ́nkɛm yi sɛngway bɛ́ ɛtayi ánáŋ ángú mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi mɛ́ndɔp chi ɛbhɛsɛ.’
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, bo abhɛn bachi arɛ téé bákókósi mmʉɛt nɛ Píta barɛm bɛ, “Nsé apu arɛ, wɔ nkwɔ́ ɔchí mmǔ amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ bho Yesu mmǔ atú Gálili wu. Ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu yɛ ɛ́ti wɔ.”
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ Mandɛm arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Ghɔ́ ká, nchí bhʉɛrɛ ntay ɛtɔk Síɔn ɛnɛn nɛ́kʉ̀ chɔŋ bo mánchɨ́ŋtí nɛkwɛ́n. Ntay ɛnɔ chi sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ ɛsɛn sɛ́kʉ̀ bo mánkwɛn ɛ̌ti yi. Kɛ mmu anɛ ánókó yi, apú bhɔŋ chɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p.”
Mbák mmu árɛ̀m bɛ akɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ ampap ntɨ nkwǎ, nɔ mmǔ wu achi nsěnse, mbɔnyunɛ mbák mmu abhɨkɨ kɔŋ ntɨ nkwǎ anɛ yi ághɔ̀, ná yi ákway bɛkaŋ Mandɛm mmu yi apu ghɔ nɛ amɨ́k?
Nɛ Mfɔ Agripa arɛm ntá Fɛstɔs bɛ, “Mbɔ abhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm bɛ mántɛn manyé yi ntá Mfɔ Rom, mbʉ sɛ́rɔ́ yi arɔŋ.”
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses bághɔ́ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn Yesu ákʉ́. Bághɔ́ nkwɔ ndǔ mǎmbɔ bábɨ̀k amɛm ɛkɛrákap mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Bakak nɛ kɛnókó ámbák nɛ Nyíɛ́-nɛwu Mfɔ Debhít!” Baghɔ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, batɨ ábé bhɔ amɛm tontó.
Akɛ́m yi ndǔ awɔ́nɛm ayoŋ. Tɛ́mté wu, bɛtaŋ Mandɛm bɛ́chwe ndu bɛkak nɛ mɛmɨ̌ bɛkak ɛbhi.
Ntá bo abhɛn báchyɛ̀ nɔ bhe ɛsɔŋɔri ndu báté bɛ bábhɔŋ bɛsyɛp mmu kɛ ambak chak bɛsí Mandɛm, mɛ̌yàŋ bɛ mámkpɨ́k mángak mmʉɛt ɛyap.
Dɔ́k ká ambɨ bɛkɔŋ batɨ nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ bakoŋó Kristo.
Mbok anɛ Mɔ́ywi áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́ngátí bhe achi bɛ, “Mandɛm achi Bɛdiɛrɛ, nɛ ɛjuri ɛpu nɛ yi wawak.”
Nchí ghati bhe ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Acha bɛ mǎmpáy ɛkáti ɛnɛ ntá bǒnkwɔ mankɛm.
Chɔŋ Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ̀ mbwɔt ntá nkwaŋankɨ nɛ ánchyɛ̀ nɛnyíɛ́ mɛnyiɛ anchyɛ be nkwɔ mbwɔt, ankʉ yɔ anjá ancha, nɛ ankʉ bɛrɨ́tí bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka mɛ́nchyɛ́ bɛyǎ mbwɔt.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, ndaká yí ɔ́jì ntɨ mǔnkwɔ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀? Yɛ̌ chí wɔ nkwɔ, ndaká yí ɔ́byàk ntɨ mǔnkwɔ ndǔ yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́kʉ̀? Chɔŋ bɛsɛ mankɛm sɛ́nte ndǔ manyé bɛsí Mandɛm.
Ntwɔ bɛkʉ bɔ̌ abhɛn babhakanɛm mánú nɛ bachi bhap, abhɛ́n baghɔrɛ́ mánú nɛ manɔ nɛ baghɔrɛ́ mánú nɛ manɔ̌ manɛ́m abhap.
mámbʉrɛ bɛsí bǒnto, nɛ bɔ mánkɔrɛ nkáp wu bɛkoŋo nté anɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap.
Nɛ bo Israɛl bábhɨkɨ ghɔ́ mɛ ndǔ nchí kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ yɛ̌ mmu amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ mɛ ndǔ nchí nyɨkɨsi batɨ̌-bho bɛ mánchyɛ ɛsɔŋɔri amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí nɛ yɛ̌ chí ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt achak amɛm ɛtɔk.
Yesu árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, ntɨ nɛ́ré sɔŋɔri yi amɛm, arɛm kpoŋoroŋ bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mmu ywɛka amɔt ǎtí chɔŋ mɛ.”
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́chí fá tété mbɔnyunɛ sɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ mmu anɛ ásɔ̀t bhɛsɛ ndǔ bɛtɨk.” Mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ wu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká nkwɔ mǎnkʉ́ bɛtɨk amɛm nkɨ wa.”
Bákɔŋ nkwɔ bɛ bo mánkaka nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ nɛfísiɛ nɛ kɛnókó. Nɛ bákɔŋ bɛ bo mambɨŋɨ nɔkɔ bhɔ bɛ, ‘Ntɔŋ’.
Nnɨkmʉɛt ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhɛ bɛ́ mámbók yɔ́ kɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛkʉ nɔ.”
Nɛ ná bo bákway bɛghati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ mbák bábhɨ́kɨ́ to bhɔ? Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Maŋák ǎya ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn bɛkak ɛbhap bɛ́pɔ̀kɔ bɔ bɛ mándɔk mángati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́!”
Ndu mbaŋ ákàŋari, Yesu ate nɛpakányɛ́n. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bakoŋo bhi kɛrɨŋɨ bɛ chi yi.
Mpok yɔ, bǒ abhɛn bachi atú Judɛ́ya mámbʉ́ɛ́, mámbɛ́sɛ́ amfay njiɛ. Abhɛn báchi amɛm ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm mámbʉ́ɛ́ mándɔ́k. Nɛ abhɛn bachi nɛfí bákɛ́ chwe ɛtɔk,
Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛnkʉ bɛ manoŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ achi chak anɛ bo báwáy, ámbák be anti, bɛ́bho nɛ manoŋ Ábɛl mmu achí nyaka chak bɛsí Mandɛm, bɛghaka ndǔ manoŋ Sakaría mmɔ̌ Barákia, mmu bǎwáy nyaka nɛntɨ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm nɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ báchyɛ̀ akap arɛ́.
Tɛ̌ndu nɛgúɛ́p anɛ Mandɛm ágʉ́ɛbhɛ́ bo Israɛl ɛbhɨ ákʉ́ bɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mámbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛbhak ndǔ kɛmʉrɛ nɛ Mandɛm, mpok Mandɛm apɛt asɔrɛ bo Israɛl amʉɛt, chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkwak ná? Chɔŋ ɛ́nkʉ bɛ bawú mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m kɛ?
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́gháti bhe, kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛsɨŋ bɔ mɛnkɛm amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ.
Yesu anáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɔŋ bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm, afa apɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk Kapɛ̌naum.
Achí fá árɛ̀m kɛpɨ kpoŋoroŋ, nɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ ntá yi. Ɛ́kway bɛbhak bɛ bǒbati bárɨŋɨ bɛ yí chí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò?
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́tɛ́m nɛkay ɛnɛn, arɛm bɛ, “Bák yɛ ka pě, mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mpok anɛ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí twɔ.” 
Yi apɛt apu chi ndiɛrɛ nsɛm. Acha nsɛm nɛ́nɛ. Arɔp chi ntɨ manɔ́ anɛ ɔ́kwáy bɛkɔŋ. Nkɔŋ yi tontó, kɛ ɔbhɔ̌ŋ mbɔŋ bɛkɔŋ yi ɛncha ɛnyu ɛnɛ nkɔ́ŋɔ́ yi. Achí nsɛm aywɛ, apɛt abhak ntɨ manɔ́ ntá yɛ ndu ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Acha mbɔ wɔ.
Ɔchyɛ́ yi bɛtaŋ amfǎy yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.” Bɛrɛm bɛ báchyɛ yi bɛtaŋ amfǎy yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɔp ɛnɛ ɛpu antɛnɛ́-yi. Kɛ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchi antɛnɛ́-yi.
Abhak arɛ́ ndǔ bataŋ árát. Ndu átòŋti mmʉɛt bɛ́sɔt áchwi andɔk Síria, aghók bɛ́ bo Israɛl bápà bɛ́kɛm yi. Ayibhiri ntɨ ɛni arɔbhɛ sɔt chí mbi atú Masidónia bɛ́kɔ́ amɨk ámpɛ́tnsɛm.
Bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn ɛtɔk Antiɔk, bájwi nɛ maŋák nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ bhɔ́ sayri.
Ɛ́kʉ́ Pɔ̌l are yaŋ bɛsɔt Tímɔti bɛ andɔk nɛ bhɔ. Akʉ yɛ básyɛ́p yi mbɔnyunɛ bo Israɛl bachi nyaka ndǔ bɛtɔk ɛbhɔ nɛ bárɨ́ŋɨ bɛ chi Tímɔti achi chi mmǔ Grik.
Píta aghati yi bɛ, “Nkwǎnɛ, mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ wɔ ɔ́rɛ̀m!” Tɛ́mté wu, ɛnɛ́ yi ábhʉɛ́t bɛrɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m, nkɔk akók.
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi mánók yɛ bárɔk ɛbhě manyu Gálili ɛchak, báchwɔp angɔkɔnyɛ́n, kɛkwɔt nɛ atú Gɛrása.
Arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Ɛyɔŋɔ́ kɛbhɔ ɛ́fù ɛtɔk Ráma. Kɛbhɔ kɛ́yá nɛ bása. Ráshɛl ǎdì bɔ̌bhi. Mánɨ̀k yi mmʉɛt bɛ ambɔt kɛbhɔ kɛ apú ka mbɔnyunɛ bágu barɔ yi.” 
Bǎrɛm bɛ yi?” Bákɛ́mɛ bɛ, “Abhɔŋ bɛ́gu!”
Tímɔti, dɔp Ɛ́fɛsɔs nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu ngati nyaka wɔ ɔ́nkʉ. Mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ atú Masidónia. Dɔp arɛ́ ghati bo abhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ baraká nse bɛ mándɔ́ bɛ́tɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ. Mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ atú Masidónia
Abhak arɛ́ ndǔ manywɔp bɛsa bɛpay Satan amɔ nɔkɔ yí. Nnya ɛbébé ɛ́bhák arɛ́ nkwɔ, kɛ bɔángɛl Mandɛm báchyɛ Yesu nɛkwak. 
Ndu ɛchi yɛ̌ nɔ, bǎkɛ́ rɔ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ánji be bɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́chí nɛ bhe ɛ̌ti mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mǎnyìɛ nɛ ɛbhɛn mǎnyù. Nɛ bǎkɛ́ rɔ bɛ mmu ampuri bhe mǎnkoŋo bɛbhé ɛ̌ti bɛpǎ mmyɛ́,   nɛ ɛpǎ ntaŋ akɔ, nɛ ɛ̌ti ɛpǎ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.
Bɛbhé ɛbhɔ mɛnkɛm bɛchi chi mbɔ ndɨ́kándi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ábhʉ́rɛ́ nyaka bɛ bɛ́twɔ chɔŋ. Mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi ansɛm ndɨ́kándi wu ankɛm chi Kristo yímbɔŋ.
Nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛ Tímɔti, wɔ mú ɔ́chí mbɔ mɔ̌wa anɛ nde kɔŋ. Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ mántɔ́ŋ wɔ bɛrɨ̌ndu, mángɔ wɔ ntínso nɛ mánchyɛ wɔ kpák. 
Mbɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ kway mmu anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ mɔ́ywɛ. Sɔt mɛ chí mbɔ nkʉbɛtɨk ywɛ̌ amɔt.”’
Nɨk nɔkɔ ka mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ nkwɔ bɛ Mandɛm ánɛ́nɛ́ bhɛsɛ mbi ndu bɛghati bho kpoŋoroŋ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo anɛ achi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́. Chi ɛ̌ti mɛ́ghàti bho yɔ kɛ nchí ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Básɔ́t mpɔŋɔ batu yɔ nɛ mɔ́ywi, bárɔ́k ntá Yesu nɛ yɔ. Básɔ́t ndɛn mfǎmʉɛt yap basɔbhɛri yɔ, Yesu akó achɔkɔ amfay.
Ndiɛrɛ ndɛ́ndɛmɛbho abhɛn, bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛbhé Moses kɛ mánóko yi. Ntá Mandɛm, bɔ mankɛm bábɛp!”
Sɛ́pú kɨŋɨ ndiɛrɛ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ ndu ɛbhɛsɛ bɛtɨk. Sɛ́bhaka ntɨ chi bɛ ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Kristo nɛ́gò nɛ́ndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, chɔŋ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛsɛ nkwɔ nɛntɨ ɛnɛka mɛ́ngo mɛndɔk nɔkɔ chí ambɨ.
Kɛ bǒ ɛtɔk yɔ kɛ ka yi anchwe arɛ mbɔnyunɛ baghɔ nyaka bɛ yi atɨ bɛrɔŋ chi Yerúsalɛm.
Sɛ́nkáká yɛ Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ ákʉ́ bɛ sɛ́mbák bo abhɛn yi achi Mfɔ wap, nɛ kɛfɔ ɛki kɛ́pú ɛkɛn mmu ákway mɛnyɨkɨsi. Ndu ɛ́chí nɔ, sɛ́nchíɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó ɛkɛn kɛ́chyɛ̀ yi maŋák, sɛ́nsɛpti mmʉɛt bɛsí bhi, sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ bɛcháy bɛsí bhi,
Bɔ̌ma, fyɛ́ yɛ́ ka bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ Mandɛm abhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe nɛ ayap bhe tɛtɛp mbɔnyunɛ mbák bákʉ̀ nɔ bǎpú kwɛn wáwák.
Bɛbho nɛ́nɛ, sɛ́pú pɛrɛ yɨŋɨ yɛ bho chí bɛkoŋo nkaysi bǒ mmɨk. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ sɛ́yɨ̀ŋɨ nyaka Kristo, kɛ nɛ́nɛ, sɛrɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyǔ mmu yi áchí.
“Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batú, ángók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm árɛ̀m ntá bɛka bǒnkwɔ. Mmu anɛ ánú ásɔ́rɛ́ awɔ́nɛm, nɛwú ɛnɛn nɛjwi apay nɛ́pú tɔk yi.” 
Nɛ mbák atú ándɛm bɛ, “Tɛ̌ndu mpú nyɛ́sɛ́, mpú ɛpókómʉɛt”, ɛyɔ ɛ́pú kʉ bɛ́ atú ákɛ bhák ɛ́pókómʉɛt.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l nchí sɨŋ bakak amɛn nɛ awɔ́ awa mɛmbɔŋ. Tɨk ka bɛ́ nchí ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Mandɛm antɔŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu.
Manyɛ́n bǒnto Yesu bhɔ bati byo nɛ apay achi bɛ, Símun anɛ Yesu áchyɛ́ nnyɛ́n nɛchak bɛ Píta; nɛ
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛbhé ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chá bɛ́chák mɛnkɛm chi ɛnɛ́ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Bo Israɛl, ghók ká. Mandɛm Acha anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɛsɛ́ mankɛm achí amɔt.’
Bákʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛyap chi ndu bɛtɔŋ mmʉɛt. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛchi bɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ǎsɔt Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ansɨ́ŋ amfyɛ amɛm bɔ̌mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ nchóŋ ambat nɛfó purɛ́ɛ́, angwɔ́t ɛ́chák ndǔ ɛrɛbháwɔ, kɛ́mbyáká bɛjɛnjɛ̌mɛ́ ndɛn ɛyap nkwɔ bɛ́sàpti mɛ́ncha ɛnyu bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhak.
Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu Ɛtaya áchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ mɛnyiɛ kɛfɔ, ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ nchí kʉ chɔŋ bɛ be nkwɔ́ manyíɛ́ kɛfɔ.
Bɛ́jwí ndɔŋ ɛ́rát, Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Símun, mmɔ̌ Jɔ̌n, ɔkɔŋ mɛ?” Píta abé ntɨ mbɔnyunɛ Yesu ábhɛp yi ɛnyɨŋ ɛrɛ ɛ́mɔt ndɔŋ ɛ́rát. Ɛ́kʉ, aghati Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ nkɔŋ wɔ.” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ne bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n aya.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Twɔ́ ká, nɛ mbɔk nsi ɛyɔ nɔ́ bǎkɛ́mɛ́.”
Báré yɨŋɨ gbɔkɔ́ɔ́ ndǔ yi árɔ̀ŋ amfay. Bápɛ́rɛ ghɔ, bo bati apay nɛ nkú pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt báté kɛkwɔt nɛ bhɔ.
Ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ɔ́ghɔ́ chi nnɛ́m ɛtɔk ɛnɛ mfɔ ywi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfǎy bafɔ̌ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkaysi bɛ mankɔ̌ abhɛn ɛpǎ nɛbhay bákway bɛbhak ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay? Nsé! Tɛ̌ndu mbǎyngɔrɛ́ abhʉɛ́t nɛ bhɔ́, bápú kway bɛtat nsay.
Jekɔ́p arɔk ɛtɔk Íjip nɛ nnɛrɛ́kɛt ywi ankɛm. Abhak arɛ́ tɛ mpok anɛ yi ágú nɛ bɔ̌bhi bo bachi bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ.
Hɛ́rɔd ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ mankɔ̌ bhɔ bárwɔ yi ndǔ yi ánóŋó bhɔ kɛghɔ́, ntɨ nɛ́nɛn yi amɛm. Achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mángwáy bɔ̌babhakanɛm mankɛm abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ cha mamiɛ́ apay ndǔ ɛtɔk Bɛ́tlɛhɛm nɛ ndǔ bɛtɔk ɛbhɛn bɛchi kɛkwɔt. Hɛ́rɔd atɨk bɛ́ ɛ́náŋ ɛ́chí mamiɛ́ apay bɛ́bhó mpok mankɔ bhɔ báyámbɨ baghɔ nɛmbe mpok bábhé Yesu.
Ɛnɛ́ mánáŋ bákɛ́mɛ́ Jɔ̌n báfyɛ́ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, Yesu arɔk atú Gálili abho bɛghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Mandɛm,
Mányòk bhɛsɛ, kɛ Mandɛm apú rɔ bɛbhak nɛ bhɛsɛ. Bádɛp bhɛsɛ amɨk, kɛ bápú kway bɛway bhɛsɛ.
Tɛtɛp, nchí ghati bhe bɛ tɛ mfǎy ámfʉɛt, mmɨk amfʉɛt, bápú kwáy bɛfɛrɛ yɛ̌ mandú ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ basɨŋ amɛn wáwák. Basɨ́ŋ amɛn ǎbhák kpátɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ́mfu tɛtɛp.
Bɛyǎ bo mánóko Yesu ɛbhak ɛyɔ.
Básɔt nnɛ́mámɨk anɛ Yesu ákʉ́ yi ághɔ̀ mbaŋ bárɔ́k ntá bǒnkwɔ Fárisi.
Mbɔk batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nkwɔ́ bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Yí sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kʉ?” Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ sɔt nkáp ntá mmu nɛ bɛtaŋ, bǎkɛ́ bhat mmu ndak amʉɛt; dɔ̌ ká akap anɛ́ báchyɛ̀ bhe ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀ ánkway bhe.”
Kɛ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp ǎtwɔ ndǔ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ maŋák, bɛ bo mangɔ bɛ Mandɛm kɛ ákwak yi ankʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ.” 
Bábhɔ́ŋ nkwɔ bɛchyɛ akap ɛ́bu wu anɛ achi ‘Bɔ̌bɛbhóŋó bɛpay, mbák ɛpu nɔ, bɛbhɛp bɛpay, bɛkoŋo ɛbhé Mandɛm.’”
Kɛ yí kɛrɔ́ŋ Násárɛt. Arɔk achɔkɔ Kapɛ̌naum. Ɛtɔk Kapɛ̌naum ɛ́bhák nɛpak manyu Gálili, atú Sɛ́bulɔn nɛ Náftali.
‘Mandɛm Acha arɛm nyaka ntá Acha wa bɛ, chɔkɔ fá ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm ɛya ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ-kɛnókó,   kpatɛ nkʉ bǒmpap abhɛ mándɔp mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɔ́nyàŋa chɔŋ bɛkak arɛ.’
Kʉ ka bo Bábilɔn mámbɔ́ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ. Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɔ bábhɔŋ nyaka maŋák, mpok bápà bɛ bachi manɛm bho nɛ, mánkʉ nɔkɔ baraká bɛbʉ́. Báchi mbɔ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ árɛ̀m nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, ‘Nchí mfɔ ngɔrɛ́. Mpu kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́! Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mmu anɛ ákway bɛgu mɛ̌ndi yi wáwák!’
Bě manɛ́mámɨk abhɛn bǎyà bho mbi, bǎsɔt mpok bɛ́fɛ́rɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mɔ́nya anɛ áchí amɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mǎnyú, kɛ mpɔŋɔ baso mǎmɛnɛmɛ́n ham.
Ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn Mandɛm áfʉɛt ntá Yesu Kristo bɛtaŋ bo mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ mɛ́ghàti bo árɛ̀m, chɔŋ antáŋ bo bɛkoŋo nkaysi anɛ achi bhɔ antɨ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́. 
Mǔngo bachiǎkap ǎsɔt nyaka manoŋ nnya anɛ báwáy ndu bɛchyɛ akap anchwe amɛm nɛbhʉɛt anɛ áchí nyáŋá anchyɛ akap bɛ Mandɛm amfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bho. Kɛ mbák chi mbɔ̌ŋ nnya ɛnɛ báwáy, báfu nyaka ɛtɔk nɛ yɔ kɛ mánsɔŋ. Bápú sɔ́ŋ yɔ́ amɛm ɛtɔk.
Nɛ Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛ́pú amɛm batɨ yɛka mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko mmu anɛ yi átó.
Asɔt yɛ manyiɛp afyɛ́ ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ, abho bɛso bɛkak bakoŋo bhi, antɛsɛ nɔkɔ nɛ táwáy anɛ yi átɛ́mɛ́ ɛbho.
Bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ fá, mbɨ́kɨ́ chɔŋti mpok. Nɛ́yí, nchyɛ́ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mánsɔ́t mmǔ wu mantwɔ ndu acha manyé nɛ yi.
Nɛka Moses nɛ Mandɛm kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ yi arɔ ɛtɔk Íjip kɛcháy bɛběntɨ Mfɔ Íjip. Akɛ́pntɨ, arɔk mbɔ bɛ yi ǎghɔ̀ nyaka Mandɛm mmǔ bo bápú ghɔ nɛ amɨ́k.
Ató mmɔ̌bɛtok anɛ ajwi bati arat. Bádɛ́n, báfyɛ́ bɛfʉɛt amʉɛt, bábók, afú arɔk.
Mmǔ anɛ ábhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp ndǔ bǎru mɛnyɨŋ, ǎbhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp mi ndǔ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ. Nɛ mmu anɛ ápú bhʉɛrɛ bariɛp ndǔ bǎru mɛnyɨŋ, apú bhʉɛrɛ bariɛp ndǔ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ nkwɔ.
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá yap bɛ, “Mbɔŋ bɛ́pɛt bɛbhak nɛ bhe ndǔ mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok kɛ ndɔ́k ntá mmu anɛ átó mɛ.
Áká yɛ bɛ́ mánkʉ́ nɛ Yesu mbɔ ɛnyu bakɔŋɔ.
Nɛchwe Píta áchwe anywɔ́p, Kɔnéliɔs akwɛ́n yi bɛkak, abho bɛ́chyɛ yí kɛnókó.
Nɛ yɛ̌ ɛmbak chi bɛ bǎbhɔ̀ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti bǎchí chak, ɛyɛka ɛ́rɨ ɛncha. Bǎkɛ chay yɛ̌ mmu, nɛ batɨ ákɛ́ sɔŋɔri be amɛm.
Nɔ kɛ ɛ́chí bɛ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo mankɛm babhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ mmu amɔt, ɛnyu ɛyɔ nkwɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ mbɔnyunɛ mmu amɔt ákʉ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛyɔ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak, bo mankɛm babhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́, kɛ babhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Mpok bághɔ́ yi, bákwɛ́n amɨk babho bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó. Kɛ mbɔk ayap bare makati mbák, sayri sayri, Yesu kɛ bɔ bághɔ̀ nɔ.
Básɨŋ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo abhɛn bághɔ́ nɛ bágháti bhɛsɛ. Batísyɛ́ bhɔ bághɔ nyaka barak ayɔ tɛ nɛbhǒnɛt, kɛ bábhak bǒ bɛtok ndu bɛ́gháti bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Fɛstɔs ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m, Agripa arɛm bɛ, “Pɔ̌l, mbák ɔbhɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ́rɛm ndu bɛ́táŋá mmʉɛt, dɛm sɛ́ngók.” Pɔ̌l abho yɛ bɛ́táŋa mmʉɛt, antɔŋ nɔkɔ nɛ awɔ́ bɛ,
: Ndǔ bɔ mankɛm, nka byo nɛ apay bafu ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Júda, nka byo nɛ ɛpay bafu ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Rúbɛn, nka byo nɛ ɛpay bafu ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Gad. Nká byo nɛ ɛpay bafu ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Asha, nka byo nɛ ɛpay bafu ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Náftali, nka byo nɛ ɛpay ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Manáse. Nká byo nɛ ɛpay bafu ndu nnɛrɛ́kɛt Símiɔn, nka byo nɛ ɛpay ndu nnɛrɛ́kɛt Lɛ́vi, nka byo nɛ ɛpay bafu ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Isáka. Nká byó nɛ ɛpay bafu ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Sɛ́bulɔn, nka byo nɛ ɛpay bafu ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Josɛ́f, nɛ nka byo nɛ ɛpay bafu ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Bɛnjamin. 
Bǒnto báfú ndǔ nɛkɔ ɛnɛn Yesu átó bhɔ bápɛtnsɛm ntá yi, bágháti yi ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bákʉ nɛ ɛbhɛn bátɔ́ŋɔ́ bho.
Ɛtaya mmu áchyɛ́ mɛ yɔ, achá bo mankɛm. Nɛ mmu apú kwáy bɛfɛrɛ yɔ ndu amɔ yi.
Mpok bájwítí bhe, bábhɛ́mɛ be nɛ Kristo. Bě nkwɔ bǎpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ yi mpok yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Ɛ́fákári nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bǎsɨkɨ nyaka ntɨ ndǔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm mmu ákʉ́ Kristo apɛtnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m.
aghati yi bɛ, “Dɔ́k ndǔ ɛ̌ntɨ́ŋnyɛ́n Sílom, sǒ bɛsí arɛ́.” Sílom chi “Bátó”. Mmu wu arɔk, aso bɛsí arɛ nɛ mpok ápɛ̀tnsɛm are ghɔ́ mbaŋ.
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ bɛ Mandɛm ǎrɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ ńchɔnti nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn barɨŋɨ́ndak nɛ kɛboŋ ɛkɛn bǒ abhɛn báchi mbɔ mmu anɛ ághɔ̀ mɛnyɨŋ chi ndu ɛ́kírísú.”
Nɔ́ kɛ ɛ́bhàk chɔŋ nɛ bo mpok Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm ábhèsi.
Bɔ̌ma, sɛmtí nɔ́kɔ́ bábhɔ́t, mǎmfyɛ nɔkɔ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛcháy ntɨ. Kwak nɔ́kɔ́ ká abhɛn mmʉɛt ápú bhɔ. Bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu.
Yesu arɔ yɛ bɛyǎ bǒ abhɛn bachi nɛfí, arɔk achwe anywɔ́p nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi. Arɛ́, baghɔkɔ́ bhi barɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛta, ghatí bhɛsɛ ntí nɛkǎy nchaŋ.”
tɛ̌ndu ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo átɔ́ŋ mɛ bɛ manywɔp aya fá amɨk ábhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ yá.
Símun Píta mmu achi nɛ akparɛnja amʉɛt, agwɔp akparɛnja wu ndǔ kɛ́nkwɔ́p, kpɔ́t atú nsɛm Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm chwát agʉɛp amɨk. Nnyɛ́n nsɛm ɛrɛ nɛ́bhak bɛ Málkɔs.
Yesu aghati Píta bɛ, “Nchí ghati wɔ bɛ, nkɔk apɛrɛ́ kok ndɔŋ ɛpay nkúbhɛ́ bɛti ɛbhɛn, chɔŋ ɔ́ndɛm ndɔŋ ɛ́rát bɛ ɔbhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ mɛ.”
Apɛt yɛ nsɛm Násárɛt nɛ bhɔ, abhak nɛ bhɔ sayri akɛtaŋntí. Máyi abhʉrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm antɨ.
Mbɔk bo báfate bábhó bɛkɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ yi. Bábhak bǒ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛnɛ bo abhɛn báfɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ kɛsɛm. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ bábhɨŋɨ nyaka yɔ. Bábhák bo Israɛl abhɛn bafu Síren nɛ mmu Aleksánda. Bɔ́bhɔ nɛ bo Israɛl bachak abhɛn bafu atú Silísha nɛ Esia bare kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ Stífin.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, bɛrɔŋ mbɔ manywɔp ánɛn, asɔt Píta, nɛ Jɔ̌n, nɛ Jems akó amfǎy njiɛ nɛ bhɔ ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt.
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ mɛnɨkmʉɛt, mbɔnyunɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ bo bábhɔ̀ŋ mpok yɔ chi ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ wáwák tɛ̌ mmɨk ábhó. Nɛ mpok yɔ ánáŋ ámfʉɛ́t, ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri yɔ ɛpu pɛrɛ bhák wáwák.
Nkwǎŋwaŋ ǎyɨkɨ chi ndǔ nnyɛ́n mmu anɛ acha yi, nɛ mpok bo bákɛ̀m ɛpʉ́ítí, mánáŋ mányú nku, ɛpʉ́ítí ɛ́may.
Mbɔ̌ŋ ntɨ bɛ́twɔ awu ntá yɛ mandú mpok. Yɛ̌ nɔ, nchí sɨŋ bɛ́gháti wɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ mbɔnyunɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́kway bɛ́fákári nkɛ wakari bɛ́twɔ awu.
Tó yɛ mmu Jopa bɛ andɔk ambɨŋɨ mmu anɛ ákà nnyɛ́n bɛ Símun Píta. Achí kɛnkɔ amɛm ɛkɛt Símun ngoko nkwɔbhɛ́nya nɛ ɛkɛt ɛyi ɛ́chí angɔkɔ manyu!’
Nchí nɛ wɔ nɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛkʉ wɔ ɛnyɨŋ. Bɛyǎ bo bachi ɛtɔk ɛnɛ abhɛn babhak chɔŋ bǒbha.”
Twɔ́ ká ntá ya mbɔnyunɛ ntu ánɛ mɛ̌chyɛ bhe achi fuyak.”
Chiɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yɛka batɨ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ nɛ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn.
Nchí mmǔ bɛbʉ́, yɛ̌ nɔ, Mandɛm aghɔ mɛ ntínso ndu áyaŋ bɛtɔŋ ɛnyǔ Yesu Kristo ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyǎ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ nɛ mɛ, mɛ mmu nkʉ́ nyaka bɛbʉ́ ncha yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak. Yesu akʉ nɔ́, bɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́mbák ɛrɨŋ ntá bho ndu bɛ́kwák bɔ mánkway mɛnoko yi, mámbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, njɨŋɨ ngɔ́ mbǐnywɔp anɛ achi fúú amfay. Nɛ mpɛt ngók ɛyɔŋɔ́ mbɨ ɛnɛ nnáŋ nyaka ngoko ndǔ ɛ́ghàti mɛ mɛnyɨŋ nɛ ɛyɔŋ mbɔ ɛnɛ́ mmbá. Ngók ndǔ yɔ ɛ́rɛ̀m ntá ya bɛ, “Twɔ́ wɛn amfay, nɛ chɔ́ŋ ntɔŋ wɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn chɔŋ bɛfakari.”
Bárɔ́ bɛ yɔ ɛ́nyok bǒbhɔ ndǔ bataŋ atay, kɛ bɛ bákɛ́ chyɛ ngɛ́mtay bɛtaŋ bɛway yɛ̌ mmu. Ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ ngɛ́mtay ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́chyɛ bo ɛbhak mbɔ bɛbe ɛbhɛn mmu ábhɔ̀ŋ mpok ngá-nɛghay ánɛm yí.
Mmu anɛ árɔ̀ŋ ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́, chi mmu Satan, mbɔnyunɛ Satan abho bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ tɛ ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt. Ntí anɛ Mmɔ Mandɛm átwɔ́ fá amɨk chi bɛchɔŋti bɛtɨk Satan.
Júda nɛ Sáilas babhak barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ. Bágháti bǒnkwɔ Yesu bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ndu bɛ́fyɛ́ bhɔ́ ntɨ nɛ bɛ́kwák bɔ mántaŋ ndu nɛsɨkɨ́ntɨ ɛnap nɛ Yesu.
Yesu akʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ntá bho bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ɛ̌ti yi ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp. Aisáya arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Asɔt mame ayɛsɛ nɛ apɔkɔ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛsɛ́.” 
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ bo Israɛl mankɛm bápú nyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ kɛ yambɨ bɛso amɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛpɨŋɨ́ bachǐmbɨ bhap ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ.
Mbák mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́kɛm ɛkɛt ɛyi sayri, ná yí ákway bɛbhak ɛrɨ́tí mǔnti ntá bǒnkwɔ abhɛn bachi antɛnɛ́ yi?
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, ɛnɛ́ Yesu ákɔ̀ nɛpak manyu Gálili, aghɔ́ bo bati apay, bɔ̌ nnɔ amɔt chi amɔt. Amɔt aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Símun. Nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛ́chák nɛ́bhák bɛ Píta. Manɔ́ ywi aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Andru. Bɔ bati apay bare gʉɛp bɛyǎ nkáp anyɛ́n ndu bɛway nsi mbɔnyunɛ bachi nyaka bawǎnsi.
Bǒ nnɛrɛ́kɛt bátɛ́n nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ nɛfí, Yesu arɔk kɛkwɔt nɛ ngú wu, ákɛ́m yi ndǔ awɔ́, mɔ́wu apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, afate.
Bo abhɛn bárɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ Pɔ̌l, barɔk nɛ yi kpát bágháka Atɛns. Pɔ̌l aghati yɛ bhɔ mpok anɛ bápɛ̀tnsɛm bɛ́ mángátí Sáilas nɛ Tímɔti bɛ mánjáŋ mbi mántɛmɛri yi ayak amɛm ɛtɔk Átɛns.
Mfɔ achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mánkɛ́m yi mángwɔ́t amɔ nɛ bɛkak, mámɛsɛ nɛfí ndǔ ɛjuri. Arɛ́, bo bábhak ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ nɛ nɛnyiɛ́ ámɛ́n.”
Mǔnti bo Israɛl amɔt achi nyaka. Aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Nikɔdɛ́mɔs. Abhak mǔnkwɔ Fárisi.
Báfú nɔ́kɔ́, báré rɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Mmǔ-nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́yaŋ bɛ mángwáy yí nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛfyɛ yi ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.”
Kɛ chí ndiɛrɛ Banábas nɛ mɛ kɛ sɛ́chí bǒnto abhɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk nɛ amɔ́ yɛsɛ́ kɛ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ nɛnyíɛ́ mɛ́nyiɛ́?
Nkwaŋa-nkɨ anɛ afyɛ́ bɛtaŋ ndǔ bɛtɨk kɛ áyámbɨ bɛbhɔŋ mbwɔ́t anɛ áfú ɛbhɨ.
Bo bárɛ̀m chɔŋ nɔ́, mbɔnyunɛ, mbák bákwày bɛ́kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ntá ya, Mmɛ mmu nchí ɛnɔk ɛbɨk, chɔŋ ɛ́mbak ná nɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́gú?”
Bǎbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bárɛ̀m bɛ nkʉ, ɛbhɨkɨ fʉɛt chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛnɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ ndɛm mpok ntée nɛntɨ ɛnap bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ bawú mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.’”
Mǔnti nkwɔ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bǒ Rom amɔt achi nyaka arɛ́. Mǔbɛtok aywi anɛ yi aré kɔŋ áre me. Arɔp chi kɛkwɔt bɛ́gu.
Kɛ chɔŋ mántɛn bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛbhak ndǔ nɛbhʉɛrɛ Kɛfɔ Mandɛm nɛfí ndǔ ɛjuri. Arɛ́, mámbak ndǔ kɛbhɔ nɛ nɛnyiɛ ámɛ́n.”
Abho bɛghati bhɔ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ bakay bɛ, “Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, nkwaŋankɨ amɔt arɔk bɛtak ɛnyǔ nchwifú amɛm nkɨ ywi.
Mbɔk bo abhɛn báchí nyaka ndǔ nkwɔ́ ywɛsɛ bárɔ́k ndǔ nnɛm bághɔ́ bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchi nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ bárɛ́mɛ́, kɛ bɔ́ kɛghɔ́ mbɔŋ Yesu.”
Pɔ̌l arɛm bɛ, “Wɔ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́rí nkok anɛ bawati nɛ mbɨ pɛ́pɛ́p bɛ bo bǎkɛ́ rɨŋɨ! Chɔŋ Mandɛm andɛp wɔ. Ɔchɔ́kɔ́ afɔ bɛ́sɔt ɛbhé ɔ́ntaŋ mɛ, nɛ ɔ̌rɛ̀m bɛ mándɛp mɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛbhé ɛbhɨkɨ chyɛ wɔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɔ̌? .”
Acha ayibhiri mmʉɛ́t ayɨŋɨ Píta. Amɨ́k ayap átɛ́mɛ́ri. Píta atɨk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ághátí yi bɛ, “Nkɔk apɛrɛ́ kók bɛti ɛbhɛn, chɔŋ ɔ́ndɛm ndɔŋ ɛrat bɛ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛ.”
Ɛ̌ntɨ́ŋnyɛ́n ɛbhak Yerúsalɛm, kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ nyǔ-ɛbhá anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ nyǔbha bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n. Bábhɨŋɨ ɛ̌ntɨ́ŋnyɛn ɛyɔ ndǔ ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ́ bo Israɛl bɛ Bɛtsáta. Bɛ́tɛm bɛtay bɛbhak kɛkwɔt nɛ ɛ̌ntɨŋ ɛyɔ.
María arɔk aghati ndak anɛ ntá bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ nɔkɔ nyaka nɛ Yesu. Atɛmɛri bɔ́ ndǔ básɛ̀mɛ mándi nɔkɔ.
Kɛ tɛ̌ndu ndak anɛ achi chi ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bárɛ̀m nɛ manyɛ́n bo nɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛka, be babhɔŋ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyǔ bátàŋ wu. Mpú kwáy bɛtáŋ ayɔ barak.”
Arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ndǔ nɛbhay, abháy achak, akwɛ̌n bɛrwɔp,
Kɛ bǒ nse bachwe ndu nkwɔ bakoŋo Yesu ansɛm ansɛm mánjaŋa nɔkɔ bɛ mansyɛp yi. Mánɔ́nɛ báchwe ndu nkwɔ ywɛsɛ ndu bɛghɔ ɛnyu sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ ngangaŋ amfǎy bɛbhé bo Israɛl, ndu sɛbharɛ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo. Báyàŋ nyaka bɛ sɛ́mpɛ́tnsɛm ndu kɛsɛm antɛnɛ bɛbhé bo Israɛl.
Yɛ̌ mmu achak kɛchɛm nɛ bhɔ ɛ̌ti bɛcháy, kɛ bo báre chyɛ̀ bhɔ kɛnókó.
Ɛnɛ́ ɛ́jwí bɛpay ɛ́chi mbɔ ɛnɛ́, nɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Kɔ́ŋ ntɨ nkwǎ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́kɔ́ŋɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ.’
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, yɛ̌ndu mɛ́rɛ̀m nɔ nɛ bhe, mbɔ̌ŋ ntɨ nɛ bhe bɛ́ bǎkʉ̀ chi bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kɔ̀ ndɔŋ amɔt nɛ nɛpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm ápɛ̀mɛ bhe.
Tɛ̌ndu Júdas kɛ ákɛm nyaka ɛbhǎ nkáp, mbɔk ɛyap báré kaysi bɛ Yesu ǎghàti yi chi bɛ ándɔ́k, ánkú mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ básɔt mɛnyiɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ. Báchák bákáysi bɛ Yesu ato yi ándɔ́k ánchyɛ́ nkáp ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho.
Nɛ́re fʉɛ́t nɛ́ntɨ́ nkɔngɔ ɛtɔk. Ɛnɔk nɛpɛ́m ɛ́bhak angɔkɔnyɛ́n ndǔ bɛbhe bɛ́páy. Ɛ́bhɔ́ŋ mɛnyǔ kɛpɛmɛ́nɔk byo nɛ kɛpay, nɛ ɛ́nyù kɛpɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ntaŋ ndǔ mmíɛ́. Bɛyé bhi chi babhé amɛn ábù bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm.
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi abhɛn bachi nyaka kɛkwɔt bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́, bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɔ̌rɛ̀m nɔ chi bɛ bɛsɛ nkwɔ sɛ́chí amɨ́k nɛ́mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ kɛ?”
Pɔ̌l afate yɛ asá nɛ awɔ bɛ bo manchɔkɔ kpák. Abho yɛ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Bo Israɛl nɛ bo bɛtɔk bɛ́chák abhɛn báchày Mandɛm, ghók ká!
Chi-bɛtɨk aghɔ́ nkʉbɛtɨk wu ntínso, afoŋori yi, afɛrɛ ntí ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákɛ̀m yi, arɔ yí ándɔ́k.
Kɛ Ábraham akɛmɛ yi chi bɛ, ‘Mɔ́wa, kɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ mpok ɔchí awu amɨk, ɔbhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Lásárɔs ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ chí bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ. Kɛ nɛ́nɛ yí achí sayri fá ɛnɛ́ wɔ ɔ́chí ndǔ nɛnyíɛ́ ámɛ́n.
Nchɛ́bhɛ́mu amɔt achí nyaka. Aka nyɛ́n bɛ Lásárɔs. Báre bhʉrɛ yi ndǔ nyǔbha mǔnkáp wu mpoknkɛm. Mmʉɛt yi ajwi nɛ bɛfʉɛt.
Ɛ́fákári bɛ, Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bákɔ̀ mámfʉɛrɛ nɔkɔ amɛm nkɨ̌ nchwi ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl. Ɛnɛ́ báfʉɛ́t, baghɔkɔ́ bhi bábho bɛkʉɛp ɛnyǔ nchwi yɔ.
Bǒnto báfú bárɔ ɛchɛmɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk bárɔ́k nɛ maŋák mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm aghɔ bɛ bɔ bakway bo abhɛn bábhɔ̀ŋ kɛyɔ́rɛ́ ɛ̌ti nnyɛ́n Yesu.
Nɛ yɛ̌ mbɔ́ŋ chí akap bɛ́gháti bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm nɛ mbák ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm,   yɛ̌ chí mɛnyɨŋ Mandɛm ɛbhɛ́n bɛchí bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, nɛ mbák mbɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌kwáy bɛ́gháti njiɛ ngo bɛ, “Fǎ fá”, amfa, kɛ nkɛ kɔŋ bo, nɔ mpú yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Baghɔk Yesu bhɔ bati apay bárɔk ɛtɔk ɛgho ɛyɔ. Bághɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mbɔnyu Yesu ághati bhɔ, bákʉ nɛnyíɛ́ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ bábhʉrɛ.
Bárɔ́k, baghɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi aghati bhɔ. Bátóŋti Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ arɛ́. 
Mɛ́twɔ̀ mandú mpok. Tě ká kpirí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ fɔŋɔ nta kɛnókó yɛka anɛ́ átɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ mǎnu bǎsɔt awɔ́nɛm.
Píta árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, ɛchɛmɛ ɛnkɛm ɛ́kwɛ́n kpák ndu bɛ́ghok ndu Banábas nɛ Pɔ̌l bághàti bhɔ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhɔ́ bɛtaŋ, bákʉ́ nɛntɨ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl.
Arɛ́, bǒbati bachiǎkap nɛ manɛ́m bo Israɛl barɔk batɛmɛri Fɛstɔs babho bɛbhat Pɔ̌l barak amʉɛt. Nɛ manɨk Fɛstɔs mmʉɛt bɛ,
Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm, nchí rɔ́ŋɔ́rɔŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ básɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti ya, kɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá mmu anɛ áti mɛ ɛ́ncha! Mbɔ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhe yi, mbʉ ɛ́rɨ́ ntá yi ɛcha!”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka mpok bɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ rwɔ́ bhe!
Yɛ̌ chi Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm, mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ bɛ bo mántók mɛ. Ntwɔ chi bɛbhak mǔbɛtok nɛ bɛchyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ ndu bɛku bɛyǎ bhó mfɛ́rɛ́ bhɔ ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́.” 
Bakoŋo Yesu bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ kɛpɨ ɛkɛn yi árɛ̀m, bɛyǎ bhap báré rɛm bɛ, “Anɛ́ ndak ataŋ acha, agha ákwày bɛka wu?”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎkʉ̀, kʉ́ ka yɔ nɛ ɛkɔŋ.
Nɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mbák bo ábhɛn báchí chak bábhɔŋ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri kɛ mámpɛmɛ bhɔ, chɔŋ ɛ́mbak ná nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm, nɛ bákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́?”
Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm yɛ bɛ yi? Bɛ́ nté ayɛsɛ bo Israɛl acha anɛ bo bachak kɛ? Wáwák! Nnáŋ ntɔŋ bɛ bɛbʉ́ bɛbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay bo mankɛm, yɛ̌ chi bo Israɛl nɛ yɛ̌ chi abhɛn bapu bo Israɛl.
Bo Israɛl bábhó yɛ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Yí bɛ ‘Nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ, bǎpú kwáy bɛ́twɔ arɛ,’ ǎyaŋ bɛway mmʉɛt kɛ?”
Nkwɔ́ bo abhɛn mánókó Yesu bábhɔ́ŋ ntɨ nɛ́mɔt nɛ nkaysi amɔt. Yɛ̌ mmu wap akɛ rɛm bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi bɛ́chí chí ndiɛrɛ ntá yi aywǐntí. Ɛnyɨŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ɛbhak ɛnyɨŋ ɛyap mankɛm.
Mbák ɛnyɨŋ ɛchi ɛnɛ bɔ báyàŋ bɛrɨŋɨ, mámbɛ́p manɛ́m abhap anywɔ́p. Ɛchi ɛnyɨŋ ntíánwɔ́p ntá ngɔrɛ́ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ amɛm ɛchɛmɛ́ bǒnkwɔ.
Bě nkwɔ bho bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ basɛm, kɛ́m ká bhɔ sayri. Bǎkɛ́ pá bɛchyɛ bhɔ ntɛmsi. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ Ɛta mmu achi amfay kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ be nɛ bhɔ, nɛ yi apú tɔŋ kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík. 
Nchí ghati yɛ bhe bɛ́: Nɨk ka mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́yàŋ, chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ wɔ. Yáŋ, chɔŋ ɔngɔ. Dɛp nɛkok, chɔŋ mánɛnɛ ntá yɛ.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, Yesu aghati baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ mándɔ́k mǎnchwe amɛm áchwí, mampe nnyɛ́n manjambɨ Bɛtsáida, ndǔ ɛbhě manyu ɛchak. Yímbɔŋ arɔp ansɛm bɛkʉ bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ mángúrɛ́.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ Jɔ̌n Njwiti acha yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak, ndǔ bo abhɛn bágú nɛ abhɛn bachi nɛpɛ́m. Yɛ̌ nɔ́, yɛ̌ chí mmu anɛ apu yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ mpáy bo abhɛn mányìɛ̀ Kɛfɔ̌ mfáy acha yi.
Fɛstɔs aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Pɔ̌l achí ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ amɛm ɛtɔk Seséria nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ nkaysi bɛrɔŋ arɛ́ mandú mpok.
Sɛ́ghɔ yɛ bɛ bápú kway nyaka bɛchwe ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko nyaka yi.
Mpɛt nchí bhɛp yɛ bɛ, mpok bo Israɛl báchɨ́ŋtí nɛkwɛ́n, bákwɛ́n ndak ámáy kɛ? Wáwák! Kɛ ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bhap, bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, bábhɔ̌ŋ mbi anɛ Mandɛm ápɛmɛ bhɔ. Mandɛm akʉ nɔ bɛ bo Israɛl mámbɔ́ŋ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ bo abhɛn bápu bo Israɛl, bɛ́ Mandɛm ampɛmɛ bhɔ bo Israɛl nkwɔ.
Ngɔrɛ́ wu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛta, chyɛ mɛ manyiɛbhɛ́ mɔ, bɛ́ manyiɛp ákɛ́ pɛrɛ kwak mɛ, nɛ bɛ nkɛ́pɛrɛ twɔ fá ndu bɛya manyiɛp.”
Kpák ambak nɛ bhe, ntínso Mandɛm nɛ́mbak nɛ bǒ Mandɛm mankɛm abhɛn bákòŋo ɛbhé ɛkɔ ɛnɛ.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi nɛ nɛkay bɛ, “Bɛsɔp bɛbhɔŋ babhok, kɛnɛn kɛ́bhɔ́ŋ manyay, kɛ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛbhak bɛsoŋ ntí.”
Ntí anɛ bɛyǎ bo bárɔ̀ŋ nyaka bɛghɔ Yesu chí bɛ, bághok bɛ́ yi akʉ ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛyɔ.
Kɛ Nkwak anɛ mɛ̌tò chɔŋ ntá yɛka, ǎfù chi ntá Ɛtaya. Chɔŋ yi angati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti ya mbɔ ntísiɛ awa. Yi chí Ɛfóŋó mmu ákʉ̀ bo mandɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp.
Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ bɛghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ árɛ̀m mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛchí amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Ɛchɔŋ, mbák mǎngok Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi,
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mmá, nokó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌ghàti wɔ. Mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ bo bápú pɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛchyɛ Ɛta Mandɛm kɛnókó yɛ̌ chi fá ndǔ njiɛ nɛ, yɛ̌ chi Yerúsalɛm.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nkárɛ́nká byo nɛ ɛpay nɛ ngósí, ɛjuri ɛ́kwɛ́n ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm. Ɛbhák kpátɛ nkárɛ́nká ɛ́rát nɛ ngósí.
Mbák mmu abhɔŋ batú bɛ́ghok mbaŋ, ángók sayri!”
Nchí kʉ nyaka bɛtɨk Yesu Acha nɛ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt nɛnkɛm, nɛ babhɛsɛ amɨ́k ɛ̌ti mamɔ anɛ ǎtwɔ̀ ntá ya ndǔ bo Israɛl bápà bɛfyɛ mɛ ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Ɛ̌ti bǎsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Yesu Kristo, be mankɛm bǎrɔp chí bɔ̌ Mandɛm.
Nɛ dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, bǎpú pɛrɛ ghɔ́ chɔŋ mɛ wáwák kpatɛ mpok anɛ bǎrɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Sɛ́mbɨ́tí mmu anɛ átwɔ̀ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Mandɛm Acha.’”
‑ Bágó nkwɔ ngɛ́bhɛ́ ntantaŋ amɔt ndǔ ɛyi ɛkotákátí ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Yesu. Bákʉ́ ɛnyumɔt nɛ achák ɛbhe awɔghɔ yi.
Bǒbhɛn, bákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp. Mandɛm akʉ nyaka Aisáya andɛm bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ mǎngoko ghok bɛyɔŋ ɛbha kɛ bǎpú jwimɛm wáwák; chɔŋ mǎnjɨŋɨ yɨŋɨ kɛ bǎpú ghɔ,
Yesu aya yí báfá nɛntɨ bho, bárɔk nɛ́kú. Asoŋ yí kɛnɔŋámɔ batú, apá batiɛ́, atɔk nɛ́rɨ ɛni.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l, kɛ nchi sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí mǔnto Yesu Kristo, bɛkoŋo nkaysi Mandɛm. Yi ayap mɛ bɛ ngati bho Mbok Ndɨndɨ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo anɛ achi ɛ̌ti bariɛp amɛm yi afyɛ́ nyaka bɛchyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti nta bo abhɛn manoko Yesu Kristo.
Baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn bákwàk bɛ́kʉ bɛtɨk Mandɛm, bábhɔŋ nkwɔ́ bɛ́bhɔŋ ɛrɨtí ɛpɨŋ. Bákɛ́ bhák bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti bo báchak, bábhɨkɨ bhɔŋ mɛ́ŋwaka ndǔ yɛ̌ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ bábhɔŋ bɛ́bhak bǒ tɛtɛp ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛchi ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ, ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́fu amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm, bárɛm ɛ̌ti nywɔp ɛnɛn nɛjwi tándrámɔt bɛ, “Mandɛm anaŋa nɔkɔ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛkʉ, aywe mmʉɛ́t ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn nɛjwi tándrámɔt.”
abhak arɛ́ ndǔ manywɔp bɛsa bɛpay Satan amɔ nɔkɔ yi. Yí kɛnyiɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ manywɔp ɛyɔ ankɛm. Ndǔ ngwɛnti manywɔp ɛyɔ nsay akɛ́m yi.
Puyɛ̌ chi mbɔŋ bɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ achak achi, kɛ mbɔk bo báfyɛ̀ bhe ɛbyɔk antɨ nɛ báyàŋ chí bɛ́yibhiri Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak.
Bo bárè yaŋ mbi mɛmɔ yi. Bábhɛ́p yi ankʉ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔŋ bɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛ́fú chi ntá Mandɛm.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛghati Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ tó ntá ángɛl anɛ ábhàbhɛri bǒnkwɔ abhɛn ɛtɔk Laodísia. Sɨ́ŋ kʉ bɔ mandɨŋɨ bɛ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛfǔ ntá mmu anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ ‘Amen.’ Yi achi mmǔ tɛtɛp nɛ Ntísiɛ anɛ tɛtɛp. Mandɛm afʉɛt chi nta yi kɛ ǎghoko mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm.”
Nchí kaka Mandɛm bɛ akʉ Táytɔs ámbɔ́ŋ nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyǔ ntɨ ɛnɛn mɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ ndu bɛkwak bhe.
Ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔŋ bɛ puyɛ̌ chi bɔ abhɛn bábhé mbɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmɔ́ achak kɛ bachi bɔ̌ Mandɛm. Chi bɔ̌ abhɛn bábhé bɛkoŋo bariɛp ami kɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛ báchí bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham tɛtɛp.
Kɛ bághoko nɔkɔ bɛ Yesu apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ bɛ́ María aghɔ yi, bákɛ noko bɛ́ ɛchi tɛtɛp. 
Abhesi yɛ ntá Jems nɛ, ansɛm mpok, ntá bǒnto mankɛm.
Bághɔ́ bɛ ntay ɛnɛn anyǔ nnɛm nɛ́rɔp chi nɛpaká nnɛm.
Ndɛm nɔ nɛ ntí bɛ mbɔk yap bágúrɛ́ ɛbhɨ nɛ bárɔbhɛ koŋo chí Satan.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔk Yesu amɔt anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Júdas Iskariɔt afʉɛ́t arɔk ntá bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm
Kɛ Mandɛm atɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ yi akɔŋ bhɛsɛ ndu Kristo ágú ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ mpok sɛbhʉɛt nyaka bǒ bɛbʉ́.
Hɛ́rɔd apɔp! Kɛ ɛ́bé yí mmʉɛt bɛkʉ ɛnyu ɛ́chák ɛ̌ti nɛyɨkɨ anɛ yí áyɨ́kɨ́ bɛsí mankɔ̌ bhi.
Júdas Iskariɔt achi nyaka mmǔ amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ baghɔk Yesu bati byo nɛ apay. Afuɛ́t arɔk ntá bǒbati bachiǎkap ndu bɛti Yesu ntá yap.
