Bábhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Ɔpú ghók nɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ̌bhɛn bárɛ̀m-ɛ?” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Nchí ghók. Nɔ́ tɛ̌ bǎchí, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re ghók wáwák ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ basɨŋɨ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm?” Básɨŋ bɛ, “Ɔkʉ mǎmbɔ nɛ abhɛ́n babhʉɛt amɔ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛchyɛ wɔ bakak nɛ kɛnókó?”
Nkwɔ́ bataŋá manyé bárɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bɔ̌ mankɛm báfáte, básɔt Yesu báré rɔ́ŋ ntá Páílet nɛ yi.
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Kɔnéliɔs, mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bɛsa bɛ́tay, kɛ ato bhɛsɛ́ ntá yɛ. Achí chak bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ ǎchày Mandɛm. Bo Israɛl mankɛm báchyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó tontó. Ángɛl Mandɛm ághátí yi ántó mámbɨŋɨ wɔ, ɔ́ntwɔ ɛkɛt ɛyi, bɛ angok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́gháti yi.”
Kɛ mbák bɛfu chi ntá Mandɛm, bǎpú kway bɛchyɛt bhɔ mbi. Bǎkway mbɔŋ bɛghɔ bɛ mánù chí nɛ Mandɛm!”
Ndu bárɔ̀ŋ, bo abhɛn báchi ambɨ nɛ abhɛn báchi ansɛm báre bɨk mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Sɛ́mbɨ́tí Mandɛm mfay! Mandɛm ánjɛ́t mmu anɛ átwɔ̀ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Acha!
Ɛ́tat nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu asɔt baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ apay nɛpak. Abho bɛ́gháti bhɔ bɛ, “Ghók ká! Sɛ́rɔŋ nɔ chí Yerúsalɛm, nɛ arɛ́, chɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm básɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm ɛ́mfakari.
Akʉ́ nɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ ǎrɛ̀m nyaka nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, “Mbák ntɔ́k yɛ̌ chí nkú yi, chɔŋ ntaŋ.”
Yesu abhɛ́p baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Mpok ntó bhe pósá ti, ɛbha ti, nkwɔbhánya bɛkak ti, bǎchɛp nyaka yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛ?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Wáwák.”
Yɛ̌ ɛnyɨŋ yɛ mmu anɛ Mandɛm árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ ɛyak ɛmbak nɛ yi apu kway bɛchwe ndǔ ɛtɔk ɛgho ɛyɔ. Ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ Mandɛm nɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn kɛ ɛbhak chɔŋ arɛ́.
Ɛnyɨŋɨ́ ngwɛnti ɛnɛ nchí ghati bhe chi ɛnɛ: Kɛ́m ká nɛbhárɛ́mʉɛt ɛnɛka nɛ Acha bɛ mǎntáŋ nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi ɛbhɛn bɛyǎ bɛcha.
Ndɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛta, wɔ kɛ ɔ́rɨ́ŋɨ́.” Arɛm ntá ya bɛ, “Chí bǒ abhɛn bafǔ ndǔ ɛrɛmɛ ɛsɔŋɔri, báso nkú ɛyap ndǔ manoŋ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n nɛ bákʉ yɔ́ ɛrɔp pɛ́pɛ́p.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ chi bɛkoŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mbák nsay ǎnù mǔmpap aywɛ, chyɛ yi nɛnyíɛ́. Mbák manyiɛp ǎkwàk yi, chyɛ yi manyiɛp ányú. Mbák bǎkʉ̀ nɔ, ɛ́bhak mbɔ bɛ bǎtò kɛfɨkɨsǐ ngó anti mǔmpap aywɛ, nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ mǔmpap ámbɔ́ŋ ntíánwɔ́p.”
Yesu abhɨŋɨ ngɛ́mtáy bho nɛ bakoŋo bhi arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Mbák mmu ǎyaŋ bɛ́bhak nkoŋo wa, abhɔŋ bɛ́ghɔ́kɔntɨk mmʉɛt yi, ampɔkɔ ɛkotákátí yi, ankoŋo mɛ.
Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Mpok aya ábhɨ́kɨ́ re kway, kɛ ntá yɛka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok akway.
Ngɔsɔ́ŋ wu nɔ ábhàbhɛri nyǔ-ɛbhá abhɛ́p Píta bɛ, “Pú wɔ nkwɔ ɔchí nkoŋo mmǔ-nɛ?” Píta akɛmɛ bɛ, “Mpú nɛ yi.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mpok akway anɛ Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bo mánchyɛ́ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá yi kɛnókó.
Bǒbati bo Israɛl bhɔ bárɛm yɛ ntá yi bɛ, “Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ re ghaka yɛ̌ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛpay nsɛm byo, ɔbhɛ́ ɔnáŋ ɔghɔ Abraham-ɛ?”
Nɛ bɛ́rɔ́ŋ ambɨ, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re pay amɛm ɛkáti Moses bɛ bachiǎkap bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt kɛ? Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ bɛ bɔ́ mánkwɛ́n ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ mmu ákɛ́ kʉ bɛtɨk ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt kɛ? Bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm bɛ bɔ bákʉ bɛbʉ́.
Kɔ nɔ́kɔ́ ká ndǔ babhi anɛ achi chak. Bo abhɛn bɛkak ɛbhap bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ sɛnɛ amɨk mánkóŋó babhi yɔ́, nɛ chɔŋ maŋɔk ayap anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ taŋ, ántaŋ.
Barak mandɛm nsé anɛ yi ákʉ̀ ndu ɛrɔ́ri mpok, akʉ bo báre ta batú bɛghók mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi árɛ̀m.
Nɛ mbák nyɛ́sɛ́ ɛnɛ nɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ́ ɔ́nkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́, poŋórí nɔ́ fɛrɛ, ɔ́ngʉɛp. Ɛ́chí sayri bɛ́ ɔ́nchwe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti nɛ nyɛ́sɛ́ nɛ́mɔt ɛcha mɛ́mɛ́sɛ wɔ amɛm nɛpǐngo nɛ amɨ́k ayɛ ankɛm apay.” 
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mmǔ anɛ anoko ǎbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Ndǔ mɔ́nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp amɔt kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛn kɛnkɛm kɛ́rɔŋ.’ “Bǒbati baya bachwi nɛ bǒbati bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk amɛm áchwi, nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk amɛm áchwí nɛ bakɔ̌siɛ abhɛn bachi amɛm áchwí báté nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nywɔbhɛ́ ngwɛnti ɛpa, nɔ́ chi, nywɔp nɛgho ɛnɛn ɛpǎ ɛyɔ, Yesu afate arɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ manyiɛp ákwak yi, ántwɔ́ ntá ya.
Hɛ́rɔd nɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bhi báré byak yi, mámfyɛ nɔkɔ yí ɛtáŋɔk. Mámɛ́sɛ yi nkú kɛfɔ amʉɛt. Arɛm bɛ́ mánsɔ́t yí mámpɛtnsɛm ntá Páílet nɛ yi.
Banábas arɔk yɛ Tásɔs bɛ́yaŋ Sɔ̌l.
Anɛ bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛtay atwɔ́ nɛ bɛbha byó, arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛta, ɔchyɛ́ nyaka mɛ bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛtay bɛ nkɔ ɛsiɛ nɛ wu. Nnu kpát bɛbha bɛ́chák bɛ́tay bɛ́ko amfay.’
Bɔ̌ma, sɛ́nsɔt ɛrɨŋ ndu nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn bo abhɛn fá amɨk. Mbák bo bati apay manka bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ, mányu nku, yɛ̌ mmu ápú kway bɛway nku yɔ, nɛ mmu ápú kway mɛmaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak arɛ́, tɛ̌ndu manyu nku.
Kɛ Yesu asɛmti bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyǔ mmu mɛ nchí.” 
Bákɔ ndǔ nywɔp nɛnkɛm mánkaysi nɔkɔ bɛ yi achi ndǔ nkwɔ́ wap. Bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ apú nɛ bhɔ, babho bɛyaŋ yi nɛntɨ mamʉɛrɛ bhap nɛ bǒnɛrɛ́kɛt awap.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ Acha, ansɔt nkɔ́p ayi ɛnɛ́ yí ábhɨ́kɨ́ kaysi bɛ́chyɛ́ mmʉɛt Acha kɛnókó, chɔŋ Mandɛm antɛmsi yí.
Ɛta, nɛ́nɛ sɔt mɛ mbak nɛ wɔ, ɔ́nchyɛ mɛ kɛnɛ́m bɛsí ɛbhɛ, nkúbhɛ́ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛn mbɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka nɛ wɔ kɛ ɔ̌ghoko mmɨk.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ́ŋ yɛ bɛ, Mandɛm ǎghɔ ntínso nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ yi áyàŋ bɛghɔ yi ntínso, angwɔ́t ntɨ̌ nɛ mu anɛ yi áyàŋ bɛgwɔt ntɨ ɛni. 
Ananías abhɛsɛ mbɔk nkáp ansɛm. Ngɔrɛ́ aywi arɨŋɨ bɛ yi akʉ nɔ. Asɔt anɛ́ árɔ́bhɛ́ arɔk abhʉrɛ bɛsí bǒnto Yesu.
Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt nɔ bɛ bo mánchyɛ́ nyɛ́n Yesu Acha kɛnókó ɛ̌ti yɛka nɛ bɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ kɛnókó nɛ yi bɛ́kóŋo bɛrɨ̌ndu abhɛn Mandɛm ywɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha bátɔ̀ŋ be.
Kɛ Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re pay amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mfɔ Debhít ákʉ́ nyaka nɛ bǒ abhɛn báchí nɛ yi mpok nsay ákɛ́mɛ́ bhɔ́?
Mbák chi be, bǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka bɛ bǎchí bo Israɛl nɛ bǎghɔ̀kɔ mmʉɛt ndǔ ɛbhé ɛnɛ bǎbhɔŋɔ nɛ bǎpà bɛ bǎchi bo Mandɛm.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn kɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ákɛ́ bhák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm. Mɛ́nyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ kɛso amɔ, apú kʉ bɛ mmu ákɛ́ bhák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm.” 
Ɛkʉ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bárɔk, básiɛ́ptí bɛkak mmǔ mbɨ, básiɛ́ptí bɛkak anɛfú.
Nti anɛ nsɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe ɛkáti ɛyɔ chi bɛ mmɔ́ be ngɔ́ mbák chɔŋ mǎnkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngátí bhe.
Mandɛm aku be nɛ bɛyǎ nkáp, bǎbhɔŋ yɛ́ bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó nɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka.
Ayɨkɨ bɛyǎ ndɔŋ ntá yi bɛ, “Chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́yàŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ, yɛ̌ chí ɛbhakátɔk ɛya ɛ́mɔt.”
Ɛnyǔ ngáŋ wu ápú pɛrɛ rɨ́ ndǔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Ápú rɨ amɨk nɛ apu rɨ yɛ̌ ndu bɛfyɛ ndu ntó-takɔ anɛ báyàŋ ámpɔ́ɔ́ ánchyɛ ntɔbhɛ́-píɔ. Báto wu to. Mmǔ anɛ áyàŋ bɛghok ántá batu angok sayri.”
Bo Israɛl mánaŋ bádɛp mɛ nnɛt nɛ ɛ́kpá ndɔŋ ɛsǎ nsɛm nɛkú nɛ ɛnwi. Bákʉ nɔ ndɔŋ ɛtay.
Bě bɛchɨŋtǐ bho! Mandɛm anɛ aghókó ɛnyɨŋ, pú yi kɛ aghoko mmɛm nɛ nsɛm ɛyi nkwɔ?
Kɛ mmu apɛrɛ́ nɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm, ánókó bɛ́ Mandɛm ǎghok yi. Ákɛ́ makati wawak, mbɔnyunɛ mmu anɛ ánɨ̀kmʉɛt amakati nɔkɔ achí mbɔ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛ́n ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chi amɛm manyu. Mpok anɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p áfòk, ádɛ̀p yɔ́ ántɛn nɔkɔ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ wú árɔ̀ŋ.
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ Natániɛl átwɔ̀ ntá yi, arɛm ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, “Nɛ́, chi mbɔ̌ŋ mmǔ Israɛl tɛ́mɛ́ tɛ́mɛ́. Bapu apú nɛ yi wáwák.”
“Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásɔ́t mmɔ́ mbɔ anɛ sayri ɛ̌ti ya, ǎsɔt chi mɛ, nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásɔ̀t mɛ sayri, ǎsɔt chi mmu anɛ átó mɛ.” 
Ɛ́fákárí ɛnyu yɔ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp. Mandɛm aghátí nyaka Aisáya andɛm ɛ̌ti yi bɛ,
Mpok Sɛ́nas ntaŋá manyé nɛ Apólos báté bɛ́rɔ́ŋ nɛkɔ, kʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ́ghɔ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhɨkɨ chɛp bɔ́ ndǔ nɛkɔ ɛnap.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ Jɔ̌n Njwiti achá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak ndǔ abhɛn bágú nɛ abhɛn bachi nɛpɛ́m. Yɛ̌ nɔ́, yɛ̌ chí mmu anɛ apu yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ mpǎy bho abhɛn Mandɛm achi nɛ bhɔ mbɔ Mfɔ wap, acha yi.”
“Stífin arɔk ambɨ bɛ́rɛm bɛ Bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ́ babhɔ̌ŋ nyaka ɛ́tɛm amɛm baso ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔ́ŋ bɛ́ Mandɛm achí nɛ bhɔ. Moses aghókó nyaka yɔ ɛ́bhák mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm aghati yi, nɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm átɔ́ŋ yi amfay Njiɛ Sináy bɛ ɛbhɔŋ bɛbhak.
Yɛ̌ mmu kɛkway bɛkɛmɛ Yesu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɛ́bhɛ́ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi. Nɛ bɛ́bhó mpok ɛyɔ, yɛ̌ mmu kɛpɛrɛ mɔ bɛbhɛp yi yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn báchí amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ manyé chɔkɔ, batɛp Stífin amɨ́k amʉɛt, bághɔ́ bɛ́ bɛsí bhi bɛ́yibhiri bɛrɔbhɛ ghɔɔ chi mbɔ ɛbhɛ́n ángɛl Mandɛm.
Ɔku bhɔ bɛ mándɔp chi bo abhɛn ɔ́chí mfɔ wap, nɛ bo abhɛn báchiákap ntá Mandɛm mmu bɛsɛ sɛ́tòk. Nɛ chɔŋ bɔ́ mámbak bafɔ ntá bo fá amɨk.”
Mbák chí nkaysi Yesu Kristo Acha bɛ́ ntó Tímɔti awu ntá yɛká, chɔŋ ntó yi mandú mpok. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nchyɛ nkwɔ mɛ maŋák mpok yi áfú awu ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ntá ya, ághátí mɛ ɛnyǔ bǎchí awu.
- Ɛ́ghaka beku ndǔ Nywɔp Ntoŋtí, ɛnɛ́ bátɔ̀ŋti mmʉɛt bɛ́chwe ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt, Josɛ́f mmǔ Arimátia amɔt, afa nɛ nɛtaŋántɨ arɔk ntá Páílet bɛ ánchyɛ́ yi bɛtaŋ ámfɛrɛ Yesu amfay ɛkotákátí. Josɛ́f achi nyaka mmǔ ɛchɛm ɛgho ɛnɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk anɛ abhɔŋɔ kɛnókó bɛsí bho, nɛ ǎnoŋ nyaka mpok anɛ Mandɛm átwɔ̀ ambak Mfɔ ntá bo abhɛn bachi abhi.
Yesu aghati yí bɛ, “Nchí ghati wɔ bɛ, ɛchɔŋ, chɔŋ ɔ́mbak nɛ mɛ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt maŋák anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Párádis.”   
Yesu apɛt arɛm ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Mǔnkáp amɔt achi nyaka. Abhɔ́ŋ mǔbɛtɨk anɛ ákɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi mɛnkɛm. Bo bágháti yi bɛ, mmʉ̌ bɛtɨk ywí wu ǎchɔŋti nkáp ywi.
Kɛ ɛwak ɛmɔt, mmǔ anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Ananías nɛ ngɔrɛ́ aywi Safíra bátí nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́mɨk.
Ghɔ́ ká ɛnyǔ nnɛ́m mmu yi achi nyaka! Yɛ̌ndu Ábraham achi nyaka chi mbɨ anɛ bo Israɛl, akɔ́rɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áfú ɛbhɨ̌nɛnu nɛ bhɔ ndǔ baru byo, achyɛ yi ndu amɔt.
Bǎbhɔŋ nyaka ntínso nɛ bǒkɛnɔŋ. Nɛ mpok báfɔ̀ŋɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛka, bǎka nɛ maŋák bɛ mankʉ nɔ, ndǔ bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛcha ɛbhɔ, nɛ bɛ bɔ bɛ́bhak mpoknkɛm.
Bɛyǎ bɛcháy bɛkɛm bo mankɛm! Bábhák maknkay, babho bɛbɨti Mandɛm, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Sɛghɔ̌ baraká maknkay ɛchɔŋ!” 
mǎnkaka nɔkɔ Ɛta. Yí kɛ ákʉ́ mǎnkwáy bɛbhɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi atoŋti ntá bǒbhi abhʉɛrɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhi bɛ́ghɔ̀.
Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm. Achi Mandɛm Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ. Achi nkwɔ Ɛtayi. Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ yi anchyɛ bhe Ɛfóŋó yi mmu ákʉ̀ mǎndɨŋɨ Mandɛm mǎndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ.
Kɛ bo Israɛl abhɛn báchí arɛ́ mányɨ́kɨ́si batɨ bǒbatí ɛtɔk ɛyɔ nɛ manɛ́m baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn mánókó Mandɛm. Bákʉ bo báchyɛ Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas nɛnyok kpát bábók bhɔ báfá atú ɛtɔk ɛyap.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, bǎkɛ́ bhak maknkay ndǔ bɛrɛm bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ ntá yɛka. Bɛ́twɔ̀ chi mɛmɔ be mbák bǎsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm tɛtɛp. Bákɛ́ sɔt bhɔ mbɔ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bábhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ kɛ bɛ́fàkari nɛ bhe.
Ndu bárɔ̀ŋ, mmǔfú arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Chɔŋ mbak nkoŋo ywɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ ɔ̌rɔ̀ŋ.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́chí nɛ bhe tontó! Nti achi bɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yɛ̌ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛtaŋ Mandɛm.
Bě batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, nɛ be bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bǒ bɛtábhá! Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha. Bǎkway bɛkɔ mǎnkɨŋɨ bɔmanyu mǎndɔk mbaŋ nɛ mbaŋ mɛ́nú bɛyaŋ yɛ̌ chí mmu amɔt bɛ ámbák mǔnkwɔ ywɛka. Kɛ mpok yi ayibhiri arɔbhɛ mbɔ bhe, nkúbhɛ́ bé kɛ̌ bǎkʉ yi ámbɛ́p ancha be babhɔŋ ndɔŋ ɛpay, ambak mmǔ anɛ árɔ̀ŋ ndǔ nɛpǐngo.
Yesu abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɔ̌yáŋ mɛ̌nkʉ wɔ yi?” Akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛta, kʉ bɛ́ mpok ɔ́bhàk Mfɔ, bɔ̌bha abhɛn bati apay, manchɔkɔ nɛ wɔ, amɔt ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm, achák ɛbhe awɔ́ghɔ.”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm básɨŋ yɔ chí ndǔ bɛtɔŋ bɛsɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm bɛ sɛ́mbɔŋ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ nɛ bɛ mɛ́mfyɛ́   bhɛsɛ ntɨ. Ɛyɔ ɛnkʉ yɛ sɛ́mbaka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ bariɛp Mandɛm amfú tɛtɛp.
Achwe ndǔ mɔ́kɛt anɛ achi Nyáŋá Áchá ndɔŋ amɔt, ndak ámáy. Puyɛ̌ chi nɛ manoŋ mmɛ́n nɛ amɛn bɔ̌mpɔŋ kɛ̌ yí achwe arɛ́ nɛ mɔ. Manǒŋ mi yímbɔŋ kɛ̌ yí áchyɛ́, nɛ ndǔ ákʉ́ nɔ aku bhɛsɛ afɛrɛ ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́ mpoknkɛm.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, ɛpʉ́ítí ɛ́kwɛ́n nɛntɨ bakoŋo Jɔ̌n nɛ mmu Israɛl achak ɛ̌ti ɛnyǔ nɛso ɛnɛn nɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ambak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm.
Nchí nyaka nɛ bhe amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm nɛ́njí nɛnji ntɔŋ nɔkɔ, be kɛkɛ́m mɛ. Kɛ ɛchi ɛnyu ɛnɛ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp.”
Ɛjɔ̌ mmɛ́m amɛn ánɛn ɛchí nyaka arɛ téé. Básɔ́t ɛkuchá fofok bágwɔ́t antí ntábhɛ́nɔk ɛnɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ haysɔp, bátáp ndǔ mmɛm mɔ básá yi anyu.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Chi mmu amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ́ ywɛka batí byo nɛ apay. Yí nkwɔ ǎsɛ̀bhɛ awɔ amɛm nkúbhɛ́ ɛkpʉrɛ́ nɛnyiɛ ɛnɛ ɛ́mɔt nɛ mɛ.
bɛ Kristo ámbák amɛm batɨ yɛka mpoknkɛm ndǔ bǎsɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ yi, nɛ bɛ mǎmbak mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ bakaŋ ɛyi áchwè amɨk sayri nɛ mbɔ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ ɛ́té sɛnɛ́ ndǔ ɛkɔŋ Mandɛm.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak ɛnɛ sɛ́ghɔ̀ ɛ̌ti nchiakap wu chi bɛ Mandɛm anyu nyaka nku bɛ Yesu ǎbhák nchiakap. Yɛ̌ nchiakap achak apú, anɛ mányú nku ɛ̌ti yi.
nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ághɛp aghɛp, nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áchí nyǔmɛ́m, nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɛ̀m bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti bo báchák, nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áchi ngɛ́p ntántaŋ, mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ mankɛm bápú kway bɛbhak ndǔ nkwɔ bho abhɛn Mandɛm achi Mfɔ wap.
Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ yi achi chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm achi mmɔ́ Mandɛm.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ mmu anɛ árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, “Mɛ kɛ nchí Nkɛmɛ kɛ́mbé.” Apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ Acha ántáŋ bǒbhi.”
Sɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri chí bɛ́ Mandɛm anchyɛ bhe nɛpɔptǐntɨ́, ampɛmɛ bhe. Nɛ Mandɛm ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ́ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ chi bɛ sɛ́nkwáy bɛchyɛ bhe nɛpɔptǐntɨ́. Ɛnkʉ mǎnkwáy yɛ bɛbhɔŋ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ ndu bɛte kákátí ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn sɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ.
Mpok anɛ ɛpa ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbho ákwáy nɔ́kɔ́, ató mɔ̌bɛtok ywi bɛ andɔk angati bo abhɛn yi anaka bɛ, ‘Twɔ́ ká, mánaŋ batoŋti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.’
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá bǒ abhɛn mánù bɛ bo mámbák ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ batɨ; mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ bɔ mámbak bɔ̌bhi!
Bɔtayɛsɛ bátwɔ̀ nyaka fá ndǔ njiɛ nɛ mánchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm kɛnókó, kɛ be bǒ Judeya bǎrɛ̀m bɛ Yerúsalɛm kɛ áchi ɛbhak ɛnɛ bo bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó arɛ.”
Fɛ́liks arɨŋɨ nyaka sayri ɛ̌ti Mbi Yesu Acha. Ɛ́kʉ́ ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ Pɔ̌l arɛmɛ, ábhʉ́rɛ́ manyé, arɛm ntá bo Israɛl bɛ́ Lísias mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu ántwɔ́ chɔŋ mkpɔ́t nnyé ɛnɛká ɛnɛn.
Bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ yí, Fɛstɔs arɛm bɛ, “Mfɔ Agripa nɛ be mankɛm abhɛn báchí fá nɛ bhɛsɛ, ghɔ́ mmǔrɛ́. Bo Israɛl mankɛm abhɛn Yerúsalɛm nɛ abhɛn fá Seséria bátwɔ ntá ya mpoknkɛm, mámbɨk nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Apú mmu anɛ bárɔ̀ bɛ ámbák nɛpɛ́m.’
Yesu Kristo achyɛ́ nyaka mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bhɛsɛ ndǔ mkpáká mmɨk bɛbʉ́ anɛ ɛchɔŋ. Akʉ nɔ bɛ́kɔ́ŋɔ nkaysi Mandɛm mmu achi Ɛtayɛsɛ.
Nɛ mmu anɛ achi ɛbhɨ ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk, ákɛ́ rɔ́ŋ kpɨ́k bɛbuɔp ndɛ yi.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chí ɛnɛ ɛ́taŋ mmu anɛ ábyak mɛ, yi kɛnókó ɛyɔŋ ɛya. Chɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndɛ́mɛ́ mɛntaŋ yi ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn bátaŋ bo.
Yesu átɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ́ nɛkay ɛnɛn, arɔk ambɨ bɛ́kɔ bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm, yi abhak ambɨ, bo abhɛn báchi nɛ yi mankoŋo nɔkɔ ansɛm.
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mpok ɔ́chí ɛsakámu, ɔre gwɔ́t mmʉɛt, ɔ́ndɔk yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ ɔ́kɔ́ŋɔ́. Kɛ mpok ɔ́kɔ́kɔ́, chɔŋ ɔ́njoŋ ámɔ́ amfay, mmu achák amfyɛ wɔ́ ndɛn amʉɛt, ansɔt wɔ andɔk ɛbhak ɛnɛ ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ bɛrɔŋ.”
Yesu kɛ ákʉ́ mbɛ́ntí nɛ áfáté. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎghɔ́ nɛ ɛnɛ́ bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ ɛfakari, mɛnkɛm bɛ́chí ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́sɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ yi. Chí ndu sɛ́sɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ yí kɛ ɛ́kʉ mbɛ́ntí nɛ áfáté kpɛrɛp mbɔ ɛnyǔ bě mankɛm bǎghɔ́.
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ Ábraham abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɔ̌babhakanɛm bati apay. Amɔt abhak mmɔ̌ nsɛm, achak abhak mmɔ̌ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ápú nsɛm.
Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha mántɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, mánchyɛ bɛ kpák. 
Sɛ́chɔ̀ŋti nɛtaŋányu nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́té bɛchɛt bo mbi bɛ bákɛ́ rɨŋɨ baraka Mandɛm. Sɛ́kɛ̀m yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ nkaysi mbɔ mǔkɛnɔŋ anɛ bákɛ́mɛ́ ɛbhɨ̌nɛnu, nɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ yɔ ándɔ́bhɛ ghok chi Kristo.
Ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ mpok ɛyɔ, mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bárɔk bágháti Yesu bɛ, “Fǎ fá dɔk ɛbhak ɛ́chák. Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd ǎyàŋ bɛ́way wɔ!”
Mpok Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Ghɔ́ mɛ́ nɛ”, bárɔ́k nɛ nsɛm nɛ nsɛm bákwɛ́nti amɨk.
Mandɛm aku bhɛsɛ nɛ manoŋ Kristo afɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ kɛsɛm ndu ábhárɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛ Kristo. Nɛ afóŋórí bhɛsɛ ndǔ sɛ́pú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé. Akʉ nɔ bɛkoŋo ɛnyǔ yi átɔ́ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mbɔk bho báchi fá abhɛn bápú gu kpátɛ mángɔ ndǔ Mandɛm abhak nɛ bhɔ mbɔ Mfɔ wap.” 
Mpok Yesu aghaka kɛkwɔt nɛ Jɛríko, nnɛ́mámɨ́k amɔt abhak nɛpak mbi chɔ́kɔ́, anɨŋɨ nɔkɔ mɛnɨ́ŋɨ́.
Arɛm bɛ, “Ntaŋá-manyé amɔt achi nyaka ɛtɔkɔfú, Mandɛm yi kɛ chyɛ kɛnókó, ntɨ nkwǎ yi kɛbhɔŋ mpok nɛ yi.
Bápáy nɔkɔ yɔ, maníɛ́ amɛn áchi amɛm ɛ́fyɛ́ bo Antiɔk ntɨ, bábhɔŋ maŋák.
Bat yɛ ka mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ mpoknkɛm, bɛ́ mɛnkwɔ mbát mmʉɛt nɛ bhe. Mbák ntabhɛ́nɔk ápú babhát ndǔ ɛnɔk, ápú nyu kɛpɛm. Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ bhe. Mbák mmǔ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhat mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ, apú kwáy mɛ́nyú kɛpɛm.
Kɛ ndak yi ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fyɛ́ nkáp awa amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́nkap? Mbɔ ɔkʉ nɔ, mbʉ́ ndu ntwɔ́ nɛ́, mbɨ́kɨ́ sɔt wú nɛ nsáy?’
Dɔ́k yɛ́ ka ambɨ mǎnáŋá bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bábhó.
Sɔt ka mpok! Mbák mɔ́mayɛ ánkʉ wɔ bɛbʉ́, ghatí yi bɛ́ ándɔ́ ɛpɨŋ ɛyɔ. Mbák atɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi, foŋorí yi.
Nɛ mǎnáŋ mamkpáŋ mɛ amfay ndǔ ɛkotákátí, chɔŋ nja bǒ mankɛm bɛ mándɔ́ mmɨk mantwɔ ntá ya.”
Chɔŋ mmok anjibhiri ándɔp ɛjuri, ntaŋ ánjibhiri andɔp manoŋ, kɛ nywɔp nɛgho ɛnɛ́n Acha átwɔ̀ nɛngaka.
nɔ chi, bɛ́fɛ́rɛ bhɛsɛ amɔ bǒmpap abhɛsɛ, ankwak bhɛsɛ bɛ́ sɛ́ntók nɔkɔ chi yi, kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy,
Mbɔ̌ŋ nyaka nkaysi bɛ́te awu ntá yɛka kɛ mfʉɛt ndɔk atú Masidónia, mpɛ́t ntě bɛ́ghɔ bhe mpok mfú atú Masidónia nchí pɛtnsɛm, bɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ mǎmbɔŋ mbi bɛ́chyɛ mɛ nɛkwak ndǔ nɛkɔ ɛnɛn mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ Judɛ́ya.
Chɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fàkari ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɔ mɛ́njɨŋɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu fá amɨk.
Tɛtɛp, mbɔ̌ŋ maŋák bɛ nsɨŋ be ɛkáti kɛ puyɛ̌ chí ɛ̌ti yɔ́ ɛ́chyɛ́ bhe basɛ́mɛ́. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ́ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ maŋák chi bɛ basɛ́mɛ́ amɛn ɛkáti ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ́ bhe akʉ bǎtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka. Bɛběntɨ ɛbhɛká bɛchi ɛnyǔ bɛběntɨ ɛbhɛ́n Mandɛm áyàŋ bǒbhi mámbɔ́ŋ. Ɛ́kʉ bɛ ɛkáti ɛyɔ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ twɔ nɛ mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ ntá yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka.
Mbák mmu mbɔ yi ǎkwáy nyaka bɛ́kwak mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ wu, Mandɛm kɛ apu kway bɛkwak bo abhɛn yi áyábhɛ́ mbák bádì kɛbhɔ ntá yi bɛ̌ti nɛ ngósí? Ǎkway bɛ́chɔ́ŋti mpok kɛ ankwak bhɔ?
Nɛ arɛm bɛ, “Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɔ̌ŋ bɛghɔ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri. Bǒ-batí ɛtɔk, nɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm, nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm bábyak chɔŋ mɛ nɛ mángwáy mɛ, kɛ ɛ́ghaka nɔkɔ manywɔp arat, mpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.” 
Píta afú yɛ nɛ nkoŋo anɛfú wu, báfá, báré rɔ́ŋ ndǔ nnɛm.
Nchwi áchák akwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk ndɨ́ndɨ́, achak, agó, achyɛ bɛyǎ nchwi. Nchwi ayá acha anɛ bápɨ́ ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛtay, achák ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛrat, anɛfu ndɔŋ ɛsa nsɛm byo.”
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tɔŋ bɛ bɛsɛ babhɔŋ sɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ sɛ́kway bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn. Mandɛm kɛ ákʉ́ sɛ́nkwáy bɛku bhɔ.
Afɛ́rɛ́ bhɛsɛ ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn ɛjuri, akʉ bɛ Mɔ́ywi mmu yi ákɔ́ŋɔ́ tontó ámbák wu Mfɔ ywɛsɛ.
Chɔŋ mbɔŋ bɛyǎ maŋák bɛchyɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́, yɛ̌ chi mmʉɛt ɛya, ndu bɛkwak bhe. Ndǔ ɛkɔŋ ɛya nɛ bhe ɛ́gò ɛ́ndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, ɛyɛka nɛ mɛ ɛ́may nɔkɔ may kɛ?
Yesu ághókó nɔkɔ nɔ, abhak maknkay tontó. Ayibhiri mmʉɛt, arɛm ntá bǒ abhɛn bákòŋo yi bɛ, “Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ yɛ̌ mmu Israɛl amɔt anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ mɛ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́.
Mmu anɛ arɛmɛ bɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛ ndǔ áyàŋ bɛ ámpɛ́mɛ́ mmʉɛt yi, apú bhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn tɛtɛp. Kɛ mmu anɛ áká bɛ́gu ɛ̌ti ya, ǎbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn tɛtɛp.” 
Ntí achí bɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ngɔrɛ́ anɛ achi nkoŋo Kristo nɛkwáy bɛkʉ nnɛ́m ambak mmǔ Mandɛm. Nɛ nɛpɛ́m nnɛ́m anɛ achí nkoŋo Kristo nɛkwáy bɛkʉ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ambak mmǔ Mandɛm. Mbɔ ɛ́pú nɔ́, mbʉ́ bɔ̌ bhɛka bápú kwáy bɛbhak bo Mandɛm. Kɛ ndǔ ɛ́chí nɔ́, Mandɛm ǎsɔ̀t bɔ̌bhap mambak bǒbhi.
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎkʉ̀, nɛ ɛnɛ́ bǎrɛ̀m, mǎnkʉ yɔ ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu Acha, mǎmfʉɛt ntá yi mǎnchyɛ nɔkɔ bakak ntá Ɛta Mandɛm. 
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bǎchí bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham. Yɛ̌ nɔ́, bǎyaŋ mbi bɛway mɛ mbɔnyunɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛya ɛ́pú chwe amɛm batɨ yɛka.
Arɔ yɛ, are kɔ andɔkɔ nɔkɔ ndǔ bɛtɔk ɛbhɛn bɛchi atú Judɛ́ya angati nɔkɔ bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Israɛl
Moses achyɛ́ nyaka bhe bɛbhé, pú nɔ́? Yɛ̌ nɔ́, yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka apú bhʉrɛ́ bhɔ. Ndaká yí bǎyáŋ bɛway mɛ?”
Kɛ mpok anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp ákwáy nɔ́kɔ́, ató Mɔ́ywi bɛ antwɔ fá amɨk. Ngɔrɛ́ abhé yi, nɛ abhak antɛnɛ́ bɛbhé bo Israɛl.
Bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ bɛbhé ɛbhɔ, mmu ǎkway bɛkaysi bɛ bɛ́chyɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak mbɔnyunɛ bo abhɛn báfyɛ̀ bhɔ bátè kpɨrí bɛ mmu abhɔŋ bɛfyɛ mmʉɛt ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ Mandɛm ɛbhɔ, nɛ bárɛ̀m bɛ mmu abhɔŋ bɛsɛpti mmʉɛt amɨk, nɛ bɛ mmu abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri. Bɛbhe ɛbhɛn bɛchi chi ndɛ́ndɛm. Bɛ́pú kway bɛkwak mmu ambɔŋ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkɛm mmʉɛt bɛ ákɛ́ koŋo bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmʉɛt ɛyi áyàŋ yi ankʉ.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, Sɔ̌l are tɔ́ŋ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu andɔk nɔkɔ chí ambɨ. Are fʉɛ́t ndu bɛyǎ babhi bɛtɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ́ Yesu kɛ áchí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò ɛnyunɛ́ bo Israɛl abhɛn báchí Damáskɔs bábhɨkɨ kwáy bɛkɛm kɛfe nɛ yí.
Sɛ́ghàti bho ɛ̌ti mmǔ anɛ sɛ́ghɔ́, nɛ sɛ́ghók mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ́ŋɔ́, bɛ́ be nkwɔ mǎmbɔŋ nɛchɛmɛ́mʉɛt nɛ bhɛsɛ. Nɛ, sayri sayri, nɛchɛmɛ́mʉɛt ɛnɛsɛ ɛnɔ nɛchi nɛ Ɛta nɛ Mɔ́ywi Yesu Kristo.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, bǎkɛ́ bhak bɛchɨŋtǐ bho. Nu ka bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Acha áyàŋ mǎnkʉ.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ́ Mmɔ Mandɛm atwɔ anɛ́nɛ́ batɨ ayɛsɛ amɛm bɛ sɛ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ Mandɛm mmu achi tɛtɛp. Nɛ́nɛ, sɛbharɛ mmʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm mbɔ ɛnyǔ sɛ́bhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Mɔ́ywi Yesu Kristo. Yí aywǐntí kɛ̌ áchí Mandɛm tɛtɛp nɛ yí kɛ̌ áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Yesu árɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi, bárɔk téé ndǔ ɛkɛt Símun nɛ Andru. Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n bábhak nɛ bhɔ́.
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛyǎ bo ndǔ bátwɔ́ bákábhɛ́ yi, aghati baghɔk abhi bɛ, “Sɛ́mpé ɛbhě manyu ɛ́nɛ awu.”
Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhɨkɨ re twɔ nyaka ntá yɛ̌ mmu wap. Yɛ̌ nɔ, manaŋ bajwiti nyaka bhɔ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Acha.
Yesu arɨŋɨ bapu map, arɛm ntá yap bɛ,
Jɔ̌n ǎghati nyaka Hɛ́rɔd bɛ, “Ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ bo Israɛl ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ ɔ́nsɔt ngɔrɛ́ mɔ́mayɛ ɔmbay.”
Yesu apɛt arɛm ntá mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ wu bɛ, “Dɔ́k sayri, nɛka ɛnɛ̌ nɛ mɛ nɛ́kʉ ɔtaŋ.”
Mbák mmǔ ywɛka achí ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri, ánɨ́k nɔ́kɔ́ mmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ánkwák yí. Mbák mmu achí sayri, ákɛ́ rɔ bɛ́chyɛ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm.
Sɛ́kɛ chyɛ bhɔ mbi yɛ mandú. Sɛ́kɛ yáŋ bɛ bɔ manchɔŋti tɛtɛp anɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, tɛ̌ndu bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ mɛnoko yɔ.
Mǔngo bachiǎkap ywɛsɛ chi mmu anɛ ághɔ̀ bhɛsɛ ntínso ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bè bhɛsɛ mmʉɛt mbɔnyunɛ yímbɔŋ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka mamɔ mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu, Yɛ̌ nɔ, akɛ kʉ bɛbʉ́.
Mpok nɛ mpok, báchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ bɛsɔŋɔri mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu, kɛ bɛsɔŋɔri bhɔ bɛpu bɔkɔti bɛtě ntɔp ɛbhɛn bhɛsɛ sɛchi. Ɛcha bhɛsɛ́ ɛnyǔ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kʉ kɛ sɛpu fɛrɛ amɔ́.
Ábraham achɔ́kɔ́ nyáká ndu bɛ́tɛ́m mbɔnyunɛ abháká nyaka ntɨ ndǔ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ɛ́bhak mpoknkɛm ɛnɛ Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nkaysi ɛnyu ɛbhɔŋɔ bɛbhak, yímbɔŋ ate yɔ.
Ɛ́kʉ bárɛ́m ntá ngɔrɛ́ wu bɛ, “Ɛpɛ́t ɛpu bɛ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́ kɛ sɛ́nókó. Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛ́ghok nɛ batú bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú yi anyu, nɛ sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ nɛ́ chí Mpɛmɛ bǒ mmɨk tɛtɛp.” 
Bákway mbʉ bɛ́ti mɔ anchyɛ nkáp anɛ́ áyá ɛ́chá nkáp anɛ nkʉbɛtɨk ányiɛ ndǔ mmiɛ, mánsɔt nkáp wu mánchyɛ ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́ bho.” Bǒbhɔ bábho bɛji mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ wu.
“Mamʉrɛ bha, nchí ghati bhe bɛ, bǎkɛ́ cháy bǒ mmɨk. Bǎkway bɛway chi mmʉɛt nkwǎ kɛ bápu kway bɛku ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak ɛnɛ ɛbɛbhɛ ɛcha ɛyɔ.
Yí Moses kɛ achi nyaka nɛ́ntɨ́ bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ́ nɛ ángɛl Mandɛm amɛm baso. Mpok yɔ, ángɛl Mandɛm árɛ́m kɛpɨ ntá yi ndu Njiɛ Sináy, akʉ yi arɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ yí ankʉ sɛndɨŋɨ, nɔ́ chí Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp mpoknkɛm.
Mbɔ ɛnyu ɛfakari nɛ mbwɔ́t anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mmɨk ndɨ́ndɨ́, nɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ bo abhɛn bághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm mánkɛ́m nɛ ntɨ nɛ́mɔ́t mankʉ nɔkɔ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́yàŋ, mándɔk nɔkɔ ámbɨ bɛkʉ ɛnyu ɛyɔ nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́.” 
Bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, barɛm ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn ángɛl Mandɛm aghati bhɔ ɛ̌ti mɔ́wu.
Ghók ká, nchí ghati bhe ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chí bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ntá yɛka. Bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́pú gu chɔŋ, kɛ báyibhiri mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chi tɛtɛp nɛ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ákwày mɛ́noko nɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛnkɛm. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́rɛ chi bɛ Mandɛm ákʉ bo mándɨŋɨ bɛ Yesu Kristo atwɔ nyaka fá amɨk ndu bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bǒ bɛbʉ́. Nɛ mɛ nchí mmu anɛ ɛbhá bɛbʉ́ bɛ́yá bɛ́chá ɛbhɛn yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak.
Bɔtayɛsɛ mányùrɛ nyaka bhɛsɛ ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɔ́ bághɔ́ bɛ ɛ́rɨ ntá yɛsɛ. Mbák chi Mandɛm, nɛnyurɛ anɛ yi ányùrɛ bɛsɛ achi ndu bɛkʉ bhɛsɛ bɛrɨ mbɔnyunɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kwak bhɛsɛ sɛmbak nyáŋá mbɔ yímbɔŋ.
Nɛ bǎkɛ́ koŋo bɔmandɛm nsé mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔk ɛyap bákʉ̀ nyaka, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Bo báchɔ́kɔ ndǔ ɛpa mányiɛ, mányú, báfáte bábhɛn bɛpɔ̌ babhɛn ɛ́púsí.”
Arɛ́, aghók mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛghati bho ɛnyǔ bɔ bɛchi, nɛ mmu apú kway mbɔŋ bɛrɛm ɛnyǔ bɛchi.
Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Mɛ kɛ nchí mbi, mɛ kɛ nchí tɛtɛp, mɛ kɛ nchí nɛpɛ́m. Yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛ́twɔ ntá Ɛta ɛnɛ́ ábhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt ntá ya.
Barak anɛ áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu are kɔ mbǎŋ nɛ mbaŋ, atú Gálili. Yi kɛyáŋ bɛkɔ atú Judɛ́ya mbɔnyunɛ bo Judeya báyàŋ nyaka mbi bɛ́way yi.
Mandɛm akósí yí amfay, afyɛ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt kɛnókó bɛ ambak Mǔntí nɛ Mpɛmɛ, bɛ́ ánchyɛ́ bo Israɛl mbi bɛtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap Mandɛm amfoŋori bhɔ.
Bápɛ́rɛ yiŋɨ́, mmu ɛbhaŋákwa amɔt atwɔ akwɛn yí bɛkak abho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Acha, mbák ɔkɔŋ, ɔ̌kway bɛkʉ mɛ ntaŋ.”
‘Yɛ̌ chí mfok ɛtɔk ɛyɛka anɛ ábátí ndǔ bɛkak ɛbhɛsɛ sɛ́kwɛ̀t sɛ́fɛ̀rɛ mbɔ ntísiɛ ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎkʉ́. Kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ka bɛ, mpok anɛ Mandɛm abhak nɛ bo mbɔ Mfɔ wap arɔp chi kɛkwɔt.’”
“Ɛyak nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí bɛyɔŋ kɛ bɛ́fù bɔ anyu mpoknkɛm.”
Bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ ákɔrɛ ápɛt ákwɛ́n nɛntɨ bo Israɛl.
yɛ̌ndu bɔ bábhʉɛt nyaka amɛm mɛniɛ, kɛkʉ yɛ̌ bɛbʉ́ nɛ yɛ̌ bɛrɨ, ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ Mandɛm ǎyàp mmu chi bɛkoŋo nkaysi anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́. Mandɛm apu yap mmu bɛkoŋo bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi. Ǎyap mmu chi bɛkoŋo nɛbhɨŋɨ anɛ yí ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ yi.
Ndu bɛrɔŋ ambɨ, chɔŋ bɔ́ mánɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yɛka. Bábhɔŋ ɛkɔŋ bɛghɔ bhe mbɔnyunɛ bághɔ bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm amʉɛt yɛka.
Kɛ ángɛl wu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Sakaría, ɔ́kɛ́ cháy! Mandɛm aghok nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnɛ. Nɛ chɔŋ ngɔrɛ́ ywɛ Ɛlísabɛt ampɔkɔ mɛniɛ ambé wɔ mɔ́mbakanɛm, nɛ ɔbhɔŋ bɛ́du yi nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Jɔ̌n.
Yesu aghati bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká.” Bɛ́fú bǒbhɔ amʉɛt, bɛrɔk, bɛchwe ndǔ nkwɔ bakók. Bakók ankɛm bárókóri básɛp ndǔ nkoko-njiɛ dúgúdúgúdúgú bágúrɛ anyɛ́n.
Puyɛ̌ bɛsyɛp mmu kɛ ákʉ̀ yi ambak mbɔ̌ŋ mmu Israɛl tɛ́mɛ́ tɛ́mɛ́, nɛ nsyɛ́p anɛ tɛtɛp puyɛ̌ anɛ nkwɔmʉɛt.
Nchí yaŋ nɛ chí bɛ bo mankak mɛ kɛ? Wáwák! Mandɛm kɛ̌ mɛ̌yaŋ ánkák mɛ. Nchí yaŋ chí bɛ́ bo mambɔŋ maŋák nɛ mɛ kɛ? Mbɔ mbʉɛ́t chí mmu anɛ nchí yaŋ bɛ bo mambɔŋ maŋák nɛ mɛ, mbʉ mpú mmɔ̌bɛtok Kristo. 
Bǎkʉ̀ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bǎbháká ntɨ ndǔ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ábhʉ́rɛ́ amfay ntá yɛka. Mpok bǎghókó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ kɛ bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, nɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ achi tɛtɛp.
Básɨŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ákʉ́ kɛ bágò yí ndǔ ɛkotákátí, ndǔ ɛbhɔ́k ɛnɔk. Bágó ɛbhɔ́k ɛnɔk ɛyɔ ndǔ ɛko amfay ntí aywi. Ɛnyɨŋ básɨ́ŋ arɛ́ ɛ́bhák bɛ, “Nɛ́ chí Yesu, Mfɔ bo Israɛl.”
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ nɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ bo abhɛn bápú bhɔ́ŋ ntínso nɛ batɨ, Mandɛm ǎtáŋ bhɔ ɛwak manyé kɛbhɔ́ŋ ntínso. Kɛ mmu anɛ ábhɔ̀ŋ ntínso nɛ batɨ, Mandɛm ǎtɔ́ŋ yí ntínso ɛwak manyé. 
‘Mɛ nchí Mandɛm Ábraham, Mandɛm Áisek, nɛ Mandɛm Jekɔ́p!’ Mandɛm achí Mandɛm bo abhɛn bachi nɛpɛ́m. Apú Mandɛm bawú.”
Mpok bɛkɔk kɛpɛm ɛ́nɔk ákwáy nɔ́kɔ́, mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ ató bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhi bachak bɛ mándɔ́k mánsɔ́t aywi ákɔ́rɛ́ mbwɔt. Kɛ bǒ bɛtɨk bhɔ kɛchyɛ. Bákɛ́m yi badɛn, bábók, apɛtnsɛm amɔ́ amɔ.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, Yesu nɛ baghɔk abhi báré kɔ mámfʉɛt nɔkɔ amɛm nkɨ̌ nchwifú ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl. Nsay are nu baghɔk abhi. Ɛ́kʉ bábho bɛ́kʉɛp ɛnyǔ nchwi yɔ, mányiɛ nɔkɔ.
Nkaysi bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́, ánáŋ yɛ ángó, ánjwi mmu antɨ, ǎtó yí ndǔ bɛbʉ́, nɛ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɔ mɛ́náŋ mɛ́njwí ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni, nɔ́ nɛwú nɛ́twɔ.
Sɛ́naŋ sɛ́chɔ́ŋti nyaka bɛyǎ mpok nɛ bɛkɔ ndu achwǐnyɛ́n ɛrɔp chi ndak anɛ́ nɛpɛ́m nɛ nɛwú mbɔnyunɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛfoŋorǐ Bɛbʉ́ ɛnaŋ ɛfʉɛt nyaka nɛ mpok babhʉɛ́p ataŋataŋ akwáy. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, Pɔ̌l achyɛ bhɔ maniɛ bɛ,
Bɛyǎ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bághɔ́, bɛ́kʉ bábhɔŋ mamɔ tontó. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bábhɔŋ bɛyǎ maŋák. Ɛ́kʉ bábhɔŋ bɛyǎ ɛkɔŋ bɛ́chyɛ akap kɛyɨŋɨ nsɛm ndu bɛ́kwak bo, yɛ̌ndu báchí ndǔ bɛyǎ kɛchɛ́p.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ághókó bɛ́tòŋ mbɔ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ághòk bɛbe mpok ánòŋsi.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ mpú pɛrɛ nyu mɛ̌mɛn, kpátɛ ɛwak ɛnɛ mɛ̌nyú mmɛ̌m bakɔ amɛm Kɛfɔ Mandɛm.”
Yɛ̌ndu yi ákʉ́ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay bɛsí ɛbhap, bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko yí.
Nɛfú Yesu áfú anyɛ́n, aghɔ́ ndǔ nɛbu nɛ́nɛ́nɛ́, nɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm asɔt mkpá ɛbhóŋó asɛp yi amʉɛt.
“Mɛ, nchí mmu Israɛl. Nchí mmɔ́ Tásɔs atú Silísha, kɛ ngo chí fá Yerúsalɛm amɔ ntɔŋ ngo ywɛsɛ, Gamáliɛl. Ngɔk ɛkáti chi antɛn ɛyi. Atɔ́ŋ mɛ bɛkoŋo bɛbhé bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhak nɛ nchyɛ́ mmʉɛt bɛkoŋo Mandɛm mbɔ be mankɛm abhɛn bǎchí fá ɛchɔŋ.
Aghɔ́ ndǔ Yesu áfʉɛ̀t, arɛm bɛ, “Ghɔ́ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n Mandɛm!”
Babhabhɛrǐ nnɛm básɔ́t yɛ nkáp bɛsɔŋ wu, bárɔk bákʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǒbati bághátí bhɔ. Nɛ mbok yɔ bɛ́ bakoŋo Yesu bághɛp yi ghɛp kɛ̌ bo Israɛl bábhʉɛ́t bɛghati bo kpatɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ. 
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bákɛ́mɛ́ bhe ndu bɛtaŋ be, bǎkɛ́ sɛmɛ ambɨ ambɨ bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm bɛ yi?’ Mpok ánkwáy, dɛm ka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fú be anyu mbɔnyunɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ kɛ ághàti chɔŋ be ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm.
Mbokó manyiɛp anɛ Jekɔ́p ábhák arɛ. Yesu ágháká nɔkɔ arɛ́, ndǔ yi ánáŋ ápɔ́bhɛ́, achɔkɔ nɛpaká mbokó manyiɛp wu. Nywɔp nɛ́bhák mbɔ nkárɛ́nká byo nɛ ɛpay.
Pú Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛghɔ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm kɛ anchwe ndǔ kɛfɔ ɛki?”
Sɛ́kɛ́ pɛrɛ ji yɛ batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ, kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛrɨ chi bɛ bǎkɛ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛkway bɛkʉ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ ankwɛn ndǔ bɛbʉ́.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, Hɛródias afyɛ́ Jɔ̌n antɨ, nɛ are yaŋ bɛrɛm mángwáy yi, kɛ yi kɛbhɔŋ mbi.
Nɛ nɛ́nɛ, chɔŋ Mandɛm amfɛrɛ ntí ndǔ ɛkɛt ɛyɛka, ɛ́ndɔp ɛnyu ɛyɔ. Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, bǎpú pɛrɛ ghɔ́ chɔŋ mɛ́, kpátɛ mpok anɛ bǎrɛ̀m chɔŋ bɛ ‘Sɛ́mbɨ́tí mmu anɛ átwɔ̀ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Mandɛm Acha.’”
Nɛ bɔ́ bhɛrɛ kɛ mányìɛ mɛnyɨŋ mánkwɛ́sɛ́ nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛkɛt ɛbhap ndǔ mangwɔ, mánkʉ nɔkɔ bɛrɔ́rí nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bapu bɛsí bho. Chɔŋ ntɛ́msi yap anjá ancha!” 
Dɔ̌ ká nkaysi bɛyǎ mpap, nɛ bɛběntɨ, nɛ ɛchoko-ntɨ, nɛ bɛ́táŋá, nɛ bɛchɔŋti manyɛ́n batɨ, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkaysi bɛkʉ batɨ bɛbʉ́.
Mmǔ ntí bo Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛbhak mmu anɛ ásɔ̀t mankɔ sayri, mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ maŋák bɛkʉ bɛrɨ, mmǔ anɛ ákɛ̀m mmʉɛt sayri, mmǔ anɛ áchí chak bɛsí Mandɛm bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛ bo báchák. Abhɔŋ bɛbhak nyáŋá, nɛ mmǔ ntɨ ɛnɛn nɛpu to yi ankʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́twɔ̀ yi nɛ áyɔ́mɛ.
Báfú amɛm manɛm ayap, nɛ Yesu ápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, bo Mandɛm bhɔ bárɔ́k Yerúsalɛm. Bɛyǎ bho bághɔ́ bhɔ.
Nɔ chi bɛ amɛm ntɨ mmu kɛ̌ nkaysi mbʉ́mbʉ áfù, antó mmu ndǔ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bɛway mmu, bɛkwɛn bɛrwɔp, kɛbhʉ́rɛ́ ɛkɛn bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhay batɨ, nɛ aghɛ́p, nɛ bɛ́té ntísiɛ ákwárɛ́, nɛ bɛ́rɛ́m bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti mmu ndǔ bɛchɔŋti nnyɛ́n ɛni.
Yesu abhɨŋɨ bɔ́ mankɛm arɛm bɛ, “Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ, ntá bǒ mmɨk, bo abhɛn básɔt bɛ báchí bafɔ, bábhɔŋ bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ amfay bǒbhap, nɛ bǒbati básɔ̀t bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ bǒbhap mangok bhɔ.
Nɛ chɔŋ bǒ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm mámbaka ntɨ chi nɛ yi bɛ ampɛmɛ bhɔ.” 
Ɛ̌tiyɔ kɛ̌ Kristo ágú, ápɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m bɛ ambak Acha ntá bo abhɛn báchí nɛpɛ́m nɛ abhɛn bágú.
Kwak bɔ mámbak mbɔ bo abhɛn babhɔŋɔ kɛboŋ nɛ bákɛ̀mʉɛt bɛ bákɛ́ fu nɛfí. Bǎbhɔŋ bɛtɔŋ bhɔ bɛ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyu bákɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhap mántɔŋ ɛrɨ́tí ɛpɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn bachi arɛ, nɛ bɛ mámbɔ́ŋ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt nɛ manɛ́m abhap. Mámbák ɛnyu yɔ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ kwáy bɛrɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, nchí sɨŋ be ɛ̌ti ɛbhé ɛkɔ ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m Yesu nɛ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka, mbɔnyunɛ ɛjuri ɛ́fʉɛ̀t, nɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɛn tɛtɛp mɛ́náŋ bɛ́ghɔ̀.
Bǎrɨŋɨ ndǔ ntwɔ́ ntɔ́ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ntá bɛká bho nɛ nkɔ nɔkɔ bɛkɛt nɛ bɛkɛt nkɛ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kwáy bɛkwak bhe.
Mmu wap amɔt ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ ataŋ, abho bɛpɛtnsɛm ntá Yesu ambɨti nɔkɔ Mandɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay.
ambo bɛdɛn batɨ̌ bɔ̌-bɛtok, anchɛm ɛkakánɛkɔ nɛ manyǔ mmɛ́m, ambo mɛnyiɛ, anyu nɔkɔ nɛ bhɔ,
Bǒ bhɔ nɔ́ batwɔ bɛghɔ Yesu bagurɛ nɔkɔ, ángɛl Mandɛm abhesi ntá Josɛ́f ndǔ kɛnɔ́ ɛkɛ́n yi aghɔ aghati yi bɛ, “Josɛ́f, Hɛ́rɔd ǎyàŋ mbi bɛway mɔ́nɛ. Faté yɛ́, sɔt mmɔ́ nɛ máyi, bʉɛ́ dɔ́k ɛtɔk Íjip. Dɔ́k, ɔ́mbák árɛ́ kpátɛ ngati wɔ ɔ́mpɛ́tnsɛm.”
Báfú nɔ́kɔ́ anyɛ́n, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ afɛrɛ Fílip arɛ́, mǔngo Ɛtǒpia wu kɛpɛrɛ ghɔ́ yi. Yɛ̌ nɔ, arɔk ambɨ nɛ nɛkɔ ɛni nɛ maŋák.
Mpok Mandɛm ákú bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, bo bábhak mbɔ bɔángɛl awu amfay. Bápú pɛrɛ bhay nɛbhay.
Mbɛ́ntí wu aghɔ nɔkɔ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n ndǔ báyaŋ bɛfʉɛt mandɔk ɛkɛrákap, abho mɛ́nɨŋɨ bhɔ nkáp.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ kɛ ɛ́kʉ́ Mandɛm áyɨ́kɨ́ nyaka ndu bɛ́tɔŋ bo abhɛn bariɛp ami achi ntá yap kpoŋoroŋ bɛ bɔ́ báká ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi atɨ bɛkʉ.
Bárɔ́ yɛ bárɔ́k, mángati nɔkɔ bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm bɛ bɔ́ mántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu apɛt atɔ́ŋ mmʉɛt ntá bakoŋo bhi. Ndɔŋ yɔ, ɛbhák chi nɛpaka Manyu Tibérias.   Sɛ́ngɔ́ ɛnyǔ yi atɔŋ nyaka mmʉɛt ntá yap.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛsɔŋɔri nɛ kɛchɛp ɛkɛka. Kɛ ndǔ baraká Mandɛm bǎbhɔŋ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒ bárɛ̀m ɛ̌ti yɛka. Bɔ́bhɔ chí bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ báchi bo Israɛl ɛnɛ bápú. Báchí chi nkwɔ Satan.
Ná bǎkway mɛnoko ɛnɛ́ báyàŋ chi bakak amɛn bǎchyɛ̀ batɨ, kɛfyɛ́ ntí ndǔ bakak amɛm Mandɛm áchyɛ.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ánú bɛrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ Acha bɛyǎ maŋák.
bɛ́pókómʉɛt ɛbhɛn bɛ́pú chyɛ mmu ntíánwɔ́p. Kɛ Mandɛm aghókó mmʉɛt yɛsɛ́ ɛnyu ɛnɛ sɛ́chyɛ̀ bɛ́pókómʉɛt ɛbhɛ́n bo bábhɔ̀ŋ ntíánwɔ́p nɛ bhɔ kɛnókó ɛ́ncha bɛ́pókómʉɛt bɛ́chák.
Yesu akók arɛm bɛ, Eé Yerúsalɛm, bǒ Yerusalɛm! Bě bo bǎwày barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm, mǎntɛmti nɔkɔ nɛ batay ndu bɛ́wáy bo Mandɛm átó bɛ mángátí bhe Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi. Ndǔ bɛyǎ mpok, njáŋ bɛsɔt be mfyɛ́ amʉɛt bɛ́ mǎmbak nɛ mɛ mbɔ bɔ̌nkɔk abhɛn nnɔ nkɔk ákútí nɛbhʉɛt amɔt nɛ bɛbhap ɛbhi, kɛ bǎpú ka bɛ nkʉ nɔ!
Bo báchák mankɛm abhɛn bágú kɛpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m mpok ɛyɔ. Mamiɛ nkǎ amɔt abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛfʉɛt kpɨk. Nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn bo Mandɛm nɛ́bhak yɛ nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn mbɨ.
mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm, akʉ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ntá ya. Nɛ yí achí nyáŋá.
Mpok Yesu achi aywǐnti, mbɔk bho nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ apay bábhak arɛ́, bábhɛ́p yi ntí bakay anɛ yi átɛ́mɛ́.
Ngufú mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ, kɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nchí rɛm, nɛ sɛ́naŋ sɛ́kʉ be mǎndɨŋɨ nɔ́ kpoŋoroŋ ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ, nɛ ndǔ bɛyǎ babhi.
Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchi nɛ bhe ɛnɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ. Bě bǎrɔ̀ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Jɛ́sɛbɛl ambak nɛntɨ ɛnɛká. Yí ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ mmʉɛt ɛyi bɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ ǎtɔ̀ŋ andwɔ nɔkɔ bǒ bɛtok abha bɛ mánkʉ nɔkɔ barak ɛ́pusi nɛ bɛ mányiɛ nɔkɔ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛ́n báyɛ́rɛ́ báchyɛ mbɔ akap ntá mandɛm nsé.
Yímbɔŋ arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Bápú chyɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ kɛnókó amɛm ɛtɔk ɛyi.”
Nɛ bǎrɛ̀m bɛ mbák mmu ámfyɛ́ bariɛp nɛ Mandɛm bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ, anjɨkɨ ambɨŋɨ nnyɛ́n ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap Mandɛm bɛtɔŋ bɛ abhɔŋ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ kɛ yi kɛkʉ yɔ, yɛ̌ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́pú bhak. Bǎrɛm nkwɔ́ bɛ Mbák mmu ánjɨ́kɨ́ ndǔ nnyɛ́n mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bábhʉ́rɛ́ ndǔ ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ bɛchyɛ akap ntá Mandɛm, abhɔŋ bɛ́bhʉrɛ bariɛp ami.
Nɛ mbák akʉ wɔ bɛbʉ́ ndɔŋ tándrámɔt ndǔ ɛwak nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ndɔŋ antwɔ́, anɨk wɔ mmʉɛt bɛ, ‘Ɛta foŋorí mɛ́,’ ɔbhɔŋ bɛ́fóŋóri yi.” 
Mbok Dɔ́kas ataka ɛtɔk Jopa ɛnkɛm. Bɛyǎ bo mánóko, básɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Yesu Acha.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, yɛ̌ agha anɛ ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ Acha, ansɔt nkɔ́p ayi anyu ɛnɛ́ ápú chyɛ yí kɛnókó, ɛnyǔ mmu wu ǎkʉ̀ bɛbʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ yí ásɔ̀t mmʉɛt Acha nɛ manoŋ ami mbɔ ɛráká ndak.
Asɔt anyiɛ́ bɛsí bhap.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, Símun nɛ mamʉɛrɛ bhi báfú báré yaŋ yi.
Kɛ bɔ́ kɛbhɔŋ yɛ̌ mmɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ Ɛlísabɛt achí nyaka nkongɔrɛ́, nɛ bɔ́ bati apay mánáŋ nyaka bákɔk.
Nkúbhɛ́ mpok yɔ, ɛkát ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛ́ghárɛ bɛbhɔk bɛpay bɛfu amfay bɛghaka amɨk.
Tɛ̌ndu bǎchi bɔ̌ Mandɛm nɛ yi akɔŋ be tontó, ŋɔkɔ́ yɛka ɛpɨŋ ɛyi.
Agha ákway bɛbhɔŋ bɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́ kɛ ɛ́kɛbhak ntá ya mbɔ bɛ mɛ kɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛbhɔ? Agha bákway bɛkʉ yi ankwɛn ndu bɛbʉ́ kɛ ntɨ̌ kɛdu mɛ amɛm nɛ bɛběntɨ?
Bě bǒ bakáp, tá ká batú mǎngók mǎncháp ɛ̌rí kɛbhɔ, mǎmbak ndǔ basɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ ambɨ ntá yɛká.
Debhít ayambɨ aghɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛkʉ ndǔ mpok anɛ átwɔ̀ ambɨ kɛ yɔ ɛmfakari. Aghɔ́ bɛ, chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, Debhít arɛm nyaka bɛ, ‘Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ chɛn Mpɛmɛ yí áyábhɛ́ ándɔ́ amɛm ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ chɛn mmʉɛt yi ámpɔ́ amɛm nnɛm.’
Bák yɛ́ ka pě, mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nywɔp ɛnɛn Acha yɛka átwɔ̀.
Bɔ̌ma, bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk mɛnyǔ bo be bǎchí nyaka mpok Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe. Puyɛ̌ bɛyǎ bhɛka kɛ̌ bachí barɨŋɨ́ndak ndǔ nɛyɨŋɨ anɛ bǒ mmɨk. Puyɛ̌ bɛyǎ bhɛka kɛ̌ báchí nyaka manɛ́m bo, nɛ puyɛ̌ bɛyǎ bhɛka kɛ̌ báfú nyaka ndǔ bɛsáyrí manɛrɛ́kɛt.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, mbák nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn mɛ́nyìɛ nɛbhɔŋ bɛkʉ ntɨ mmu nkwɔ ánkwɛn, chɔŋ mkpɨ́k ndɔ mɛnyiɛ nnya ndu nɛpɛ́m ɛna, tɛ̌ndu mpu yaŋ bɛkʉ ntɨ mmu nkwɔ ankwɛn.
Mbák mmu abhɔŋ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk kɛ aghɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mɔ́mayi angwɔ́t ntɨ nɛ yi, ná ɛkɔŋ Mandɛm ɛbhak yi antɨ?
Chɔŋ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ bɔ́ báchí ndǔ bɛpɨŋ ɛbhap, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mmu árɨŋɨ ɛnɔk ndǔ kɛpɛm ɛki. Bápú rɔŋ ndǔ támfáŋ mánkɔ́k nɛpɨ. Nɛ bápú rɔŋ ndǔ nnɛt áróŋóri mánkɔ́k bakwa.
- Nnókó bɛ nchí twɔ chɔŋ bɛghɔ bhe mandú mpok. Mpok yɔ, chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm kɛpɨ bɛsí nɛ bɛsi. Kpák Mandɛm ámbak nɛ bhe. Mamʉrɛ bhɛ mankɛm ndǔ nkwɔ Mandɛm abhɛn fá bátò wɔ bakak. Kaká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmʉɛrɛ wa anɛ achi ndǔ nkwɔ Mandɛm abhɛn awu.
sɛ́ndɔ́k kɛkwɔt nɛ Mandɛm nɛ batɨ anɛ tɛtɛp nɛ sɛ́nsɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ ɛnyu ɛnɛ sɛpu pɛrɛ makati yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Sɛ́nkʉ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ Yesu anáŋ amyakati manoŋ ami ndǔ batɨ yɛsɛ nɛ áchí pɛ́pɛ́p, nɛ yɔ ápú pɛrɛ taŋ bhɛsɛ ndǔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Asó mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ nkwɔ nɛ manyiɛp amɛn abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bakwap.
Aghɔ́ ɛnɔk fig nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ nɛ bɛyé arɛ́ gɛbhɛɛɛ, arɔk bɛyɨŋɨ mbák ǎkway bɛ́ghɔ yɛ̌ sɛpɛmɛ́nɔk arɛ. Aghaka nɔkɔ arɛ́, akɛ ghɔ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛbhɨkɨ fʉɛt chi bɛyé, mbɔnyunɛ mpok mɛnɔk fig mɛ́nyù kɛpɛm abhɨkɨ re ghaka nyaka.
Mbák mǎndɔk ambɨ bɛbhat mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ, nɛ bɛyɔŋ ɛbha mɛ́mbak amɛm batɨ yɛka, nchí chyɛ bhe yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ babhɛbhɛ mɛ.
Bakokosi bhi nɛ bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bárɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka yi mbɔ nnɨŋɨ́ mɛnɨ́ŋɨ́, bábho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Pú mmú nyaka áchɔ̀kɔ anɨŋɨ nɔkɔ mɛnɨ́ŋɨ́ nɛ?”
Yesu aghati yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Nnɛ́m mmu amɔt arɔ́ nyaka ɛtɔk yi arɔk ɛtɔk ɛ́chák nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ bɛ́ mánkʉ́ yí mfɔ ntá bǒbhi kɛ ampɛtnsɛm.
Ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ bɛyǎ bó báfʉɛ̀t, abhɛ́p ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fàkari.
Yesu árɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ, afa Yerúsalɛm arɔk Bɛ́tani, abhʉrɛ arɛ. 
Tɛ̌ndu bǎrɨŋɨ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, kʉ́ ka amɔ ywɛka anɛ áwɛ̀t ántáŋ ndu bɛkʉ bɛtɨk. Tɛ̌ ka sɛnɛ́ bɛ bɛkak ɛbhɛka bɛ́kɛ́ pɛrɛ wɛt gbagbǎgbak.
Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd nkwɔ́ abhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ yɛ̌ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛbhě yi mbɔnyunɛ atǒ yi apɛtnsɛm ntá ya. Nchí ghati bhe bɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ yi abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ mangway yi.
Nɛ mbák ángɔ́ bɛ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kway, ǎto bo ntá mfɔ wu mpok batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bhi babhʉɛt nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ bɛ mánsókórí ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bápú nu nɛ batɨ.”
Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ yɛ bɛ́ mpok mpɛ́t nchí pɛtnsɛm ntá yɛká, ntí ámbák anɛ be bǎbhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ maŋák ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Yesu Kristo ákʉ́ ntá ya.
Yesu arɨŋɨ bɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi báyàŋ bɛbhɛp yi ɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti ndak anɛ. Arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Ngátí bhe bɛ mandú mpok, bǎpú pɛrɛ ghɔ́ mɛ, kɛ mandú mpok chɔŋ mǎmpɛt mǎngɔ́ mɛ. Yɔ́ kɛ ɛ́sɔŋɔri nɛ́ bhe?
Kɛ chɔŋ bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi ambɨ nɛ́nɛ, mándɔp ansɛm, nɛ abhɛn bachi ansɛm, mándɔp bayǎmbɨ.”
Bɔ̌ma, yap yɛ ka bǒbati tándrámɔt. Bábhɔŋ bɛbhak bo abhɛn bo bárɛ̀m ɛrɨ́rɨ́ ɛ̌ti yap, mámbak bo abhɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achi nɛ bhɔ sayri, nɛ mámbak barɨŋɨ́ndak. Yap ka bhɔ́. Sɛ́kway bɛchyɛ bhɔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn.
Mbák nsay ǎnu mmǔ, ánjámbɨ ányíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛkɛt ɛyi, bɛ́ mpok bǎchɛ́mɛ́ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt, bǎkɛ́ kʉ Mandɛm ámbé ntɨ. Bɛ́yɨŋɨ barak áchák, chɔŋ mɛmbɔŋ ntwɔ́ awu nchyɛ́ bhe maníɛ́ ɛnyǔ babhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ.
Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm asɔt mkpá ɛbhóŋó asɛp yi amʉɛt. Ɛyɔŋ ɛ́fú amfay ɛrɛm bɛ, “Wɔ ɔchí Mɔ́wa. Nkɔŋ wɔ tontó. Ɔ̌chyɛ̀ mɛ bɛyǎ maŋák” 
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ǎkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛyǎ babhi. Kɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu ɛyi, achí mmu anɛ ájwí pɔɔt nɛ ǎkwáy nkwɔ́ bɛkɛm mmʉɛt ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi.
Mbák ndiɛrɛ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn fá amɨk kɛ sɛ́bháká ntɨ nɛ Kristo, nɔ ndǔ bǒ mmɨk mankɛm ɛbɛp ɛbhe yɛsɛ́ ɛcha.
Mmǔ ntí bǒnkwɔ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛbhak nkwɛnɛ́-mɛ́m. Abhɔŋ bɛ́bhak mmu anɛ ápú tɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ. Abhɔŋ bɛ́bhak sayri nɛ bho. Abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛbhak ntaŋ-bɛ́táŋá nɛ mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ngoŋó nkáp.
“Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásɔ̀t bhe sayri, ǎsɔt chi mɛ. Nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásɔ̀t mɛ sayri, ǎsɔt chi Ɛta mmu átó mɛ.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anyíɛ́ ajwi. Baghɔkɔ́ bhi bábwɔ́pti nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́, nɛ́jwí bɛkay tándrámɔt. Mpǎy bho abhak mbɔ nka ɛnwi.
Puyɛ̌ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛrɨ́rɨ́ ɛ̌ti mmʉɛt ɛyi kɛ Mandɛm Acha ásɔt nɛ maŋák, chi mmu anɛ Mandɛm árɛ̀m ɛrɨrɨ ɛ̌ti yi.
Nɛ mbwɔt anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mmɨk tákɔ nsěnse, até ndǔ mmu anɛ ághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, kɛ básɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ mmɨk atwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi antɨ, nɛ ngoŋó nkáp, angɔkɔntɨk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ ɛchi arɛ, Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm yɔ kɛkwak yi ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni.
Mandɛm mmu ákʉ̀ bɛ batɨ ayɛsɛ ambak amɛm kpák, ámbák nɛ bhe. Yi kɛ ákʉ́ Acha yɛsɛ Yesu Kristo áfú ndǔ nɛwú, apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Yi, Yesu, chi Mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ngo, anɛ ábhabhɛri bo Mandɛm mankɛm. Ɛ́chí ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ manoŋ ɛmi arɔŋ nyaka amɨk ndu bɛkʉ bɛ nku anɛ Mandɛm ányú nɛ bo ánté mpoknkɛm.
Mbák bǎpú bhʉɛrɛ bariɛp ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn báfyɛ́ amɔ yɛka, yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛchyɛ bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amfay?
Yesu abho yɛ bɛrɛm ntá batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bɛ, “Bě batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, nɛ be bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bo bɛtábhá! Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ntá yɛka ɛncha mbɔnyunɛ bǎchyɛ̀t bo mbǐnywɔp bɛ bákɛ́ rɔ Mandɛm ambak Mfɔ wap. Bě babhɔŋ bǎpú ka Mandɛm ambak Mfɔ ywɛká, nɛ bǎchyɛ̀t mbi ntá abhɛn bákway bɛyaŋ bɛchwe arɛ! [Bě batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, nɛ be bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bǒ bɛtábhá! Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha. Bǎsɔt bɛkɛt mánkwɛ́sɛ́, mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ bɛrɔ́rí nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt, bɛrwɔ bho bɛ bǎchi bɛsayri bo Mandɛm. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, chɔŋ ntɛ́msí yɛka ancha anɛ bo bachak.]
Bɛtɨk ɛbhap bɛchi mbɔ ndɨkandi anɛ ákʉ̀ sɛ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fàkari amɛm ɛtɛm ɛnɛ amfay. Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛchi nɔ mbɔnyunɛ mpok Moses ábhɔŋ nyaka bɛte ɛ́tɛm akap, Mandɛm aghati yi bɛ, “Ɔbhɔŋ bɛghɔ bɛ ɔté ɛtɛm ɛyɔ mbɔ ɛnyu ntɔ́ŋɔ́ wɔ amfay njiɛ.”
Mandɛm apu tɔŋ kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ́yàŋ bɛkʉ kɛ? Mpú mǔnto Yesu Kristo? Mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ nɛ amɨ́k kɛ? Pú bɛtɨk ɛbhá kɛ bɛkʉ bǎchí bakoŋo Acha?
Nnya yɔ abhak mbɔ mbé. Bayarɛ́kak ayi ábhak mbɔ anɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ bɛ́ɛ. Nnyu yi ábhák mbɔ anɛ nkʉ. Nnya mbʉ́mbʉ achyɛ nnya yɔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi nɛ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyi nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́.
Mmu kɛ áte yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛkɛt, kɛ Mandɛm kɛ ághókó mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm.
Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, afɛ́p bhɔ ɛ̌yú, arɛm bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ka Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ámbák nɛ bhe.
‘Dɔ́k ntá bǒbhɛn ghatí bhɔ bɛ chɔŋ mǎngok ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ, kɛ bǎpú jwimɛm wáwák. Chɔŋ mǎnjɨŋɨ ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ kɛ bǎpú ghɔ́,
Bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri bo bɛ́re rɔ bhɔ mɛ́mbɨkɨ nɔkɔ nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ. Bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi bhʉrɛ́ nɛ bakɛm bátaŋ nkwɔ.
Mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́kway, ngɔ́ ɛkɛt Mandɛm amɛm ɛtɛm amfay. Ɛ́bhak fúú.
Bakoŋo bhi bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, bɛbʉ́ agha bɛkʉ amɨ́k mmǔ nɛ ánɛ́mɛ́? Ɛbhi yímbɔŋ, kɛ ɛbhɛn chi nɛ nnɔ?”
Bakoŋo bhi bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɛtɔk ɛ́pú fá, chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́kway bɛyǎ bǒbhɛn fá?”
Mbɔ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bɔ báfú arɛ kɛ̌ bákàysi, mbʉ́ báyàŋ nyaka mbi bɛpɛtnsɛm arɛ́.
Nɛ chɔŋ ambé mɔ́mbakanɛm. Nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛ́mbak bɛ Yesu, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ yí ampɛmɛ bɔ̌bhi ndǔ ntɛmsi bɛbʉ́ bhap.”
Ntí anɛ bǎyàŋ yɛ mɛmɔ Mandɛm, bɛ́ghɔ mbák chɔŋ yi ambé ntɨ achí bɛ́ yí? Ndaká yí bǎchyɛ̀ batu anɛ yɛ̌ chi bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ babhɨkɨ kway nyaka bɛpɔkɔ ntá bo abhɛn bachi bakoŋo Yesu? Yɛ̌ chi bɛsɛ nkwɔ sɛ́bhɨkɨ kway bɛpɔkɔ batǔ yɔ.
Abhɨŋɨ mǔbɛtɨk wu arɛm bɛ ‘Ntɨkɨ ndak nɛ́ ngoko ɛ̌ti yɛ? Dɔ́k twɔ́ mɛ́ nɛ bɛkáti ɛbhɛn ɔ́sɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛya arɛ́. Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ kwáy bɛ́kɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbha.’
Mmǔ bɛtɨk wu ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, akwɛ́n bɛkak mfɔ wu abho mɛ́nɨkmʉɛt bɛ, ‘Acha, chyɛ̌ mɛ́ mpok, chɔŋ nkɛmɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌kɛm wɔ́.’
Nɛ bɛyɨŋɨ nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re pay amɛm ɛkáti Moses ɛ̌ti mɔ́nɔk anɛ ágò ɛbhɨ ndu ádù nyaka kɛsɔŋɔ? Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ pay ndu Mandɛm ághátí Moses bɛ, ‘Mɛ nchí Mandɛm Ábraham, Mandɛm Áisek nɛ Mandɛm Jekɔ́p’?
“Mɛ kɛ nchí Alfa nɛ Ɔmɛga! Mɛ kɛ nchí Ambɨ nɛ Ansɛm. Mɛ kɛ nchí ndǔ Nɛbhǒnɛt nɛ Ngwɛnti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.”
Yesu kɛpɛrɛ kɔ yɛ kpoŋoroŋ atú ɛtɔk bo Israɛl. Afa arɛ́, arɔk atú ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ɛchi kɛkwɔt nɛ baso, amɛm ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Ɛfraim, abhak arɛ nɛ bakoŋo bhi.
Kɛ bakoŋo abhɛn bárɔ́bhɛ́ amɛm áchwí báré nok bɛkoŋo yi angɔkɔnyɛ́n, mánja nɔkɔ bɛyǎ nkáp anɛ ajwi nɔ nɛ nsi. Nɛbhʉɛt anɛ báfú bɛ́rɔ́ŋ angɔkɔnyɛ́n kɛ sap. Abhak mbɔ bayat bɛsa bɛtay.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, mbák mmu ánsɔt sɔ́ ampɨ, sɛ́chàk, sɛ́ngó, ɛnɔk ɛ́nchɨk áncha bɔ̌mɛnɔk báchák mankɛm, nɛ ɛ́ngat batáp ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ kɛnɛn kɛ́twɔ kɛnte manyay ndǔ batábhɛ́ yi.”
Kɛ mmu amɔt anɛ áchi kɛ́kwɔ́t, agwɔp akparɛnja ywi akpɔ́t atú nsɛm Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm chwát agʉɛp amɨk.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́rɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi ághàti Nikɔdɛ́mɔs, arɔk bɛbhak bɛchak atú Judɛ́ya nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi. Abhak arɛ́ nɛ bhɔ anjwiti nɔkɔ bho.
Moses arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Chɔŋ Mandɛm Acha antó be ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ ywi mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ato mɛ. Nɛ chɔŋ yi ambak mmu ywɛka amɔt nɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ághàti bhe mǎnkʉ.
Kɛ mbák bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛ́chàk mmʉɛt, Mandɛm apú táŋ bhɛsɛ́.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, ɛnɛ báchí ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay nɛ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt mánchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm kɛnókó, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ arɛm bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ká Banábas nɛ Sɔ̌l, mámbák nyáŋá ndu bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn mbɨŋɨ bɔ mankʉ.”
Ɛchí mɛ maknkay bɛ́ bǎtɨŋ bǎrɔ̀ Mandɛm mmu ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ be ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu Kristo bɛ mambák bǒbhi, nɛ bárɔ́bhɛ́ koŋo chí Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ achak.
Bɔ̌bha, sɛ́ndɔ bɛrɛm chi nɛ ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu bɛ sɛ́kɔŋ batɨ. Sɛ́ntɔ́ŋ tɛtɛp bɛ sɛ́kɔŋ batɨ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́kʉ̀. 
Baghɔrɛ́ nɛbhay, sɛptí nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt ntá manɛ́m abhɛka mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎsɛpti mmʉɛt ntá Acha.
Chɔŋ anchyɛ mɛ kɛnókó mbɔnyunɛ ǎsɔ̀t chɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá ya, angati bhe.
kpatɛ nkʉ bǒmpap abhɛ mándɔp mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ chɔŋ ɔ́nyàŋa bɛkak arɛ.’
Yesu atɛ́m nɛkay ɛnɛn bɛ, “Nywɔp Mandɛm átwɔ̀ bɛbhak Mfɔ bǒbhi, mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛchi ndǔ nɛkǎy baghɔsɔ́ŋ bati byo abhɛn básɔ́rɛ́ nyaka bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛbhap, barɔk bɛtɛmɛri mbǎyngɔrɛ́ amɔt.
kɛ bo abhɛn chɔ́ŋ bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, mǎnchwe ndǔ mmɨk nkɔ, bápú pɛrɛ bháy nɛbhay
Yí aywǐnti kɛ áchí Mandɛm ntá bo mankɛm nɛ mmǔ amɔt kɛ ásɔ̀t bo ntá yi. Mmu wu chí Yesu Kristo mmu ákʉ́ mmʉɛt bɛ ambak nkwǎŋwaŋ.
Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, bárɔ́k ambɨ nɛ nɛtarɛ́nsay nɛ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt. Mányáŋa yɛ amɔ anti Banábas nɛ Sɔ̌l manɨkmʉɛt, barɔ yɛ bɔ mandɔk. 
Bɛrɛnɛ ɛbhap mɛ́mbak gʉɛpti gʉɛpti ndǔ nkɔngɔ ɛgho ɛnɛ bágó nyaka Acha wap ndǔ ɛkotákátí arɛ́. Bábhɨ̀ŋɨ yɔ ndǔ kɛ́mbʉ́ɛp bɛ, “Sódom”, mbák ɛ́pú nɔ, mambɨŋɨ bɛ, “Íjip.”
Jɔ̌n ájwìti nyaka bo nɛ manyiɛp, kɛ ndǔ mpǎy manywɔp, chɔŋ Mandɛm anjwiti bhe nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.”
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu arɛm ntá Píta bɛ, “Símun, Símun, ghók! Báchyɛ́ Satan bɛtaŋ bɛ́ ámɔ́ bhe, amfap abhɛ́n bárɨ́ nɛ abhɛn babɛbhɛ mbɔ mmǔ ǎnyɨ̀kɨsi kasárá ndu bɛsɔt anɛ yi ághàŋ gari.
Ɛpǎ bo Israɛl ɛnɛ́ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ ɛ́rɔ́p kɛkwɔt.
Chɔŋ anchyɛ bhe nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ndǔ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛka, anchyɛ bhɛsɛ nkwɔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt. Chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ nɔ́ mpok Yesu Acha ábhèsi nɛ bɛtaŋtí bɔángɛl bhi amɛm ngó anɛ ákàp bhɔ nɛ ádù gum gum gum.
Bofú básɔ́t bɔ̌bhap bárɔ́k ntá Yesu nɛ bhɔ bɛ yi anyaŋa bhɔ amɔ anti, anɨkmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm anjɛt bhɔ. Bakoŋo bhi bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bábho bɛsayti bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́ sɔŋɔri Yesu.
Báchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yerúsalɛm, bǒnkwɔ, nɛ bǒnto Yesu nɛ bǒbatí ɛtɔk básɔt Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas nɛ bo bachak nɛ maŋák. Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas bágháti yɛ bhɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛ́n Mandɛm ákwáká bɔ mankʉ.
Bágó mɛ ndǔ ɛkotákátí nɛ Kristo. Nɛ́nɛ, nɛpɛ́m ɛna fá amɨk puyɛ̌ ɛna, chi ɛ́nɛ́n Kristo mmu achi nɛ mɛ. Nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛna nɛ́nɛ chi ɛnɛn Mmɔ Mandɛm mmu akɔŋ mɛ, achyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛ̌ti ya ndu mbɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ yi.
Bɔ̌ma, nchí anyǔ nɛwú mpoknkɛm. Nchí rɛm nɔ ntá yɛka mbɔnyunɛ mɛ̌pànyu ɛ̌ti yɛka nɛ ntí bɛ bɛtɨk Yesu Kristo Acha yɛsɛ ɛbhɛn mɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ́kʉ́ bǎchi bǒbhi.
‑ Josɛ́f nkwɔ afa Násárɛt atú Gálili arɔk Bɛ́tlɛhɛm, atú Judɛ́ya. Bɛ́tlɛhɛm abhak ɛtɔk ɛnɛ babhe Mfɔ Debhít. Josɛ́f arɔk arɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ achi nyaka ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Debhít. Arɔk nɛ María, ngɔrɛ́ anɛ yi atɨ bɛbhay bɛ mánsɨ́ŋ manyɛ́n. Abhak nɛ mɛniɛ.
andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mbɔ be bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ chí ɛchɔŋ, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ bo mámbɔ́ŋ kpák, mbʉ́ ɛ́rɨ-e! Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, bɛchi bhɛsɛ bhɛsɛ nta yɛka nɛ bǎpú ghɔ bhɔ.
Yesu akɔŋ nyaka Matá nɛ bɔ̌mayi María nɛ Lásárɔs tontó.
Tɨk yɛ ka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ́ bǎkwɛ́nɛ́ ansɛm, mǎntɨ́k nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka mǎmpɛt mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ bɛrɨ́tí bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀ nyaka. Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ, chɔŋ ntwɔ ntá yɛka mfɛ́rɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɛka ɛnɛ ɛ́pɔ̀kɔ bɛrɔŋɔ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yɔ ɛchi.
Nɔ chi ɛnyɨŋ bárɛ́mɛ́ bɛ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò abhɔŋ bɛghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri angú, nɛ ambak mmǔ mbɨ bɛ́pɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m angati bo Israɛl nɛ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl ɛ̌ti ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnɛ ɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m.”
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm asɔt yi bɛ achi chak bɛsí bhi ɛbhɨkɨ yɨŋɨ nyaka chi yi aywǐntí.
Nchí yaŋ bɛ be mǎnkɛm mǎndɛm bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, kɛ sayri sayri, nchí yaŋ mǎngati bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ be antɨ. Mmu anɛ árɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ yi antɨ achá anɛ árɛ̀m bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn yi abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ mbák mbɔ̌ŋ mmu akabhɛ́ bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk abhɨ́kɨ́ nɛ́nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ ɛnchyɛ bo bɛtaŋ.
mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mandɛm Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm, Acha, wɔ mmu ɔ́chí ɛchɔŋ, ɔbhak nyaka, sɛ́chyɛ̀ wɔ bakak ndu ɔ́sɔ́rɛ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhe, nɛ wɔmbɔŋ ɔnáŋá ɔ́bhó bɛkɛm mmɨk mbɔ Mfɔ.
Ɛbyɔk ɛ́kwɛ́n yɛ ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm nɛ bo babho bɛjɛt mándɔkɔ nɔkɔ ndǔ ɛkɛrákap. Bákɛ́m Pɔ̌l baya gbaka gbaka gbaka báfú nɛ yi batɨŋ batiɛp babhǐnywɔp ɛkɛrákap.
Akʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mbi bɛkʉ ntá ya. Awátí mɛ nɛ bawɛrɛ́riɛp kɛ mpok bɛ́bhɛ́mɛ mɛ ankwáy.
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ bǎtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka tɛtɛp. Bǎkɛ́ chɔkɔ mǎndɛm bɛ́ bǎchí bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ́ Mandɛm ǎkwáy bɛsɔt batay ánɛ ankʉ yɔ́ ámbak bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham.
Ǎtɔ̀ŋ nyaka mbɔ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛmay, puyɛ̌ mbɔ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses.
Ndɛm yɛ nɛ mmʉɛ́t ɛya bɛ, ‘Ɔnáŋ ɔbhɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛsɔt bɛyǎ mamiɛ́. Kɛ́pɛrɛ sɔŋɔri mmʉɛt. Nyiɛ́, nyú, ɔ́nkʉ maŋák.’
Afú nɛfí, adi kɛbhɔ, nɛ bɛyǎ basɛ́mɛ́ antɨ. 
Bɛyǎ baghɔrɛ́ bábhák arɛ nkwɔ. Abhɛn bákòŋo nyaka Yesu bɛfu tɛ atú Gálili mánkwak nɔkɔ yi, babhak téé, nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ, mámkpɔkɔ nɔkɔ.
Dɔ́k yɛ ka ghati bakoŋo bhi, sayri sayri Píta, bɛ́ achi be ambɨ ǎrɔ̀ŋ atú Gálili. Chɔŋ mǎngɔ yi arɛ́, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyu yi ágháti nyaka bhe.”
Yesu atɛ́m nɛkay nɛ́chák bɛ, “Mbák Mandɛm ambak nɛ mmu mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mfɔ ábhák nɛ bɔ̌bhi, nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛ́bhák mbɔ nkɨ anɛ́ mmǔfu ápɨ́ nchwi.
“Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ ɔ́chyɛ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ntá mmu anɛ ɛyi ɛ́pú, kɛ́ dɛp akánkáŋ mbɔ bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ chi bɛ mángɔ́ bhɔ. Bákʉ nɔ amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt nɛ ndu mántɨ́tɔk bɛ bo mámbɨti bhɔ. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ nɛbɨti anɛ bo bábɨti bhɔ chi awap akap ankɛm anɛ́ bɔ mǎnáŋ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́.
Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ngati nyaka bhɔ bɛ, ‘Bě bǎpú bǒbha’, arɛ́ chɔŋ Mɛ Mandɛm mmu nchí nɛpɛ́m ndɛm bɛ, ‘Bǎchi bǒbha.’”
“Ɛtaya, mbák ɔkɔŋ, fɛrɛ́ nkɔ́p ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ bɛ́ ámfórí mɛ. Kɛ ɔ́kɛ́ kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌yáŋ, kʉ chi ɛnɛ́ wɔmbɔŋ ɔ́yàŋ.”
Yesu atɛ́m nɛkay ɛnɛ́nɛ́fú ntá bo abhɛn bakaysi nyaka bɛ bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm, mámbyaka nɔkɔ bo bachak.
Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ́ bɛ́ghɔ bɛ́ bɛyɔŋɔ́nyu ɛbhɛká nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bǎkʉ, mǎnkʉ bhɔ mbɔ bo abhɛn bákòŋo ɛbhé Mandɛm ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ́fɛ́rɛ bɛsɛ́ ndǔ bɛbʉ́. Ɛbhé ɛyɔ kɛ̌ Mandɛm ásɔ̀t bɛ́táŋ bɛsɛ ndǔ ɛwak manyé.
Ndɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́jwí ɛpay, bábhɨ́ŋɨ nnɛ́mámɨk anɛ Yesu ákʉ yi ághɔ̀ mbaŋ, baghati yi bɛ, “Dɛm tɛtɛp aywɛ bɛsí Mandɛm. Sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mmǔ anɛ ɔ́rɛ̀m nɔ bɛ anɛ́nɛ́ wɔ amɨ́k chi mmǔ bɛbʉ́.”
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mmu anɛ ábhʉ̀rɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛya, apú gú wáwák.”
Nchí chyɛ be ɛbhé ɛkɔ. Kɔŋ ka batɨ mbɔnyu nkɔ́ŋ be. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ̌ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkɔŋ batɨ.
Mɛnyǔ nnya mɛnkɛm bɛ́bhak ndu ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ. Nnya ɛnɛ́ bɛkak mɛnwi ɛbhak arɛ́ nɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́sù mɛniɛ amɨk nɛ kɛnɛn.
Kɛ ɔ́kɛ́ fyɛ manyɛ́n mánkwɛ́sɛ́ abhɛn bábhʉɛ́t nɛ manoŋ amʉɛt ndǔ nkwɔ mánkwɛ́sɛ́ abhɛn báyàŋ nɛkwak mbɔnyunɛ mbák ɛkwak bɛbhɔŋ nnɛ́m ɛ́nkó bɔ́ antí, bághɔkɔntɨk Kristo,
Ndú nɛnu ɛnɛn mǎnù nɛ bɛbʉ́, yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka abhɨ́kɨ́ re chyɛ ntí ɛ̌ti nɛnu ɛnɔ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mbák mmok ánɛ́m beku, nɛbu nɛ́mbak chuuu, be bǎrɛ̀m bɛ, Chɔŋ nywɔp nɛndɨ mborɛ.
Mpok yí ábhʉɛ́t nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ fá Yerúsalɛm. Chɔkɔ́ ká noŋ akap anɛ́ Ɛta afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ́tó mbɔ ɛnyǔ ngátí bhe.
Ɛ́kʉ kpát batɛmɛ́ nɛnu mankɛm abhɛn bábhàbhɛri ɛ́kírí Mfɔ Rom nɛ bo báchák mankɛm, bárɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛ̌ti nchí nkoŋo Kristo kɛ̌ báfyɛ́ mɛ fá amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ, “Mbɔ mǔkɛnɔŋ.”
Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ chɔŋ mǎmbɔŋ akap anɛ Yesu Acha ábhʉ́rɛ́ ntá bǒbhi. Chi Kristo Acha kɛ bátòk nɔ!
Kɛ mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu wu arɛm bɛ, “Acha, mbɨ́kɨ́ kway mmu anɛ ɔ́twɔ́ ɛkɛt ɛyi. Chiɛ́ chí ɛyɔŋ, chɔŋ mmɔ̌bɛtok wa antaŋ.
Ángɛl ágháti yɛ Píta bɛ, “Fíɛ́ nkú nɛ nkwɔbánya ɛyɛ.” Píta akʉ nɔ. Apɛt aghatí yi bɛ, “Bhat ndɛ́ yɛ amʉɛt, koŋó mɛ.”
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ápú pɛrɛ koŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Kristo átɔ́ŋɔ́, kɛ ǎmàka nkaysi achák arɛ́, apú bhat mmʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm. Kɛ mmu anɛ árɔ̀ŋ ambɨ bɛkoŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Kristo átɔ́ŋɔ́, Ɛta ǎbhák nɛ yi, Mɔ́ywi nkwɔ ǎbhak nɛ yi.
Basɛ́mɛ́ aya mɛ antɨ tontó nɛ ntɨ nɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri mɛ amɛm mpoknkɛm ɛ̌ti bɔ̌maya, bo Israɛl, bo ɛtɔk ɛya.
Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǒbhɔ bárɛ́mɛ́, ntí átáka yi amɛm. Ɛ́bhák ɛnyumɔ́t nɛ bǒ mankɛm amɛm ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm.
Baghɔrɛ́ fú báté nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ mánjɨŋɨ nɔkɔ. Mbɔk ɛyap báchi nyaka María anɛ ɛtɔk Magdala, nɛ Salóme nɛ María nnɔ Jems anɛ mɔ́nkwɛn nɛ Jóses.
Mbák abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ nɔ, ǎkwáy bɛghoko nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt kɛ yí kɛte ɛkɛt ánáŋá, nɛ bo abhɛn bághɔ́ yɔ mámbo bɛ́wáy yi bɛ,
Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti bafɔ nɛ bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfay bo bachak. Kʉ ka nɔ́, bɛ sɛ́mbák sayri nɛ batɨ, kɛbhɔ́ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri. Sɛ́nkoŋo nɛpɛ́m bo abhɛn bághòk Mandɛm nɛ nɛpɛ́m bo abhɛn mánòko mmʉɛt.
“Mpɛt nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm Yerúsalɛm, ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t ndǔ nchí nɨkmʉɛt amɛm ɛkɛrákap, ngɔ́ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antifu.
“Bo Israɛl mankɛm bárɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ tɛ kɛ̌mbɔ́ ɛka. Ngo chí nɛ bǒbha nɛ amɛm ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm.
Bǎbhak mamʉɛrɛ bha mbák bǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ngátí bhe.
Nɛghók Ananías ághókó bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn, akwɛ́n amɨk agú. Bɛyǎ bɛcháy bɛ́kɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ághoko ndak anɛ.
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ bɛkʉ bɛrɨ, nɛ bɛkwak batɨ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhɔŋɔ. Ɛnyǔ akap wu kɛ Mandɛm ábhɔŋ maŋák nɛ wu.
Nɛ́nɛ, bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎsɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti nɛnyíɛ́ bɔmandɛm nse, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́gháti bhe chí bɛ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎrɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, “Bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ.” Kɛ ɛnyǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ ɛnɔ nɛ́kʉ̀ mmu anjoŋ nɔkɔ mmʉɛt. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chyɛ̀ bǒ nkwɔ́ Yesu bɛ́táŋ chí ɛkɔŋ.
Apú fá. Mandɛm akʉ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyu yi arɛmɛ bɛ ɛbhɔŋ bɛfakari. Twɔ́ ká ghɔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhʉ́rɛ́ yi.
Ngɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ bo abhɛn ɔ́tó, mfá nde twɔ́ nkɛkɛ́m ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ mmu. Ghatí yɛ mɛ ntí anɛ ɔ́bhɨŋɨ mɛ́!”
Nɛ́nɛ, mpɛt mpú fá amɨk, kɛ bɔ́ bábhʉɛ́t arɛ. Nchí twɔ ntá yɛ. Ɛta! Wɔmbɔŋ mmú ɔ́chí Nyáŋá, kɛ́m bɔ̌ nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ, bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ́n ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ bɛ mambak mbɔ mmu amɔt, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ wɔ nɛ mɛ sɛchi mmu amɔt.
Bǒbhɔ bati apay bágháti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari ambi, nɛ ɛnyu bɔ́ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ yi mpok yi abɔkɔti brɛt achyɛ bhɔ manyíɛ́.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɔchí ntɔŋ ntá bo Israɛl anɛ bo bárɨŋɨ sayri, yɛ̌ nɔ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n-ɛ?
Nɔ́ kɛ ɛchi bɛ Kristo asɔt akap amɔt akʉ bo abhɛn Mandɛm ákʉ́ mambák abhi mánkwáy ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi bɛsí Mandɛm mpoknkɛm.
Ngɔsɔ́ŋ wu apɛtnsɛm áyák ntá mfɔ arɛm bɛ, “Chiɛ́ mɛ ntí Jɔ̌n Njwiti amɛm nchán myákátí nɛ, nɛ́nɛ!”
Lɛ́vi afate, arɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, abho bɛkoŋo Yesu.
Nɛpǎy-bho ɛnɔ nɛ́bhak ɛnɛ́n mbɨ mpok Kwiríniɔs achi gɔ́bhanɔ ɛtɔk Síria.
Nkɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ ntɨ ɛna nɛnkɛm.
Mbɔk bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Lɛ́vi bachi bachiǎkap Mandɛm. Ɛbhé Moses ɛ́ghàti bhɔ bɛ mánsɔt ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ amɔt ndǔ anɛ byo ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu Israɛl, yɛ̌ndu bɔ nɛ bo Israɛl mankɛm bachi bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham, nɔ chi bǒ nnɛrɛ́kɛt amɔt.
Ɛchi ɛnyumɔt nɛ bhe nkwɔ. Mǎnáŋ bǎghok ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp, nɛ chí Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ chɔŋ bhe, nɛ mǎnókó Kristo. Mpok anɛ mǎnókó, Mandɛm achyɛ bhe Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mbɔ sɛbhaŋ ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ bǎchi bǒbhi nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu yi afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎkʉ.
Bě manɛ́m, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ ngɔrɛ́ ywi nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Kristo ákɔ́ŋ bǒnkwɔ nɛ agú ɛ̌ti yap.
Mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnɨkmʉɛt, nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bɔ bachi arɛ anyɨkɨsi. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ bhɔ tontó akʉ bábhó bɛghati Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy. 
Kɛ́ rɔ akap anɛ́ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ myákámyáká, nɔ chí akap anɛ́ nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bágháti ɛ̌ti yɛ nɛ ɛ́kʉ bǒ batí mányáŋa wɔ amɔ́ antí bɛ́ ántwɔ́ ntá yɛ.
Chɔŋ bafɔ byo bhɔ mánkʉ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm ákʉ bɔ́ mámbɔ́ŋ nkaysi amɔt ndu bɛkʉ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ bɔ mánkʉ. Chɔŋ mánka yɛ bɛrɔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ babhɔŋɔ mbɔ bafɔ amɔ nnya mbʉmbʉ kpatɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm atɨ̌ bɛ mɛ́mfákárí mɛ́mfakari.
Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ yi ánɛ́nɛ́ batɨ̌ yɛka sayri ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bǎrɨŋɨ manɛ́m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbháká ntɨ arɛ bɛ chɔŋ yi ankʉ ntá bo abhɛn yi ábhɨ́ŋɨ́. Nchí yaŋ bɛ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛyǎ áfɔ́k anɛ yi afyɛ́ bariɛp ndu bɛkʉ manɛ́m mɛnyɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn bachi abhi.
Bakoŋo bhi bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Ɔghɔ̌ bɛyǎ bho ndu bákábhɛ́ wɔ, yɛ̌ nɔ, ɔ̌bhɛ́p bɛ, ‘Agha átɔ́kɔ́ mɛ?’”
Kɛ nkʉbɛtɨk anɛ ɛbhǎ nkáp ɛ́mɔt, ásɔ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ aywi nkáp, arɔk atɛ́m chí mbok amɨk abhɛsɛ ɛbhǎ nkáp ɛyɔ arɛ.
Ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛbhɔŋ yi bɛkʉ nɛ bɔmandɛm nsé? Bɛsɛ bo sɛ́nókó Yesu kɛ sɛ́chí ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm mmu achi nɛpɛ́m. “Chɔŋ nnte ɛkɛt ɛya nɛntɨ ɛnap, mbak nɛ bhɔ. Chɔŋ mbak Mandɛm wap, bɔ́ mámbak bǒbha.”
Bɔangɛl mankɛm batée bakap ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ nɛ bǒbati bhɔ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛpɛ́m mɛnwi bhɔ. Bákwɛn amɨk bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ báre chyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó,
Bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́ghɔ̀ bɛsɛ antɨ chi nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bɛsɛ babhɔŋ sɛchi chi mbɔ bɛtě ntɔp, bɛtaŋ ti. Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ, bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Mandɛm bɛ́fù chi ntá yi, puyɛ̌ ntá yɛsɛ.
Yɛ̌ mmu kɛpɛrɛ mɔ bɛ́bhɛp yi yɛ̌nyɨŋ. 
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ bɔángɛl abhɛn babhɨkɨ ka bɛbhak ndǔ bɛchɔkɔ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bhɔ, asɔt nyaka bhɔ abhʉ́rɛ́ amɛm nɛpi ɛnɛn nɛ́giri pyɔɔ nɛ ngɛm bɛkak, nɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ bábhak mpoknkɛm. Arɛ́, mánòŋ tɛ nywɔp nɛgho ɛnɛn Mandɛm átàŋ bho.
Kɛpɨ ɛkɛn kɛ́fù wɔ anyu kɛ̌ yi ásɔt antáŋ wɔ ɛwak ɛ́mɔt. Mbák bɛrɨ́tɨ́ kɛpɨ kɛ kɛ́fù wɔ anyu, ɛwak ɛyɔ, yi ǎrɛm bɛ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ manyé. Kɛ mbák bɛbɛ́ptí kɛpɨ kɛ kɛ́fù wɔ anyu, ɛwak ɛyɔ, Mandɛm ǎrɛm bɛ ɔ́kwɛ̌n manyé.” 
Pú bǎrɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Mbák ɛ́ngáká bataŋ anwi, chɔŋ mámfɛrɛ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ?’ Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ mǎnjoŋ amɨ́k mǎnjɨŋɨ nkɨ, mǎngɔ́ ndǔ mbwɔt ánáŋ ágháká bɛ́fɛ́rɛ ɛbhɨ.
Píta arɛm bɛ, “Yɛ̌ bǒ mankɛm mámbʉ́ɛ́ wɔ, mɛ, mpú bʉɛ́!”
Mbák bǎkʉ̀ nɔ, bo bághɔ bɛ bǎchí bɔ̌ ɛtayɛka mmu achi amfay. Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ yi ǎto mmok ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ bɛbʉ́ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́. Mandɛm ǎto manyiɛp ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ nɛ mmu anɛ ápú kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ mmu wu ankʉ.
Ɛ́kʉ́ básɔ́t nnɨk anɛ básɛrɛ ndo arɛ́, mámɛ́sɛ ndo anyɛ́n bɛ mándɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ nnyɛ́n nɛchwe amɨk. Bághɔ́ bɛ mmɨkɨ nyɛ́n arɔp mbɔ mɛta bɛsa bɛpay. Bɛ́rɔŋ ambɨ mandú, bápɛt bákʉ nɔ, bághɔ́ bɛ mmɨkɨ nyɛ́n arɔp bɔ mɛta ɛsǎ nsɛm byo.
Kɛfɔ Mandɛm fá amɨk kɛ́chi mbɔ mɔ́sɛpɛm anɛ ɛ́nɔk ɛnɛ́ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ mɔ́stat, anɛ bápɨ́ amɛm nkɨ, sɛ́chák, sɛ́gó, sɛ́rɔ́p ɛnɔk ɛnɛ kɛnɛn kɛ́twɔ̀ kɛ́nte manyay ndǔ batáp ayi.” 
Mbák sɛ́ndɔ́ yi andɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, chɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anoko yi. Nɛ mbák ɛ́mfákárí ɛnyu yɔ, bǒ Rom bátwɔ́ mánchɔŋti ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛyɛsɛ nɛ ɛtɔk ɛyɛsɛ.”
Ɛ́chí nɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm anáŋ arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɔ̌bhi ambɨ ambɨ. Ndu ɛchi nɔ, áyap bɔ́ nkwɔ bɛkʉ bɛ mándɔp chi mbɔ Mɔ́ywi.
Yɛ̌ nɔ́, mpok sɛ́chí nɛ bo abhɛn mǎnáŋ básɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm, sɛ́ghàti bhɔ́ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chyɛ bhɔ́ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak, kɛ puyɛ̌ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛkɛn bǒ mmɨk. Nɛ ɛ́pú bhák ɛnyǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛ́n bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ fá amɨk, bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fʉɛ̀rɛ fʉɛt.
Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm bɛ bǎkɛ́ kʉ nɛfwɔp. Sɛ́pú kʉ nɔ chi bɛkʉ bo mángɔ́ bɛ sɛ́chí chak. Sɛ́yáŋ chi bɛ mǎmbák chak, yɛ̌ndu bǎkway bɛyɨŋɨ bhɛsɛ mbɔ bo abhɛn babhɔŋɔ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́.
Básá ɛyɔŋ babhɛp mbák mmu anɛ ákà nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Símun Píta achí arɛ́.
Basɛm, ghók nɔ́kɔ́ ka bachi bhɛka abhɛn fá amɨk ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Bǎkɛ́ kʉ nɔ chi ndiɛrɛ mpok anɛ amɨ́k ayap achi be amʉɛt, mbɔ bo abhɛn báyàŋ chi bɛchyɛ bhɔ maŋák. Ghók ká bhɔ nɛ batɨ ayɛka ankɛm mbɔnyunɛ bǎchyɛ̀ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Yesu atɛ́m nɛkay nɛ́chák bɛ, “Kɛfɔ Mandɛm fá amɨk kɛchi mbɔ sɛpɛm mɔ́nɔk anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ mɔ́stat, anɛ bápɨ́ amɛm nkɨ.
mbɔnyunɛ manywɔp ayɔ chi anɛ ntɛmsi, bɛ́kʉ bɛ, mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm mɛ́mfú tɛtɛp.
Nkoŋo Yesu amɔt ndǔ abhɛn bati byo nɛ apay, anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Tɔmás, nɔ chí ɛfák, apú nyaka nɛ batɨ, mpok Yesu átwɔ́.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ sɛ́nsɔt bɛ ɛbhé ɛpu yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛ? Wáwák! Mbák sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu, sɛ́kɛ̀m bɛbhé sayri.
Mpok nchí ɛtɔk Damáskɔs, Gɔ́bhanɔ anɛ mfɔ ngo Arɛtas afyɛ́, áchyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu mambabhɛri nɔkɔ nyǔbha anɛ́ ɛtɔk ɛnyu ɛnɛ bɔ bákway bɛkɛm mɛ.
Mpok ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re tí yɔ́, mmɨk achi nyaka chi ayɛ. Nɛ mpok ɔ́tí yɔ́ nkáp abhak chi aywɛ. Ndaká yí ɔkaysi bɛkʉ ɛnɛ ɛnyǔ ɛnyɨŋ? Ɔsensé chi ntá Mandɛm, puyɛ̌ ntá nkwǎ!”
Yesu akʉ nyaka bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak. Mbɔ básɨ́ŋ bɔ́ mɛnkɛm amɨk ɛ́mɔt ɛ́mɔt, nkáysí bɛ́ mbʉ mmɨk nkɛm ajwí nɛ bɛkáti, kpátɛ mbɔk andɔp.
bɛ sɛ́mbɨ́tí yi ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn yi átɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɛsɛ ndɛ́ndɛm, ndu ábhárɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛ Mɔ́ywi mmu yi akɔŋ tontó.
Chɔŋ bakɔ̌siɛ́ fá amɨk mandi Bábilɔn tontó mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ mmu apɛt apú anɛ ákù mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́syɛ bhap.
Yesu abhɨŋɨ yɛ bakoŋo bhi arɛm bɛ, “Ntínso nɛ́kɛ̀m mɛ nɛ bǒbhɛn. Báchí fá nɛ mɛ ndǔ manywɔp arat, nɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ mɛnyiɛ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ yáŋ bɛrɔ bɔ mandɔk kɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ bákway bɛgu nsay ambi.”
Bakak ámbák nɛ Mandɛm mmu ánù ansɔt chi awɔ́nɛm. Asɔt bhɛsɛ́ mbɔ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bákɛ́mɛ́ ɛbhɨ̌nɛnu nɛ ǎya bɛsɛ mbi mpoknkɛm ndu sɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ nu chi ɛbhe Yesu nɛ́nɛ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ sɛ́rɔ̀ŋ, Mandɛm áfʉɛ̀t ntá yɛsɛ bɛkʉ bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́ Kristo ndu sɛ́kʉ̀ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ántáká nɔ́kɔ́ mbɔ ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp mbǎnkɛm
Sayri sayri, puyɛ̌ chi mɛ kɛ nchí kʉ yɛ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ. Chi bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bɛchi mɛ antɨ.
Mbák ɛchi nɔ, chɔŋ sɛ́nkway bɛrɔŋ bɛghati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ amɛm bɛtɔk bɛchak ɛbhɛn yɛ̌ mmu abhɨkɨ re kʉ bɛtɨk arɛ́, kɛpányu ɛ̌ti bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ́ ndǔ ɛbhe mmu achak.
Chɔŋ ɛ́mbak nɔ mbɔnyunɛ yi ǎbhák chɔŋ ɛrɛmɛ́mu bɛsí Acha. Bápɛrɛ́ bhé yí, chɔŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ambak nɛ yi tontó. Abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mɛ́nyú mmɛ́m amɛn ákɛ̀m mmu, nɛ yɛ̌ chí mmɛm bataŋbataŋ.
Bakak nɛ kɛnókó ámbák nɛ Mandɛm anɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ ngwɛ́nti. Achi Mfɔ anɛ ápú gú nɛ bápú ghɔ́ yi nɛ amɨ́k nɛ ndiɛrɛ yí kɛ achí Mandɛm. *Amen.
Mbák mmu abhɔ̌ŋ ntíánwɔ́p ɛ̌ti ya nɛ ɛ̌ti ɛyɔŋ ɛya, chɔŋ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɔ̌ŋ ntíánwɔ́p bɛ́sɔ́t yi mbɔ mmǔ wa mpok anɛ mɛ̌twɔ̀ nɛ kɛnɛ́m ɛka ɛkɛn kɛchi kɛnɛ́m Ɛta nɛ ɛkɛn bɔángɛl abhi.
Abhé mɔ̌mbɨ ywi, abhak mɔ́mbakanɛm. Anɛ́p yi nɛ ndɛn, abhʉrɛ amɛm ɛkwɔbhɛ́ nɛnyiɛ nnya mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka ɛbhak bɛchɔkɔ amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ mankɔ. 
Yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛpu ɛnɛ mmu ányìɛ ɛ́nkʉ bɛ yi akɛ́ bhak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú mmu anyu kɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ákɛ́ bhák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm. Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batú bɛghok ángók.”
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp ánɛn, bakoŋo Yesu bápɛ́t babhak anywɔp ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt. Tɔmás abhak nɛ bhɔ. Babhǐnywɔp ábhák femfé, Yɛ̌ nɔ, Yesu atwɔ́, ate nɛntɨ ɛnap, arɛm bɛ, “Kpák ámbák nɛ bhe.”
Kɛ mmǔ anɛ akɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ Mandɛm árɨŋɨ mbɔ aywǐ mmu.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ mǎnkóŋó chí ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́rɨ́ ɛ́chá bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bakwap nɛ bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bo bákwày bɛji bhe. Bák ká chi ɛnyu yɔ kpatɛ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn Kristo átwɔ̀.
Ngáŋ áchí ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ. Kɛ mbák ngáŋ ábhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ manyɨŋti mi, ná bákway bɛkʉ wu ampɛt ambak ɛrɨ́tɨ́ ngáŋ? Bɔ́ŋ ká ngáŋ amʉɛt, mǎnchɔkɔ ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ batɨ.”
Chɔŋ antɔ́ŋ be mɔ́kɛt anɛ achi amfay nɛ achɨk anɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛsɔbhɛri. Toŋtí ká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ arɛ́.”
‘Ansɛm mpok, chɔŋ mpɛtnsɛm mpɛt ntee ɛkɛt Debhít ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́. Chɔŋ njoŋ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ ɛ́báy mmʉɛt amɨk nkʉ yɔ ɛmpɛt ɛnte.
Ɛnyǔ ntay ɛnɛn nɛjwi atay nɛ́bhák ɔ́niks, ɛnɛn nɛ́jwí atandat nɛ́bhak kanɛ́lian. Ɛnɛ́n nɛ́jwí tándrámɔt nɛ́bhák krísolayt, ɛnɛn nɛjwi ánɛn nɛ́bhak bɛ́ril. Ɛ́nɛ́n nɛ́jwí nɛ́nɛnamɔt nɛ́bhák tɔ́pas, ɛnɛn nɛjwi byo nɛ́bhak krisópras. Ɛnɛ́n nɛ́jwí byo nɛ nɛmɔt nɛ́bhák jásint, ɛnɛn nɛjwi byo nɛ apay nɛ́bhak ámɛtis.
Nsóŋó yí abhɔŋ bɛ́kó nɔ́kɔ́ kó, aya ansɛp nɔkɔ.
Sɔt ka mpok nɛ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ, mmú ɛyɔ nɔ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ bábhɔŋ bɛkpɔt mmʉɛt mbakanɛm kɛ ambak mmu Mandɛm, ɛnɛ́ ɛyɔ ɛ́twɔ̀ chi nɛ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Bárɛ̀m nyaka ntá yɛka bɛ, “Ndǔ manywɔbhɛ́ ngwɛnti mmɨk, chɔŋ bǒ kɛyɔ́kɔ́ mámfú mánjɔkɔ nɔkɔ bhe. Ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap, bɔ́ bákòŋo chí bɛbɛ́pti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmʉɛt ɛyap ɛ́tò bɔ mánkʉ.”
Nɛka kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm asɔt chi ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu ɛyi kɛ ǎghoko mmɨk. Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghɔ̀ nɛ amɨ́k bɛ́fù chi ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu apu kway bɛghɔ nɛ amɨ́k.
Bátwɔ́ nɛ ntó ɛnɔ ntá Yesu mpok yi ábù bɛyǎ bho abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka mame mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu. Ǎbòk nyaka nkwɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ mɛ́ndɔ nɔkɔ bho, ankʉ nɔkɔ manɛ́mámɨk mángɔ mbáŋ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi átɨ́ nyaka bɛkʉ ɛnɛ́ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́re rɨŋɨ nyaka, atɨ̌ bɛkʉ yɔ bɛfʉɛt ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Kristo ákʉ́.
Ghɔ́ ka, chɔŋ nto be akap anɛ Ɛtaya afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ ǎtò ntá yɛka. Kɛ bǎbhɔŋ mɛ́noŋ fá amɛm ɛtɔk kpátɛ bɛtaŋ mɛ́mfu amfay mɛ́mbak nɛ bhe.” 
Mbák ɔsɔt mmu sayri mbɔnyunɛ ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ yi achi ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ wa, chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ wɔ nkúbhɛ́ akap anɛ yi áchyɛ ntá ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ ywi. Nɛ mbák ɔsɔt mmu sayri mbɔnyunɛ ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ ǎkʉ̀ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mankʉ, chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ wɔ akap mbɔ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mankʉ.
Mandɛm abhɨkɨ fyɛ bariɛp chi ndiɛrɛ nɛ Ábraham, kɛ nɛ Rɛbɛ́ka nkwɔ mpok yi achi nyaka nɛ mɛniɛ̌ bɛfak ɛbhɛn chi mbi ywɛsɛ Áisek afyɛ́,
Manywɔp ayɔ áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, sɛ́tóŋti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛsɛ, sɛ́fá sɛbho bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ mɛ bɛ, ‘Acha, Acha’, ɛnɛ́ bǎpú kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌ghàti bhe?
Afɔ̌ kɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ ntá yap bɛ, “Bǎchɨŋti bǎcha! Nɛ batɨ̌ yɛka ápú wakari mɛ́nóko mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bárɛmɛ!
aghati yi bɛ, “Josɛ́f, faté sɔt mmɔ́ nɛ máyi pɛtnsɛm ndǔ mmɨk Israɛl. Bo abhɛn báyàŋ nyaka bɛway mmɔ́ manaŋ bagu.”
Mandɛm are tɔ́ŋ bɛrɨŋ, ankʉ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu ndu bɛtɔŋ nkwɔ bɛ́ bɛchí tɛtɛp. Are fʉɛ́t nkwɔ ndǔ akap anɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ̀ bho, bɛ́kóŋo nkaysi yi.
Nɛ mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́kʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyu Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti yi, báfɛ́rɛ yi amfǎy ɛkotákátí barɔk babhʉrɛ amɛm nnɛm ɛnɛ́n bághókó ndu sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́.
Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛ́bhɔŋ yɛ bɛchyɛ mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ nɛkwak bɛ sɛ́mbák batɨ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk nɛ bhɔ ndu bɛghati bho tɛtɛp Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ Ɛtaya chi ɛya nkwɔ. Nɔ́ kɛ ngátí bhe bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ághàti chɔŋ bhe, ǎsɔt chi ntá ya.” 
Bɛyǎ bho babho bɛrɔŋ ntá yi nɛ bǒmame, nɛ bakɛm, nɛ bo abhɛn bachi bhʉrɛ, nɛ manɛ́mámɨk, nɛ babhók nɛ bǒmame báchák, mámbʉrɛ nɔkɔ bhɔ bɛsí bhi. Abú bhɔ́ mankɛm.
Chi-bɛtɨk, átát nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nɛkɔ ɛnɛn yi árɔ́ŋɔ́, apɛtnsɛm, abhɨŋɨ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bɛ mántwɔ́, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap andɛm ɛnyǔ yi akʉ nɛ aywǐ nkáp.
Sɛ́tò yɔ ntá yɛka bo Mandɛm, be batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ abhɛn bábhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp awu ɛtɔk Kɔlɔse nɛ Mandɛm abhat be nɛ Kristo. Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ ántɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu anchyɛ bhe kpák. 
Mandɛm ákʉ́ sɛ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu yí átó kɛ̌ ákʉ́ sɛ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɔ́. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ arɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, arɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chí tɛ amɛm ntɨ̌ Mandɛm.
Mbák bǎbhɔŋ ntɨ mɛnoko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛm, dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ sayri sayri mpok anɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bárɛ́mɛ́ bɛ Ɛláija ǎtwɔ̀, bárɛ̀m nyaka chi ɛ̌ti Jɔ̌n.
Mbɔ nku nsɨ́ yɔ ǎkway nyaka bɛkwak bo mambak chak bɛsí Mandɛm, mbʉ ntí apu bɛbhɔŋ nku achák.
Nchí ghati yɛ bhe bɛ, tɛ̌ndu bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛbhɔŋ akap anɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm áchyɛ̀, fyɛ́ ká ntí tontó ndǔ akap anɛ́ ákwak bǒnkwɔ mántaŋ mandɔkɔ nɔkɔ chi ambɨ.
“Yí ɛkʉ ɔ́rɔ́ŋ ɔ́chwé amɛm ɛkɛt bo ɛtɔk ɛ́chák abhɛn bábhɨkɨ syɛp bhɔ kpátɛ ɔ̌nyìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bhɔ́?”
Nywɔp nɛmɔt, ɛ́fákari bɛ Yesu ǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt aywǐnti nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi babhak kɛkwɔt nɛ yi. Ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnɨkmʉɛt abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bo bárɛ̀m bɛ́ nchí agha?”
Báchí amɛm ɛjuri nɛ báfap nyaka bhɔ nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ̀, mbɔnyunɛ bachi amɨ́k nɛ́mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ ndǔ nɛjwǐmɛm ɛnap nɛ bágwɔ́t batɨ ayap amɛm.
Pú bɔ̌mayi abhɛn baghɔrɛ́ báchí fá mankɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt nɛ bhɛsɛ? Aré bhɔŋ ɛnyǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́kɛpɨ ɛnɛn, nɛ ɛnyǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn fá?”
Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo mánchyɛ bhe nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ nɛ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ nɛ bɛrɛm chi bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ.
nɔ achí paka nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Ɛnyǔ mmu wu abhɔŋ chí ɛpɔ̌ ɛpɨŋ bɛ́kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí, nɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ́táŋá ɛ̌ti bɛyɔŋ, ɛnɛ́ ɛyɔ ɛ́twɔ̀ chí nɛ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ bo mántáŋ nɛ batɨ, mándɛm nɔkɔ ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti batɨ, nɛ mánkaysi nɔkɔ bɛ mmu ákú ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngufú abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ.
Sólomon kɛ áté ɛkɛt ɛyɔ ntá Mandɛm.
Nkúbhɛ́ Mandɛm kɛ ákʉ́ sɛ́nkwáy bɛbhak bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk, ndu bɛ́gháti bho ɛ̌ti Nku Nkɔ. Nku Nkɔ anɛ ǎyàŋ bɛ, nɛbho nɛ́nɛ, bo bákɛ́ koŋo chi ɛbhé mbɔ ɛnyu básɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka, kɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛghok chi Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ. Ɛbhé ɛ́twɔ̀ mmu chi nɛ nɛwú kɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ǎtwɔ̀ chi nɛ nɛpɛ́m.
Chi-bɛtɨk achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mánsɔt ɛbhǎ nkáp mǔbɛtɨk wu manchyɛ ntá anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhǎ nkáp byo.
Bɔ̌ma, tɛ̌ndu manoŋ Yesu árɔ́ŋɔ́ amɨk ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ, sɛ́kway yɛ bɛrɛm bɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛchwe ndǔ nɛbhʉɛ́t anɛ achi Nyáŋá.
Mmu abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛyɨkɨ ambɨŋɨ mmɨk mbɔnyunɛ mmɨkɨ nɛ achi mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ Mandɛm ásɨ̀kɨ bɛkak arɛ. Nɛ mmu abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛyɨkɨ ambɨŋɨ Yerúsalɛm, mbɔnyunɛ chi ɛtɔk ɛrɛmɛ́ Mfɔ ywɛsɛ.
Chɔŋ sɛ́nkʉ yɛ ná? Bɔ bábhɔŋ chɔŋ bɛghok bɛ wɔ ɔtwɔ!
Kɛ akɛmɛ ɛtayi chi bɛ, ‘Yɨŋɨ, bɛyǎ mamiɛ́ anɛ ankɛm, nchí fá nɛ wɔ, nkʉ nɔkɔ bɛtɨk ntá yɛ mbɔ nsɛm. Yɛ̌ ɔrɛm bɛ yi, nkʉ kʉ, nkɛ taŋ ntí. Yɛ̌ nɔ, ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ re chyɛ mɛ yɛ̌ chi mɔ́mɛn bɛ́ nkʉ mǎŋák nɛ mamʉɛrɛ bha.
Bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn-nɛ bǎkʉ̀ bɛ́kwàk nkwɔ bo Kristo ndu mɛnyu bɛpay. Bɛ́kwàk bɔ mámbɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchɛbhɛ bhɔ nɛ bɛ́kwàk bɔ mánchyɛ́ Mandɛm bɛyǎ bakak.
Bɔ̌bha, mmɨk arɔp chi kɛkwɔt mɛmay. Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ sɛ́ghati nyaka bhe bɛ mǔmpap Kristo ǎtwɔ̀. Yɛ̌ chí nɛ́nɛ, bɛyǎ bǒmpap abhɛn Kristo mánaŋ bátwɔ. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ bɛsɛ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mpok anɛ mmɨk ámay achi kɛkwɔt.
Bǒ-bhɔ mángwáy yi, kɛ ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp arat, Mandɛm ankʉ yi ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.” Bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛkʉ bakoŋo bábhɔŋ bɛyǎ basɛ́mɛ́. 
Bo abhɛn báchi arɛ́, bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛyɔ, bárɛ́m bɛ, “Tɛtɛp, nɛ́ chi ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛ́twɔ fá amɨk.”
Tɔ́ŋ mánkwɛ́sɛ́ abhɛn bábhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nɛkwak bɛrɨ̌ntɨ bɛ bɔ́ mámbɔ́ŋ mɛnwɔp.
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Máya nɛ bɔ̌maya chi bo abhɛn bághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ mánkʉ mbɔ ɛnyu yɔ ɛ́rɛ̀m.” 
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛ́bhʉɛ́t nɛ bhe ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok. Dɔk yɛ ka ambɨ bɛkɔ ndǔ mpok anɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛ́bhʉɛ́t nɛ bhe, bɛ ɛjuri ɛkɛ twɔ ɛmfɔkɔri bhe. Mmǔ anɛ ákɔ̀ amɛm ɛjuri, apú rɨŋɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi árɔ̀ŋ.
Ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ̀m nɔ, bɔ́ kɛjwimɛm bɛ́ yi árɛ̀m chí ɛ̌ti Ɛta.
Mpok nchí bhák nɛ bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ re sɛnɛ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm, nchí bhak mbɔ bhɔ́ ndǔ nchí nu bɛ́kwák bɔ́ mántwɔ ntá Yesu Acha. Nká bɛbhak yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ntá bǒ mankɛm, ndǔ nchí nu bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi bɛ́kwák bɔ́ mántwɔ ntá Yesu Acha, yi ámpɛ́mɛ́ bhɔ́.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ ndiɛrɛ ɛbhɨ Mísia nɛ Bitínia, báré yaŋ bɛrɔŋ atú Bitíni, kɛ Ɛfóŋó Yesu kɛka bɔ́ mándɔ́k.
Mandɛm apú rɔ bɛkʉ nɔ́ ntá yɛká mbɔnyunɛ yí ǎkʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yí árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ́ yí ǎkʉ. Nɛ yímbɔŋ kɛ̌ ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhé bɛ mǎmbat mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ. 
Ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɨ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɨŋɨ chi bɛ mpok anɛ nɛtwɔ́ Yesu Kristo árɔ́bhɛ́ kɛkwɔt, bo bátwɔ chɔŋ abhɛn báway bhe ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mǎnókó, mánkʉ nɔkɔ chi bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù bɔ antɨ.
“Wɔ mmu ɔ́kway mɛmokoti ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, nɛ ɔ́nte yɔ́ ndǔ manywɔp arat! Pɛmɛ́ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ mbák ɔchí Mmɔ Mandɛm! Fú ndǔ ɛkotákátí sɛp amɨk sɛ́ngɔ́!”
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá mmu anɛ Acha ápú sɔt bɛ abhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bhi.”
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu ákɔ̀ nɛpaká Manyu Gálili, aghɔ́ Símun nɛ mɔ́mayi Andru ndǔ bágʉɛ̀p bɛyǎ nkáp ndu bɛway nsi mbɔnyunɛ báchí nyaka bawǎnsi.
Mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batú ángók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm árɛ̀m ntá bɛka bǒnkwɔ. Mmǔ anɛ ánú asɔt awɔ́nɛm, chɔŋ nchyɛ́ yi nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ mána, ɛnɛn bábhɛ́sɛ́ amfay. Nɛ chɔŋ nchyɛ́ yí ntay nkwɔ ɛnɛn nɛchi pɛ́pɛ́p, ɛnɛ́n básɨ́ŋɨ́ nnyɛ́n nɛkɔ arɛ́. Yɛ̌ mmu abhíkí rɨŋɨ nnyɛ́n nɛkɔ ɛnɔ, ɛbhɨkɨ fʉɛt chi mmu anɛ báchyɛ̀ yi nɔ.” 
Tɛ́mté wu, bárɔ bɛyǎ nkáp yap bakoŋo Yesu.
Yesu arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Nɛ́ chi manoŋ ma. Ǎkʉ nku anɛ Mandɛm ányú nɛ bɔ̌bhi ántéé.
nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ bɛ bo mántók mɛ. Ntwɔ chi bɛbhak mǔbɛtok, nɛ bɛchyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛna ndu bɛku bɛyǎ bhó, mfɛ́rɛ́ bhɔ ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́.” 
Ntɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm amɔt arɔk yɛ ntá Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, chɔŋ nkoŋo wɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ ɔ́rɔ̀ŋ.”
Achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bákɛ́m Jems manɔ Jɔ̌n báwáy nɛ akparɛnja.
Píta abho yɛ bɛ́ghati bhɔ́ sayri yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákári tɛ ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt bɛ,
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Chí ɛ̌ti nɛtaŋántɨ ɛnɛka kɛ̌ Moses áká nyaka bɛ bǎkway bɛrɔ baghɔrɛ́ bhɛka ndǔ nɛbhay. Ɛ́pú nyaka ɛnyu yɔ ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt.
Ángɛl wu áfoŋ yɛ ngak ndǔ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm, akpɔ́t kɛpɛmɛ́nɔk, anyokoti, ato amɛm nɛyarɛ́ grep.   Ɛyɔ̌ ɛnkɛm ɛ́tɔ́ŋ bɛ Mandɛm anaŋ aběntɨ tontó.
Mbɔ bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ́ tɛtɛp, mbʉ́ bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ Ɛtaya nkwɔ́. Nɛbho nɛ́nɛ, bǎrɨŋɨ yí nɛ mǎnáŋ bǎghɔ́ yí.”
Ngɔ́ yɛ mɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ. Báchyɛ́ bo abhɛn bachɔkɔ arɛ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛbhak bafɔ. Ngɔ́ nkwɔ bɛfóŋó bo abhɛn báwáy nyaka mbɔnyunɛ bághati bo tɛtɛp anɛ Yesu ákʉ́ bo mandɨŋɨ, nɛ ɛ̌ti Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Bɔ bábhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ nyaka yɛ̌ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ yɛ̌ mandɛm nsé yi kɛnókó. Nɛ bɔ kɛka mámfyɛ ɛrɨŋɨ́ nnya mběmbe yɛ̌ ndǔ bafó yap nɛ yɛ̌ ndǔ amɔ yap. Bápɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m bábhak bafɔ nɛ Kristo ndǔ mamiɛ́ nká amɔt.
Jopa kɛsap nɛkɔ nɛ Lída. Bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn Jopa bághók bɛ Píta achi Lída. Bátó bo batí apay, ntá yi. Bárɔk manɨk yi mmʉɛt bɛ, “Ɛta, twɔ ghɔ bhɛsɛ́ ayak, kɛ́chɔŋti mpok.”
Júdas áfú nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Nɛ́nɛ, chɔŋ bo mángɔ́ ndu báchyɛ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm kɛnoko, nɛ bɛfʉɛt ntá yi mángɔ ndu bachyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Tí ká mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ mǎnchyɛ nkáp ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho. Bɔ́ŋ ká bɔ̌bɛbhǎ-nkap abhɛn bápú chɔŋɔ bɛ nkáp anɛm. Bʉrɛ́ ká kɛfɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ɛkɛka amfay. Arɛ́, kɔ́ kɛ́bhak mpoknkɛm. Yɛ̌ ngɛ́p apu kway bɛghɛp ɛnyɨŋ arɛ, nɛ kɛngɔk apú chwe ánchɔŋti yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
“Sɛ́rɔŋ, sɛghɔ babhǐnywɔp femfé, nɛ babhabhɛri nɛfí téé, kɛ sɛ́nɛ́nɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ babhǐnywɔp, sɛbhɨkɨ ghɔ́ yɛ̌ mmu amɛm.”
Kwáé! Bǎyàŋ bɛkʉ bɛběntɨ́ Mandɛm mɛ́mbák nɛ bhɛsɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo Israɛl bákʉ́ nyaka? Bǎkáysí bɛ́ sɛ́taŋ sɛ́chá Mandɛm kɛ́?
Nɛ Yesu arɔk ndǔ Ɛfóŋó aghati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ntá bɛfóŋó bo abhɛn bábhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú mɛnoŋ manyé anɛ ngwɛnti mmɨk.
Bɛbho ɛchɔŋ, yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́pɛrɛ chyɛ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔnyunɛ bɛrɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi mɛ amʉɛt bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ nchí mmu Yesu.
Báre rɔŋ ntiɛ̌ntiɛt, kɛ nkoŋo anɛfú wu ajɛt acha Píta. Ayambɨ aghaka ndǔ nnɛm.
Yesu akɛmɛ Píta bɛ, “Símun mmɔ̌ Jóna, ɛ́rɨ ntá yɛ ɛcha! Ɛtaya mmu áchí amfay kɛ ákʉ́ ɔ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ ndak anɛ, puyɛ̌ nkwǎ.
Yesu aghati bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bɛ, “Fíɛ́ ká manyiɛp amɛm bɛjɔ ɛbhɔ kpát mɛ́njwi.” Báfyɛ́ manyiɛp amɛm bɛjɔ, bɛ́jwí tɛ anyu.
Mbɔ̌ŋ ntí-ndak anɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m chi bɛ sɛbhɔŋ ɛnyǔ mǔngo bachiǎkap anɛ áchɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́ kɛnókó nɛ Mandɛm mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm awu amfay.
báfyɛ́ amɛm nchán myákátí, bárɔk bachyɛ ntá mmɔ̌ Hɛródias. Asɔt, arɔk achyɛ ntá máyi.
Kaká ká Rúfɔs mmu achi nnɛ́m mmú ndǔ nkwɔ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛn Acha. Kaká ká máyi nkwɔ mmu ásɔ́rɛ́ mɛ mbɔ mɔ́ywi.
Píta akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛɛ.” Píta apɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ Yesu. Kɛ ápɛ́rɛ rɛm ɛnyɨŋ, Yesu ayambɨ abhɛp yi bɛ, “Píta, ɔkáysí bɛ́ yí? Ntɨ́kɨ́ bhó báchyɛ̀ nkábhɛ́nti ntá bafɔ̌ mmɨk? Chí bɔ̌mɨk kɛ chi mankɔ?”
Moses akaysi bɛ bǒbhi bárɨŋɨ bɛ́ Mandɛm kɛ átó yi ámfɛ́rɛ́ bhɔ́ ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri, kɛ bɔ́ kɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyu ɛyɔ.
Bǒnto Yesu barɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Acha, kwak bɛ́ nɛka ɛnɛsɛ nɛ́ntáŋ nɛndɔk ambɨ.”
Kʉ́ ka mbǐ ywi ambak chak.
Mpok ǎtwɔ̀, tɛtɛp anáŋ atwɔ, anɛ bǎtaka chɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu andɔk ɛyi ɛbhak mǎndɔ mɛ awánti. Kɛ sayri sayri, mpú mɛ awánti mbɔnyunɛ, Ɛta achi nɛ mɛ.
Ngɔrɛ́ Samária amɔt atwɔ́ ndu bɛya manyiɛp arɛ́. Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Mma, chyɛ mɛ manyiɛp nnyú.”
Mbák mmu ánchɔ́ŋtí ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, chɔŋ Mandɛm ǎnaŋa yí. Mandɛm ǎnaŋa yí mbɔnyunɛ ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛbhak chí ntá yi aywǐntí, nɛ be bakoŋo Yesu bachí ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛyɔ.
Arɨ́ŋɨ́ ndu ákɛ̀m sayri bo abhɛn bábhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ yɛ̌nyɨŋ nɛ abhɛn babhɔŋɔ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ tɛ̌ndu yímbɔŋ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nkwɔ bɛyǎ bɛkwɛnɛ bɛsí Mandɛm.
Bǒbhɔ bati anwi báfa Yerúsalɛm barɔk Antiɔk. BɔPɔ̌l bábhɨ́ŋɨ nkwɔ́ Yesu báchɛ́m nɛbhʉɛt amɔt bachyɛ bhɔ ɛkáti ɛnɛ bapɔkɔ.
Yesu arɛm ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Sɔt ka mpok bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ byak yɛ̌ amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ bǎru bɔ̌bha abhɛn. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap abhɔŋ ángɛl amfay anɛ ákway bɛghati Mandɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ yi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok. [Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm, ntwɔ́ chí bɛpɛmɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánɛ́mɛ́ ɛbhɨ]
Mpok yɔ, bo báchák kɛ mánè yi, mambabhɛri nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi, kpátɛ mpok ɛ́táyi afyɛ́ ankwáy.
Mɔ́ywi wu áchwé nɔ́kɔ́ amɛm nkɨ, bákɛ́m yi baya báfú amɛm nkɨ nɛ yi, barɔk baway.” Yesu átɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɛkay ɛnɛn, abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎkaysi bɛ chɔŋ mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ wu ankʉ yi ntá bǒbhɔ?
Mɛ Pɔ̌l, mǔkɛnɔŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí fá nɛ mɔ́mayɛsɛ Tímɔti. Filɛmɔn, nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛ anɛ ɛkɔŋ, nɛ ntɨ nkʉbɛtɨk ywɛsɛ.
Yesu aghati Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti-nɛ tó ntá ángɛl anɛ ábhàbhɛri bǒnkwɔ abhɛn ɛtɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs. Sɨ́ŋ, kʉ bɔ́ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá mmu anɛ ákɛ́mɛ́ mambe tándrámɔt ndǔ awɔ́nɛm aywi, nɛ ǎkɔ̀ nɛ́ntɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ pú tándrámɔt ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́pɔ̀kɔ bɛrɔŋɔ.”
Nsɨ̌ŋ barɔ́ŋ ɛkáti ntá nkwɔ Kristo abhɛn awu, kɛ Diyotrifis mmu ákɔ́ŋ bɛbhak mǔnti, abhɨ́kɨ́ fyɛ́ ntí ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu áfʉɛ̀t árɔ̀ŋ, aghɔ́ mmú anɛ achi nnɛ́mámɨk tɛ ndǔ nɛbhe ɛni.
Bǒbati bhɔ bakɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Mpok anɛ mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ wu ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm, ǎkʉ bɛbɛ́ptí bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bhɔ mángú ɛbɛ́ptí nɛwú, ansɔt nkɨ wu anchyɛ ntá bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛn bápú nɔ́k bɛchyɛ yi aywi ákɔ́rɛ́ mbwɔt tɛ́mté, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́fú ɛbhɨ.”
bɛ chɔŋ ampɛmɛ bhɛsɛ ndu amɔ́ bǒmpap abhɛsɛ, nɛ amfɛrɛ bhɛsɛ amɔ bo abhɛn bapabhɛ bhɛsɛ.
Yesu abhɛ́p yɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bábhàbhɛri ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk abhɛn bátwɔ́ bɛkɛm yi bɛ, “Bǎtwɔ bɛkɛm mɛ nɛ bɔakparɛnja nɛ nkɨ́k mbɔ bɛ nchí chí ngɛ́bhɛ ntantaŋ?
Bakoŋo Yesu bárɔ́bhɛ́ nɔkɔ, báre kɔ mángati nɔkɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ mbǎnkɛm. Yesu Acha abhak nɛ bhɔ, achyɛ bhɔ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ bɔ bághàti bho achi tɛtɛp.
Mandɛm ápɛ́rɛ ghoko mmɨk, anáŋ ayap nyaka yi. Kɛ ndǔ manywɔp ngwɛnti anɛ kɛ yi abhesi ɛ̌ti ɛyɛka.
Arɛ́, arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Mbák ɔchí Mmɔ Mandɛm, dók, tɛ̌ndu ɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɔángɛl bhi mántwɔ́ manchyɛ wɔ nɛkwak. Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́pɛt ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, chɔŋ mánkpʉɛp wɔ nɛ amɔ́ yap bɛ́ ɔ́kɛ́ tɛm ɛkak ndǔ ntay.’”
Ɛ́fákári ɛnyumɔt nɛ nkú bɛtɨk amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm amɔt anɛ nnɛrɛ́kɛt *Lɛ́vi. Mpok yi aghaka arɛ, aghɔ́ yi, kɛ afʉɛ́t nkwɔ chi ɛbhe ɛchak, arɔk.
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Básɨŋ bɛ, Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò abhɔŋ bɛ́ghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri, angú, nɛ bɛghaka manywɔp árát, ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Mbák chí bo abhɛn bachi mbɔ mmú, nɛ bǒ babú, nɛ bǒ ɛpúsí, nɛ bawǎy bho, nɛ bo abhɛn bákòŋo bɔmandɛm nsé, nɛ bo abhɛn bɛkɔŋɔ nsé nɛ básénse, bɔ́ mankɛm bábhak chi nɛfí.
Báre rɛm bɛ, “Pú Yesu mmɔ̌ Josɛ́f nɛ́? Pú sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛtayi nɛ máyi? Ɛ́kɔ ná kɛ yi arɛm bɛ, ‘Mfu amfay kɛ nchí ntwɔ fá amɨk’?”
Mbɔk bo básɔ̀t mbɔk manywɔp bɛ acha achak. Bachak básɔ̀t manywɔp ankɛm bɛ achi ɛnyumɔ́t. Ɛrɨ mbɔ̌ŋ mmu angɔ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákàysi amɛm ntɨ ɛni ɛchi chak.
