Nchí rɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndu bɛkwak bhe, puyɛ̌ chi ndu bɛchɛt bhé mbi. Nchí yaŋ chi bɛkwak mǎnkɔ́ ndǔ mbi anɛ́ achi chak nɛ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka ankʉ bɛtɨk Acha nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ bǒ ɛka yɔ bárɛ̀m bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu, báchɛm nɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap, bátó babhabhɛrí abhɛn ɛkɛrákap bɛ mankɛm yi.
“Ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu yap ɛ́nɛ̀m mbɔ ɛriɛp ɛnɛ ɛ́fú ndǔ nnɛm ɛnɛ́n ɛnɛ́n mánɛ́nɛ́, bárɔ́ fúú. Básɔ̀t bárɨ́ yap bɛrwɔ bho.” “Bɛyɔŋɔ́nyu bhap bɛ́wày mmu way mbɔ ɛfé mpok ɛ́nɛ́m mmu.”
Mpok Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n anɛnɛ ɛbhánɛ́ ɛnɛ ɛjwi mɛnwi, ngók ndu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛjwi mɛnwi ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Twɔ́!”
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ “Ndaká yí ɔ́bhɨŋɨ mɛ bɛ mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́? Yɛ̌ mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́ apú. Mandɛm aywǐnti kɛ achi Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Bákway bɛbhak babhɔ́t, mánkɔ nɔkɔ bɛkɛt nɛ bɛkɛt. Bakway bɛbhak bo kɛ́mbwɔ́bhɛ́ nɛ bǒ ɛnáŋtí, nɛ bo abhɛn báchwè ndǔ baraká bo báchák, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛrɛm.
Yesu aghati bɔ bɛ, “Bě bǎchí bo abhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ mmʉɛt bɛ bǎchi chak bɛsí bho. Kɛ Mandɛm arɨŋɨ batɨ yɛka. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bo báyɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ ɛbhɔŋ mɛnwɔp chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ápàp.”
Bǎkɛ́ ka yɛ bɛ mmu ánsɔ́t bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi fuu andwɔ̀ bhe. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ kɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ Mandɛm ambentɨ, nɛ chɔŋ antɛmsi bo abhɛn bapu ghok yi.
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ káŋ mmu mbɔ awú, mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌agha anɛ ápú mǔmpap ywɛka achí mmǔ ywɛka.” 
Tɛ́mté wu, abho bɛghɔ mbaŋ! Nɛ abho bɛkoŋo Yesu, ambɨti nɔkɔ Mandɛm. Bo mankɛm bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, babhɔ bɛbɨti nkwɔ Mandɛm.
Bɛ́kóŋo ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bachiǎkap Mandɛm, bágʉɛp nyaka ɛbháŋá ndu bɛyap mmu anɛ árɔ̀ŋ ndǔ mɔ́kɛt anɛ achi tɛ amɛm ɛkɛrákap Acha ndu bɛsɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chyɛ̀ ɛrɨ́tí   ɛriɛp amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Bagʉɛp ɛbháŋá, ɛ́kwɛ́n amʉɛt Sakaría.
Ghatí ká mɛ. Bǎrɔŋ nyaka amɛm baso bɛghɔ ntɨkɨ ɛnyʉ̌ mmu? Ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ? Ɛ́chi tɛtɛp. Kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mmu anɛ bǎghɔ́ achá ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ.
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ mmu ándwɔ́ bhe mbɔnyunɛ, mbɔ ɛnyǔ miámiaŋ ákɔ̀t, angɔɔ, bɛfu ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nɛbu ɛ́mɔt bɛghaka ɛchak, nɔ́ kɛ̌ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhak mpok Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí twɔ.
Yɛ̌ ɛmbak chi bɛ nchí dɛp awɔ antɨ tontó mandú ncha ɛnyǔ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ ɛ̌ti bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu Acha áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ, ɛyɔ ɛpu kʉ mbɔ̌ŋ ntíánwɔ́p. Achyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɔ chi bɛkʉ mǎngo, puyɛ̌ bɛkʉ mǎnkwɛn.
Kɛ bǎyàŋ mbi bɛway mɛ, mɛ mmu ngátí bhe tɛtɛp anɛ ngókó ntá Mandɛm. Ábraham apú kʉ nyaka nɔ.
Bǎkɛ́ nyɔ́p mmʉɛt nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨkɨ noko Yesu. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm, ɛ́bhɔŋ yi bɛkʉ nɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pú chak. Bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ bɛkway bɛ́bhak nɛbhʉɛt amɔt nɛ ɛjuri kɛ?
Bárɛ́m bɛ́ Banábas chí mándɛm anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Sús, nɛ bɛ Pɔ̌l chi mándɛm anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Hɛmes mbɔnyunɛ yí kɛ achi nyaka ndɛmɛ kɛpɨ.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Mandɛm kɛ áchyɛ́ wɔ bɛtaŋ. Mbɔ ɛ́pú nɔ́, mbʉ ɔbhɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ amfay ya fá? Nɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ bɛbʉ́ mmu anɛ ákɛ́mɛ́ mɛ́ áchyɛ́ ntá yɛ, bɛ́chá ɛbhɛ.”
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mbák mɛ̌yaŋ bɛ́ yi wu ambak nɛpɛ́m tɛ mpɛtnsɛm, ɛyɔ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ́ ná? Koŋó mɛ́!”
Bofú básɔ́t bɔ̌bhap bárɔ́k ntá Yesu nɛ bhɔ bɛ yi anyaŋa bhɔ amɔ anti anjɛt bhɔ. Baghɔkɔ́ bhi bábho bɛsáyti bhɔ.
Sɛ́chi nɛ amík ambɨ sɛ́nòŋ áfɔ́k anɛ Mandɛm ábhʉ́rɛ́ amfay ntá bǒbhi. Abhʉ́rɛ́ wu ntá yɛka. Áfɔ́k wu apu may nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú kwáy bɛchɔŋti wu nɛ ápú gú manyiɛp.
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá yap bɛ, “Sɛ́nsɔ́t bɛ mmu ywɛka amɔt arɔ̌ŋ ntá mmʉɛrɛ ywi mpok nywɔp nɛ́gháká nɛ́ntɨ́bhɛti, adɛp nɛkok arɛm bɛ, ‘Nkwǎnɛ, nnɨkmʉɛt pwɔ mɛ bɛkpkɔkɔ́ brɛt bɛ́rát.
“Nkʉ bo mándɨ́ŋɔ́ wɔ, bo abhɛn ɔ́yábhɛ́ fá amɨk ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ. Báchí bǒ bhɛ, nɛ wɔ kɛ ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ bhɔ. Bábhʉ́rɛ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛyɛ.
Mbák chi bo abhɛn bákàysi bɛ bɛbhʉ́rɛ bɛbhé bo Israɛl kɛ ákʉ̀ bɔ mámbák chak bɛsí Mandɛm, ɛyak ɛchi nɛ bhɔ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Ɛyak ɛchi nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ápú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm.”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu arɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mmu anɛ áyɛt ntɨ kɛ áchá mmu anɛ yi áyɛ́rɛ́.
Kɛ sɛ́ghàti bho chí bɛ́ báway Kristo ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Nɛ mbok yɔ́ ákʉ́ batí bo Israɛl átáká amɛm. Nɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl básɔ̀t yɔ́ chí mbɔ ɛchɨŋti.
Mandɛm áfɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ, ayap Debhít bɛ ambak mfɔ wap. Mandɛm arɛm ɛ̌ti Debhít bɛ, ‘Debhít mmɔ̌ Jése, chí mmu anɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ maŋák nɛ yi, mmu anɛ apú nɔ́k bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛ́mɛ́ yi ankʉ.’
Mɛmbɔŋ nchí te ntísiɛ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m chí mbɔ̌ŋ ndak, nɛ Ɛtaya mmu átó mɛ ǎtè mɛ ntísiɛ nkwɔ́ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m ɛchi tɛtɛp.”
Yɛ̌ nɔ, bǎpú noko mbɔnyunɛ bǎpú ndǔ nkwɔ́ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n aya.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap anyiɛ́ kpát ajwi. Baghɔk Yesu mányókóti nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛrɔbhɛ. Nɛ́jwí bɛkay byo nɛ bɛpay.
Yesu aghati yɛ bhɔ́ bɛ́ mángúrɛ́. Bo mankɛm bárɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́, asɛp anyɛ́n nɛ bakoŋo bhi, asɔt áchwí arɔk atú Magádan.
Bǎkaysi bɛ chɔŋ mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ wu ankʉ yi ntá bo bhɔ? Chɔŋ antwɔ́ angwáy bhɔ anchyɛ nkɨ wu ntá bo bachak.
‘Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ, mámaka yi bɛ́chák, ambɔ́ŋ mɛ́nja mɛncha. Kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ, yɛ̌ chí mandú anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, básɔt ntá yi.’
Ndu mánòk bárɔ̀ŋ, Yesu akwɛ́n kɛnɔ́. Mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ abho mɛnu. Nnyɛ́n nɛ́bho bɛdɛp áchwí, manyiɛp anchwe nɔkɔ amɛm. Ɛ́rɔp chi mandú bɛ mámbɛt anyɛ́n.
Kɛchi mbɔ yís anɛ ngɔrɛ́ ásɔ́rɛ́ achɛm nɛ nchán fláwa ɛ́rát. Mandu yís wu akʉ fláwa nkɛm amwɔt, kpát ajwi amɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi achi arɛ́.” 
Mbák chi Sɔ̌l, are yáŋ mbi mɛ́nɛ́mɛ bǒnkwɔ Yesu. Ɛ́kʉ abho bɛ́chwé ɛkɛt nɛ ɛkɛt anja nɔkɔ abhɛn mánókó, baghɔrɛ́ nɛ babhakanɛm, amfyɛ nɔkɔ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Sɛ́rɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ nkwǎŋwaŋ abhɔŋ chí mmʉɛt amɔt, kɛ bɛ́pókómʉɛt bɛchi nyáŋá nyáŋá. Yɛ̌ndu bɛ́pókómʉɛt bɛyǎ, ndiɛrɛ mmʉɛt amɔt kɛ áchí. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ Kristo.
Bɛrɛm bɛ mmu achi nɛntɨ bho, ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛ bakwɔ́ bho achi apay anɛ yi áté nɛntɨ ɛnap. Kɛ mpok Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp ntá Ábraham, abhak chi aywǐnti. 
Nu bɛ́twɔ ndǔ mpok anɛ mbaŋ ábhɨ́kɨ́ re bho bɛ́kwɛn tontó. Nɔ́ chí ndǔ mpok nnɛ́m nɛbháŋ. Ɛbúlɔs nɛ Púdɛns nɛ Láinɔs nɛ Kláúdia nɛ bo nkwɔ́ Yesu báchak fá Rom báto wɔ bakak.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bo abhɛn bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔŋɔri bhɔ bághɔ́ nyaka yi, bákwɛn yi bɛkak mámbɨkɨ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mmɔ Mandɛm!”
Ndǔ bɛtǐ bhɔ, nkwɔ́ babhabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n bábhak nɛfí nɛ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ɛyap ndǔ atú ɛtɔk wu.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛ́chí amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, ‘Puyɛ̌ nɛnyíɛ́ nɔ́nɔ́ kɛ nɛ́kɛ̀m nɛpɛ́mɛ́ mu.’”
Batí yap ápay bárɔ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛ́n tɛtɛp bágurɛ ɛbhɨ ndǔ bátɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ Mandɛm anáŋ akʉ bo bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Bákʉ kpát mbɔk bho abhɛn mánókó Yesu bápú pɛrɛ noko yi.
Nɛ mpok bǎghókó nsóŋó-nɛnu bǎkɛ́ chay. Mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛfakari, kɛ ɛyɔ ɛpu tɔŋ bɛ ngwɛnti mmɨk aghaka.
Pɔ̌l nɛ bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ nɛ yi bachwe ɛtɔk Pafɔs, bákɔ́ anyɛ́n anyɛ́n barɔk bágháka Pɛ́ga atú Pamfília. Jɔ̌n Mák arɔ bhɔ́ arɛ apɛtnsɛm Yerúsalɛm.
“Yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nywɔp nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ mpok anɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fàkari chɔŋ. Bɔángɛl Mandɛm bábhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ, yɛ̌ mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ. Ɛta Mandɛm aywǐnti kɛ árɨŋɨ.
Ɛ́chi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mandɛm afyɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ antɛn yi.” Kɛ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm bɛ́chí antɛn yi” abhɨ́kɨ́ tɔŋ bɛ Mandɛm mmu afyɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm antɛn Kristo ǎbhák nkwɔ antɛn yi.
Batɔŋ-ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bábho bɛbhɛp mmʉɛ́t bɛ, “Agha nɛ́? Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m chi nsɔk ntá Mandɛm! Mandɛm aywǐnti kɛ ákway bɛfoŋori bɛbʉ́ mmu!”
Ɛbyɔk ɛ́kwɛ́n ɛtɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs ɛnkɛm. Bo barɔk ayak bákɛ́m Gáyɔs nɛ Arístakɔs báyá, bárɔk amɛm acha ɛtɔk nɛ bhɔ́. Gáyɔs nɛ Arístakɔs babhak bǒ Masidónia abhɛn bákɔ̀ nɛ Pɔ̌l.
Yesu akók arɛm bɛ, “Eé Yerúsalɛm, bǒ Yerusalɛm! Bě bo bǎwày barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm, mǎntɛmti nɔkɔ nɛ batay ndu bɛway bo Mandɛm átó bɛ mángátí bhe Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi. Ndǔ bɛyǎ mpok, njáŋ bɛsɔt bhe mfyɛ́ amʉɛt bɛ́ mǎmbak nɛ mɛ mbɔ bɔ̌nkɔk abhɛn nnɔ nkɔk ákútí nɛbhʉɛt amɔt nɛ bɛbhap ɛbhi, kɛ bǎpú ka bɛ nkʉ nɔ!
Kɛ mbák yɛ̌ mmu apú mɛnɛnɛ ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́mbɔŋ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ akap wu ánchɔ́kɔ́ kpák amɛm ɛchɛmɛ Nkwɔ Kristo, andɛm nɔkɔ bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nɛ mmʉɛt yi nɛ ntá Mandɛm.
Kɛ nkáká bhé tontó bɛ́ bǎchɛm amɔ nɛ mɛ ndǔ nɛkwak ɛnɛ́n bǎchyɛ́ mɛ́ mpok mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́táŋá mɛ amʉɛt.
Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ Yesu Kristo aku bhe afɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ bɛpɔ̌ bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎsɔ́rɛ́ nyaka ntá bachǐmbɨ bhɛka. Abhɨ́kɨ́ ku bhe chí nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chɔ̀ŋti nkáp.
“Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nchí ghati bhe chi bɛ mankɔ́ŋ batɨ mbɔnyu nkɔ́ŋ be.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl, sɛ́fú amɛm ɛtɔk sɛ́rɔk angɔkɔnyɛ́n ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ sɛ́káysí bɛ́ bo báchɛ̀m arɛ mɛ́nɨkmʉɛt. Sɛ́chɔ́kɔ amɨk sɛ́ndɛm nɔkɔ kɛpɨ nɛ baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn báchɛ́mtí arɛ́.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, Mandɛm akʉ yi apɛtnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m.
Nɛ́nɛ, mbákántɨ bɛ chɔŋ ńdɔk Spen. Mpok nchí rɔŋ chɔŋ mbɔ̌ŋ maŋák bɛghat bɛ mbak nɛ bhe ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok kɛ ndɔk nɔkɔ ambɨ. Nɛ mpok bɛrɔ be akway nɔkɔ, nkaysi bɛ chɔŋ mǎnkwak mɛ nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ nɛkɔ ɛna.
Píta arɔk yɛ ntá Yesu abhɛp yi bɛ, “Acha, mbák mmu ántóŋórí bɛkʉ mɛ bɛbʉ́, mbɔ̌ŋ bɛ́fóŋóri yi ndɔŋ ɛ́ní? Ndɔŋ tándrámɔt kɛ?”
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, Mandɛm apú kwáy bɛbhak ntá mmu mbɔ Mfɔ ywi kpátɛ mámbé yi nɛ manyiɛp* nɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm.
Bǎrɔŋ nyaka amɛm baso bɛghɔ yi? Mmu anɛ afyɛ́ bɛrɨ́tí ndɛn amʉɛt kɛ? Bǒ abhɛn báfyɛ̀ mɛnyǔ ndɛn ɛbhɔ báchɔ̀kɔ chi amɛm bɛkírí-bafɔ!
Bɔ̌ma, sɛ́ghàti bhe bɛ mǎnchyɛ́ nɔkɔ bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk Acha ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka kɛnókó bɛ mánchyɛ nɔkɔ bhe maniɛ bɛ bǎkɛ́ kʉ bɛbʉ́.
Nɛ mbák Satan ankʉ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bhi mɛnu nɛ batɨ, ná yi ákway bɛbhak ɛnyǔ mfɔ anɛ yi achi ndǔ ɛrɔri mpok? Nchí bhɛp be mbɔnyunɛ bǎrɛ̀m bɛ ndǔ bɛtaŋ Satan kɛ̌ mɛ̌bòk bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ.
Mpok nɛnyíɛ́ ákwáy nɔ́kɔ́, asɔt ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt. Áchyɛ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm. Abho yɛ bɛ́bɔ́kɔ́ti anchyɛ nɔkɔ ntá yap.
Kɛ nkɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ ɛpɨŋɨ́ bǒ Rom ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ mángwáy mmu ɛnɛ́ babhɨkɨre taŋ yi. Mmu abhɔŋ bɛ́té bɛsí nɛ bɛsí nɛ bo abhɛn bátí yí anchyɛ ɛyi ɛyɔŋɔ́ manyé.
Yi akɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Ɛta, mmu wu chi agha? Ghatí mɛ, bɛ nnókó yi.”
Mandɛm aghókó mmǔ mbɨ chí nɛ ntɔp, anɛ átwɔ́ ansɛm afú chi amfay.
Bátɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛpɨŋɨ́tɔk ɛbhɛ́n ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ́ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ sɛ́nkóŋó. Sɛ́chí bo Rom nɛ sɛ́pú kwáy bɛ́kóŋo bɛpɨŋɨ́tɔk ɛbhap.”
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ápú bhʉɛrɛ yɛ̌ chí mɔ́bhé amɔt, antɔŋ nɔkɔ bo bachak bɛ mánkʉ́ ɛnyumɔt mbɔ yi, chɔŋ ambak ansɛm ndǔ nkwɔ bhó mankɛm abhɛn Mandɛm achi Mfɔ wap. Kɛ mmu anɛ ábhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm mɛnkɛm, antɔŋ nɔkɔ bo bɛ mankʉ nkwɔ mbɔ yi, ǎbhák mǔngo ndǔ nkwɔ bho abhɛn Mandɛm achi Mfɔ wap.
Bǎkɛ́ kɛmɛ bɛbʉ́ amfay bɛbʉ́. Káysí nɔ́kɔ́ ká bɛkʉ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛrɨ bɛsí bo mankɛm.
Pɔ̌l ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ kɛnɔ́ ɛkɔ, sɛ́ká bɛ́ Mandɛm abhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɛsɛ́ sɛ́ndɔ́k sɛ́ngátí Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ntá bǒ atú Masidónia. Tɛ́mté wu, Mmɛ Lukas nchɛm nɛ bhɔ sɛ́tóŋti mmʉɛt bɛ́rɔ́ŋ arɛ́.   
Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ, kɛ̌ ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ áyaŋ bɛ́panyu, ámpányu chí ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm Acha ákʉ́.”
Bǎkɛ́ nɛmɛ ngó Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.
Kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛmɔ ɛnɛn nɛ́tɛ́mɛ́rí mmu ywɛka, chí ɛnyǔ nɛmɔ ɛnɛ́n nɛ́náŋ nɛ́tɛ́mɛ́rí bo báchák nkwɔ. Mandɛm apú nɔ́k bɛbhʉrɛ bariɛp ami, nɛ apú kwáy bɛrɔ yɛ̌ nɛmɔ nɛ́ntwɔ́ ntá mmu ywɛka ɛnɛn nɛtaŋa nɛcha yi. Mpok nɛmɔ nɛ́twɔ́ ntá mmu ywɛka, Mandɛm ǎtɔŋ yi mbi bɛ́ yi ántaŋ ancha nɛmɔ ɛnɔ, ante kpirí kɛ kwɛn.
Báfá, bárɔk ayak bághɔ Josɛ́f nɛ María. Bághɔ́ mmɔ̌rɛ́ nkwɔ́ bhʉ́rɛ́ amɛm ɛkʉbhɛ́ nɛnyiɛ nnya.
Ɛ́chí nɔ mbɔnyunɛ mbák Mandɛm ayap mmu nɛ ayɛt yi, apú pɛrɛ wupsi ntɨ ɛni nɛ mmu wu.
Mpú pɛrɛ bhɨŋɨ be bɛ́ bɔ̌bɛtok, mbɔnyunɛ mmɔ̌bɛtok apu rɨŋɨ nkaysi chi-bɛtɨk ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ̀. Mbɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe bɛ́ mamʉɛrɛ bha mbɔnyunɛ ngátí bé mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n ngókó ntá Ɛtaya mɛnkɛm.
Ntí nnya yɔ ámɔt ábhɔ́ŋ ɛrɛm ɛbhé ɛfʉɛt ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ báchyɛ nyaka yɔ ɛfʉɛt ɛnɛ ɛkway bɛway yɔ kɛ ɛfʉɛt ɛ́rɛ ɛ́gú. Bǒ mmɨk mankɛm bábhák maknkay, babho bɛghok chi nnya yɔ.
Nkɛ ghɔ́ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm amɛm ɛtɔk mbɔnyunɛ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛnɛ mánɨ̀kmʉɛt arɛ chi Mandɛm Acha Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm nɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn.
Bɛ́jwí ndɔŋ ɛpay, Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Símun, mmɔ̌ Jɔ̌n, ɔkɔŋ mɛ?” Símun akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛɛ, Acha, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ nkɔŋ wɔ.” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Babhɛri nɔkɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n aya.”
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák chi bɛ mǎndɔ́k ambɨ bɛbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Kristo, bɛ nɛ́mbák ɛkuti ɛyɛka mbɔ ɛnɛ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu ákɛ̀m awɔ́ bɛ anchyɛt bakɔŋ anɛ ádù nɛ ngó anɛ́ mbʉ́mbʉ átò.
Ɛ̌ti Kristo, nchí yɛ maŋák bɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ, yɛ̌ básɔ̀kɔti mɛ sɔkɔti, yɛ̌ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́taŋa taŋ ntá ya, nɛ yɛ̌ nchí bhɔŋ nɛnyok mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu, nɛ yɛ̌ báchyɛ̀ mɛ chi bɛsɔŋɔri. Ɛchi nɔ mbɔnyunɛ mpok anɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ kɛ nchí taŋ sayri. 
Ɛnɛ kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ mǎnkɔ́ŋ batɨ.” 
Mbák bakwǎŋwaŋ bárɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ sɛ́noko bhɔ. Sɛ́bhɔŋ yɛ́ mɛnoko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm árɛ̀m ɛ̌ti Mɔ́ywi ɛ́ncha ɛnɛ nkwǎ árɛ̀m mbɔnyunɛ yi achi Mandɛm. Nɛ Mandɛm até ntísiɛ ɛ̌ti Mɔ́ywi.
Bápɛ́rɛ ghɔ́ nɛnyɨkɨsí mmɨk nɛ́kwɛ́n, kpát mmɨk anɛ báté ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ arɛ́ anyɨkɨsi. Babhǐnywɔp ánɛ́nɛ ndǔ mmʉɛt yap tɛ́mté, ngɛm ɛnɛ́ báfé bǒkɛnɔŋ nɛ yɔ ɛ́káŋári ɛnkɛm, ɛ́kwɛ́nti amɨk.
“Bápu chyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó wáwák!”
Kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́fàkari chi bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm básɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ́mfú tɛtɛp.” Afɔ̌ kɛ̌ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ́ yi bábʉɛ́.
Chɔŋ ɛ́mbak nkwɔ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛchi nyaka mpok Lɔt. Bo mányìɛ̀ nyaka nɛ mányu nɔkɔ. Bákù nyaka mɛnyɨŋ nɛ abhɛn bɛ́ti mánti nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhap. Mbɔk bákwàŋ nyaka nɛnyíɛ́, abhɛ́nɛ́fú mánte nɔkɔ bɛkɛt.
Ɛpáfras nkwɔ ǎtò be bakak. Achi mmǔ ywɛka amɔt nɛ mǔbɛtok Yesu Kristo. Ǎnɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛka nɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛnkɛm mpoknkɛm bɛ mǎnsɛnɛ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm, nɛ bɛ mǎndɨŋɨ sayri yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ mǎnkʉ.
Yesu arɔ bhɔ arɔk. Ápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm ndɔŋ anɛ ajwi ɛrat, arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bǎbhʉɛ́t bɛbhʉrɛ kɛnɔ́? Bǎbhʉɛ́t bɛ́ywěmʉɛrɛ? Ɛ́kway nɔ! Mpok akway anɛ bákɛm Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mánchyɛ ntá bǒbɛbʉ́.
Mǔnti amɔt ndu bǒbati ɛsa nsɛm manwi aghati mɛ bɛ, “Kɛ́pɛrɛ di! Yɨŋɨ́ mmú anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Nkʉ Nnɛrɛ́kɛt anɛ bo Yúdah, Nnɛ́m ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Mfɔ Debhít. Anu asɔt awɔ́nɛm. Abhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛbhakari bɛ́bhánɛ́ tándrámɔt ánɛ́nɛ ɛkáti nɛnɛp.”
Yesu arɨŋɨ nkaysi yap. Arɛm ntá mmǔ wu bɛ, “Faté, twɔ́ fá ambɨ.” Mmǔ wu afate arɔk ate arɛ́.
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Nnáŋ njǎŋ mɛnyiɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ ɛnɛ́ nɛ bhe tontó kɛ nchwe ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ mányɨkɨsí batɨ̌ bǒ batí ɛtɔk amɛm, nɛ batɨ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm, nɛ batɨ bǒ mankɛm. Bákɛ́m yɛ Stífin barɔk bɛsí ɛchɛmɛ bǒ batí ɛtɔk nɛ yi.
Nɛ bápú durɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ mánsɔt ɛnyɨŋ mánkuti. Bádurɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ mánte chi ɛbhak ɛnɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛte yɔ bɛ́ mbaŋ ángɔ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ achi anywɔ́p.
Báchí bo abhɛn bákway nyaka bɛka yɛ̌ chí nɛwú ndu bɛpɛmɛ mɛ nkɛ́ gu. Puyɛ̌ chi ndiɛrɛ mɛ kɛ nchí kaka bhɔ. Bakwɔ́ bho abhɛn bapu bo Israɛl bákaka bhɔ nkwɔ.
Ngátí bhé yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ nkaysi Mandɛm nɛ yɛ̌ ɛ́mɔ́t mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɛsɛ.
Bɛ́bhó nɛ́nɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ bo bachi arɛ bati atay, chɔŋ ákɔ́rɛ́ ámbak nɛntɨ nap. Bati arat kɛka abhɛn bati apay. Bati apay kɛka abhɛn bati arat.
Bɛbho ndǔ mpok anɛ Mandɛm aghoko mmɨk, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi aghoko bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi nɛ ɛnyǔ mmu yi achi mbɔ Mandɛm. Ndu ɛchi bɛ, bápú ghɔ yi nɛ amɨ́k ntí apu anɛ bɔ bárɛ̀m bɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛpu nɛ bhɔ ndu bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm.
“Bǎrɨŋɨ ndǔ ɛbhé Moses ɛ́ghàti nyaka bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bɛ mmu ákɛ́ wáy ntɨ, nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áway mmu, bákʉ̀ manyé nɛ yi.
Kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ mɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ nkʉ. Ɛ́rɨ bɛ́ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn ɔ́kʉ̀ mɛ́mfú chi wɔmbɔŋ antɨ, kɛbhak bɛ mɛ̌jirɛ wɔ jirɛ.
Kɛ Banábas nɛ Pɔ̌l, bǒnto Yesu, bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǒbhɔ báyàŋ bɛkʉ, batɨ achɔŋti bhɔ amɛm kpát bádákáti ndɛn ɛ́yap amʉɛt. Bájɛt báchwe amɛm ɛká bo ɛyɔ nɛ bǎrí mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ,
Kɛ ngɔ bɛ ɛbhé ɛchak ɛ́chí ndǔ amʉɛt ɛya ɛnɛ́ ɛ́nù nɛ nkaysi aya, ɛ́nkʉ nɔkɔ bɛ mbak ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bɛbhʉɛt ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna.
Akʉ mǎmbɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm mmu akʉ yi ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ akʉ yi ambɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ kɛnókó, bɛ́ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ́mbák chi nɛ Mandɛm nɛ bɛ́ mǎmbaka ntɨ nɛ yi.
Kɛ mbák mmɔ̌bɛtok achi ɛbɛ́ptí mmu, andɛm nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, ‘Mbɨ́kɨ́ kaysi bɛ chɔŋ chi-bɛtɨk awa ampɛtnsɛm ndu nɛkɔ̌ ɛnɛn yi árɔ́ŋɔ́ áyák’,
Kɛ Yesu ayibhiri mmʉɛt aghati bhɔ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bárɛmɛ ɛ́pú chak.
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ bɛsɛ mankɛm abhɛn bájwítí bɛ Mandɛm achɛm bhɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo, bájwiti nyaka bhɛsɛ chi bɛ sɛmbak mbɔ bɛ sɛ́gu nyaka nɛ yi mpok yi agu?
Kɛ ntínso Mandɛm nɛya tontó. Atɔ́ŋ yɛ bhɛsɛ chi ɛkɔŋ ɛyi ɛnɛ ɛ́yá ɛ́chá.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Mpok Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm átwɔ̀ mbɔ Mfɔ nɛ kɛnɛ́m ɛki, bɔángɛl Mandɛm bátwɔ̀ nɛ yi, ambak chɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ yi nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi mɛnkɛm.
Kɛ chɔŋ nkʉ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛ, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ fá amɨk bɛfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bho.” Arɛm ntá mbɛ́ntí wu bɛ, “Nchí ghati wɔ, faté, pɔkɔ́ bɛkpaka bhɛ gurɛ!”
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, Yesu are kɔ amɛm bɛtɔk bɛgho nɛ ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk angati nɔkɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm ábhak nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap. Baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ apay bábhák nɛ yi.
Sakaría amak nɛ amɔ bɛ́ mánchyɛ́ yi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi ánsɨŋ arɛ́. Báchyɛ nɔkɔ yi ɛnyɨŋ asɨ́ŋ arɛ́ bɛ, “Nnyɛ́n ɛni chí Jɔ̌n.” Bɔ mankɛm babhak maknkay tontó.
Nɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú pɛrɛ ghók chɔŋ ɛyɔŋɔ́ nɛkɨ́ŋ nɛ bɛyɔŋɔ́ bakwǎy bakway, nɛ bɛyɔŋɔ́ babhaŋ, nɛ bɛyɔŋɔ́ mmba arɛ. Ndǔ ɛtɔk ɛgho ɛyɔ yɛ̌ mmʉ̌ ɛka apɛt apu. Ndaká nchwi bɛkɔk ámay nɛ batay bɛ́kɔ́k nchwi apu pɛrɛ chyɛ ɛyɔŋ.
Mandɛm aku bhe nɛ bɛyǎ nkáp afɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ kɛsɛm. Bǎrɔp chí basɛm Yesu Kristo. Bǎkɛ́pɛrɛ kʉ yɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka basɛm ntá bǒ mmɨk.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, sɛ́chí bɔ̌ Mandɛm nɛ́nɛ, yɛ̌ nɔ, bábhɨ́kɨ́re tɔŋ bɛsɛ ɛnyu sɛ́bhàk mburɛ́ mpok Kristo ápɛ̀tnsɛm. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ chi bɛ mpok yi ábhèsi chɔŋ sɛ́mbak mbɔ yi mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́ghɔ̀ ɛnyu yi achi.
‘Bě bho bǎbyàk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm árɛ̀m, yɨŋɨ́ ka mbaŋ sayri, mǎmbák maknkay, nɛ mǎngu, nɛ ntí bɛ́ mɛ̌kʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ndu manywɔp ayɛka, ɛnɛ yɛ mángátí bhe, bǎpú noko wawak!’”
Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhe apú kʉ mǎmbak basɛm bɛ mǎmpɛt mǎmbɔŋ bɛ́chay. Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ǎkʉ mǎmbak bɔ Mandɛm. Nɛ ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ yi bɛ, “Ɛta, Ɛtaya!”
Bǒbhɔ bárɔ́k mbaŋ ɛnkɛm bákáp ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bo Mandɛm bachi arɛ, nɔ chi, ɛtɔk ɛnɛ Mandɛm akɔŋɔ. Kɛ ngó áfú amfay ndǔ nɛbu ásɔ́ŋ bɔ kurukotok.
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎghɔ́kɔ́ ntá ya, nɛ ndu bɛ́kóŋo yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkaysi anɛ áfú ndǔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ́ bǎsɔrɛ ntá ya, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎghókó ntá ya, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎghɔ́ mɛ́ nkʉ. Nɛ chɔŋ kpák anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ ambak nɛ bhe. 
Kɛ bǒbhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bábhɨ́kɨ́ jwimɛm. Báchí mbɔ nyǎbhɨ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ kɛboŋ, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kó yɔ́ anti, ɛ́kʉ kʉ. Nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ kɛ bɛ́wày bhɔ.
Bɛyǎ ndɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ntɨ bɛ́twɔ bɛghɔ bhe mbɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛkʉ nɔ.
Ángɛl achak atwɔ atee kɛkwɔt ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap nɛ mɔnchan pú anɛ básɔ̀ŋ insɛns amɛm awɔ́. Báchyɛ́ bhɔ insɛns   bɛ yi anchɛm nɛ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Mandɛm mankɛm, amfay ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap ɛnɛ pú bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, bǒbati bo Israɛl abhɛn Yerúsalɛm bátó bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒnɛrɛ́kɛt Lɛ́vi ntá Jɔ̌n bɛ mámbɛ́p yi angati bhɔ ɛnyǔ mmu yi achi. Nɛ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú Jɔ̌n anyu mbɔ ntísiɛ.
Yɛ̌ndu bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ ntí anɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́rɛm bɛ mangway yi, bárɛm bɛ Páílet andɔ mangway Yesu.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, mpok Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ngɔrɛ́ wu ǎbhák anɛ agha? Ndu bɔ́ mankɛm, bati tándrámɔt, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap abhay nyaka yi.”
Hɛ́rɔd akaysi bɛ Yesu chi Jɔ̌n Njwiti ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́ nyaka ntá Jɔ̌n. Achyɛ́ nyaka ɛyɔŋ, bákɛ́m Jɔ̌n, bagwɔt, nɛ báfyɛ́ yi ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ bɛkoŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi Hɛródias áyàŋ. Hɛródias ayámbɨ achi nyaka chi ngɔrɛ́ Fílip, manɔ Hɛ́rɔd, kɛ Hɛ́rɔd ǎsɔt yi ndǔ nɛbhay.
Mǔnti amɔt arɛm yɛ ntá ya bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ bho nɛ́ nɛ bɛwɛt pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt? Báfú fá?”
Kɛ chɔŋ nchyɛ́ ntɛ́msí ntá bǒ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ́ bɔ bátòk. Nɛ ansɛm mpok, chɔŋ mámfa mántwɔ, mánchyɛ̀ nɔkɔ mɛ kɛnókó fá.’
Akʉ kpát are yáŋ bɛgʉɛp ɛbyɔk amɛm ɛkɛrákap awu Yerúsalɛm, kɛ sɛ́kɛ́m nɔ́ yi. [Mbʉ́ sɛ́taŋ yi bɛkoŋo ɛbhé, kɛ Lísias mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu atwɔ́ afɔŋɔ yí amɔ yɛsɛ nɛ bɛtaŋ,
Abhɛ́p yɛ anɛfú bɛ, ‘Ɔ̌kɛ́m ná?’ Akɛmɛ bɛ, ‘Bɛbhǎ nchwi bɛsa bɛtay.’ Mmǔ bɛtɨk wu achyɛ yí ɛkati barɛm arɛm bɛ, ‘Sɔt, wupsí sɨ́ŋ bɛbhǎ nchwi bɛsa mɛnwi ndǔ ɛnɛ ɛkɔ.’
Afɔ̌ kɛ Ánas átó Yesu nɛ ngɛm amɔ ntá Káyfas, mǔngo bachiǎkap. 
sɛ́mbák nyáŋá nɛ chak bɛsí bhi ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ nɛnkɛm. ndǔ manywɔp yɛsɛ́ fá amɨk ankɛm.
Afoŋori bɛbʉ́ bhap ndu básɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Yesu nɛ akɛ tɔ́ŋ bɛ́ bɛsɛ bo Israɛl sɛ́chí kɛkúrí nɛ bhɔ.
Tɛ̌ndu sɛ́rɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, sɛ́pu fɛrɛ amɔ. Yɛ̌ndu bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn nkwɔmʉɛt mɛ́mày mɛ́ndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, Mandɛm ǎkʉ̀ sɛmbɔŋ nɔkɔ bɛtaŋ bɛkɔ amɛm batɨ ayɛsɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Chɔŋ ntwɔ nkʉ yi antaŋ.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛká anɛ, mbák abhɔŋ ághɔ́ŋɔmɛn amɔt, ákwɛ́n nɔ́kɔ́ amɛm nɛpi ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt, andɔ, kɛfɛrɛ wu?
“Mmu amɔt abhak Damáskɔs anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Ananías. Abhak mmu anɛ ákòŋo Mandɛm sayri, mmu anɛ ábhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛsɛ́ bo Israɛl, nɛ mmu bo Israɛl mankɛm abhɛn báchí arɛ́ báchyɛ̀ kɛnókó.
mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mandɛm ákʉ bɔ bákɛ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ, áchyɛ bhɔ amɨ́k anɛ ápú ghɔ mbaŋ, nɛ batú anɛ apu ghok mbaŋ, nɛ nɔ kɛ bɔ bachi kpatɛ ɛchɔŋ.”
Mpú ghɔ yɛ̌ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chí nɛ mɛmbɔŋ. Kɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tɔ́ŋ bɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́, Acha aywǐntí kɛ̌ átàŋ mɛ́, puyɛ̌ chi mɛmbɔŋ.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mmǔ anɛ ápú fʉɛ́t ndǔ nnyǔbha ánchwe ndǔ nkwɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n, kɛ ǎko chí ɛbhak ɛ́chák anchwe amɛm, chí ngɛ́p. Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ, chí ngɛ́bhɛ́ ntantaŋ.
Júdas áchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, afʉɛ́t téé, abhɛnɛ Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ!” Abhɛnɛ yi.
Ɛnyu yɔ ɛnyu yɔ kpát mankɛm bati tándrámɔt bágú kɛrɔ yɛ̌ mɔ amɔt. Ndǔ ngwɛnti, ngɔrɛ́ wu nkwɔ agú.
Kɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, mbɔk bo Israɛl báfú Antiɔk anɛ atú Pisídia, báchák báfú Ikɔ́niɔm. Bákʉ́ bɛyǎ bo mánká nɛ bhɔ. Ɛkʉ bátɛ́mti Pɔ̌l nɛ batay, básu bárɔk bárɔ antí ɛtɔk nɛ nkaysi bɛ́ anáŋ agu.
bɛ ndu afyɛ́ yɔ bhɛsɛ amʉɛt, sɛ́kɛ́ bhak bɛbho bɛwɔ.
Sɛ́ghàti bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n sɛ́ghɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k mbɔ batísiɛ, nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu Mandɛm achyɛ́ ntá bo abhɛn bághòk yi achi ntísiɛ nkwɔ.”
Yɛ̌yi yɛ̌yi, sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ bɛrɨŋɨ tɛtɛp anɛ Mandɛm ákʉ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́.
Kristo arɛm bɛ, “Ɔpú yaŋ, mánchyɛ́ wɔ akabhɛ́nya nɛ akabhɛ́ mbwɔt, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ɛnyǔ akap achak, nɛ akabhɛ́nya ɛnɛ básɔ̀ŋ ango nɛ ɔpú bhɔŋ maŋák nɛ akap ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́. Báchyɛ̀ akap anɛ́ bɛkoŋo bɛbhé Moses. Arɛm nɔ yɛ̌ndu bo báchyɛ nyaka akap chi bɛkoŋo bɛbhé Moses.”
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌ghati bhe nɛ́nɛ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábháy ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ápú nkoŋo Yesu, nɛ mɛmbɔŋ kɛ̌ nchí ghati bhe yɔ́, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fú chí ntá Yesu Acha. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mǔnkwɔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Yesu, kɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu akɔŋ bɛ́chɔ́kɔ nɛ yí, nnɛ́m ákɛ́ rɔ yí ndǔ nɛbhay.
Tɛ́mté wu, mmu wu ataŋ. Asɔt bɛkpaka bhi abho bɛkɔ. Nywɔp ɛnɔ nɛ́bhak chí nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl.
Ɛnyumɔt kɛ ɛchi bɛ nɛ́nɛ, bo Israɛl bátàŋ ntí nɛ Mandɛm bɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ághɔ̀ bhe ntínso, ángɔ́ bɔ́ nkwɔ ntínso.
Nɛ mpok Mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n anɛ ngo abhesi, chɔŋ anchyɛ bhe akap anɛ́ árɨ́ achá, akap anɛ apu yibhiri ɛnyu.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔŋɔ bɛrɨŋɨ chí bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛ́bhʉrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm áyàŋ yí ambak. Ɛnɛ́ kɛ̌ ɛ́chí ɛbhé ɛnɛ́ nchí chyɛ bǒnkwɔ mankɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ ɛkɔŋɔ́ nkáp ɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm. Chí ɛ̌ti ngoŋó nkáp kɛ̌ mbɔk bho bárɔ́ mbi Mandɛm bárɔp ndǔ nɛměntɨ ɛ̌ti nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ ɛnɛn nɛchi nɛ bhɔ. 
Mpok nɛ mpok, nchí rɔŋ nyaka ndǔ bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt mɛnkɛm nchyɛ́ nɔkɔ bhɔ ntɛ́msi bɛkʉ bɔ mandɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Yesu. Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ bɛběntɨ nɛ bhɔ́ kpát ndɔk nɔkɔ bɛtɔk bo báchák ndu bɛ́chyɛ́ bhɔ nɛnyok arɛ́. 
Abhɨŋɨ batí apay, ató ntá Acha bɛ mámbɛ́p yi bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ anɛ Jɔ̌n árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ ǎtwɔ, kɛ chi bɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ mɛnoŋ mmu achak?”
“Yɛ̌ mmu apú durɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ansɔt ɛnyɨŋ ankuti, mbák ɛ́pú nɔ ante antɛn bɛkɔk. Ǎte yɔ chí nɛbhʉɛt anɛ babhɔŋɔ bɛte yɔ bɛ mbaŋ angɔ́ɔ́ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ achwe anywɔ́p.
Yesu abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt afɔ mɛ́ní?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛkpɔk tándrámɔt, nɛ bǎru nsi.”
Mbák mbɔŋ bɛdɛp awɔ antɨ chɔŋ nkʉ nɔ chi ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ.
Bɛyǎ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhak ndǔ mɔ́kɛt anɛ áchí amfay anɛ bhɛsɛ́ nɛ bhɔ́ sɛ́chɛ́mɛ́ arɛ́.
Ndak awu ákʉ́ bakoŋo bhi bátɨk bɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Chɔŋ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ ɛkɛt ɛyɛ ɛ́ngway mɛ.”
Pɔ̌l apɛt atat nɛ bǒnkwɔ Yesu abhɛn Kɔrint ndǔ bɛyǎ manywɔp. Arɔ yɛ bhɔ, asɔt achwǐnyɛ́n arɔk atú Síria nɛ Prisíla nɛ Akwíla. Báchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛtɔk Kɛnkreya, Pɔ̌l amu ntí bɛtɔŋ bɛ ǎbhʉ́rɛ́ bariɛp amɛn yi afyɛ́ bɛsí Mandɛm.
Ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ mmu anɛ ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo arɔp yɛ chi mmǔ nkɔ. Mɛnyɨŋ bɛsɨ́ bɛ́fʉɛt, ɛbhɛn bɛkɔ kɛ bɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́, achí nsɛmɛ́-bɛbʉ.
Arɛ́, Pɔ̌l aghɔ́ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antifú nɛ bɛti ndǔ mmu Masidónia áté ánɨ̀kmʉɛt andɛm nɔkɔ ntá yi bɛ, “Twɔ́ fá Masidónia kwak bhɛsɛ!”
Bábhɔ́ŋ maŋák tontó, nɛ báká bɛchyɛ yi nkáp.
Bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bábhó bɛsayti manɛ́mámɨk bhɔ bɛ, “Kusí ká!” Kɛ bákpɨk bare bɨk nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay bɛ, “Acha, Mmɔ̌ Mfɔ Debhít! Ghɔ́ bhɛsɛ ntínso!”
Mbák nyɛ́sɛ́ ɛnɛ nɛmɔt nɛ́tò wɔ ndǔ bɛbʉ́, fɛrɛ́ nɔ gʉɛp. Ɛ́rɨ bɛ ɔ́nɛ́m ɛpókómʉɛt ɛyɛ ɛ́mɔt ɛcha wɔ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́, mánsɔt mmʉɛt ɛyɛ nkɛm mámɛsɛ amɛm nɛpǐngo.
Mbabhɛri ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ arɔk aghati bɔPɔ̌l bɛ, “Bǒbatí báto ɛyɔŋ bɛ ndɔ be mǎndɔ́k. Bǎkwáy yɛ bɛrɔŋ. Mǎnkɔ sayri.”
Nɛnyiɛ Mandɛm chi mmu anɛ áfú amfay atwɔ, nɛ ǎchyɛ nɛpɛ́m ntá bǒ mmɨk.”
Bǎkɛ́ kpɔ́t manyé mmu bɛkoŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ́ yi ákʉ̀. Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkpɔt manyé sayri bɛkoŋo tɛtɛp Mandɛm.” 
Yi ǎyaŋ bɛpɛmɛ bo mankɛm nɛ ǎyaŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ándɨ́ŋɨ́ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo.
Básɔ́t Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n bákʉ bɔ́ báte bɛsí bhap, bábhɛ́p yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ndu nnyɛ́n agha bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn? Agha áchyɛ́ bhe bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ bhɔ?”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ́ basyɛpti bhe arɛ́, bák ká amɛm ɛkɛt ɛ́mɔt kpátɛ mǎndɔ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ.
Píta ataŋa, arɛm bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́rɛ̀m. Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ntí nɛ nnɛt arɛ́.” Arɛm nɔkɔ nɔ, afa arɔk ate ndǔ nyǔbha ɛnɛ sɛnta, [nkúbhɛ́ mpok ɛyɔ nnɛ́m nkɔk akók].
Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ mɛ̌kwáy mɛnɨkmʉɛt nta Ɛtaya antó mɛ tɛ́mté bɔángɛl mánja máncha nka byo nɛ ɛpay, mántwɔ́ mánu ntá ya?
Ayɛt bɛ̌ká bǒ nkwɔ́ abhɛn Kɔrint ndǔ babhi ankɛm. Sayri sayri, akʉ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo abhɛn bábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu bábhɔ́ŋ bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ. Nɛ achyɛ́ bhé akap bɛ́gháti bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n yí ákʉ́ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́.
Ntá mmu amɔt, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ǎchyɛ akap bɛchyɛ maníɛ́. Ntá mmu achak Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ anchyɛ akap bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́ yi andɨ́ŋɨ́.
Arɛm yɛ ntá nkoŋo wu bɛ, “Ghɔ́ máyɛ nɔ!” Nɛ bɛbho ɛwak ɛyɔ nkoŋo wu asɔt nnɔ Yesu arɔk ɛkɛt ɛyi nɛ yí. 
Mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́rɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bárɛ̀m, Jems afate abho bɛ́rɛm bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, ghók ká ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m!
Nɛ mpok bǎghókó nsóŋó-nɛnu nɛ ɛbyɔk, bǎkɛ́ chay. Mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛbhɔŋ bɛfakari, kɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́pú tɔŋ bɛ ngwɛnti mmɨk arɔp kɛkwɔt.”
Yesu abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Kɛ bě babhɔŋ bǎrɛ̀m bɛ mɛnchí agha?”
Angɛl wu aghati yɛ mɛ bɛ, “Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp nɛ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnoko. Mandɛm Acha mmu áchyɛ̀ Ɛfóŋó yi ntá barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ kɛ átó ángɛl bɛ́ ántɔ́ŋ bɔ̌bɛtok abhi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛ́fákári mandú mpok.”
Yesu arɨŋɨ nkaysi yap, abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎkàysi bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ?
Hɛ́rɔd abhɨŋɨ bǒbatí bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt. Abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bábhɔŋ bɛbhe Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò fá?”
Ndu ánɨ̀kmʉɛt, bɛsí bhi bɛ́bhó bɛyibhiri. Ndɛn ɛ́yi nkwɔ ɛ́yíbhíri ɛ́nkɔt nɔkɔ ŋwaŋwǎŋwaŋ.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mbɔ mbɔŋɔ́kɛt ǎrɨŋɨ nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp ɛnɛn ngɛ́p átwɔ̀, mbʉ apú rɔ mándak ɛkɛt ɛyi.
Sɛ́yámbɨ ndu áchwí sɛnok bɛrɔŋ Asɔs. Yímbɔŋ anaŋa atɨ nyaka bɛ́kɔ́ amɨk. Sɛ́ré rɔ́ŋ nɛ́ nkaysí bɛ́ Pɔ̌l arɔbhɛ tɛmɛri bhɛsɛ́ ɛtɔk Asɔs nɛ sɛ́nsɔt yí arɛ́.
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ mɛnkwɔ́ mbɔ̌ŋ bǒ abhɛn, mbák mángátí mɛ nkʉ ɛnyɨŋ, mbɔ̌ŋ bɛghok bhɔ. Nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ nkwɔ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu antɛnɛ ya abhɛn mbák ngati bhɔ ɛnyɨŋ, bábhɔŋ bɛghok mɛ́. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap anɛ ndɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, ‘Dɔ́k’, ǎrɔ́ŋ, nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ndɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, ‘Twɔ́’, ǎtwɔ. Nɛ mbák ngátí mmɔ̌bɛtok awa bɛ, ‘Kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ’, abhɔŋ bɛkʉ yɔ.”
Nɛ mbák bǎchwɔp ɛtɔk kɛ bo kɛsyɛpti bhe nɛ maŋák nɛ bɔ́ kɛka bɛghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎghàti bhɔ, fá ká arɛ́. Nɛ bǎpɛrɛ fá arɛ́, kwɛt ka mfok anɛ achi bhe bɛkak. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́mbak mbɔ ntísiɛ ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bákʉ́.”
Mǔnti ɛtɔk ǎkʉ̀ chi bɛtɨk Mandɛm ndu bɛkwak bhe. Kɛ mbák ɔ̌kʉ̀ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ, ɔbhɔŋ bɛ́chay yi mbɔnyunɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́pú ndɛ́ndɛm. Mandɛm achyɛ́ yi bɛtaŋ chi bɛ antɛmsi nɔkɔ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ.
Akɛmɛ bɛ, “Chí anɛ ághɔ́ yi ntínso.” Yesu aghati yɛ yi bɛ, “Dɔ́k yɛ́ kʉ mbɔ yí.” 
Nɛchwe báchwé, bágháti bhɔ bɛ, “Acha apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m tɛtɛp! Atɔ̌ŋ mmʉɛt ntá Símun!”
Kʉ ka bɛrɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ mbi bɛkʉ nɔ, mbɔnyunɛ bɛyǎ bo bákʉ̀ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ nɛ́nɛ.
Ɛ́tɔ́k baghɔk Yesu tontó, babho bɛbhɛp yi amɔt amɔt bɛ, “Acha, chi mɛ kɛ?”
Arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ bariɛp Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛfu tɛtɛp. Yi kɛmakati yɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm árɛ́mɛ́, kɛ abhɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm andɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ nɛ anchyɛ nɔkɔ yi kɛnókó.
Ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ batɨ kɛ ɛ́kwàk bhɛsɛ babhɔŋ sɛ́ndɨŋɨ bɛ sɛ́chi bɔ̌ Mandɛm mmu achi tɛtɛp. Ɛyɔ ɛ́fyɛ̀ bɛsɛ ntɨ ndǔ mpok anɛ sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm,
Mpú rɛm nɔ́ chí bɛ mɛ́yàŋ mǎntó mɛ́ akap áchák. Ɛnyɨŋ mɛ̌yáŋ chí bɛ́ mǎndɔ́k ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛrɨ, mɛ́máka ndǔ ɛbhɛ́n mǎnáŋ bǎkʉ́ ansɛm mbɔ mmǔ anɛ ámàka nkáp ndǔ anɛ́ yí ánáŋ áyámbɨ afyɛ́ amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́nkap bɛ nsáy yi ánja.
Mandɛm ǎyɛt mmɨk anɛ ányù manyiɛp amɛn ákwɛ̀n arɛ, ankʉ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ́ngó, nɛnchyɛ mbwɔt ntá mmu anɛ ákwáŋá yɔ.
Bo báchák báchí mbɔ mmɨk sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ anɛ mbwɔt achak akwɛnti arɛ́. Bághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm mánsɔt yɔ́ nɛ maŋák tɛ́mté.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Pú njap be bati byo nɛ apay? Yɛ̌ nɔ, mmǔ ywɛka amɔt abhɔŋ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ.”
Sɛ́tò manɔ achak nkwɔ nɛ Táytɔs. Nkwɔ́ bo Kristo mbaŋ ɛnkɛm bárɨ́ŋɨ́ yi sayri ɛ̌ti bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀ ndu bɛ́gháti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Achyɛ́ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn nsay ánù bhɔ, abók abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́, bárɔk amɔ amɔ.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛ́rɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ bɛtɔk mɛ́nu nɛ bɛtɔk bɛ́chák, bafɔ̌ ɛtɔk mánu nɛ batɨ̌ bafɔ̌ ɛtɔk.
Kɛ mmu anɛ ǎghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌rɛ̀m, yi kɛ kʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ndɛ́mɛ́, achí mbɔ ɛchɨŋtímu anɛ áté ɛkɛt ndǔ ɛ̌siɛ́p.
Bɛyǎ bho bápú barak bábáy yi antí, kɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bárɛ́mɛ́ kɛbhák ɛnyumɔt mbɔnyunɛ báchi nyaka bɛyɔŋ bɛyɔŋ.
Ɛ́taŋ bɛ́ mmu ánká bɛgu ɛ̌ti mmu anɛ achi chak, yɛ̌ndu mmu akway bɛka nɛwú ɛ̌ti ɛrɨ́tí mmu.
Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas báchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Ikɔ́niɔm, bárɔk báchwe ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl baghati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Yesu arɛ. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ bhɔ. Ɛ́kʉ́ bɛyǎ bo mánóko. Bo abhɛn mánóko bábhák bo Israɛl nɛ bo bɛtɔk bɛchak.
Tɨk nɔkɔ bǒnkwɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ngáti-nɛ́ wɔ. Yɛp nɔkɔ bɔ́ batú ndǔ nnyɛ́n Mandɛm bɛ́ mándɔ́ bɛ́kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí ɛ̌ti bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ chi nɛ bɛ́táká. Ɛyɔ̌ ɛnyǔ ɛpʉ́ítí ɛ́pú kwak yɛ̌ mmu, ɛ́twɔ̀ chí nɛ mɛnɛmɛ ntá bo abhɛn bághòk.
Yesu apɛt yɛ nsɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bhɔ bati arat, aghɔ́ ndu bábhʉ̀rɛ kɛnɔ́. Abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎbhʉɛ́t bɛbhʉrɛ kɛnɔ́? Bǎbhʉɛ́t bɛ́ywěmʉrɛ? Mpok akway anɛ bátì Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ntá bǒ bɛbʉ́.
Mankɛm bábho bɛdi kɛbhɔ mámbɛnɛ nɔkɔ yi nɛ mándiɛbhɛ nɔkɔ yi nɛkɔ bɛ, “Ɔ́nkɔ sayri.”
Kɛ bo Israɛl abhɛn bábhɨkɨ noko mbok Yesu bábho bɛrɛm bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́nyɨkɨsi batɨ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. Bárɔ́bhɛ bé chí ntɨ nɛ bhɔ.
Yesu asɔt brɛ́t achyɛ bhɔ. Akʉ ɛnyumɔt nɛ nsi.
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bhɔ bárɛm bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ akʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ fú chi ntá Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ apú noko nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt ɛnɛsɛ.” Kɛ bachak báré rɛm bɛ, “Ná mmu bɛbʉ́ ákway bɛkʉ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn?” Akɔrɛ akwɛn nɛntɨ ɛnap.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Nɛ́nɛ, ntɨ ɛna nɛ́pú amɛm kpák. Chɔŋ ndɛm bɛ yi? Chɔŋ ndɛm chí bɛ ‘Ɛta, fɛrɛ́ mɛ ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ ɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ́ kɛ?’ Wáwák! Mbɔ̌ŋ ɛ̌ti ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ kɛ ntwɔ́ fá amɨk!
Nkoŋo wu akokosi mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Acha, chí agha?”
Mbɔk ɛyap bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ bo Israɛl bátó Aleksánda ambɨ, bákáysi bɛ́ yí kɛ átwɔ́ nɛ ɛsɔŋɔri, ɛ́kʉ́ Aleksánda asá áwɔ́ amfay ndu áyàŋ bɛ́rɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ndu bɛ́táŋa mmʉɛt.
Nɛ mbák mmbá nɛnu ábhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ ɛyɔŋ sayri, agha ákway bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ chi mmbá nɛnu, antoŋti mmʉɛt bɛ́ ándɔ́k ɛbhɨ̌nɛnu?
Ɛkʉ bɔ bábhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhat mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo, mǔnti wap. Yí kɛ achi mbɔ ntí nɛ bǒnkwɔ bachi mbɔ mmʉɛt ɛyi. Básɔ̀t bɛtaŋ ɛbhap mɛnkɛm chi ntá yi nɛ ǎkʉ̀ bɔ mánchɛm mmʉɛt ndǔ nkwɔ amɔt mbɔ ɛnyǔ barɨŋ ákɛm byoŋómʉɛt. Bágò yɛ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi áyàŋ. 
dɔ̌ akap aywɛ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bo báchyɛ̀ akap, dɔ́k kpɨ́k kʉ mǎmbák ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ yi kɛ ɔ́mpɛtnsɛm ɔnchyɛ akabhɛ ywɛ ntá Mandɛm.
Yesu asɛmti bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́ ghati bo bachak ɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi.
Bǎrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak bɛkʉ mbɔnyunɛ bǎghɔ̀k bɛbhé.
Ngwɛnti yap chi mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́. Mandɛm awap chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fʉɛ̀t bɔ anyu ɛ́nchwe bɔ mɛniɛ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chák ɛbhɛn bɔ báfyɛ̀ ngoŋo arɛ́. Bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bághɔ̀ mámbɔ́ŋ chí ntíánwɔ́p, yɛ̌ nɔ, bɔ́ babhɔŋ bápànyu ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ. Nɛ bábhʉrɛ batɨ yap ndǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk.
Bǎbhɔŋ chí amɨ́k ntíako? Bábhɔŋ chí batú nɛmak-a?
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Wɔ bɛ́ mbák mɛ̌kwáy bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋɨ́! Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́kway bɛkɔ ntá mmu anɛ ánókó Mandɛm.”
Kɛ ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ mbʉ́ɛ́p ákʉ̀ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛ́kò tɛ amfay kɛ ɛ́nsɛp, abho bɛcháy nɛ abho bɛgurɛ anyɛ́n tɛ́mté. Abɨk yɛ arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Acha, pɛmɛ́ mɛ!”
Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mbi árɔ̀ Njiɛ Mɛnɔk Ólif ásɛ̀p Yerúsalɛm, ngɛ́mtáy bakoŋo bhi bábhó mɛŋák, mámbɨti nɔkɔ Mandɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bághɔ́.
Mbák mmu abhʉ́rɛ́ ntɨ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ báyaŋ, ɛyɔ ɛ́twɔ̀ yi chi nɛ nɛwú. Kɛ mbák mmu abhʉ́rɛ́ ntɨ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áyaŋ, Mandɛm ǎchyɛ yi nɛpɛ́m nɛ kpák.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap anyiɛ́ kpát ajwi. Baghɔk Yesu mányókóti nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛrɔbhɛ. Nɛ́jwí bɛkay byo nɛ bɛpay. 
Píta akɛmɛ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ bǒ mankɛm mámbʉ́ɛ́ wɔ, mɛ, mpú bʉɛ́!”
nɛ yi kɛbhak gum gum, nɛ nɛkɛ́mɛ́mʉɛt. Yɛ̌ ɛbhé ɛpu ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kaŋ bo bǎkɛ́ kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká afɔ ɛtɔk ɛgho, chɔŋ mǎngɔ́ mmǔ fú. Nɛghɔ́ bǎghɔ́ yí, ghatí ká yi bɛ Ntɔŋ arɛm bɛ mpok akway, nɛ yi abhɔŋ mɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ amɛm ɛkɛt ɛyɛ nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi”.
Yesu abhɛ́p yɛ bhɔ bɛ, mbák Mfɔ Debhít ǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ nyaka Mpɛmɛ́ rɛ́ bɛ Acha. Ná Achǎ-rɛ áyibhiri ambak ɛbhárɛ́mɔ ywi?”
Batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ abhɛn Rom bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ sɛ́twɔ̀, bábho bɛ́twɔ bɛtɛmɛri bhɛsɛ. Mbɔk ɛyap bátɛ́mɛri bhɛsɛ ndǔ Ɛsyɛ Apius, bachak ndǔ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́, “Bɛkɛrɛ́ Mankɔ Bɛrat.” Pɔ̌l ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ́, ɛyɔ ɛ́fyɛ́ yi ntɨ nɛ akaka Mandɛm. 
Bɛyǎ bhó bákóŋo yi arɛ, abú abhɛn mámè.
Bǒ nkwɔ́ Yesu abhɛn bachí bo Israɛl, nɔ́ chí abhɛn báfú Jopa nɛ Píta, bábhak maknkay tontó mbɔnyunɛ bághɔ́ bɛ Mandɛm achyɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nkwɔ.
Bǒbati ɛsa nsɛm manwi abhɛn báchí chɔ́kɔ́ bɛsí Mandɛm ndǔ mɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ bákwɛ́n amɨk báchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó
Mmǔ anɛ áté mɛ ntísiɛ achi nyáŋá, nɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi árɛ̀m ɛ̌ti ya ɛbhɔŋ mɛnwɔp.
Píta arɛm bɛ, “Acha, ndáká yí mpú kwáy bɛ́kóŋo wɔ nɛ́nɛ? Yɛ̌ chí nɛwú, nká bɛ́gu ɛ̌ti yɛ.”
Kristo yímbɔŋ ákʉ́ bhɛsɛ́ bo Israɛl nɛ be bho bǎpu bo Israɛl bɛ sɛ́mbák kpák nɛ batɨ. Mpap achí nyaka nɛntɨ ɛnɛsɛ mbɔ nkók anɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ bhɛsɛ. Afɛ́rɛ́ mpap ayɔ mpok yi ágú, akʉ sɛ́rɔp chi mmu amɔt.
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ maŋák bɛ Stɛfánas nɛ Fɔtunátɔs nɛ Akaikɔs bátwɔ fá, mbɔnyunɛ nɛtwɔ́ wap achi mbɔ bhɛ bě nkwɔ bǎtwɔ.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ Seséria, báchyɛ ɛkáti ntá gɔ́bhanɔ, bárɔ Pɔ̌l amɔ yi.
Bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́ndɔ́ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo abhɛn bábhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm bákʉ̀, bɛ́ sɛ́ndɔ́ bɛfyɛ ngoŋo ndu mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ̀ bo maŋák fá amɨk. Bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ nkwɔ bɛ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ fá amɨk, sɛbhɔŋ bɛ́rɨŋɨ ndu sɛ́kɛ̀mmʉɛt bɛ́kʉ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí chak bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ bɛbhʉɛrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm áyàŋ.
Nɛ ndǔ mpok ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Ɛláisha, bɛyǎ bǒ ɛbhaŋákwa bachi nyaka amɛm ɛtɔk Israɛl. Kɛ yɛ̌ amɔt Ɛláisha ábhɨ́kɨ́ bu, ɛbhɨ́kɨ́fʉɛt chi mmǔ ɛtɔk ɛchak, Náman, mmu Síria.”
Bɛbhé kɛ bɛ́chí yɛ̌ nyaka mbɔ mmǔ anɛ ábhàbhɛri, ányurɛ nɔkɔ bhɛsɛ, kpatɛ mpok anɛ Kristo átwɔ́, bɛ sɛ́nkwáy bɛbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm ɛ̌ti sɛ́sɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ yi.
Bábho bɛ́bɨk bɛ, “Dɛm mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí.”
Ajɛt arɔk ambɨ, akó amfǎy ɛnɔk ɛnɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Síkámɔ ndǔ mbi anɛ Yesu ákɔ̀ arɛ ndu áyàŋ bɛghɔ yi.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk báré way nkwɔ yi, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Ápɛ̀mɛ nyaka bo báchák, kɛ apú kway bɛpɛmɛ mmʉɛt yi!
Baghɔk abhi barɛm yɛ ntá yi bɛ, “Mhm! Nɛ́nɛ ɔ̌rɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ kpoŋoroŋ nɛ sɛ́jwimɛm. Ɔpú pɛrɛ rɛm kɛpɨ ndǔ bakay!”
Ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔ́t nɛ nɛtwɔ́ wa, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm. Mǎnáŋ mǎngɔ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n-nɛ ngátí bhe bɛ́fàkari, dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mpok anɛ Kɛfɔ Mandɛm kɛ́twɔ arɔp kɛkwɔt.
Mandɛm ákʉ́ nyaka ɛbhé ɛntwɔ bɛ bo mángó sayri bɛ bɛbʉ́ bhap bɛyǎ tontó. Kɛ mpok bo bákʉ̀ nyaka bɛyǎ bɛbʉ́ mandɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, Mandɛm atɔ́ŋ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛ́yá mbɔŋ ɛ́chá,
Yesu arɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bárɛ̀m. Ɛ́kʉ́ arɛm bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎsɔŋɔri ngɔrɛ́ nɛ? Akʉ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ ntá ya.
“Mbák mmu áyàŋ bɛ́bhak nɛ mɛ apú kwáy bɛbhák nkoŋo wa mbák abhɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ mɛ ánchá ɛtayi nɛ máyi, nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi, nɛ bɔ̌bhi, nɛ, bɔ̌mayi abhɛn babhakanɛm nɛ abhɛn baghɔrɛ́ nɛ ankɔŋ mɛ ancha yɛ chí mmʉɛrɛ́ yi.
Bɛyǎ bhó bare fú mbaŋ nɛ mbaŋ mánkoŋo nɔkɔ Yesu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi árɔ̀ŋ. Mbɔk ɛyap báfú atú Gálili, báchák báfú Dikápolis, nɔ chi atú bɛtɔk byo, báchák báfú Yerúsalɛm, báchák báfú atú Judɛ́ya, nɛ abhɛ́nɛ́fú báfú ɛbhěnyɛ́n nɛgho ɛnɛn babhɨŋɨ bɛ Jɔ́dan.
Nyamwʉɛ́t ɛya kɛ áchí mbɔ̌ŋ nɛnyíɛ́ mɛnyiɛ, nɛ manoŋ ama kɛ áchí mbɔ̌ŋ mmɛ́m amɛn mɛnyu.
Bɛyǎ bo bare fu ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk abhɛn bachí kɛkwɔt nɛ Yerúsalɛm, mándɔkɔ nɔkɔ nɛ bǒmame, nɛ abhɛ́n bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri bhɔ. Bɔ mankɛm bataŋ. 
Mbɔ̌ŋ ɛrɨ́tí mbi bɛkʉ ɛsayri bɛtɨk fá yɛ̌ndu bɛyǎ bo mánù bɛchyɛt mɛ mbi.
Nkwǎ ǎkwáy bɛ́bhʉɛ́rɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ nyǎbhɨ, kɛnɛn, nnya ɛnɛ́ ɛ́sù mɛniɛ amɨk nɛ ɛnɛ ányɛ́n, ankʉ yɔ́ ɛ́ngók yi, nɛ bo mánáŋ bákʉ́ nɔ.
Yesu ákʉ́ nɔkɔ nɔ, achwe anywɔ́p. Bakoŋo bhi bábhɛ́p yi ansɛm ansɛm bɛ, “Ndaká yí sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛbok ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ?”
Shɛ́la mmɔ̌ Kaínan, Kaínan mmɔ̌ Afásad, Afásad mmɔ̌ Shɛ́m, Shɛ́m mmɔ̌ Nóa, Nóa mmɔ̌ Lámɛk,
Nɛ́ chi nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛ́n nɛ́fú amfay nɛ́twɔ́ fá amɨk. Nɛ́pú mbɔ ɛnɛ́n bachǐmbɨ bhɛka mányíɛ́ nyaka, bágú. Mmǔ anɛ ányíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn ǎbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.”
Píta arɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛchák ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm ndǔ bɛcháy bɛkɛmɛ bhɔ tontó.
Bo abhɛn bábhàbhɛri bakók, bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari, bárɔk ɛtɔk ɛgho nɛ mbaŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi kɛkwɔt ntiɛ́t ntiɛt bágháti bho.
Kɛ bo Israɛl, bo báfyɛ́ nyaka bɛtaŋ ndu bɛbhʉrɛ bɛbhé, bɛ mámbák chak bɛsí Mandɛm, bɛkʉ nɔ ɛyɔ ɛ́bhak chi ndɛ́ndɛm.
Bafɔ batay bágú. Amɔt achi nɛpɛ́m. Amɔt achi mfɔ nɛ́nɛ. Mbák chí anɛ ajwi tándrámɔt abhɨ́kɨ́ twɔ. Ánáŋ ántwɔ́ ǎbhák Mfɔ ndǔ mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok.
Kɛ yɛ̌ndu bɛyǎ bo mánóko nyaka Yesu, bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm kpoŋoroŋ bɛ mánóko, ndu báchày bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bɛ bákɛ́ bók bhɔ ndǔ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkímʉɛt.
Atɔ́ŋ mɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí nyaka bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, ákú ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɔ, mbɔ ɛnyǔ nsɨ́ŋɨ́ mandú ngátí bhe ɛ̌ti mbɔk mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ.
Kɛ mbák chí bhe, bǎtwɔ̀ kɛkwɔt nɛ njiɛ Síɔn nɛ yɔ chi ɛtɔk Mandɛm mmu achi nɛpɛ́m. Ɛtɔk ɛyɔ chi Yerúsalɛm anɛ amfay. Ngɛ́mtay bɔángɛl Mandɛm báchí arɛ́ ndǔ ɛpǎ maŋák.
Baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ báfú ndǔ nnɛm báre rɔ́ŋ ntiɛ́t ntiɛt mángwɛrɛ nɔkɔ nɛ bábhak maknkay tontó. Bɛcháy bɛkʉ bɔ́ kɛrɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ ntá mmu. 
Chɔŋ antɔ́ŋ yɛ be mɔ́kɛt anɛ áchɨ́kɨ́ amfay, ndǔ ɛkɛrɛ́mfáy. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́yàŋ ɛ́chí amɛm. Toŋtí ká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ arɛ́ ntá yɛsɛ.”
“Bǎchí mbɔ ngáŋ ntá bǒ mmɨk mankɛm. Kɛ mbák ngáŋ ábhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔ́ŋ manyɨŋti mi, ná bákway bɛkʉ wu ampɛt ambak ɛrɨ́tí ngáŋ? Bápú pɛrɛ kway bɛkʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ nɛ wu. Árɔp chi ɛnyɨŋ bɛto nɛfí ɛbhak ɛnɛ bo báfʉɛ̀t mánjati nɔkɔ wu.
“Nchí nyurɛ bo abhɛn nkɔ́ŋɔ́, nchyɛ́ bhɔ ntɛmsi. Fiɛ́ yɛ ka bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak, mantɨk nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, bǎpú yaŋ mɛ ɛ̌ti bǎghɔ́ bɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay, kɛ ɛ̌ti brɛt anɛ mǎnyiɛ́ bǎjwi.
Nɛ ɔ́kɛ́ ka sɛ́nchwe ndǔ nɛmɔ ɛnɛn nɛ́kʉ sɛ́nkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́, kɛ fɛrɛ́ bhɛsɛ ndu amɔ mbʉ́mbʉ.’
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákòŋo Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achí mmɔ́ Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛ́bhʉrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ nɛ́pú chyɛ mmu áchák ɛsɔŋɔri ndǔ ɛni nɛpɛ́m, Yɛ̌ chí mmu Israɛl, yɛ̌ chí mmu anɛ ápú mmu Israɛl, nɛ yɛ̌ chí bǒ nkwɔ́ Mandɛm.
Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ bǎchi. Mmu ǎghɔ be ankaysi bɛ bǎchi chak nɛ bho, kɛ batɨ yɛka ájwí amɛm nɛ bapu nɛ bɛbʉ́.” 
Ɛ́fákárí nyaka ɛnyu yɔ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ághátí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya andɛm ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp. Aisáya arɛm nyaka bɛ:
Nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɛgú-nnya ɛchi, arɛ́ kɛ̌ kɛnɛn ɛkɛ́n kɛ́nyìɛ bɛgú nnya kɛ́chɛmti. 
Mmɛ Jɔ̌n, kɛ ngókó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ ngɔ́ bhɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k. Mpok anɛ ngókó nɛ ngɔ́ bho, nkwɛ́n bɛkak ángɛl anɛ átɔ́ŋ mɛ bhɔ ndu bɛ́chyɛ yi kɛnókó.
Bǒ ɛtɔk Lída nɛ Shárɔn babhak arɛ́. Bɔ mankɛm bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndu Aénias ákɔ̀, mánókó Yesu Acha.
Sɔt yɛka mpok bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ básɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ́kɛ́ fakari nɛ bhe. Nɔ́ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ básɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ,
Sɛ́bhɔ̌ŋ bǒ batí nɛ manywɔp anɛ bátaŋ manyé. Mbák Dɛmɛ́triɔs nɛ bǒ ɛka bábhɔŋ ndak nɛ mmu, mántwɔ́ arɛ́ nɛ wú bɛ mántáŋ.
Bo abhɛn bárɔ́ŋɔ́ ntá Yesu nɛ bǒmame bhap, mánɨkmʉɛt bɛ́ yi andɔ bǒmame mántɔk yɛ̌ chi nkokoŋ ndɛn ayi. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánú átɔ́kɔ́ nkokoŋ ndɛn Yesu, ataŋ.
Mǎnáŋ mǎmpay ɛkáti ɛnɛ ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka, kʉ ká mámpay yɔ ntá nkwɔ́ Laodísia nkwɔ. Pay ká nkwɔ ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ ntó ntá nkwɔ́ ɛtɔk Laodísia mpok anɛ bɔ bátó yɔ ntá yɛka.
Mmǔ nkáp amɔt afǔ nyaka ɛtɔk Arimátia. Aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Josɛ́f. Abhak nkoŋo Yesu amɔt. Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ beku,
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu ákɔ̀ bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm nɛ bakoŋo bhi bati byo nɛ apay, asɔt bhɔ nɛpak, abho bɛghati bhɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fákari nɛ yi.
Yɛ̌ mmu apú kwáy bɛ́twɔ ntá ya mbák Ɛtaya mmu átó mɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ ya yi ntá ya. Nɛ mmu anɛ átwɔ́ ntá ya, chɔŋ nkʉ yi ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ndǔ nywɔp ngwɛnti.
Yesu yi bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ táŋ batɨ kɛka mántáŋ be. Bǎkɛ́ rɛm bɛ mánchyɛ́ batɨ ntɛ́msi, nɛ mbák bǎpú rɛm nɔ, bápú rɛm bɛ manchyɛ bhe ntɛmsi. Foŋorí nɔ́kɔ́ ka batɨ nɛ chɔŋ mámfoŋori nɔkɔ bhe.
Bě bǒnkwɔ mankɛm bǎchí mmʉɛt Kristo nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka achi ɛ́pókómʉɛt Yesu.
Ná nɛ ngɔrɛ́ nɛ, mmɔ́ Ábraham   anɛ Satan ágwɔ́rɛ́ ndǔ mamiɛ́ nɛku nɛ arat. Ɛ́chí ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ bɛfɛrɛ yi ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt kɛ?”
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi, abhɨŋɨ yí arɛm bɛ, “Mmá, nɛme ɛnɛ nɛ́may.”
Pɔ̌l akaka bhɔ́ aghati bhɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ nɛ́ntɨ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mpok yí ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk Mandɛm nɛntɨ nap.
Dɨŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt kɛ ɛrɨ ɛcha. Yɔ́ kɛ̌ María áyábhɛ́, nɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛsɔt yɔ ntá yi.”
Sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mmʉɛt ayɛsɛ́ anɛ fá amɨk achí mbɔ bɛ́tɛm. Mbák bɛ́tɛm ɛbhɛn mɛ́nkwɛ́n, Mandɛm ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ ɛkɛt ɛkɔ awu amfay. Puyɛ̌ chi bakwǎŋwaŋ kɛ bághókó yɔ, mbɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ áchyɛ̀ mmʉɛt nkɔ yɔ, nɛ yɔ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
bɛ ankʉ sɛmbak chak bɛsí Mandɛm ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi. Akʉ nɔ bɛ́ sɛmbak bɔ̌bhi, sɛ́mbáká ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ sɛmbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ beku, ɛnɛ́ mmok ánɛ́mɛ́, bo báré sɔt bǒmame mankɛm nɛ abhɛn bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri mándɔk nɔkɔ ntá Yesu nɛ bhɔ́.
Mbɔ mbɨ́kɨ́ kʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay bɛsí bhap ɛbhɛ́n yɛ̌ mmu áchák ábhɨ́kɨ́ re kʉ, mbʉ́ bákway bɛtaŋa mmʉɛt bɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ bɛbʉ́. Kɛ bághɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n nkʉ́, yɛ̌ nɔ bápàp mɛ, nɛ bápáp Ɛtaya.
Nɛbho mbó bɛ́gháti bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ atwɔ́ ntá yap nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́fákári nyaka nɛ bhɛsɛ ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt.
Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batú ángók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ághàti bɛka bǒnkwɔ́.”
Bǎkwày mɛ́nyiɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nnya anɛ bátì ɛsiɛ́, kɛbhɛ́p mbák chí nnya anɛ báchyɛ́ mbɔ akap ntá njɔ̌ fú. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ bɛ mǎnkʉ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chɔŋti batɨ yɛka amɛm.
Ɛliákim mmɔ̌ Mɛléa, Mɛléa mmɔ̌ Mɛ́na, Mɛ́na mmɔ̌ Matáta, Matáta mmɔ̌ Nátan, Nátan mmɔ̌ Debhít,
Ji bo abhɛn bápú rɔ bɛbʉ́ bɛsí bǒ mankɛm bɛ bakoŋo Yesu bachak mámbɔ́ŋ bɛcháy.
Bákɛ́m Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n bárɔ́k báfe, nɛ tɛ̌ndu beku mɛnaŋ bɛ́gháká nyaka, barɔ bhɔ arɛ tɛ ntɨnywɔp.
Kɛ ǎtó bhɔ nɛfí bɛ́ mándɔ́k mángátí bho ɛnyu Mandɛm abhak nɛ bo mbɔ Mfɔ wap nɛ bɛ mámbú bǒ mame.
Pɔ̌l arɔk yɛ ambɨ bɛ́chɔ́kɔ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ ndu mmíɛ́ nɛ bataŋ átándát, antɔŋ nɔkɔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Tímɔti, kɛ́m bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn báchyɛ́ wɔ sayri. Ɔ́kɛ́ chwe ndǔ kɛpɨ ɛkɛn kɛpu chyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó nɛ ɛpʉ́ítí nti ti ɛnɛ ɛpu kɔ ndɔ́ŋ ámɔt nɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Bo bákaysi bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ chi nɛrɨŋɨ́, ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pú nɔ.
Hɛ́rɔd ǎyàŋ nyaka bɛrɛm mángwáy Jɔ̌n, kɛ are cháy bǒ abhɛn yi achi mǔnti wap. Bo Israɛl mánoko nyaka bɛ Jɔ̌n achi ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.
Kɛ mbák mmu ywɛká abhay ngɔrɛ́, abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ bɛbʉ́. Nɛ mbák mɔ́nkwɛn ngɔrɛ́ abhay nnɛ́m, abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ bɛbʉ́. Kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ́ bǒ abhɛn bábhày nɛbhay bábhɔ̀ŋ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri fá amɨk, nɛ nchí yáŋ chí bɛkʉ bɛ bǎkɛ́ chwe ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Ɛ́nkʉ mámbaka ntɨ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp ɛ̌ti nɛpɛmɛ́ nɔ tɛndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt, nɛ Mandɛm ápú sense.
“Ntínso nɛ́kɛ̀m mɛ nɛ bǒbhɛn. Báchí fá nɛ mɛ ndǔ manywɔp arat, nɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ mɛnyiɛ.
Yesu Acha arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Bǎghok nɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ntaŋá manyé anɛ ápú chak árɛ́mɛ́?
Mandɛm achyɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ mbi bɛfyɛ nkú mwaŋmwaŋ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bakwap.” Ndɛn ɛyɔ ɛ́te ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chi chak ɛbhɛn bo Mandɛm bákʉ̀.
Mbák ɛnyǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ wɔ ɔ́nyìɛ ɛ́chyɛ̀ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ ɛsɔŋɔri, nɔ ɔpú pɛrɛ kʉ mɛnyɨŋ nɛ ɛkɔŋ. Ɔ́kɛ́ rɔ ɛnyǔ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn ɔ́nyìɛ nɛ́ntwɔ́ nɛ mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ ntá ntɨ mǔnkwɔ mbɔnyunɛ Kristo agu nyaka ɛ̌ti yi nkwɔ.
Bǎrɛ̀m bɛ́ bábhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Kɛ puyɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ kɛ̌ ɛ́kwàk mmu. Nɛ bǎrɛ̀m bɛ́ bǎbhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, kɛ puyɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ kɛ̌ ɛ́kwàk mmu ántáŋ ndǔ barak Mandɛm.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́fákári nɔ́kɔ́, bǒmame báchák ɛtɔk ɛyɔ ɛnkɛm bátwɔ́ ntá Pɔ̌l mankɛm abú bɔ nkwɔ.
Kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ndǔ mpok anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́. Kristo kɛ áyámbɨ ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Mpok yi apɛt átwɔ́ kɛ̌ bǒbhi bápɛt chɔŋ nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Yesu ayibhiri mmʉɛt aghɔ bhɔ ndu bákòŋo yi. Abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎyàŋ yi?” Bákɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Rábay, ɔ̌chɔkɔ fá?” [Rábay chi Ntɔŋ]
Bo bárɛ̀m bɛ agha arɨŋɨ kpɨk bhɛsɛ́, yɛ̌ nɔ bo bárɨŋɨ bhɛsɛ sayri. Ɛ́chí mbɔ bɛ sɛ́gùgu, yɛ̌ nɔ, sɛ́chi nɛpɛ́m. Báchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ ɛsɔŋɔri, kɛ sɛ́pú gú.
Nkáysí bɛ bǎrɨŋɨ ntó ɛnɛn yi ató nyaka ntá yɛsɛ bo Israɛl bɛ chɔŋ ankʉ bo mambak sayri nɛ yi ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Kristo akʉ. Yi Yesu achí Acha amfǎy bo mankɛm.
Yesu ayɨŋɨ yí, arɛm bɛ, “Ɛ́bèmʉɛt tontó bɛ mǔnkáp anka Mandɛm ambak Mfɔ ywi.
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kwáy bɛrɛm ɛ̌ti yɛka nɛ nsɔt bɛtaŋ be. Kɛ mpú kʉ nɔ, mbɔnyunɛ mmu anɛ átó mɛ ǎbhʉɛrɛ bariɛp ami, nɛ ndiɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ághàti mɛ kɛ nchí ghati bǒ mmɨk.”
Josɛ́f abhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Ɛ́kʉ́ yí kɛyáŋ bɛchyɛ María ntíánwɔ́p. Akʉ yɛ ntɨ bɛway nɛbhay nɛ María ansɛm ansɛm.
Mmǔ amɔt aghati Yesu bɛ, “Máyɛ nɛ bɔ̌mayɛ báchí nɛfí téé, báyàŋ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ wɔ.”
Mbák yɛ mbɔ̌ŋ mmɔ́ amfɛrɛ be ndǔ kɛsɛm, chɔŋ mǎmbak ngǎngaŋ tɛtɛp.
Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛsɔŋɔri yi. Ɛ́kʉ ǎchɔkɔ ambo bɛbɨk, ɛ́ngʉɛp yi amɨk, ɛ́nkʉ yi ande wɛt ɛ́fɛ́n ɛ́mfu nɔkɔ yí anyu. Nɛ ɛ́taŋ kɛ ɛ́ndɔ yi. Ɛ́dɛ̀n yi, ɛ́mfyɛ yi mɛnɨ amʉɛt.
Bápɛ́rɛ ghɔ, mmu anɛ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́sɔŋɔri atwɔ́ achwe amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí are bɨk bɛ́,
Mandɛm akʉ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ ndu bɛchyɛ nnyɛ́n Yesu kɛnókó bɛ bǒ abhɛn báchi amfay nɛ abhɛn báchí fá amɨk, nɛ abhɛn báchí ndǔ ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap abhɔŋ bɛ́tɛ́p mánɛ́n bɛsí Yesu anchyɛ yí kɛnókó.
Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, Ɛláija anáŋ atwɔ kɛ bo bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yi. Bákʉ́ nɛ yi mbɔ ɛnyǔ bákɔ́ŋɔ́. Nɔ́ kɛ̌ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm nkwɔ ábhɔŋ chɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri amɔ yap.”
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi abhɛn bachi arɛ́ baghɔ nɔkɔ nɔ, báfú, bárɔ́k. Báte ɛyu, batɨ bɛway Yesu. 
Kɛ sɛ́kɔ́pti bhe mbɔ ɛnyǔ nnɔ ákɛ̀m bɔ̌bhi.
Ɛ̌! Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɔ chi bɛtaŋ-ɛ! Foŋorí ká mɛ bɛ mpú kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ ntá yɛka. Chɔŋ ndɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm mbɔ ɛchɨŋtímu. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ mmu ándɛp awɔ antɨ, mɛ nkwɔ mɛ̌kwáy bɛdɛp awɔ antɨ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ.
Mmǔ ǎkway yɛ bɛbhɛp bɛ, “Tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm áyap mbɔ ɛnyǔ nchí rɛm nɛ, ndaká yí yi ájì yɛ bho? Nɛyap anɛ yi áyàp bho apu tɔŋ bɛ mmu ákʉ̀ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ásɔ̀t bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛkʉ mmu ankʉ?”
Nchí nɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yap. Mpú nɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti mmɨk nkɛm. Nchí nɨkmʉɛt chi ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ bɔ́ báchí bǒ bhɛ.
Mmu anɛ akɔŋ bo apú bhɔŋ maŋák mpok bákʉ́ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ, ǎbhɔŋ maŋák mpok bo bákʉ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛchí chak.
Áfú nɔ́kɔ́, akɛpɛrɛ kwáy bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ bhɔ. Are mak nɛ amɔ́ ntá yap. Bághɔ́ bɛ aghɔ̌ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k anti fúú amɛm ɛkɛrákap.
Kɛ bo Israɛl abhɛn Tɛsalónika bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ Pɔ̌l ǎghati Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛtɔk Bɛ́roa nkwɔ́, bárɔ́k arɛ́ mányíkɨ́si batɨ̌ bo, bɛ mánchyɛ́ bɔPɔ̌l ɛsɔŋɔri.
Mpok yɔ, bakoŋo Yesu báre yá mándɔkɔ nɔkɔ chi ambɨ. Bɛ́táŋá bɛ́kwɛ́n. Bo Israɛl abhɛn bárɛ̀m ɛyɔŋ Grik nkwɔ báré nywinti bɛ abhɛn bárɛ̀m chi ndiɛrɛ ɛyɔŋ bo Israɛl bákɔ̀rɛ mɛnyɨŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛwak kɛfyɛ́ ntí ndu bɛchyɛ mánkwɛ́sɛ́ bhap.
Bɔ́ kɛ báchi bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham nɛ Áisek nɛ Jekɔ́p. Nɛ bábhé Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò chi ɛtɔk ɛyap. Bábhé yi chi ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛrɛ wu. Yí Kristo, achí Mandɛm nɛ abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm. Sɛ́mbɨ́tí yi mpoknkɛm. Amen.
Ayibhiri mmʉɛt, ayɨŋɨ, aghɔ́ ndǔ ngɛ́mtay bho bátwɔ̀ ntá yi. Abhɛ́p Fílip bɛ, “Chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔŋ brɛt bɛ́ku fá anɛ ákway bǒbhɛn?”
Bǒ mankɛm bábhák maknkay, nɛ bábho bɛbhɛp batɨ bɛ, “Ɛnɛ́ ɛnyu ɛchi ná? Chi ɛnyǔ nɛtɔŋ ɛnɛn nɛkɔ kɛ? Mmǔ-nɛ abhɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn ásay bɛfɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ nɛ mɛ́ngok yi!”
Mpok anɛ chi nɛ nnɔ bághɔ́ yi, ɛbhak bhɔ chi ɛnyɨŋ maknkay. Nnɔ abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Mɔ́wa, mbʉ ɔbhɨkɨ kʉ ɛtayɛ nɛ mɛ ɛnyunɛ!”
Kɛ batɔŋɔ́ nse bhɔ bárɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mmʉɛt ɛyap ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ, mbɔ nyǎbhɨ ɛnɛ́ bábhe chi bɛ mankɛm mangway. Bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́way bhɔ mbɔ nyǎbhɨ.
Mmu anɛ akaysi chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ báyàŋ bɛkʉ achí mǔmpap Mandɛm. Apú sɛptimʉɛt bɛkoŋo bɛbhé Mandɛm, nɛ apú kway bɛkʉ nɔ wáwák.
Bo abhɛn bábú nyaka amɛm manyu barɔk nkwɔ bɛ mántaŋ bɔ. Báfú ndǔ nɛwú nɛ ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú, bátáŋ bɔ mankɛm bɛkoŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ́.
Kɛ bárɔ́k ambɨ bɛkɛmɛ bɛ, “Ǎkɔ̀ atú Judɛ́ya ankɛm antɔŋ nɔkɔ bho ndu mɛ́nyɨ́kɨ́si batɨ̌ yap amɛm bɛ mángʉ́ɛ́p ɛsɔŋɔri ɛtɔk. Akʉ nɔ́, bɛbho atú Gálili kpát bɛ́gháka fá Yerúsalɛm.” 
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ átoŋti mmʉɛt ndu bɛjɛt ntiɛt anɛ bɛbhɔŋ akap, ǎkɛm mmʉɛt ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Bákʉ̀ nɔ ndu bɛbhɔŋ akap anɛ átàt ánchɔŋti. Kɛ akap anɛ́ sɛ́nù bɛbhɔŋ, chí akap anɛ ábhak mpoknkɛm.
Acha amɔt kɛ sɛ́tòk. Bɛsɛ mankɛm sɛ́noko chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt. Sɛ́bhɔŋ chi nɛjwiti nɛmɔt.
Nsɔt yí ntwɔ́ ntá bakoŋo bhɛ, kɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛbu yi.”
Stífin chí mmu anɛ Mandɛm átɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu, achyɛ yí bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ. Stífin akʉ bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay nɛ atɔ́ŋ bɛrɨŋ bɛsí bo.
Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ̀ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nɛ ǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay nɛntɨ ɛnɛka, ǎkʉ̀ nɔ chi ɛ̌ti bǎbhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé Moses kɛ? Kɛ chi ndǔ bǎghókó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ mǎnókó?
Nɛ ndǔ yi ákò baghɔkɔ́ bhi báré chyɛ yi kɛnókó. Bápɛ́t yɛ nsɛm Yerúsalɛm nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák.
Bǎkʉ̀ nyaka sayri. Agha áchɛ́rɛ́ bhe mbi bɛ bǎkɛ́pɛrɛ koŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp?
Básɔ́t ɛkotákátí ɛnɛ́ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛgo Yesu arɛ báchyɛ́ yímbɔŋ ámpɔ́kɔ́. Apɔkɔ kpát bárɔ́k bágháká ndǔ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ Golgóta, nɔ́ chi “Nɛbhʉɛt Ɛnkɔ́nti.”
Mǔnkwɔ Fárisi wu aghɔ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, are kaysi amɛm ntɨ ɛni bɛ, “Mbɔ mmǔ-nɛ achi ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm tɛtɛp, mbʉ arɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyǔ mmu anɛ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ átɔ̀k yi achi. Chí ngɔrɛ́ nɛkɔ.”
Bɔ mɔ́mayɛka anɛ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ bátò bhe bakak nkwɔ.
Ɛchi yɛ bɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ árɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ndǔ nɛbhay, akwɛ̌n bɛrwɔp. Nɛ mmǔ anɛ ábháy ngɔrɛ́ anɛ nnɛ́m árɔ́ ndǔ nɛbhay, akwɛ̌n nkwɔ bɛrwɔp.” 
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Twɔ́ ká nɛ bhɔ.”
Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nchí ghati bhe chi bɛ, yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábèntɨ nɛ mɔ́mayi Mandɛm ǎtaŋ yi. Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásɔ̀kɔti mɔ́mayi mbɔ bɛrɛm bɛ, ‘Wɔ ɔchí agha?’ Básɔ̀t yi bɛsi acha manyɛ́. Nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɛ̀m ntá mɔ́mayi bɛ, ‘Wɔ ɛchɨŋtímu’ chí mmu anɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛmɛsɛ amɛm nɛpǐngo.
Báré way Yesu way. Kɛ Yesu abók bɔ́ mankɛm atɛ́n nɛfí. Asɔt chimɔ nɛ nnɔmɔ nɛ bakoŋo bhi bati arat arɔk, achwe ɛbhak ɛnɛ mɔ́wu áchí bhʉrɛ́.
Mmǔ anɛ áyàŋ bɛpɛmɛ mmʉɛt, chɔŋ anɛ́m nɛpɛ́m ɛni. Kɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áká mɛ́nɛm nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛ̌ti ya, chɔŋ ambɔ́ŋ nɔ́.
Nɔ́, kɛ ɛ́chi nɛ be nkwɔ́. Nɛ́nɛ basɛ́mɛ́ ajwí be antɨ, kɛ chɔŋ mpɛt ngɔ́ bhe, nɛ mpok yɔ chɔŋ mǎmbɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ maŋák, nɛ yɛ̌ mmú apu kway bɛfɛrɛ mɔ́ amɛm batɨ ayɛka.
Kɛ mpok mmok áfú, ásɔ́ŋ yɔ ndǔ bakaŋ ayi ábhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛchwe amɨk sayri. Anɨŋti, awɔsi.
Nɛ mbɔ Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ kpɔt manywɔp yɔ bɛ akɛ ya, mbʉ yɛ nkwǎŋwaŋ amɔt apu rɔp nɛpɛ́m. Kɛ Mandɛm akpɔt mpok ɛsɔŋɔri yɔ mbɨŋ ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn yi áyábhɛ́ bɛ mambak abhi.
Ɛ́kʉ mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ wu arɛm nɛ mmʉɛ́t ɛyi bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ nkʉ ná? Chɔŋ ntó mbɔ̌ŋ mmɔ̌ntɨ wa. Yɛ̌ yí, bábhɔŋ bɛ́chyɛ yi kɛnókó.’
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mmʉɛrɛ wa, dɔ́k ambɨ, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́twɔ́ bɛkʉ, kʉ yɔ́.” Tɛ́mté wu, bǒ abhɛn Júdas átwɔ́ nɛ bhɔ bárɔ́k téé bákɛ́m Yesu bábáyti.
Nkúbhɛ́ mpok ɛyɔ, ɛrɛmɛ́ nɛnyɨkɨsǐmɨk ɛ́kwɛ́n, nɛ ɛkɛt ɛ́mɔt ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ bɛkɛt byo amɛm nnɛ́m ɛtɔk, ɛ́báy mmʉɛt amɨk. Nká bho tándrámɔt bǎgu ndǔ nɛnyɨkɨsǐmɨk ɛnɔ. Bɛ́cháy bɛ́kɛ́m abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ gu. Báré chyɛ kɛnókó ntá Mandɛm mmu achi amfay.
Bo mankɛm abhɛn bághòk mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi árɛ̀m bábhák maknkay ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi arɨŋɨ nɛ ɛnyǔ ɛnɛ yi ákɛ̀mɛ bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bábhɛ̀p yi.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, mmǔ amɔt átwɔ́. Áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Josɛ́f. Abhak mmǔ ɛtɔk Arimátia. Achí nyaka mmu anɛ ákòŋo Yesu. Ǎcháy nyaka bo Israɛl ndu yi achi nkoŋo Yesu. Afʉɛ́t arɔk ntá Páílet bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, anɨkmʉɛt bɛ Páílet andɔ yi ámfɛ́rɛ́ mmʉɛt Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Páílet achyɛ yi bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ nɔ. Josɛ́f arɔk yɛ, afɛrɛ mmʉɛt Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí.
Bɛrɨ ɛbhɛka bɛkɛ fú chi ndǔ mmʉɛt bɛsɔbhɛri nɛ bati bɛ́ghóko nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ pú nɛ ndu bɛfyɛ bɛrɨ́tí ndɛn.
Dɔ́k ká mǎngati nɔkɔ bhɔ bɛ, ‘Mpok arɔp kɛkwɔt anɛ Mandɛm abhak nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap.’
Yesu abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Nnyɛ́n ɛnɛ nɛchi bɛ yi?” Akɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Nnyɛ́n ɛna nɛchi bɛ ngɛ́mtáy, mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́yǎ tontó.”
Mpok Yesu árɔ́bhɛ́ chí nɛ bakoŋo bhi, bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ndaká yí sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛbok ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ?”
Abhɛn ɛchɨŋti bati atay babho bɛrɛm ntá abhɛn kɛ́ŋwáŋ bɛ, ‘Kwak ka bhɛsɛ nɛ mbɔ bawɛt ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́. Ɛbhɛsɛ́ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́twɔ̀ nɛmɛ.’
Mpok yi arɛmɛ nɔ, Ananías mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm, achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ bo abhɛn bachi kɛkwɔt nɛ Pɔ̌l mándɛp nnyu yi.
Ápú koŋo kɛnkɔ̌ mmu. Ǎbʉɛ̀ yi bʉɛ, mbɔnyunɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi.”
Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm mmu ákʉ̀ bɛ bo mámbáká ntɨ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ, ánkʉ́ bɛ batɨ yɛka ánjwí nɛ maŋák nɛ kpák ndǔ mǎnókó yi. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ, bǎkway bɛrɔŋ ambɨ bɛbhaka ntɨ nɛ yi ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ tontó tonto. 
Mbɔ̌ŋ barɛm bɛkwɔ ntá bo abhɛn amɨ́k anɛnɛ bhɔ nɛ ntá bǒbhɨ, nɛ ntá barɨŋɨ ɛ́káti nɛ abhɛn babhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ ɛkáti.
Kɛ́ wakari mɛ́nyáŋa mmu amɔ antí ndu bɛ́kʉ yi mǔnti bǒ nkwɔ́ kɛ́ka ɔ́mbɔŋ mbát ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bo bachak. Kɛ́m mmʉɛt ɛyɛ bɛ ɔ́kɛ́ kwɛn ndǔ bɛbʉ́.
Mpok mɔ́wu árɔ̀ŋ ntá Yesu, ɛfóŋó yɔ ɛpɛt ɛ́gʉɛp yí amɨk, ɛkʉ yi are wɛt. Kɛ Yesu ásáy ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ, bɛ ɛ́ndɔ́ mɔ́wu. Yesu abú yi, akɛmɛ ntá ɛtayi.
Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ ɛnɛ bo Israɛl ɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t, Yesu akó, arɔk Yerúsalɛm ndu mɛnyiɛ ɛpǎ ɛyɔ.
Kɛ Yesu Acha apú nɔ́k bɛbhʉrɛ bariɛp ami. Chɔŋ ankʉ batɨ antaŋ be amɛm, ankuti bhe bɛ mbʉ́mbʉ ákɛ́ kʉ be yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Kɛ faté, dɔ́k amɛm ɛtɔk ɛgho. Chɔŋ mángati wɔ́ arɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kʉ.”
Kɛ yɛ̌ ɛmbák chi bɛsɛ, yɛ̌ chí ángɛl kɛ ághátí bhe mbok anɛ áchí kɛkúrí nɛ anɛ sɛ́ghátí bhe, ɛyak ɛmbak nɛ yi.
Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha mántɔŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, mánchyɛ bhe kpák. 
Yesu aghati yɛ mmu wu bɛ, “Faté, dɔ́k ɛbhak ɛyɛ. Nɛka ɛnɛ́n ɔbhɔŋɔ nɛ mɛ nɛ́kʉ ɔtaŋ.” 
Abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ nyaka yɛ̌ bɛbʉ́, nɛ yɛ̌ mmu yi abhɨkɨ rwɔ.
Bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn bábʉɛ̀ bátáka mbankɛm báre kɔ mángati nɔkɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu.
Baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ báchwe amɛm nnɛm, bághɔ ɛsakámu chɔkɔ ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm ɛyap nɛ nkú pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt. Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bɔ́ tontó.
Ɛnɛ́ yi áyɛ̀t bhɔ, arɔ bhɔ́, Mandɛm asɔt yi ámpɛ́tnsɛm amfay.
Nɛ bɔ mankɛm mányú nkúbhɛ́ manyiɛp maknkay amɛn áfù ntá Mandɛm. Nkúbhɛ́ manyiɛp mɛ́rɛ́ kɛ̌ bɔ́ mányú mbɔnyunɛ manyiɛp amɛn áfú ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ ɛsɛ́n sɛ́kɔ̀ nyaka nɛ bhɔ kɛ̌ mányú. Nɛ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ ɛsɔ sɛ́bhák Kristo.
Nɛ mbák bǎkaka chi bǒ abhɛn mǎnyìɛ nɛ bhɔ, nɔ́ bǎkʉ yi? Yɛ̌ chí bǒ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bákʉ̀ nɔ.
Bɔ̌bha, bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ bɔ mandɛm nsé.
“Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm Acha achí nɛ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ, ayap mɛ bɛ́ ngátí Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho. Ato mɛ, bɛ ntwɔ́ ngátí bo abhɛn bachi ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ kɛsɛm, bɛ chɔŋ mámfɛrɛ bhɔ arɛ. Nɛ bɛ́ chɔŋ amɨ́k anɛnɛ manɛ́mámɨk, nɛ bɛ chɔŋ mánchyɛ ngǎngaŋ ntá bo abhɛn batɨ̌ bakwǎŋwaŋ mányìɛrɛ bhɔ amɨk.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk báchɔ́kɔ betí betí báká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛnyǔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ bɛ mángwáy Yesu.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ Ɛta akɔŋ Mmɛ Mɔ́ywi, nɛ ǎtɔŋ mɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yímbɔŋ ákʉ̀. Nɛ chɔŋ antɔŋ mɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn bɛcha ɛbhɛn, bɛ manyu ánchók bhe.
Sɛ́kway bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́sɨ̀kɨ ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo.
Mmǔ wu abhɛ́p nkáp anɛ bákɛ̀m yi, kɛ yɛ̌ mmu wap kɛ kway bɛkɛmɛ anɛ́ yi ákɛ̀m. Afɔ̌ kɛ̌ yi afoŋori bhɔ́ mankɛm, afɛrɛ ntɨ ndǔ nkáp wu. Ghatí yɛ́ mɛ, ndǔ bati yap ápay, ntɨkɨ mmu ákway bɛkɔŋ mpwɔnkáp wu ancha anɛfu?”
Kɛ mbɔk bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn bachi bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, báfáte babho bɛ́rɛm bɛ, “Bábhɔŋ bɛsyɛp bɔ, mángati bhɔ bɛ mámbʉrɛ bɛbhé Moses.”
Agháká nɔ́kɔ́ árɛ́, aghɔ́ ndu Mandɛm átɔ́ŋɔ́ bǒbhɔ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi, abhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ maŋák, abho bɛ́fyɛ́ bhɔ́ ntɨ bɛ mámbak tɛtɛp nɛ Yesu, mánte kpirí mpoknkɛm nɛ ntɨ nɛnkɛm.
Kɛ mbɔŋ bɛcháy bɛ bǒfú bákway bɛrwɔ bhe mbɔ ɛnyǔ Satan ásɔ́rɛ́ nyaka bapu mi arwɔ́ Ifa, ɛ́nkʉ nkaysi ayɛka ampɔkɔ bhe mǎngurɛ ɛbhɨ, kɛpɛrɛ koŋo mbi Kristo nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt ɛnɛn nɛchi pɛ́pɛ́p.
Arɛm ntá yap batí arat bɛ, “Basɛ́mɛ́ ajwí mɛ antɨ mbɔ bɛ ǎway mɛ way. Chɔkɔ́ ká fá, mǎmbak pě nɛ mɛ.”
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛ́pú chak bɛsɔt nɛnyíɛ́ bhɔ mánchyɛ́ ntá mmú.”
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bǒ abhɛn bárwɔ̀ batɨ bachi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak. Bábhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ Yesu Kristo atwɔ nyaka fá amɨk mbɔ nkwǎŋwaŋ. Ɛnyǔ mmǔ wu achi mmu amɔt ndǔ mpáy bho abhɛn bárwɔ̀ bho, nɛ achí mǔmpap Kristo.
Yí kɛ achí akap anɛ́ ápɔ̀kɔ bɛbʉ́ bhɛsɛ. Nɛ ɛ̌ti yi, Mandɛm ǎfòŋori bɛbʉ́ bhɛsɛ, nɛ puyɛ̌ ndiɛrɛ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ, kɛ bɛbʉ́ bo mankɛm.
Mmɛ kɛ nchí ɛrɨ́tɨ́ Mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n aya, nɛ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n aya árɨŋɨ mɛ,
Arɔk yi nɛ́kúmʉɛt atɔk yi ndǔ awɔ. Mbʉ́ɛ́p wu ámay. Afate akʉ nɛnyíɛ́ abho mɛne Yesu.
Ngɔ́ Yesu Acha téé ndǔ ághàti mɛ bɛ, ‘Kʉ ayak dɔ̌ Yerúsalɛm. Bǒ abhɛn fá bápú noko chɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́ghàti bhɔ́ ɛ̌ti ya.’
Bábhó bɛbɨk mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Dɔ̌ mángwáy yi! Dɔ̌ mǎngwáy! Dɛm mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí!” Páílet arɛm bɛ, “Ngó Mfɔ ywɛka ndǔ ɛkotákátí?” Bǒbati bachiǎkap bákɛ́mɛ bɛ, “Mfɔ amɔt kɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́, nɛ chí Sísa.”
“Kɛ sɔt ka mpok! Chɔŋ mánkɛm be mánchyɛ ntá bǒbati ɛtɔk bɔ́ mántaŋ be. Chɔŋ mángwapti bhe amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt. Chɔŋ mǎnte bɛsí bɔgɔ́bhanɔ nɛ bafɔ ɛ̌ti ya bɛ mǎngátí bhɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti ya.
“Bǎchí ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ntá bǒ mmɨk. Ɛtɔk ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí amfǎy njiɛ ɛ́pú bhɛsɛ.
Nchí yáŋ bɛ́gháti be ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhɛ́bhɛ́ mɛ ndǔ ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ bǎsɨ́ŋɨ́. Nká nɛ bhe bɛ́ ɛ́rɨ́ mmu ánchɔ́kɔ́ kɛbháy ngɔrɛ́.
Páílet abhɛ́p yɛ Yesu bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí nɛ́ Mfɔ bo Israɛl?” Akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́.”
Mmǔ amɔt abhɛp yi bɛ, “Acha, chɔŋ Mandɛm ampɛmɛ chi bǎru bho?” Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ,
Bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ghatí bhɛsɛ, ɔchí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò?” Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mbák ngátí bhe bǎpú noko;
Mmɔ̌ bɛtok amɔt anɛ mǔngo bachiǎkap abhak arɛ́. Atú mɔ́mayi kɛ̌ Píta ákpɔ́rɛ́ nyaka. Yí wu abhɛ́p Píta bɛ, “Pú ngɔ̌ nyaka wɔ amɛm mɔ́nkɨ nɛ yi?”
Bǎkɛ́ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndu bɛtɔŋ mmʉɛt bɛ́ bǎchá batɨ, kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛsɛptimʉɛt ntá batɨ mbɔ bɛ bɔ́ báchá yi.
Yesu asáy Ɛfóŋó yɔ bɛ, “Kusí! Fú yi amʉɛt!”
Bě bɛchɨŋtǐ manɛ́mámɨk! Ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm kɛ̌ ɛ́chá mɛnyɨŋ gol, kɛ mɛnyɨŋ gol kɛ bɛcha ɛkɛrákap ɛnɛ ɛkʉ́ mɛnyɨŋ gol mɛ́mbak nyáŋá?
Nɛ ɛ́chí bɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm amfɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ághókó ndǔ kɛsɛm antɛn mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ bɔ mɛ́mpɔ́ɔ́ bɛ bɔ nkwɔ mɛ́mbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛbhɔŋ kɛnɛ́m mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɔ̌ Mandɛm bábhɔŋ kɛnɛ́m.
Mǔngo wu achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mánkʉ ɛ́kárɨk ɛ́nté. Ɛ́té nɔ́kɔ́, bɔ́ nɛ Fílip básɛp báchwe anyɛ́n, Fílip ajwiti yí.
Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, Mandɛm asɔt yi apɛtnsɛm amfay. Báte mánjɨŋɨ nɔkɔ yi ndu árɔ̀ŋ. Nɛbháŋ nɛ́kúti yi, bɔ kɛpɛrɛ ghɔ́ yi.
Ɛnɛ́ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n bághàti bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛnyu yɔ, mbɔk bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ mǔnti babhabhɛri ɛkɛrákap nɛ mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bátwɔ́ ntá yap.
Nkúbhɛ́ ɛbhé ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ nyaka bɛ ɛnkʉ mɛ mbɔ̌ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛ́twɔ́ mɛ chi nɛ nɛwú.
nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ ɛfóŋó yɔ ɛ́kɛ́m yi, ɛ́gʉɛp yi amɨk, bɛfɛn mɛ́mfu nɔkɔ yi anyu. Mpok yɔ, ande nyiɛ amɛn nɛ anɔkɔ. Nnɨk baghɔkɔ́ bhɛ mmʉɛt bɛ́ mámbók yɔ ɛ́ndɔ́ yi, kɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛkʉ nɔ.”
Ngók ɛyɔŋ ndu ɛ́ghàti mɛ bɛ ‘Píta, faté, wáy nyiɛ!’
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Mbɔ ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ akap anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ bho, nɛ mmu anɛ árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́ bɛ, ‘Chiɛ mɛ manyiɛp’, mbʉ ɔrɛm mɛ nchyɛ́ wɔ manyiɛp amɛn áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m.”
Aghati bɔ́ mankɛm bɛ, “Fú ká kpɨ́k, mɔ́nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ gú. Ǎbhʉrɛ chí kɛnɔ́.” Bɔ́ mankɛm báré way Yesu way.
Yesu abhɛ́p bɛ, “Agha átɔ́kɔ́ mɛ́?” Bǒ mankɛm bataŋa. Píta arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Ɛ̌tá, bɛyǎ bo bákàp wɔ nɛ mányìɛrɛ wɔ!”
Nɛ mbák sɛ́ndɛ́m bɛ, ‘Bɛ́fǔ nyaka ntá nkwǎ’, bǒ mankɛm bátɛmti bhɛsɛ nɛ batay mangway, mbɔnyunɛ bɔ́ mankɛm mánóko sayri bɛ Jɔ̌n achi nyaka ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.”
Kɛ ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ mbɔ nɛ́ntɨ́bhɛti, Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas babho mɛnɨkmʉɛt mánkway nɔkɔ bakwáy ndu bɛbɨti Mandɛm, batɨ̌ bǒkɛnɔŋ bachak mángoko nɔkɔ.
Yesu abhak maknkay mbɔnyunɛ bǒ ɛtɔk ɛyi bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ yi. Yesu are kɔ ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk abhɛn bachi kɛkwɔt, antɔŋ nɔkɔ bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Mpok yɔ nkɛm, Píta are dɛp nɛkok. Mánɛ́nɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mbǐnywɔp, bághɔ́ bɛ chi Píta tɛtɛp.
Bafu nɔkɔ, bakɛm Sɔstɛ́nes mmu anɛ achi nyaka mǔnti ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛyɔ bádɛ́n nɛfí acha manyé. Yɛ̌ nɔ, Galío akɛ fyɛ́ ntí arɛ́.
Páílet akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɔkáysí bɛ nchí mmu Israɛl? Bǒ ɛtɔk ɛyɛ nɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm kɛ bákɛ́m wɔ batwɔ ntá ya nɛ wɔ. Mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́kʉ́ chi yi?”
Mmu anɛ ápábhɛ́ mɛ, apap Ɛtaya nkwɔ́.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎgwɔ́rɛ́ fá amɨk, Mandɛm ǎgwɔt awu amfay. Nɛ ɛnɛ́ bǎkáŋárí fá amɨk, Mandɛm ǎkaŋari yɔ awu amfay.
Nɛ mmǔ ywɛka amɔt ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi, andɔk antɨ́k yí nɛfí andɛm bɛ, “Ɔ́nkɔ sayri, Mandɛm anjɛt wɔ ɔ́mbɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ ndɛn nɛ nɛnyíɛ́”, kɛ yí kɛchyɛ yi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áchɛ́bhɛ́, nɔ́ akwak yi ndǔ ntɨkɨ mbi?
Bɔangɛl bárɔ bhɔ, bapɛtnsɛm amfay. Babhabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n babho bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Sɛ́ndɔ́k ká Bɛ́tlɛhɛm sɛ́ngɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari, ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm akʉ sɛndɨŋɨ.”
Ɛ́kʉ bɛyǎ-bhap mánóko Yesu Acha. *Manɛ́m baghɔrɛ́ Grik nɛ bɛyǎ babhakanɛm mánóko nkwɔ́.
Bɔ̌ma, bɛsɛ sɛ́pú yɛ bɔ̌ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ achí nsɛm, sɛchi chi bɔ̌ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ apu nsɛm.
Nɛ mǎnáŋ mángók ɛyɔŋ ɛya, báfù ndǔ manɛm ayap. Abhɛn bákʉ́ nyaka bɛrɨ ndǔ mmɨk nɛ, máŋɛmɛ, manchwe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti, nɛ abhɛn bákʉ́ nyaka bɛbʉ́, máŋɛmɛ mámbɔ́ŋ ntɛmsi.” 
Kɛ nchwi áchák akwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk ndɨ́ndɨ́, agó achyɛ bɛyǎ nchwi. Ayá acha anɛ bápɨ́ ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛtay.” Ndǔ ngwɛnti, Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ áyàŋ bɛghok, ántá batú angok sayri.” 
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ yɛ bɛbhɔŋ maŋák ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, yɛ̌ndu nɛ́nɛ, bǎkway bɛbhɔŋ bɛyǎ bɛsɔŋɔri nɛ mamɔ mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok.
Ɔ́kɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ́ ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ basɨ́ŋ amɛn áchí amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm tɛ kɛ̌mbɔ́ ɛkɛ. Basɨŋ amɛn achi Nyáŋá ǎkwáy bɛ́kwak wɔ ɔ́mbɔŋ kɛboŋ bɛbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo nɛ ɔ́mbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m.
Mpú rɛm nɔ chi bɛ mámfɛ́rɛ́ ntu amʉɛt bǒ bachak mámbay be anti.
Fílip arɛm bɛ, “Acha, tɔ́ŋ bhɛ́sɛ́ mbɔŋ ɛtayɛ. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ɛnɛ sɛ́yàŋ ɛ́pú.”
Bɛ́rɛ́m tɛtɛp, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ɛ́rɔp chi mbɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mfɛ́rɛ́ ndu áchwí nto anyɛ́n bɛ ntí wa ándɔp mɛ̌mbát mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo. Bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ Yesu Kristo Acha wa achá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna nɛ́nɛ. Ɛ̌ti mɛ́yàŋ bɛrɔp nɛ Yesu, mfɛ́rɛ́ ntí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛ́n nkáysí nyaka bɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ Mandɛm ámpɛ́mɛ́ mɛ. Nɛ bɛ́rɔp ntá ya chi mbɔ mɛ́nyɨ́ŋ ɛbhɛn bátó ndǔ ɛbhwɔ́rɛ́ mɛnyɨŋɨ́.
Bɛyǎ bǒmame bábhák arɛ́; manɛ́mámɨk, nɛ babhɛ́nti, nɛ abhɛn bachi bhʉrɛ́. Báré noŋ bɛ nnyɛ́n nɛ́mboŋ. Mpok nɛ mpok, ángɛl Mandɛm ǎsɛ̀p nyaka amɨk amboŋ ɛ̌ntɨ́ŋnyɛn ɛyɔ. Nɛ mmǔ nɛme anɛ áyámbɨ ásɛ́bhɛ́ amɛm, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ nɛme ɛnɛn yi abhɔŋɔ nɛ́may.
bábhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Mmɔ̌ ywɛka nɛ, bárɛ̀m bɛ́ amɨ́k anɛmɛ yi tɛ̌ndu nɛbhe ɛni? Ɛ́fakari ná kɛ yi ághɔ̀ mbaŋ nɛ́nɛ?”
Báchyɛ́ yɔ mbi bɛ́panyu nɛ bɛ́rɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm. Báchyɛ́ yɔ mbi bɛbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay bo ndǔ bataŋ bɛsa bɛpay nsɛm apay.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm, nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses bághok nɔkɔ nɔ, báre yáŋ mbi bɛway yi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ báchày nyaka ngɛ́mtay bo abhɛn báchi arɛ, nɛ ntí bɛ́ bǒbhɔ bachi nyaka maknkay tontó ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu átɔ̀ŋ.
Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bakokosi bhap mankɛm. Nɛ mbok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ ataka ndǔ bɛtɔkɔ́ njiɛ mɛnkɛm atú Judɛ́ya.
Nɛ yí kɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛ ankʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, yɛ̌ chi ɛnɛ́ fá amɨk nɛ yɛ̌ chi ɛnɛ amfay, bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛpɛt bɛbhak ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ yi ɛ̌ti nɛwú Mɔ́ywi ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Nɛ́nɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́kwày bɛbhak ndu kpák ndu nté anɛ yɔ́ ɛchi nɛ Mandɛm. 
Bǒ ɛtɔk Bábilɔn, ɛ́bɛp ntá yɛka ɛcha! Bákù nyaka batu pú nɛ anɛ silbha nɛ batǔ mɛnyɨŋ bɛsɔbhɛri mmʉɛt ɛbhɛn bɛ́kɔ̀t ŋwaŋwǎŋwaŋ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ mwaŋwaŋ bɛchak. Bákù nyaka bɛyǎ ndɛn chu ɛnɛ ɛya nkáp nɛ ɛchak mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu.
Mɛnyɨŋ mɛnwi ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛpɛ́m bɛrɛm bɛ, “Amen!” Nɛ bǒbati bákwɛ́n amɨk bare chyɛ kɛnókó ntá mmu anɛ achi ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ nɛ ntá Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n.
Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ bɛbhak chak ndǔ babhi ankɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛtayɛka Mandɛm mfay achi chak ndǔ babhi ankɛm!”
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, bárɔ́k bachwe amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm bábhó bɛtɔŋ bo mbɔ ɛnyǔ ángɛl aghati bhɔ. Mǔngo bachiǎkap nɛ nkwɔ́ ywi bábhɨŋɨ bǒbati ɛtɔk Israɛl mankɛm, bákɛ́m ɛchɛmɛ, bachyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mandɔ́k mamfɛrɛ bǒnto ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ mantwɔ nɛ bhɔ.
Afɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ ntá bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ fá amɨk, akʉ bɛ bɔ́ bɛ́kɛ́ bhɔŋ kɛnókó bɛsí bho ndǔ ású bhɔ́ amɨk. Atɔ́ŋ bhɔ mbɔ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bákɛ́mɛ́ ɛbhɨ̌nɛnu. Ɛbhɨ̌ nɛnu ɛyɔ ɛbhak nɛwú Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Asɔt awɔ́nɛm amfǎy bɛfóŋó ɛbhɔ ɛnyuyɔ bɛfʉɛt ndǔ nɛwú Kristo ndǔ ɛkotákátí.
Ghók ká mmu anɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́chay. Cháy ka mmu anɛ ákway bɛway mmʉɛt yɛka, nɛ ankwáy mɛmɛsɛ be amɛm nɛpǐngo!
Nkʉ bo mángɔ́ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛ ndu nnáŋá bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ.
Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yí ákʉ́ ɛ́chyɛ̀ bo Israɛl maŋák, arɔk ambɨ nɛ bɛbʉ́ bhi, achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mánkɛ́m Píta nkwɔ́. Ɛyɔ ɛ́fákárí ndǔ mpok Ɛpǎ brɛt anɛ kɛbhɔŋ yís.
Ghok ka, yi ǎtwɔ̀ amɛm nɛbháŋ, nɛ chɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu angɔ yi nɛ amɨ́k. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áyɛ́mɛ́ yi nɛ nɛkɔŋ ǎghɔ̀ chɔŋ yi nkwɔ. Manɛrɛ́kɛrɛ́ bho ankɛm fá amɨk bádì chɔŋ kɛbhɔ ɛ̌ti yi. Ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛfakari ɛnyu ɛyɔ. Amen.
Mɛ, ndɨ́ŋɨ́ sayri bɛ́ tɛ̌ndu bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo, yí afyɛ́ bhe ntɨ ndǔ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ yí ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ bhe. Nɛ tɛ̌ndu bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ, ǎkʉ bɛ́ mǎnkɔ́ŋ batɨ, mǎntɔŋ bɔ́ bɛrɨ̌ndu.
Arɛ́, bákʉ́ yi nɛnyíɛ́ běku. Matá kɛ áfʉɛ̀t nyaka nɛnyíɛ́. Lásárɔs abhak mmu amɔt ndǔ bo abhɛn bachɔkɔ mányiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ Yesu.
Yesu apɛt atɛ́m nɛkay nɛ́chák bɛ, “Kɛfɔ Mandɛm kɛchi mbɔ bɛyǎ nkáp anɛ́ bágʉɛ́bhɛ́ anyɛ́n nɛ ákɛ́m nsi mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu.
Ngátí bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ ngati bhɔ. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, mmɨk apap bhɔ mbɔnyunɛ bápú bǒ mmɨk anɛ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mpú mmǔ mmɨk.
Nɛfú Yesu áfú amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, nkoŋo ywi amɔt arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, yɨŋɨ. Báte ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛnɛ-o! Batǎy anɛ́ básɔ́rɛ́ báté yɔ́ árɨ ácha!”
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ yɛ Kapɛ̌naum bárɔ́k atú Judɛ́ya. Bákɨ́ŋɨ Manyu Jɔ́dan. Ngɛ́mtay bho, bápɛt báre rɔŋ ntá yi. Are tɔ́ŋ bɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ákʉ nyaka mpoknkɛm.
Chɔŋ nkʉ yɛ yi? Chɔŋ nnɨ́k nɔkɔ mmʉɛt nɛ ɛfóŋó ɛya nɛ nnɨkmʉɛt nɛ nkaysi ya nkwɔ. Chɔŋ nkway nɔkɔ bakway nɛ ɛfóŋó ɛya nɛ nkwáy nɔkɔ nɛ nkaysi ya nkwɔ́.
Chi ndu ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ kɛ Mandɛm abhɨŋɨ bhe mbɔ ɛnyǔ Yesu Kristo nkwɔ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti yɛka, arɔ be ɛrɨŋ bɛ mǎnkóŋó nɔ́kɔ́ bayat yi.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyuyɔ mbɔnyunɛ akap anɛ́ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhé átɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ mbok anɛ sɛ́ghàti bhé ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo achwe amɛm batɨ yɛka sayri.
Bafa bare rɔŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nkwɔ Yesu bátó bhɔ́. Ɛnɛ́ bárɔ̀ŋ atú Foníshia nɛ atú Samária, báre téé ndǔ bɛtɔk ɛbhɛn bɛchi ambi mángati nɔkɔ bǒnkwɔ́ bɛ́ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mánóko mbok Yesu nkwɔ. Ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ bakoŋo Yesu bɛyǎ maŋák.
Bǎrɨŋɨ mbi anɛ árɔ̀ŋ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ.”
Yɛ̌ ɛ́mbak chí bɛ́ mɛ́tàŋ bhó, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ mɛ́tàŋ ɛ́chí ɛrɨ́rɨ́ mbɔnyunɛ puyɛ̌ mɛ awántí kɛ nchí taŋ bo. Mɛ nɛ mmu anɛ átó mɛ kɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m ɛnyǔ mmu áchí.
Wɔ nkwɔ́ ɔpú kwáy bɛghɔ mbʉ ntɨ mǔbɛtɨk ntínso mbɔ ɛnyǔ ngɔ́ wɔ ntínso?’
Bɛyǎ bo bárɔ́k ntá yi mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Jɔ̌n ábhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛ́mɔt, kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti mmǔ anɛ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp.”
Bɔ̌ma, nchí nɨk be mmʉɛt bɛ mǎnsɔt mpok nɛ bo abhɛn bátwɔ̀ nɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ nɛntɨ ɛnɛka nɛ bákʉ̀ bo mántɨ́knsɛm ntá Mandɛm ndǔ bátɔ̀ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi kɛkúrí nɛ ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ́kɔ́. Bák ká nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ nɛ bhɔ́.
María ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, afate, áyák arɔk ntá Yesu.
Arɛm bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ mbák bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ yibhiri mǎndɔ́p mbɔ mǎmbɔ, bǎpú kway bɛbhak ndǔ mpǎy bho abhɛn Mandɛm achi Mfɔ wap wáwák.
Ntɛ́msí anɛ bɛyǎ bhɛka bǎká bɛ mánchyɛ mmu wu akway nɔ.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka abhɔŋ yɛ́ bɛrɔ bɛpɔ̌ bɛpɨŋ mɛnkɛm nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́gháŋá yi amʉɛt. Sɛptí ká mmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm, mǎmfyɛ́ ntí ndǔ Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛnɛ yi ápɨ̀ amɛm batɨ yɛka. Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛnɛ ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bhe.
nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ mánchɔŋti bɛsí bhap nɛ Yesu ndu bábhíkí bhʉɛrɛ nku mbɨ anɛ mányú nɛ yi.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ná ɛchi yɛ bɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ákʉ nyaka Mfɔ Debhít ambɨŋɨ yi bɛ ‘Acha?’ Mfɔ Debhít arɛm nyaka bɛ,
Nikɔdɛ́mɔs, mmǔ wap amɔt anɛ ánáŋ árɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka ntá Yesu abhɛp bhɔ bɛ,
Chwé ká mǎmbak chi arɛ. Bǎkɛ́ kɔ bɛkɛt nɛ bɛkɛt. Nyíɛ́ ká, mǎnyú yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bachyɛ bhe. Ɛchi chak bɛ nkʉbɛtɨk ambɔŋ akap ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhi.
Tɛ̌ndu bǎsɔ́rɛ́ bɛ Yesu Kristo achi Acha, bʉrɛ́ ká nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi áyàŋ.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, ntɨ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɔp mɛ amɛm ndu mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ mmʉɛrɛ wa Táytɔs arɛ́.   Ngati yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mǎnchɔkɔ sayri.” Mfa ndɔk atú Masidónia. 
Yesu atɛ́m bɔ nɛkay ɛnɛ́n bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́ ká ɛnɔk *fig nɛ mɛnɔk bɛ́chák.
Mbɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ̌ áyábhɛ́ bo abhɛn bápú barɨŋɨ́ndak bɛsí bǒ mmɨk bɛ́ mámbák bǒbhi. Akʉ nɔ́ bɛ́ ntíánwɔ́p ámbák nɛ bǒ abhɛn básɔ̀t mmʉɛt ɛyap mbɔ barɨŋɨ́ndak. Ayap nkwɔ́ bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛsí bǒ mmɨk bɛ́ ntíánwɔ́p ámbák nɛ bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ ɛkɛn, mǔnkwɔ Fárisi amɔt abhɨŋɨ yi ndǔ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛkɛt ɛyi. Yesu arɔk achwe anywɔ́p, achɔkɔ amɨk mɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́.
Ngɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ mɛ̌kwáy bɛkʉ bɛ mbɔŋ nɛjwǐmɛm ndu barak anɛ, mbɛ́p Pɔ̌l mbák yi akɔŋ bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm bɛ mántaŋ nnyé ɛni arɛ́.
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyu ɛkáti ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Hoseya ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ Mandɛm arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Bo abhɛn bapu nyaka ‘Bǒbha’ chɔŋ mbɨŋɨ bhɔ bɛ bǒbha. Nɛ abhɛn mbɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ nyaka, chɔŋ mbɨŋɨ bhɔ bɛ ‘Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ.’
Apɛt atɔk amɨ́k yi. Ndɔŋ yɔ, mmǔ wu ayɨŋɨ dǐǐ, apɛt abho bɛghɔ mbaŋ, nɛ are ghɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ sayri.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ áchwe ndu nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt Mandɛm, ǎywɛ́mʉɛt ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhi mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋ nyaka nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt mpok ánáŋá bɛghoko mmɨk.
Kɛ bǒ abhɛn mányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ Yesu bábho mɛnywinti mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Agha nɛ́, anɛ árɛ̀m tɛ bɛ yi ǎfòŋori bɛbʉ́?”
Atɛ́mtí mɛ́ bawɛrɛ́riɛp amɛn amʉɛt bɛ bákɛ́pɛrɛ fyɛ́ mɛ bawɛt amʉɛt kɛ mámbɛmɛ mɛ.
Ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɨ ɛnɛ́ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɨŋɨ chi bɛ, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ barɛmɛ nyaka, ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm, yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛsɔt kɛboŋ ɛki ánɛ́nɛ́ bhɔ ntá bho,
Bɔ̌ma, mpok nchí awu nɛ bhe, mpú kwáy nyaka bɛghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m kɛpɨ ntá bo abhɛn Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achi nɛ bhɔ. Mbɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ chi mbɔ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m kɛpɨ ntá bo abhɛn mánóko Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, kɛ bǎkoŋo chi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn fá amɨk mbɔnyunɛ bǎchí nyaka mbɔ bɔ abhɛn bábhʉɛ́t amɔ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka mbɔ bakoŋo Kristo.
Ɛnɛ́ Píta ábhʉɛ́t amɛm sɛnta mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm, ngɔrɛ́ bɛtok aywi amɔt arɔk ɛbhak ɛnɛ Píta achi.
Anɛ ákòŋo asɔt kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ wu ndǔ nɛbhay agú kɛbhɔŋ mmɔ́.
Sɛ́ghɔ́ yɛ bɛ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm kɛ báchí bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham.
Mbuɔt anɛfu akwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk anɛ tákɔ nsěnse ágò arɛ́. Achak are gó, kɛ tákɔ nsěnse agó áchók yɔ.
Jems nɛ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n báchí nyaka mbɔ bɛkwap nɛntɨ bǒnkwɔ. Bághɔ́ nɔkɔ bɛ́ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn amɔ́ya tɛtɛp, bákáka mɛ nɛ Banábas nɛ amɔ́ ndu bɛ́tɔŋ bɛ́ bɛsɛ́ nɛ bhɔ sɛchi ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt. Sɛ́ka nɛ bhɔ bɛ́ mɛ nɛ Banábas sɛbhɔŋ bɛ́rɔŋ ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, bɔ mándɔk ntá bo Israɛl.
Bɔ́ mankɛm babhɛp yi bɛ, “Nɔ́ ɔchí Mmɔ̌ Mandɛm-ɛ?” Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎrɛ́mɛ́.”
Bɛrɨ̌ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ áchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó tɛtɛp bɛ́fú chí ndǔ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ abhɛn yi ákʉ̀.
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngátí nyaka bhe bɛ ‘Mmǔ bɛtok apú cha chi-bɛtok aywi.’ Mbák bǒ mmɨk báchyɛ́ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri, chɔŋ mánchyɛ be nkwɔ́ ɛsɔŋɔri. Mbɔ bábhʉ́rɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ngátí bhɔ, mbʉ́ chɔŋ mámbʉrɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ be nkwɔ bǎghàti bhɔ.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi báchyɛ́ nyaka ɛyɔŋ bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɨŋɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ Yesu achi, ángátí bhɔ́ bɛ mánkɛ́m yi.
nɔ́ bǎbyak bɛbhé Mandɛm, nɛ bǎbhʉ̀rɛ chi bɛpɨŋɨ́tɔk.
Nikɔdɛ́mɔs abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ná bákway bɛbhe mmu anɛ ánáŋ áchɨ́kɨ́? Ǎkway bɛ́pɛ́tnsɛm amɛm mɛniɛ máyi bɛ mámbé yi ndɔŋ achak kɛ?”
Mbuɔt anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mɔ́mbi anɛ achi amɛm nkɨ, até ndǔ mmu anɛ ághókó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti ɛnyu Mandɛm ábhak Mfɔ ywi, kɛ yi kɛjwimɛm, Satan atwɔ́ yɛ afɔŋɔ mbok anɛ Mandɛm ápɨ́ amɛm ntɨ ɛni.
Ɛchi mbɔ bɛ bǎgu mpok anɛ Yesu ágú. Nɛ́nɛ, nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ ɛnɛka nɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ awɔ́ Kristo ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi achi nɛ Mandɛm.
Ɛká bho bárɔk ntá Páílet bɛ́ ámfɛrɛ mǔkɛnɔŋ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyu yi ákʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmíɛ́ mpok Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ.
Yɛ̌ndu bághɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ nɔ Mandɛm ákʉ̀ ntá yap, bɛyǎ ɛbhap báré kʉ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛkʉ Mandɛm ámbé ntɨ nɛ bhɔ́. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, bɛyǎ bhap bágú amɛm baso, bɛrɛnɛ bhap bɛ́rɔ́p arɛ́, mbǎŋ nɛ mbaŋ.
Chɔŋ mámbɛbhɛ nɔkɔ bhe bɛ, “Yí afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎpɛtnsɛm, atwɔ kɛ́? Tɛsáy bɔtayɛsɛ bágú, mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́bhʉɛ́t chi ɛnyumɔ́t mbɔ mpok anɛ Mandɛm ághókó mmɨk.”
Ɛkʉ abho bɛ́káysi andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ nkʉ yi? Mbɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ nɛbhʉɛt bɛ́bhʉrɛ mbwɔt?’
Nɛ́nɛ, sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ antɨ bɛbhɛp wɔ. Ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ sɛ́nókó bɛ́ ɔfu chí ntá Mandɛm.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ághókó mɛnkɛm mɛ́nòŋ nɛ bɛyǎ ɛkwak nywɔp ɛnɛn yi átɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ bo abhɛn bachi bɔ̌bhi.
Bápɛ́rɛ fe Jɔ̌n, anáŋ ǎjwìti nyaka bho. Ajwiti Yesu nkwɔ. Nɛ mpok Yesu ánɨ̀kmʉɛt, nɛbu nɛ́nɛ́nɛ.
Yesu apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ mǎngɔ ‘Ɛrɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ápábhɛ́’ téé ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɛ́bhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛbhak. Mpok yɔ, bo abhɛn bachi atú Judɛ́ya mámbʉ́ɛ́ mámbɛ́sɛ́ amfǎy njiɛ. [Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ápáy ɛkáti-nɛ ámbʉ́rɛ́ antí, anjwimɛm.]
Kɛ mbák mmu anɛ ápú nkoŋo Yesu, yɛ̌ chí mbakanɛm, yɛ̌ chí ngɔrɛ́, ǎyáŋ bɛ́rɔ́ ntɨ, mándɔ́ yí ándɔ́k. Ɛ́mbák nɔ́, ɛbhé Mandɛm ɛ́pú kɛ́m yɛ̌ chí ngɔrɛ́, yɛ̌ chí mbakanɛm, mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm apú yáŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́nsɔ́ŋɔ́rí ntɨ mɔ́ywi amɛm.
Yesu apɛt arɔk nɛpaká Manyu Gálili. Ngɛ́mtay bo báre rɔŋ ntá yi, antɔŋ nɔkɔ bhɔ.
Chɔŋ mɛnyǔ bho mɛnkɛm mámpap be ɛ̌ti ya. Kɛ Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áté kpirí tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti.
Sɛ́fú amɛm áchwí sɛ́kó sɛ́rɔ́k ɛtɔk. Sɛ́ghɔ́ mpay bakoŋo Yesu arɛ, sɛ́chɔ́kɔ nɛ bhɔ́ ndǔ manywɔp tándrámɔt. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ akʉ bɔ baghati Pɔ̌l bɛ ákɛ́mɔ bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm.
Bɛti mɛ́mɔt, Yesu Acha aghati Pɔ̌l ndǔ kɛnɔ́ amɨk anti fúú bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ cháy. Dɔ́k ambɨ bɛ́gháti bo ɛ̌ti ya. Kɛ́chɔkɔ kpak.
